### [1] [DreamCharacter-1: From 3D Generative Foundation Models to Product-Ready Character Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07817)
*Weizhe Liu,Yunjie Wu,Xiangqian Shu,Guangwei Wang,Xiangyu Xu,Peng Li,Yujie Li,Hengkai Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DreamCharacter-1 是一个轻量级的后适应框架，用于将预训练的3D基础模型校准为高保真、可投入生产的3D角色生成。该框架基于3D基础骨干网络，包含三个任务导向组件：几何后训练（提升精细表面细节）、纹理后训练（合成高分辨率纹理并优化遮挡区域外观）和推理加速（实现可扩展部署）。大量定量和定性实验表明，DreamCharacter-1 生成的3D角色资产在视觉表现和结构鲁棒性上均优于现有最先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前3D角色生成方法在细节表现、纹理质量和部署效率方面仍存在不足，难以满足工业级生产需求。因此需要一种高效、轻量且能显著提升生成质量的后适应框架。

Method: 基于3D基础模型构建，通过几何后训练、纹理后训练和推理加速三个模块进行优化，分别针对表面细节、纹理质量和计算效率进行改进。

Result: DreamCharacter-1 在视觉质量与结构稳定性上均超越现有方法，生成的3D角色资产具备高保真度与生产可用性，同时支持高效部署。

Conclusion: DreamCharacter-1 成功实现了对3D基础模型的高效后适应，显著提升了3D角色生成的质量与实用性，为工业级3D内容创作提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: We present DreamCharacter-1, a lightweight post-adaptation framework that calibrates pretrained 3D foundation models toward high-fidelity, production-ready 3D character generation. Building upon a 3D foundation backbone, our pipeline incorporates three task-oriented components: (1) geometry post-training, which enhances fine-grained surface details through geometric preference optimization; (2) texture post-training, which synthesizes high-resolution textures and refines the appearance of occluded regions; and (3) inference acceleration, which enables scalable deployment. Extensive quantitative and qualitative experiments demonstrate that DreamCharacter-1 produces visually compelling and structurally robust 3D character assets, consistently surpassing state-of-the-art character generation methods.

</details>


### [2] [GIRAF: Towards Generalizable Human Interactions with Articulated Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07880)
*Xiaohan Zhang,Sebastian Starke,Alexander Winkler,Federica Bogo,Samir Aroudj,Yuting Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种文本条件的扩散模型，用于生成逼真的全身人类与关节物体交互动作。通过物体中心表示、混合域训练策略和基于接触的增强方案，解决了运动与操作协同、跨物体泛化等挑战，在未见物体配置上表现出优越的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型在处理全身人类与关节物体交互时存在局限：部分仅关注静态物体上的简单活动，另一些则局限于手部操作。缺乏能够协调行走、精细接触与物体运动的通用方法，且真实配对数据稀缺，限制了模型在多样化物体位置与形状下的泛化能力。

Method: 采用物体中心表示将手-物接触与物体表面统一建模；使用混合域训练策略平衡行走与交互学习；引入基于接触的增强方法扩展训练多样性。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在未见过的物体配置下具有强泛化能力，优于当前最先进的方法。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效解决了全身人类与关节物体交互生成中的关键挑战，为机器人训练和虚拟代理应用提供了更真实、通用的解决方案。

Abstract: Synthesizing realistic full-body human interactions with articulated objects is a fundamental challenge for embodied AI and graphics, with applications in robotics training and virtual agents. Existing models remain limited: some focus on simple activities with static objects, while others restrict attention to hand-only manipulation. This leaves open the problem of generating coordinated full-body motion that approaches, manipulates, and moves articulated objects in a realistic and generalizable way. The key difficulty lies in reasoning jointly about locomotion, fine-grained contact, and object articulation. Models must capture subtle hand-object correspondences that transfer across object geometries, while also producing seamless transitions from navigation to manipulation. At the same time, the scarcity of large-scale paired motion-scene data makes it difficult to generalize across diverse object positions and shapes. We introduce a text-conditioned diffusion model that addresses these challenges through three core ideas: an object-centric representation that unifies hand-object contact with object surfaces, a mixed-domain training strategy that balances locomotion and interaction, and a contact-based augmentation scheme that expands training diversity. Through experiments, our method demonstrated strong generalization to unseen object configurations, surpassing current state-of-the-art methods.

</details>


### [3] [3D Reconstruction of deciduous Trees using low-cost UAV- and Crane-based Photogrammetry for Monitoring Shoot Elongation across entire Canopies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07905)
*Stephan Nebiker,Micha Tschanz,Nando Amport,Frederik Baumgarten*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究利用低成本无人机摄影测量和多相机CraneCam系统，在整个生长季节内对落叶树进行三维重建，以监测枝条伸长（初级生长）。研究评估了传感器性能、数据采集与处理策略，并分析了三维点云的精度、分辨率和完整性。结果表明，使用重量小于250克的消费级无人机可实现5-6毫米的三维点云精度，三维重建完整度达92%-98%。研究还引入3D打印的地面真值枝条，用于评估细小结构（如细枝）的重建能力，并探讨了基于点云进行全树骨架化处理的初步实验与操作挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对气候变暖导致的极端天气事件（如高温、干旱、晚霜）对树木初级生长的影响尚不明确，主要由于缺乏有效的枝条伸长监测技术。尽管径向生长已有连续监测手段（如树干仪），但枝条伸长监测长期被忽视，限制了对气候变化下树木生长响应的理解。因此，亟需发展一种可广泛部署的三维重建方法，以支持对整株树冠枝条生长的量化监测。

Method: 采用低空无人机摄影测量（UAV photogrammetry）与多相机移动平台（CraneCam系统）在真实环境条件下获取两个研究区域的树冠影像数据。通过多视图立体视觉技术生成高密度三维点云，并结合3D打印的地面真值枝条评估细部结构（如细枝）的重建精度。进一步开展点云后处理，包括配准、去噪、密度优化，并探索基于点云的树冠骨架化算法。

Result: 使用消费级无人机（<250 g）获得的三维点云精度达到5–6毫米，整体重建完整性在92%至98%之间，具体取决于无人机型号。3D打印的地面真值枝条成功验证了系统对细枝等微小结构的识别能力。初步实验表明，基于点云的树冠骨架化具有可行性，但面临遮挡、密度分布不均等挑战。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了低成本无人机与多相机系统在实现整株树冠三维重建方面的有效性，为长期监测树木初级生长提供了可靠的技术路径。该方法具备可扩展性与成本优势，有望推动对气候变化下树木生长动态的系统性研究。

Abstract: Tree growth determines how much CO2 is sequestered from the atmosphere and temporarily stored in woody biomass. At the same time tree growth is affected by increasing temperatures, more frequent drought periods, late frosts and other extreme events associated with climate change. While continuous measurements of radial (secondary) tree growth using dendrometers are well established, monitoring of shoot elongation (primary growth) has largely been neglected because suitable measurement techniques are lacking. As a result, the effects of climate change on primary tree growth remain insufficiently understood. This work aims at reconstructing native deciduous trees in 3D as a basis for measuring and monitoring shoot elongation over entire tree canopies. Here we explored the use of low-cost UAV photogrammetry and of a multi-camera CraneCam system under real-world conditions. Data were collected in two study areas over an entire growing season. We present sensor evaluations, photogrammetric data acquisition and processing strategies. A special focus is placed on the analysis of the resulting photogrammetric 3D point clouds in terms of accuracy, resolution and completeness. Results demonstrate 3D point accuracies of 5-6 mm for entire trees using consumer-grade UAVs weighing less than 250 g and a 3D reconstruction completeness between 92% and 98% depending on the UAV type. The paper introduces a novel 3Dprinted ground-truth branch to evaluate the capability to reconstructing fine-detail structures such as thin tree shoots. Finally, we discuss operational challenges and initial experiments towards a skeletonization of entire trees based on photogrammetric point clouds.

</details>


### [4] [Adversarial Decoys: Misdirecting Attention-Based Defenses in ViT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07922)
*Giulia Marchiori Pietrosanti,Giulio Rossolini,Giorgio Buttazzo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为对抗性诱饵（adversarial decoys）的新方法，通过独立优化的图像补丁来重新分配注意力，从而绕过基于注意力的测试时防御。该方法将错误分类与防御规避解耦：原始对抗区域负责误导预测，而独立的诱饵则操纵防御所依赖的注意力排名。通过分层目标提升目标令牌的注意力，使其超过非目标令牌。该方法不依赖于具体攻击，可与任何现有对抗补丁攻击兼容。在ImageNet上的实验表明，诱饵能有效将高注意力分数从真实对抗区域转移，同时保持攻击有效性，揭示了仅以注意力强度作为对抗性相关性指标的根本局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于注意力的测试时防御方法依赖于高注意力得分的图像标记来检测对抗性补丁，但这种方法存在漏洞：攻击者可以通过引入独立优化的对抗性诱饵，主动引导注意力到特定目标标记上，从而避开防御机制。因此，需要一种能够解耦错误分类与防御规避的新策略，以更有效地生成鲁棒性更强的对抗样本。

Method: 提出对抗性诱饵（adversarial decoys），即独立优化的图像补丁，其作用是诱导模型注意力集中在特定目标标记上。采用分层目标函数，最大化目标标记的注意力得分，并抑制非目标标记的竞争。该诱饵与原始对抗攻击独立优化，实现攻击与防御规避的解耦。

Result: 在多个ViT架构和对抗攻击类型下，实验结果显示，对抗性诱饵能成功将高注意力分数从原始对抗区域转移至目标标记，同时维持较高的攻击成功率。这表明当前依赖注意力大小作为对抗性标志的方法存在根本缺陷，无法有效区分真实威胁与被诱导的注意力热点。

Conclusion: 对抗性诱饵揭示了基于注意力的测试时防御机制的内在弱点：注意力强度并非对抗性有效性的可靠指示器。通过解耦攻击目标与注意力操控，该方法提供了一种通用且高效的对抗攻击增强策略，对构建更鲁棒的视觉Transformer系统具有重要启示。

Abstract: Vision Transformers (ViTs) remain vulnerable to localized adversarial attacks, e.g., adversarial patches, while recent test-time defenses mitigate them by suppressing image tokens with abnormally high attention scores. These defenses exploit a strong coupling between attention and adversarial effectiveness: adversarial tokens often need to attract substantial attention to influence the prediction. We introduce adversarial decoys, independently optimized image patches that redirect the attention, and therefore related defenses, toward selected target tokens. Rather than jointly optimizing misclassifications and defense evasion, our approach decouples the two objectives: the original adversarial region induces the incorrect prediction, while a separate decoy manipulates the attention ranking used by the defense. A layer-wise objective increases target-token attention and promotes these tokens above competing non-target ones. Since the decoy is optimized independently of the underlying attack, the method is attack-agnostic and can be easily integrated with any existing adversarial patch attack. Experiments on ImageNet across multiple ViT architectures and attacks show that decoys can redirect high attention scores away from the true adversarial region while preserving much of the attack effectiveness. These results reveal a fundamental limitation of using attention magnitude as an indicator of adversarial relevance.

</details>


### [5] [Beyond Thermal Imaging: Inferring Thermophysical Properties from Time-Resolved Thermal Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07962)
*Chenghao Xu,Malcolm Mielle,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ThermoField是一种统一热场景重建与热物理参数估计的框架，通过可微分热传导模拟实现复杂3D场景中几何、热扩散率的空间分布估计及热演化预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有热成像方法在复杂3D环境中难以同时恢复温度场和热物理属性；而传统逆问题方法受限于简化几何和受控条件，缺乏对复杂场景的适用性。因此亟需一种能联合重建几何、估计热物理参数并预测热演化的统一框架。

Method: 将热物理属性和场景几何表示为可学习的神经场，结合不同微分热传导求解器，利用时空热观测数据约束模型，实现端到端的联合优化。

Result: ThermoField成功实现了复杂3D场景下的几何重建、空间变化热扩散率估计以及未知环境条件下热演化的预测，在真实与合成数据上均表现出优异性能。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了热场景重建与逆热传导分析之间的桥梁，提出了一种在复杂三维场景中实现物理可解释参数推断的新范式，为数字孪生、基础设施监测、机器人感知等应用提供了新工具。

Abstract: Inferring latent physical properties from sensory observations is a fundamental challenge in machine perception. Among available sensing modalities, thermal imaging is particularly promising because temperature evolution is directly governed by heat-transfer physics and therefore encodes information about underlying thermophysical properties of a scene. Recovering spatially resolved thermophysical properties from thermal observations could transform applications ranging from digital twins and infrastructure monitoring to robotics and scientific imaging. However, existing thermal scene reconstruction methods can recover temperature fields in complex 3D environments without identifying the thermophyiscal properties that govern thermal evolution, whereas inverse methods provide physically interpretable parameter estimation but typically rely on simplified geometries and controlled experimental conditions.
  Here we introduce ThermoField, a framework that unifies thermal scene reconstruction and thermophysical parameter estimation through differentiable heat-transfer simulation. The proposed framework represents these quantities as spatially varying neural fields and constrains them through scene geometry, governing heat-transfer physics, and temporal thermal observations. We demonstrate that ThermoField jointly reconstructs geometry, estimates spatially varying thermal diffusivity, and predicts thermal evolution under previously unseen environmental conditions. By integrating neural scene representations with differentiable heat-transfer solver, the framework enables physically interpretable parameter inference in complex 3D scenes. Our results establish a bridge between thermal scene reconstruction and inverse heat-transfer analysis, providing a unified approach for geometry reconstruction, thermophysical property estimation, and predictive thermal simulation from thermal observations.

</details>


### [6] [LOGOS: Language-guided Oriented Object Detection in Aerial Scenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08004)
*Trong-Thuan Nguyen,Minh-Triet Tran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LOGOS 是一种基于Transformer的新型方法，利用文本提示引导航空影像中定向目标的检测。通过引入提示调制的内容查询，动态调整模型关注点，显著提升复杂环境下的检测精度，尤其在密集和旋转目标场景中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在处理遥感图像中目标方向变化、密度差异和复杂背景时存在角度不连续、查询尺寸固定及稀疏或杂乱场景效率低等问题，因此需要一种更灵活、高效且鲁棒的检测方法。

Method: 提出基于Transformer的LOGOS框架，利用文本提示调制内容查询，实现对定向目标的动态注意力聚焦，增强模型在复杂场景中的适应性与准确性。

Result: 在DOTA数据集上的大量实验表明，LOGOS优于现有最先进方法，特别是在密集排列和旋转目标场景中表现出更强的检测性能。

Conclusion: LOGOS为遥感应用中的定向目标检测提供了更稳健、可扩展的解决方案，显著提升了复杂地理空间场景下的检测能力。

Abstract: Object detection in geospatial scenes, such as satellite and aerial imagery, poses significant challenges due to the varying orientations and densities of objects, as well as the complex backgrounds inherent to remote sensing imagery. Traditional methods for oriented object detection have struggled to address issues such as angular discontinuity, fixed query sizes, and inefficiencies in handling sparse or cluttered scenes. In this paper, we propose LOGOS, a novel transformer-based approach that leverages textual prompts to guide the detection of oriented objects in aerial scenes. In particular, our proposed approach incorporates prompt-modulated content queries to dynamically adjust the model's focus based on the provided text, thereby improving object detection accuracy in complex environments. Empirically, extensive experiments on the DOTA dataset demonstrate that LOGOS outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods, particularly in densely packed and rotated object scenarios. Our approach offers a significant step forward in improving the robustness and scalability of oriented object detection in remote sensing applications.

</details>


### [7] [FedTR: Federated Learning Framework with Transfer Learning for Industrial Visual Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08014)
*Vikash Sathiamoorthy,Shuo Huai,Hao Kong,Di Liu,Wendy Yong Yi Loy,Christian Makaya,Daren Ho,Ravi Subramaniam,Qian Lin,Weichen Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FedTR 是一种结合迁移学习的新型联邦学习框架，专为自主工业视觉检测（IVI）中的标签缺陷识别任务设计。该方法先在公开数据集上预训练模型，再在分布式私有数据上进行联邦学习微调，有效应对数据稀缺和任务复杂性挑战。实验表明，FedTR 在同质与异质数据下分别达到 95.5% 和 94.2% 的端到端文字识别准确率，性能接近集中式训练水平，验证了其有效性与可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业视觉检测中数据隐私保护与数据稀缺问题严重制约了联邦学习的性能，尤其在标签缺陷识别这类复杂任务中，现有方法难以兼顾隐私性与准确性。因此亟需一种能有效利用有限私有数据并保持高性能的联邦学习框架。

Method: FedTR 首先在公开数据集上预训练模型，利用迁移学习获取通用特征表示；随后在各参与方本地私有数据上进行联邦学习，通过模型微调逐步适应特定任务。该过程在保护数据隐私的同时提升模型泛化能力。

Result: FedTR 在私有墨盒数据集上实现 95.5%（同质数据）和 94.2%（异质数据）的端到端文字识别准确率，性能与集中式训练相当，显著优于传统联邦学习方法。

Conclusion: FedTR 通过融合迁移学习与联邦学习，成功解决了工业视觉检测中数据受限与隐私保护之间的矛盾，为自主标签缺陷识别提供了高效、可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) is a collaborative learning scheme to train deep learning models, where collaborating parties can consolidate their models without sharing local data with other parties, hence preserving data privacy. Nevertheless, when implementing FL in Industrial visual inspection (IVI), the constraints posed by limited data availability and the intricate nature of the inspection tasks significantly impact the performance of the resulting model. This paper introduces FedTR, a novel FL framework incorporating transfer learning designed for Autonomous IVI, focusing on the challenging task of identifying label defects through end-to-end text recognition. Transfer learning is a method that leverages the knowledge of a pre-trained model to adapt to a different dataset. FedTR initially trains the model using a publicly available dataset, after which performs the essential federated learning process with model fine-tuning on the distributed and limited private data. Extensive experiment results demonstrate the effectiveness and feasibility of FedTR on private ink cartridge datasets for label defect identification. FedTR achieves an end-to-end text recognition word-level accuracy of 95.5% and 94.2% on homogeneous and heterogeneous data respectively. Additionally, it attains performance levels that are on par with those achieved through centralized training.

</details>


### [8] [LightCrafter: PBR-Conditioned Video Diffusion Refinement for Controllable and Consistent Relighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08016)
*Zixin Guo,Yehonathan Litman,Yifeng He,John Miller,Chuhan Chen,Deva Ramanan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LightCrafter提出一种混合视频重光照方法，将重光照任务重构为对基于物理的渲染（PBR）代理视频的视频翻译。通过将目标光照信息烘焙到PBR代理中，避免了扩散模型学习复杂光照概念的需求，提升了光照控制精度与长时序一致性。结合合成数据和真实无配对视频的后训练策略，有效捕捉全局光照等复杂效果，在真实世界基准上超越现有最先进方法，并贡献了新的合成基准与开源资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频重光照方法存在重建噪声大、难以建模全局光照等问题；而基于扩散模型的生成式方法受限于长期视频翻译能力及训练数据配对需求，导致控制力弱、时序不稳定。亟需一种兼具物理合理性与强时序一致性的高效重光照框架。

Method: 提出LightCrafter框架：先利用逆向渲染生成输入视频的PBR代理，再将该代理在目标光照下进行前向渲染，作为视频翻译的目标；使用扩散模型以该代理视频为输入，生成最终输出。通过后训练CogVideoX模型融合光度先验，增强对全局光照等复杂效应的建模能力。

Result: 在多个真实世界重光照基准上性能优于现有最先进方法；在合成数据集上验证了方法的有效性；提供了新基准、评估指标与开源代码，推动领域发展。

Conclusion: LightCrafter通过结合物理渲染与生成模型的优势，实现了高质量、高可控性且时序一致的视频重光照，为未来视频编辑与虚拟内容生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Video relighting requires balancing long-form temporal consistency with a physically grounded understanding of light transport, which depends on accurate estimation of intrinsic scene properties such as materials, geometry, and illumination. Existing methods follow two paradigms: (1) reconstruct a video's photometric properties via inverse rendering and relight them to a target illumination via forward rendering, using physically-based rendering (PBR) or a neural renderer; these suffer from noisy reconstructions and struggle with hard-to-model effects such as global illumination. (2) Frame the task as generative video-to-video translation conditioned on relighting targets (a target environment map or text); this limits relighting control and temporal stability, since diffusion models struggle to translate long-form videos, and is constrained by the availability of input/relit training pairs. We propose LightCrafter, a hybrid pipeline that reformulates video relighting as video translation of a proxy video: rather than translating the input video directly to the target, we translate a PBR rendering of the input under the target illumination to the final target. This bakes illumination targets into the PBR proxy, removing the need to teach the diffusion model illumination concepts like environment maps, and enables more intricate lighting control while naturally providing long-form temporal consistency. We show PBR renders alone already outperform some prior art but struggle with effects like global illumination; to capture these, we leverage photometric priors in video generation models by post-training CogVideoX on synthetic video pairs and real-world unpaired videos. We outperform prior state-of-the-art on existing real-world relighting benchmarks and contribute a synthetic benchmark for further analysis. We will release our dataset, benchmark, metrics, and code.

</details>


### [9] [SAGA: Stable Acceleration Guidance for Autoregressive Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08020)
*Thanh-Nhan Vo,Trong-Thuan Nguyen,Trung-Hoang Le,Tam V. Nguyen,Minh-Triet Tran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出SAGA，一种无需训练的稳定加速度引导方法，用于自回归视频生成。通过引入基于有限窗口Slepian投影的加速度域谱引导目标和结构化自回归噪声初始化策略，SAGA有效抑制短时程时间相关性，同时保留长时程运动结构，显著提升视频生成的时序质量，减少闪烁、抖动和结构漂移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归视频扩散模型在流式传输和长时视频生成中效率高，但重复使用生成的潜在表示作为因果上下文会放大时间误差，导致闪烁、运动抖动和结构漂移等不稳定现象。

Method: 提出SAGA方法，结合加速度域谱引导目标（基于有限窗Slepian投影）与结构化自回归噪声初始化策略，无需重训练或修改骨干网络，可直接应用于现有的分块自回归扩散模型。

Result: 实验表明，SAGA在多个自回归扩散模型上均显著提升时序质量；在Self-Forcing模型上，时序质量从97.30提升至97.91，图像质量从69.60提升至70.51；谱分析与人类偏好测试均证实其有效降低时间不稳定性并保持视觉保真度。

Conclusion: SAGA是一种高效、通用且无需训练的时序稳定性增强方法，可广泛应用于现有自回归视频生成框架，显著改善生成视频的时间一致性。

Abstract: Autoregressive video diffusion enables efficient streaming and long-horizon video generation, but repeatedly reusing generated latents as causal context can amplify temporal errors, resulting in flickering, motion jitter, and structural drift. In this paper, we investigate this failure mode from a spectral kinematic perspective and identify discrete latent acceleration as an effective signal for revealing unstable high-frequency temporal perturbations. To this end, we propose SAGA, a training-free \textbf{\textit{s}}table \textbf{\textit{a}}cceleration \textbf{\textit{g}}uidance approach for \textbf{\textit{a}}utoregressive video generation. SAGA integrates an acceleration domain spectral guidance objective based on finite-window Slepian projections with a structured autoregressive noise initialization strategy that suppresses short-range temporal correlations while preserving long-range motion structure. Without retraining or modifying the backbone, SAGA can be directly applied to existing chunk-wise autoregressive diffusion models, which is the prevalent setting for high-quality generation. Extensive experiments show that SAGA consistently improves temporal quality across multiple autoregressive diffusion models. On Self-Forcing, SAGA improves Temporal Quality from 97.30 to 97.91 and Image Quality from 69.60 to 70.51. Moreover, spectral analysis and human preference studies demonstrate that SAGA reduces temporal instability while maintaining visual fidelity.

### [10] [APIVOT: Adaptive Planning with Interleaved Vision-Language Thoughts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08024)
*Emily Jin,Joy Hsu,Yiqing Xu,Weiyu Liu,Nick Haber,Jiajun Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: APIVOT 是一种基于视觉-语言模型（VLM）的规划器，通过自适应地交替使用语言和视觉思维来实现长时程机器人规划。它利用语言进行语义推理，同时用视觉思维作为未来状态的内部验证，以确保几何可行性。在空间受限的厨房任务中，APIVOT 显著优于通用 VLM 和先前的规划框架，尤其在复杂空间约束下表现突出。实验表明，该方法能学习到有效的模态选择行为，提升规划成功率与推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时程机器人规划需要同时处理语义任务结构与几何可行性问题。现有方法难以有效融合语言理解与空间感知，尤其在空间受限环境中表现不佳。因此，亟需一种能够自适应融合语言与视觉信息的规划机制。

Method: 提出 APIVOT 框架，通过动态交替使用语言思考（用于语义分解与目标选择）和视觉思考（用于生成未来状态并验证空间可行性），实现对复杂任务的高效规划。

Result: 在长时程厨房任务中，APIVOT 在各类场景下均优于通用 VLM 与传统规划方法，尤其在空间受限条件下取得显著提升；同时展现出良好的模态选择能力与推理效率。

Conclusion: 自适应地交错使用语言与视觉思维可显著提升长时程机器人规划的成功率与效率，为复杂环境下的智能体决策提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Long-horizon robot planning requires jointly reasoning over semantic task structure and geometric feasibility. To successfully execute a task, a robot must decompose goals, select task-relevant objects, and sequence actions, while ensuring that plans satisfy spatial constraints such as limited free space and object collisions. In this work, we propose APIVOT, a VLM-based planner that adaptively interleaves language and visual thoughts for long-horizon planning. APIVOT learns to leverage language for semantic reasoning, while using visual thoughts as imagined future states for internal verification of geometric feasibility. On long-horizon kitchen tasks, APIVOT outperforms general-purpose VLMs and prior planning frameworks, achieving the largest gains in spatially constrained settings. We find that APIVOT learns meaningful modality selection behavior, demonstrating that adaptive interleaving of vision-language thoughts improves both planning success and reasoning efficiency.

Method: 通过定义后训练在自动驾驶中的范围，将现有研究按监督形式组织为四类，并系统分析每类方法的特性与挑战。

Abstract: End-to-end models that map multimodal inputs directly to future trajectories/maneuvers have emerged as an increasingly prominent research paradigm in autonomous driving. This class of models includes both Vision-Language-Action models and trajectory-generative planners. Unlike classic machine learning applications, autonomous vehicles operate in safety-critical and interaction-intensive environments where traditional open-loop imitation of expert demonstrations is not sufficient to ensure reliability. In particular, small execution errors can accumulate over time, while recovery behaviors are scarce in training data. In addition, long-horizon objectives such as safety and driving comfort are not captured by pointwise labels either. These limitations have motivated a shift toward post-training techniques, which further refine driving policies beyond pure imitation. This survey presents a unified view of post-training for autonomous driving by defining its scope and organizing the existing literature into four major families based on the form of supervision they use. For each family, we discuss its capabilities, limitations, and open challenges. We aim to facilitate a systematic understanding of this emerging area and stimulate future research on reliable and efficient post-training for autonomous driving.

Considering the scarcity of instance-level annotations in UAV scenarios, we propose AeroTrack, a training-free unified framework. ### [13] [LDFE: Laplacian Decoupled Feature Enhancement Block for Dual-Stream CNN-based RGB-IR Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08076)
*Wenhao Dong,Xiaoyan Luo,Linlin Yang,Haodong Zhu,Xiaorong Shi,Guodong Guo,Baochang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Laplace解耦特征增强模块（LDFE），通过全局-局部分解、去噪、融合与重建，实现RGB和红外图像在多阶段双流CNN主干网络中的有效特征融合。LDFE采用拉普拉斯金字塔分离特征，结合全局状态空间增强（GS2E）与局部卷积相关增强（LC2E）模块，分别处理主模态与辅助模态间的跨模态注意力与长程依赖，并通过双分支交替角色实现双向交互；同时利用三重卷积提取局部细节。该方法在多个基准数据集上显著超越现有技术，mAP提升达2.0%至6.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极端环境下，RGB与红外图像具有互补信息，但现有方法仅关注双流CNN的特征融合设计，缺乏对模态特性与结构特性的综合考虑，导致融合效率不足。

Method: 提出LDFE模块，基于拉普拉斯金字塔将特征分解为全局与局部成分；使用GS2E进行跨模态噪声抑制与长程依赖建模，采用双分支交替主/辅角色机制；使用LC2E通过三重卷积增强局部细节，实现精细特征融合。

Abstract: The complementary information between RGB and IR images can significantly enhance object detection performance under extreme conditions. Existing methods prefer dual-stream CNN backbones built upon YOLO for feature extraction and focus on the design of feature fusion. In this paper, we introduce the Laplacian Decoupled Feature Enhancement block (LDFE) to fuse features from different stages of the dual-stream CNN backbone. By design, LDFE simultaneously considers the characteristics of modalities and structures for feature fusion by employing global-local decomposition, denoising, fusion, and reconstruction, sequentially. The LDFE first separates features into global and local components based on Laplacian Pyramid, and then performs denoising and fusion based on Global State Space Enhancement module (GS2E) and Local Convolutional Correlation Enhancement module (LC2E) separately. Specifically, the GS2E conducts a two-branch architecture for the main and auxiliary modalities. It dynamically suppresses noise in the main modality through cross-modal attention derived from the auxiliary modality, while employing a State Space Model to capture long-range dependencies within the global feature representations of the main modality. To obtain bidirectional interaction, the two modalities systematically alternate their main/auxiliary roles. Moreover, the LC2E suppresses noise in local features and leverages spatial and channel dimension along with triple convolution to extract fine-grained details for fusion. These innovative designs achieve a significant performance improvement, with mAP surpassing the SOTA methods 6.2%, 3.7%, 4.7%, 2.3%, 4.1% and 2.0% on M3FD, DroneVehicle, LLVIP, FLIR-Aligned, KAIST and VEDAI datasets,respectively.

### [16] [EVIS: A Physics-Grounded Event Camera Plugin for NVIDIA Isaac Sim](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08098)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 事件相机在机器人领域具有微秒级时间分辨率、低延迟和高动态范围的优势，但针对特定机器人和场景的标注事件数据稀缺且采集成本高昂，制约了事件感知与控制的发展。因此需要一种高效、真实且可扩展的数据生成方法。

Method: 开发EVIS事件相机插件，基于物理建模实现对数强度对比事件生成，支持每像素异步参考更新；通过稀疏关键帧+双向运动矢量插值技术降低计算开销；集成于Isaac Sim环境，兼容现有场景与物理引擎，支持噪声与运动模糊模拟。

Result: EVIS可在单个GPU上实现实时生成高质量、全标注的事件流，生成数据与真实事件相机特性高度一致，可直接用于训练或测试事件神经网络，显著提升事件感知系统开发效率。

Conclusion: EVIS为事件相机数据生成提供了一种高效、真实、可扩展的解决方案，有效缓解了真实数据稀缺问题，推动了事件基机器人感知与控制的发展。

Abstract: Event cameras offer microsecond temporal resolution, low latency, and high dynamic range, making them attractive for robotics. However, labeled event-camera data for a specific robot and scene is scarce and expensive to collect, which slows the development of event-based perception and control. We present EVIS: a physics-grounded event camera plugin for NVIDIA Isaac Sim that generates high-rate, fully labeled event streams directly inside a physics simulator. The plugin implements a faithful log-intensity contrast event model with per-pixel asynchronous reference updates; it migrates from a normal RGB camera with few changes and integrates into any Isaac Sim / Isaac Lab scene, inheriting the simulator's physics and frame-perfect ground truth. It is fully configurable, and offers an interpolation option that renders only sparse keyframes and synthesizes the in-between frames through bidirectional motion-vector warping, making real-time generation on a single GPU possible. Optional sensor noise and motion blur further narrow the gap to real cameras. The generated streams are directly usable by pretrained event networks for downstream tasks. Code repository: https://github.com/spikelab-jhu/isaac-sim-event-camera-plugin

### [17] [VSRo-200: A Romanian Visual Speech Recognition Dataset for Studying Supervision and Multimodal Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08112)

Result: 人工标注在小样本下表现更佳，而伪标签在大规模数据下仍具增益潜力；多模态融合在噪声条件下显著提升鲁棒性；基于VSRo-200训练的模型在LRRo基准上实现显著性能提升，证明其良好迁移能力。

Conclusion: VSRo-200 为低资源视觉语音识别提供了新的研究平台，支持对监督质量、域泛化和多模态融合的深入分析，推动了非主流语言在该领域的研究进展。

Abstract: We introduce VSRo-200, the first large-scale dataset for visual speech recognition (lip reading) in Romanian, comprising 200 hours of real-world podcast videos. Building on this dataset, we establish a benchmark for visual speech recognition in low-resource settings. We systematically study the impact of supervision quality, showing that while human annotations provide better performance at fixed data scales, pseudo-labels enable continued improvements through scalability. We further evaluate robustness under domain shift using curated out-of-distribution (OOD) test sets, and analyze audio-visual speech recognition (AVSR) under noisy conditions, where multimodal fusion significantly improves robustness compared to audio-only models. Finally, we demonstrate that representations learned on VSRo-200 transfer effectively to the LRRo benchmark for isolated word recognition, substantially outperforming previously reported results. Overall, VSRo-200 provides a new testbed for studying supervision, domain generalization, and multimodal fusion in low-resource visual speech recognition.

### [18] [Understanding and Mitigating the Video-Action Generalization Gap via Temporal Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08127)
*Utkarsh A. Mishra,Yongxin Chen,Danfei Xu,Yang Liu,Xi Chen,Jiayuan Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究生成式视频基础模型在微调至机器人动作数据时出现的组合泛化能力下降问题（即视频-动作泛化差距），提出一种基于注意力的时序比率（TR）度量，用以衡量动作头对未来的潜在轨迹依赖程度。TR不仅能预测模型的组合泛化能力，还能反映任务阶段变化中对未来的关注转移。基于此，提出一种推理时自适应引导方法，动态增强组合视频条件信号，有效缓解分布外-内部（OOD-ID）的组合泛化差距，在LIBERO基准和真实世界任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式视频基础模型虽具备强组合先验，但在微调为机器人动作模型后常丧失此类先验，导致泛化能力下降。该现象被称为视频-动作泛化差距，亟需理解其成因并提出解决方案。

Method: 引入时序比率（TR）作为注意力机制度量，分析模型对当前帧与未来潜在轨迹的依赖关系；基于TR的动态特性，设计推理时自适应引导策略，动态增强未来条件信号以提升组合泛化能力。

Result: 所提方法显著缓解了视频-动作模型在分布外-内部任务中的组合泛化差距，在LIBERO基准和真实世界任务中均取得良好性能。

Conclusion: TR是衡量模型对未来潜在轨迹依赖程度的有效指标，能解释模型泛化能力差异；通过在推理阶段利用TR的动态特性进行条件信号增强，可有效恢复模型的组合泛化能力。

Abstract: Generative video foundation models exhibit strong compositional priors, yet world-action models (WAMs) and video-action models (VAMs) often lose these priors after finetuning on robotic action data. We refer to this discrepancy as the video-action generalization gap. In this paper, we systematically investigate this gap by evaluating a comprehensive design space of VAMs, demonstrating that standard design choices yield no emergent explanation pattern. To explain this behavior, we introduce the Temporal Ratio (TR), an attention-based measure of how strongly the action head relies on future latent rollouts relative to the anchored current frame. TR has two key properties: first, a model's structural reliance on future-predictive latents, measured via TR, acts as a predictor of its compositional generalization capacity; second, it natively fluctuates based on task phase, shifting attention to future frames during planning and reverting to the present frame for precise manipulation. Finally, based on these findings, we propose an inference-time adaptive guidance method, which exploits this intrinsic feature attention pattern to dynamically amplify compositional video conditioning signals precisely when the policy relies on future rollouts. Evaluated on the LIBERO benchmark and real-world tasks, our approach mitigates the OOD-ID compositional generalization gap. More details: https://umishra.me/temporal-ratio/

### [20] [ProsMAE: Multi-Source MAE Pretraining for ISUP Grade Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08162)

Conclusion: ProsMAE通过多源预训练有效提升了组织病理学图像的表征学习能力，在前列腺癌分级任务中表现优于基线方法，但未来需进一步验证其在不同数据划分下的稳定性。

Abstract: Whole slide images (WSIs) provide rich diagnostic information for computational pathology, but their gigapixel scale, stain variation, scanner differences, tissue artifacts, and limited expert annotation make robust model training challenging. This paper presents a multi-source Masked Autoencoder (MAE) framework, named ProsMAE, for histopathology representation learning. Tiles from Prostate cANcer graDe Assessment (PANDA), CAncer MEtastases in LYmph nOdes challeNge 2017 (CAMELYON17), and BReAst Carcinoma Subtyping (BRACS) are used for ProsMAE pretraining to expose the encoder to diverse tissue morphology and acquisition conditions. The learned encoder is transferred for International Society of Urological Pathology (ISUP) grade classification through ProsCLS, using a frozen encoder and a linear classification head. ProsMAE achieved a higher mean validation quadratic weighted kappa (QWK) than the vanilla MAE frozen linear-probe baseline under the evaluated disjoint PANDA split. Repeated-split evaluation remains necessary to further establish robustness across split compositions.

### [21] [Continual Test-Time Adaptation in Computer Vision: Methods, Benchmarks, and Future Directions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08164)
*Sarthak Kumar Maharana,Shambhavi Mishra,Yunbei Zhang,Shuaicheng Niu,Taki Hasan Rafi,Jihun Hamm,Marco Pedersoli,Jose Dolz,Yunhui Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文全面综述了持续测试时自适应（CTTA）问题，定义其挑战，分析不同评估协议下的持续领域偏移模式，并提出一个分层分类法，将现有方法分为三类：基于优化的策略（如熵最小化、伪标签、参数恢复）、参数高效方法（如归一化层调整、自适应参数选择）以及基于架构的方法（如师生框架、适配器、视觉提示、掩码建模）。文章系统回顾了各类代表性方法，并在标准设置下进行对比基准测试与实验结果分析。最后，讨论了当前方法的局限性，指出了未来研究方向，包括基础模型和黑盒系统的自适应，为鲁棒的持续测试时自适应研究提供路线图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界部署中数据分布持续变化，导致预训练模型性能下降。现有方法难以同时应对灾难性遗忘和噪声伪标签累积问题，因此亟需一种无需源数据或标注目标、可在测试时持续适应非平稳分布的新范式。

Method: 提出正式定义的CTTA问题，构建层次化分类体系，对现有方法按优化策略、参数效率和架构设计三大类进行归纳；通过系统梳理与实验对比，评估不同方法在多种持续分布偏移场景下的表现。

Result: 总结出三类主流方法的有效性与适用场景，揭示当前方法在长期适应中的瓶颈，指出基础模型与黑盒系统适应等新兴方向具有重要潜力。

Conclusion: CTTA是实现模型在动态环境中长期可靠运行的关键技术。未来研究应聚焦于提升泛化能力、降低对标注依赖、增强对复杂分布变化的鲁棒性，尤其需关注大规模基础模型与实际应用系统的集成。

Abstract: Deep neural nets achieve remarkable performance when training and test data share the same distribution, but this assumption frequently breaks in real-world deployment, where data undergoes continual distributional shifts. Continual Test-Time Adaptation (CTTA) addresses this challenge by adapting pretrained models to non-stationary target distributions on-the-fly, without access to source data or labeled targets, while mitigating two critical failure modes: catastrophic forgetting of source knowledge and error accumulation from noisy pseudo-labels over extended time horizons. In this comprehensive survey, we formally define the CTTA problem, analyze the diverse continual domain shift patterns that characterize different evaluation protocols, and propose a hierarchical taxonomy that categorizes existing methods into three families: optimization-based strategies (entropy minimization, pseudo-labeling, parameter restoration), parameter-efficient methods (normalization layer adaptation, adaptive parameter selection), and architecture-based approaches (teacher-student frameworks, adapters, visual prompting, masked modeling). We systematically review representative methods within each category and present comparative benchmarks and experimental results across standard evaluation settings. Finally, we discuss limitations of current approaches and highlight emerging research directions, including adaptation of foundation models and black-box systems, providing a roadmap for future research in robust continual test-time adaptation. We encourage visiting our repository at [https://github.com/sarthaxxxxx/Awesome-Continual-Test-Time-Adaptation](https://github.com/sarthaxxxxx/Awesome-Continual-Test-Time-Adaptation)

</details>

They are associated with various neurological conditions, including vascular and inflammatory demyelinating diseases. Despite differing in etiology, WMHs from these conditions often appear similar on Fluid Attenuated Inversion Recovery (FLAIR) images. This similarity makes differential diagnosis challenging. In this work, we highlight the potential of combining attention-based segmentation with feature-driven classification. This approach supports more accurate and efficient classification between vascular and demyelinating white matter pathologies. For segmentation, we evaluate the effectiveness of attention mechanisms, specifically the Bottleneck Attention Module (BAM) and the Convolutional Block Attention Module (CBAM). Our experiments utilize five publicly available datasets with diverse imaging protocols to promote model generalizability, despite limited sample sizes. The results suggest that attention-based segmentation and feature-driven classification offer a promising direction for discriminating vascular and demyelinating white matter lesions. ### [23] [LEEVLA: Seeing What Matters in Latent Environment Evolution for Vision-Language-Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08182)
*Qi Lyu,Baicheng Liu,Xudong Wang,Jiahua Dong,Lianqing Liu,Zhi Han*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LEEVLA提出一种新的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）架构，通过显式引导模型关注任务关键区域并保持潜在世界表示的结构化演化，以应对复杂动态场景。核心创新包括：（1）漂移引导的动态优先级（DGDP），结合动态位置优先和语义漂移引导，实现对重要视觉区域的注意力控制；（2）结构化特征流生成（SFFG），通过原型到边缘（P2P）预测建模特征在潜在空间中的演化，并利用互邻对比损失保持邻域拓扑一致性。两者共同构成任务感知的“哪里-如何”训练框架，在多个基准测试中显著优于现有方法，验证了任务证据引导与结构化潜空间推理的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型在处理复杂动态场景时表现不佳，主要因为对所有视觉标记一视同仁，且依赖人工选择的因素进行推理，缺乏对任务关键证据的强调机制，也忽视了潜在环境的内在演化规律。因此需要一种能自动识别并聚焦于任务相关区域、同时保持潜空间结构一致性的新方法。

Method: 提出LEEVLA架构，包含两个核心组件：1) 漂移引导的动态优先级（DGDP），融合动态位置优先（DPP）与语义漂移引导（SDG），用于在训练过程中指导模型关注最相关的视觉区域；2) 结构化特征流生成（SFFG），通过原型到边缘（P2P）预测建模优先特征在潜在空间中的演化路径，并采用互邻对比（MC）损失维持局部邻域结构的一致性。整体形成任务感知的‘哪里-如何’联合训练框架。

Result: 在多个标准VLA基准数据集上的实验结果表明，LEEVLA在各项任务上均显著优于现有方法，尤其在复杂动态场景下性能提升明显。证明了显式任务证据引导与结构化潜空间推理对于构建可扩展、鲁棒的VLA系统至关重要。

Conclusion: LEEVLA通过引入任务导向的注意力机制与结构化的潜空间演化建模，有效提升了VLA模型在复杂动态环境中的泛化能力与决策准确性。该工作揭示了在多模态机器人控制中，不仅要关注‘看到什么’，更要理解‘如何演变’，为未来智能体的感知-推理-行动一体化设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models aim to map multimodal inputs to robot actions. However, most existing approaches struggle to cover complex dynamic scenarios due to treating all visual tokens uniformly and reasoning with human-selected factors, which lack mechanisms to emphasize task-critical evidence and ignore underlying factors. To address this issue, we propose LEEVLA, a VLA architecture for seeing what matters in Latent Environment Evolution that explicitly guides the model toward informative regions while preserving the structured evolution of latent world representations. To identify salient and instruction-relevant regions, we introduce drift-guided dynamic prioritization (DGDP), which combines dynamic position prioritization (DPP) with semantic drift guidance (SDG) to guide the VLA agent where to attend during training. On top of this, we introduce structured feature flow generation (SFFG), which models how these prioritized features should evolve in latent space via prototype-to-periphery (P2P) prediction, and a mutual-neighborhood contrastive (MC) loss to maintain topological consistency among neighborhoods. Together, DGDP and SFFG form a task-aware "where-how" training framework. Extensive experiments on VLA benchmarks show that LEEVLA consistently outperforms prior methods, confirming that explicit task-evidence guidance and structured latent reasoning are both crucial for scalable VLA. Our code is available at https://github.com/LyuQi127/LEEVLA.

</details>

Abstract: Enhancing images to make them visually appealing is a persistent challenge in computer vision. Many deep-learning methods train models on paired datasets to replicate expert editing styles. However, these approaches struggle with two key issues: (1) interpretability and (2) a parametrization suitable for user adjustments. To address these challenges, we present NamedCurves+, an approach inspired by the concept of Color Naming, a universal set of familiar colors widely used in software tools for intuitive editing. Our method integrates color names into a learning-based framework, enabling global adjustments for each named color through tone curves. To address local image variations, we incorporate a transformer block that captures spatial dependencies, enabling context-aware edits across the image. NamedCurves+ enhances the retouching process's interpretability and supports user interaction, allowing flexible modifications of individual tone curves to refine the retouched image according to personal preferences. Extensive experiments on tasks such as image retouching, tone mapping, and exposure correction demonstrate that NamedCurves+ outperforms state-of-the-art methods. Notably, our approach is both explainable, as the tone curves explicitly represent how each color name contributes to the enhancement, and interactive, allowing users to customize the retouching process and achieve results tailored to their liking.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RGBT视频目标检测方法在复杂环境下受限于模态间空间错位，且缺乏大规模、多样化的基准数据集，影响模型评估与进步。

Method: 设计基于块的局部空间对齐模块（PSAM）实现跨模态特征在局部区域的逐级对齐；引入双超图融合模块（DHFM），分别构建时序与跨模态超图，通过双相关性学习增强目标判别能力。

Abstract: RGB-Thermal (RGBT) Video Object Detection (VOD) has gained significant traction due to its ability to overcome the limitations of conventional RGB-based VOD under challenging conditions. However, spatial misalignment commonly exists between RGBT image pairs. To address this, we propose a Dual-Correlation Hypergraph Network (DHNet) that captures high-dimensional complementary information by explicitly modeling two types of correlations: temporal correlation across consecutive frames and spatial correlation from cross-modal features. Specifically, we first design a Patch-based Spatial Alignment Module (PSAM) to sequentially align the multimodal features at the local region level. The dataset covers diverse scenarios, including campuses, parks, transportation, rural areas, night scenes, rain, and snow. Comprehensive experiments on VT-VOD50 and our DVT-VOD1000 demonstrate that DHNet achieves state-of-the-art detection accuracy. The dataset and source code will be made publicly available on https://github.com/tzz-ahu/ to support academic research.

### [26] [Dive Into the Implicit Biases of Low-rank Vision-language Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08194)
*Mingjia Shi,Shuo Wang,Xiaobo Wang,Sifan Zhou,Kai Wang,Tianyu Fu,Chenxu Zhao,Anyang Su,Ping Jiang,Minghui Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文挑战了视觉-语言对齐阶段需全参数微调的传统观点，提出使用低秩适配（LoRA）替代全参数更新。实验表明，低秩对齐不仅降低计算成本，还在多数基准上表现更优。作者系统分析了低秩适配引入的隐式偏差，发现其使模型行为从幻觉转向保守，并保持视觉特征的逐标记线性可分性（称为LS诅咒），而全参数对齐会破坏这一特性。几何上，低秩对齐模型具有更均匀、结构稳定的视觉表征，保留模态特异性知识而非过早融合实体语义。理论上，作者证明两个定理，说明低秩对齐倾向于平坦梯度的参数子空间和对抗扰动的特征子空间，从而为结构保持提供了理论解释。实验涵盖超过100种配置、三种低秩算子及多种设置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉-语言对齐依赖全参数微调，计算开销大且可能引入不稳定性。本文旨在探索低秩适配在该阶段的可行性与优势，以提升效率并改善模型行为。

Method: 采用低秩适配（LoRA）对大型语言模型进行视觉-语言对齐，系统评估其在不同配置下的性能；通过实证分析、几何观察和理论推导揭示其隐式偏差机制。

Result: 低秩对齐在多数基准上优于全参数对齐，减少计算成本，提升模型稳健性与表征质量，尤其在保持视觉特征线性可分性和模态分离性方面表现突出。

Conclusion: 低秩适配是一种高效且优越的视觉-语言对齐方法，其优势源于对参数与特征空间的结构性偏好，为未来多模态预训练提供新范式。

Abstract: Vision-language alignment, the stage that bridges pretrained vision encoders and large language models, is widely treated as a form of pretraining requiring full-parameter updates. We challenge this view and investigate what happens when low-rank adaptation is applied to the LLM during this stage instead. We find that low-rank alignment not only reduces computational costs but also outperforms full-parameter alignment on most benchmarks. To understand this phenomenon, we systematically characterize the implicit biases introduced by low-rank adaptation during alignment. Empirically, we find that low-rank alignment shifts model behavior from hallucinatory to conservative and preserves per-token linear separability of visual features that full-parameter alignment disrupts, a phenomenon we term LS-curse. Geometrically, low rank aligned models exhibit more homogeneous and structurally stable visual representations, maintaining modality-specific knowledge rather than prematurely fusing entity-level semantics. Theoretically, we establish two theorems showing that low-rank alignment induces preferences for parameter subspaces with flat gradients and feature subspaces robust to perturbations, providing a principled explanation for the observed structure-preserving behavior. Extensive experiments cover ablation over 100 alignment configurations, three families of low-rank operators, and various rank, encoder, and other settings.

TL;DR: 该论文研究从边缘观测中学习联合分布的问题，提出了一种基于潜在变量的概率框架LUD-MSR，通过辅助表示建模联合分布，并仅使用边缘数据优化证据下界。在温和假设下，建立了分布近似误差的上界，揭示了表示学习中领域一致性与信息保留之间的权衡。为此，引入多尺度图像表示（MSR）映射，利用粗尺度结构相似性同时抑制域特定变化，实现了更优的权衡。实验在真实世界去噪基准（如冷冻电镜）上验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从边缘观测中学习联合分布是一个固有病态问题，因为可行耦合存在歧义。现有方法难以有效平衡领域一致性和信息保留，亟需新的框架来解决这一挑战。

Method: 提出LUD-MSR框架，采用潜在变量建模联合分布，通过辅助表示优化证据下界；设计多尺度图像表示（MSR）映射以利用粗尺度结构相似性并抑制域特异性变化。

Result: 理论分析表明，在温和假设下，分布近似误差具有上界；实验结果显示，所提方法在冷冻电镜等真实世界去噪任务中表现优异，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: LUD-MSR框架通过多尺度表示有效平衡了领域一致性与信息保留的权衡，显著提升了从边缘数据学习联合分布的性能，尤其在复杂实际应用中展现出强大潜力。

Abstract: This paper studies the problem of learning a joint distribution from marginal observations, which is inherently ill-posed due to the ambiguity of feasible couplings. We propose LUD-MSR, a latent-variable probabilistic framework that models the joint distribution via auxiliary representations and optimizes evidence lower bounds using only marginal data. Under mild assumptions, we establish an upper bound on the distribution approximation error. This analysis reveals a trade-off in representation learning between domain consistency and information preservation. To address this trade-off, we introduce a Multi-Scale image Representation (MSR) mapping that exploits structural similarity at coarse scales while suppressing domain-specific variations. We show that MSR achieves a more favorable balance of this trade-off compared to existing approaches. Experiments on real-world denoising benchmarks, including cryo-electron microscopy (cryo-EM), demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework.

### [28] [TMI: Text-to-Image Meets Image-to-Image for Complementary Data Synthesis to Boost Long-Tailed Instance Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08201)
*Hyeonseop Song,Seokhun Choi,Hoseok Do*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合管道，结合文本到图像（T2I）生成与上下文感知的图像到图像（I2I）编辑，以解决大规模词汇实例分割中的长尾分布和细粒度类别混淆问题。T2I分支提供多样化的类别与场景，通过教师-学生机制确保标签可靠性；引入VRAIN（基于指令的稀有类别增强）I2I编辑器，在真实场景中精准插入高置信度实例，提升稀有类别的监督信号并减少域差距。在LVIS基准上，方法显著提升整体AP（+4.0）和稀有类AP（+9.5），且可随主干网络容量扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模词汇实例分割面临长尾类别分布和细粒度类别间模糊性挑战。现有数据合成方法存在局限：文本到图像（T2I）生成易引入噪声伪标签，对稀有类别表现差；复制粘贴方法则破坏场景真实感。亟需一种既能保证多样性又能保持语义一致性和视觉自然性的合成策略。

Method: 提出T2I与I2I联合的混合框架。首先利用T2I生成多样化图像及类别，通过教师-学生结构筛选仅符合提示的类别以保障标签质量；随后引入VRAIN（Verified Rare-class Augmentation via INstructed editing）——一种上下文感知的I2I编辑器，根据语义位置精准插入高置信度实例，增强稀有类别的训练样本，同时保持场景真实感。

Result: 在LVIS基准测试中，该方法实现整体平均精度（AP）提升最多达+4.0点，稀有类别AP提升最多达+9.5点，优于现有基线模型，并展现出良好的可扩展性，能有效适配不同规模的主干网络。

Conclusion: 所提出的混合生成与编辑框架有效缓解了长尾分布与细粒度歧义问题，通过T2I提供多样性、I2I强化真实性与针对性，尤其显著提升了稀有类别的性能，为大规模词汇实例分割提供了高效可靠的数据增强新范式。

Abstract: Large-vocabulary instance segmentation is constrained by long-tailed category distributions and fine-grained inter-class ambiguity. While data synthesis offers a promising alternative, current paradigms have complementary limitations: text-to-image (T2I) methods inherit noisy pseudo-labels and struggle on rare classes, whereas copy-paste methods compromise contextual realism. To address these issues, we propose a hybrid pipeline coupling T2I generation with context-aware image-to-image (I2I) editing. The T2I branch provides broad category and scene diversity, while a teacher-student scheme ensures label reliability by selectively retaining only prompt-specified categories. To strengthen supervision for rare classes, we introduce VRAIN (Verified Rare-class Augmentation via INstructed editing), a novel I2I editor. VRAIN inserts high-confidence instances at semantically appropriate locations within in-the-wild scenes, yielding semantically coherent and visually natural edits that reduce domain gaps and enable targeted augmentation. On the LVIS benchmark, our method surpasses existing baselines, improving overall AP by up to +4.0 points and rare-class AP by up to +9.5 points, while scaling effectively with backbone capacity. Our project page is available at https://seokhunchoi.github.io/TMI

### [29] [Metrics or Mirage? An Audit of Evaluation Inconsistencies in Colonoscopy Polyp Segmentation Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08203)
*Aisha Urooj,Zain Ul Abdien,Neelu Madan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文分析了2015至2026年间27篇结肠镜息肉分割研究，指出当前评估体系存在三大问题：多数论文遗漏具有临床意义的豪斯多夫距离指标；不同研究使用不兼容的数据划分协议导致结果不可比；绝大多数论文未进行统计显著性检验。即使在《Metrics Reloaded》框架发布后，仍有四篇论文延续这些问题。作者通过统一评估协议重新测试五个代表性模型，发现原始报告结果掩盖了边界和召回率的重大缺陷，且最佳模型随指标变化而改变，排名在不同随机划分下反转。为此提出一个轻量级、领域适配的结肠息肉分割报告检查清单（PSRC）以改进评估标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前结肠镜息肉分割研究的进展依赖于公开基准上的排行榜比较，但这种评估方式存在严重缺陷，导致研究结果难以验证和可比。作者旨在揭示并纠正评估过程中的系统性问题，提升研究透明度与科学性。

Method: 对27篇相关论文进行系统审计，识别评估中的结构性问题；通过在统一协议和单一评分器下重评五个代表性模型，验证问题的实质性影响；提出针对结肠息肉分割任务的报告检查清单（PSRC）。

Result: 发现25/27篇论文遗漏豪斯多夫距离，至少五种训练/测试划分协议共存导致结果不可比，26/27篇未做统计显著性检验；重评估显示原始报告结果隐藏重大边界与召回失败，最佳模型及排名随指标和数据划分变化而波动。

Conclusion: 当前结肠镜息肉分割领域的评估体系存在严重缺陷，亟需标准化。提出的PSRC检查清单可作为轻量级解决方案，推动更透明、可比和可靠的模型评估实践。

Abstract: Progress in colonoscopy polyp segmentation is routinely reported through leaderboard comparisons on a small set of public benchmarks. We argue that this apparent progress is difficult to verify: a systematic audit of \textbf{27 papers} published between 2015 and 2026 reveals three structural problems in how the community evaluates models. \textbf{First}, 25 of 27 papers \textit{omit the Hausdorff distance}. Hausdorff distance is a boundary-accuracy metric with direct clinical relevance for detecting flat or small polyps, and is a standard in radiotherapy segmentation. \textbf{Second}, at least five \textit{incompatible train/test split protocols} co-exist across papers reporting results on the same two datasets (Kvasir-SEG and CVC-ClinicDB), making published Dice scores non-comparable even when they appear in the same leaderboard column. \textbf{Third}, 26 of 27 papers make \textit{performance claims without any statistical significance test}. Strikingly, four papers published \emph{after} the Metrics Reloaded framework~\cite{metricsreloaded2024} (Maier-Hein et al., \textit{Nature Methods} 2024) perpetuate these same problems, suggesting that general-purpose metric guidance has not yet reached the colonoscopy sub-community. To show these problems are not merely cosmetic, we re-evaluate five representative models under three controlled protocols with a single uniform scorer, and find that the reported metric conceals large boundary and recall failures, that the ``best'' model changes with the metric, and that near-tied rankings reverse across random splits. We propose a five-point \textbf{Polyp Segmentation Reporting Checklist}~(PSRC) as a lightweight, domain-adapted corrective.

Federated learning (FL) is a feasible approach to overcome these challenges. Due to the continuous emergence of FL algorithms and the highly heterogeneous nature of medical data, objectively evaluating their performance in real-world clinical settings remains difficult. Therefore, a comprehensive federated medical imaging benchmark, serving as a unified evaluation standard, is crucial for advancing the technology toward reliable clinical application. Existing federated medical imaging benchmarks have not yet adequately incorporated state-of-the-art algorithms, are limited to data from single organs or modalities, and overly emphasize model accuracy, making it difficult to comprehensively assess the overall efficacy of FL in real-world medical environments. To address these challenges, we developed the MobenFL benchmark. This benchmark integrates 20 cutting-edge FL algorithms and 22 medical imaging datasets, covering 12 critical organs across the human body, surpassing existing benchmark in breadth. In terms of evaluation dimensions, MobenFL not only assesses performance but also systematically incorporates key metrics such as algorithmic efficiency and privacy protection capabilities. Additionally, it conducts specialized evaluations for complex real-world clinical scenarios involving different diseases, devices, and imaging modalities, thereby providing a comprehensive and in-depth evaluation framework for the clinical application of FL in the medical field.

</details>


### [31] [LUMI: Tokenizer-Agnostic LLM-Based Lossless Image Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08221)
*Chris Xing Tian,Chengkai Wu,Ziyu Wang,Rongqun Lin,Kecheng Chen,Xiandong Meng,Haoliang Li,Shiqi Wang,Siwei Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LUMI提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的无损图像压缩框架，摆脱了传统方法对分词器的依赖。通过像素嵌入模块将原始像素值映射到LLM的连续嵌入空间，并引入局部位置编码以保留二维空间结构，同时使用256路预测头输出像素级概率分布。仅训练像素嵌入、位置编码、软前缀和预测头，保持LLM主干冻结。在自然、医学和遥感图像数据集上，LUMI展现出跨分词器家族的统一性、竞争力的压缩率及更强的跨域鲁棒性，表明无损图像压缩应视为对冻结基础模型的像素空间适配，而非依赖分词器的语言符号建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的无损图像压缩方法依赖分词器将像素转换为文本形式，导致压缩性能受制于特定分词器行为、词汇表设计和模型家族特性，缺乏通用性和一致性。因此需要一种不依赖分词器的统一框架，实现更灵活、鲁棒的图像压缩方法。

Method: 提出LUMI框架，采用像素嵌入模块替代像素转文本的分词过程，将原始像素强度与通道信息映射至LLM的连续嵌入空间；引入跨块内位置编码以恢复扁平化后的二维空间结构；使用256路预测头直接预测像素值的概率分布；仅训练嵌入模块、位置编码、软前缀和预测头，保持预训练LLM主干固定不变。

Result: 在多个自然、医学和遥感图像基准测试中，使用LLaMA、Qwen和Gemma等不同架构的LLM作为骨干网络，LUMI均表现出优异的压缩性能，达到或优于现有基于分词器的LLM压缩方法，在跨领域任务中具有更强的鲁棒性，并实现了对不同分词器家族的统一接口。

Conclusion: LUMI成功将基于大语言模型的无损图像压缩从依赖分词器的语言符号建模转变为对冻结基础模型的像素空间适配，具备良好的通用性、跨域适应能力与压缩效率，为未来研究提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based lossless image compression methods typically represent pixel data through the native text interface of a pretrained model, converting pixel values into token sequences that the LLM processes through its vocabulary head. This design shows that pretrained language models can provide probability estimates for image coding, but it also couples compression to tokenizer behavior, vocabulary-specific numeric tokens, and model-family-specific adaptation. In this paper, we present LUMI (LLM-based Unified Model-agnostic lossless Image compression), a tokenizer-agnostic framework for lossless RGB image compression with frozen LLM backbones. LUMI replaces pixel-as-text tokenization with a pixel embedding module that maps raw intensity and channel information into the continuous embedding space of the LLM. It further introduces intra-patch position encoding to retain two-dimensional spatial structure after flattening, and uses a 256-way prediction head to produce probabilities over the native pixel alphabet. Only the pixel embedding, position encoding, soft-prefix parameters, and prediction head are trained, while the LLM backbone remains fixed. Experiments on natural, medical, and remote-sensing image benchmarks with LLaMA, Qwen, and Gemma backbones show that LUMI provides a unified interface across tokenizer families, achieves competitive compression rates, and improves cross-domain robustness over tokenizer-based LLM compression baselines. These results formulate LLM-based lossless image compression as pixel-space adaptation of frozen foundation models rather than tokenizer-specific language-symbol modeling.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Photorealistic Style Transfer (PST) aims to transfer the color and tonal style of a reference to a content image while strictly preserving its structural integrity. To address these bottlenecks, we propose StatLUT, an innovative multimodal framework for 3D LUT generation. First, we bypass traditional encoders and introduce a Lab-Extractor to derive spatially-agnostic statistical features, fundamentally decoupling color distributions from structural semantics to ensure artifact-free rendering. Second, we formulate LUT generation as a Transformer-based Seq2Seq translation task, utilizing a Multi-dimensional Residual Mapper (MR-Mapper) to predict topologically smooth 3D LUTs. Finally, to break the single-modal barrier, we propose the H-Diffuser, a lightweight Diffusion Transformer that directly synthesizes statistical features from natural language prompts, enabling flexible text-driven color grading. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that StatLUT significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both visual quality and quantitative metrics, pioneering a highly robust and flexible paradigm for multimodal photorealistic style transfer.

### [33] [TVTA: Trajectory-Aware Viseme-Guided Temporal Aggregation for Event-Based Lip Reading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08236)

Conclusion: 本文提出的时序增强框架有效解决了事件驱动唇读中的关键问题，通过局部时间建模、视觉音素引导监督和鲁棒训练策略，显著提升了识别性能，并揭示了模型对发音结构的深层理解能力。

Abstract: Event-based lip reading has recently emerged as a promising direction for visual speech recognition, benefiting from the high temporal resolution and motion sensitivity of event cameras. However, existing methods typically perform spatial compression before sufficient temporal modeling, which may suppress sparse and localized motion trajectories that are crucial for distinguishing similar lip movements. Moreover, most current approaches optimize temporal representations mainly at the word-classification level, leaving the underlying articulatory structure weakly constrained. To address these limitations, we propose a temporally enhanced framework for event-based lip reading. First, we introduce Trajectory-Aware Differential Aggregation (TDA), which performs local temporal modeling at each spatial location before adaptive spatial aggregation. Second, we propose Viseme-Guided Aggregation (VGA), a unified temporal module composed of a CTC decoder and a viseme-guided gated aggregation branch, which injects viseme-aware sequence supervision and improves final temporal aggregation for word recognition. Third, we incorporate an EMA teacher--student training strategy to enhance robustness under strong event perturbations. Experiments on the DVS-Lip benchmark verify the effectiveness of the proposed design, and extensive ablation studies further validate the contributions of TDA, VGA, and teacher--student consistency. Qualitative decoding results also demonstrate that the proposed CTC-based temporal modeling learns meaningful viseme-aware structure from event streams.

### [34] [Closing the Null Space: Guidance-Aware Quantization for Classifier-Free Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08241)
*Abdullah Al Shafi,Sumaiya Rahim Suma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文针对部署无分类器引导（CFG）扩散模型时因计算预算限制而需量化的问题，指出现有后训练量化（PTQ）方法忽视了CFG模型中条件与非条件分支的配对结构，导致系统层面延迟开销被忽略，算法层面出现‘分支漂移陷阱’。为此提出指导感知混合精度（GAMP）方法，通过直接基于引导输出校准、分析每层激活位敏感性并采用贪心背包算法分配比特，从构造上防止非条件分支漂移，有效提升量化后生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PTQ方法将CFG模型视为单分支网络，忽略了其条件与非条件分支的配对结构，导致在量化后出现分支漂移问题，影响生成质量；同时传统指标无法反映实际推理延迟，造成理论效率与实际性能脱节。

Method: 提出Guidance-Aware Mixed Precision（GAMP）方法，直接以引导输出为校准目标，通过分析引导输出退化情况获取各层激活位敏感度，采用贪心背包算法进行比特分配，确保非条件分支不发生漂移。

Result: 实验证明标准校准方法存在虚假正例——最佳诊断结果对应最差生成质量；GAMP方法成功避免分支漂移，在保持高引导一致性的同时显著提升生成样本质量。

Conclusion: CFG模型量化必须考虑其双分支结构特性；GAMP通过引导感知的混合精度设计，从根本上解决了分支漂移陷阱，实现了高效且高质量的量化部署。

Abstract: Deploying classifier-free guidance (CFG) diffusion models under real-world compute budgets requires quantization, yet existing post-training quantization (PTQ) methods treat CFG models as single-branch networks, ignoring the paired conditional/unconditional structure that CFG inference fundamentally relies on. This structural blind spot has two consequences. At the system level, the two-pass CFG execution pattern imposes a latency overhead that parameter-count and bit-operation metrics conceal entirely, and commodity INT8 inference stacks fail to realize the theoretical efficiency gains that BOPs calculations promise. At the algorithmic level, calibrating against the guidance gap alone admits an exact null space: a quantized model can achieve perfect gap-fidelity diagnostics while the unconditional branch drifts arbitrarily, corrupting every guided prediction at inference time. This paper terms this the branch-drift trap, proves its existence analytically, and confirms it empirically through a false-positive result in which the best-calibrated model by standard diagnostics simultaneously produces the worst sample quality. To close the trap, Guidance-Aware Mixed Precision (GAMP) is proposed, which calibrates directly on the guided prediction, derives per-layer activation-bit sensitivity from guided-output degradation, and allocates bits via a greedy knapsack -- provably preventing unconditional branch drift by construction.

### [36] [HSA: Hierarchical Slot Attention for Multi-granularity Scene-Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08249)
*Neelu Madan,Rongzhen Zhao,Andreas Mogelmose,Juho Kannala,Joni Pajarinen,Graham W. Taylor,Thomas B. Moeslund*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出层级槽注意力（HSA），通过单一模型实现多粒度语义场景分解，涵盖整体（前景/背景）、语义（物体类别）和全景（个体实例）三个层次。利用仅10%标注数据与层级对齐损失，联合学习三层次结构，并引入分组纯度与包含性指标评估表示空间中的层次编码效果。在COCO和PASCAL VOC上显著优于现有平面基线，最大提升达+41.5 ARI（整体）、+14.6（语义）、+10.4（全景），且仅需一个模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类理解场景依赖于语义层次结构（如前景/背景、物体类别、个体实例），但现有槽注意力方法仅在单一粒度上基于外观进行扁平化分解，缺乏语义层次，且无法在无监督条件下自动形成此类结构。因此需要一种能从少量标注数据中联合学习多粒度语义层次的模型。

Method: 提出层级槽注意力（HSA），采用统一模型在三个层次上同时分解视觉场景：整体、语义、全景；使用10%标注数据结合层级对齐损失进行训练；引入分组纯度和包含性作为评估指标，以验证层次结构是否被有效编码于表示空间中。

Abstract: Slot attention is a powerful framework for object-centric learning, decomposing visual scenes into latent slots through iterative competitive attention. However, existing methods share two critical limitations: they decompose scenes into a flat set of slots at a single granularity, and this decomposition is based on appearance rather than semantics. Yet humans understand scenes through semantic hierarchies: separating foreground from background, recognizing object categories, and identifying individual instances. Crucially, such semantic hierarchies cannot emerge without supervision, because category names are human constructs, not visual patterns. We propose Hierarchical Slot Attention (HSA), which learns multi-granularity semantic scene decomposition from a single model. HSA decomposes scenes at three levels: holistic (foreground/background), semantic (object categories), and panoptic (individual instances). Using only 10\% labeled data, combined with hierarchical alignment loss, HSA learns all three levels jointly. We further introduce grouping purity and containment to measure whether the hierarchy is encoded in representation space, not just output masks. Experiments on COCO and PASCAL VOC demonstrate that HSA outperforms the strongest flat baseline by up to \textbf{$+$41.5} ARI at holistic, \textbf{$+$14.6} at semantic, and \textbf{$+$10.4} at panoptic level on COCO, with even larger gains on Pascal VOC, while requiring a single model instead of three. Code will be made available upon acceptance.

### [37] [On the Design of Mixture-of-Experts for Dynamic Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08250)
*In-Hwan Jin,Hyeongju Mun,Joonsoo Kim,Kugjin Yun,Kyeongbo Kong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究动态3D高斯表示中的多变形建模问题，提出两种基于专家混合（MoE）框架的解决方案：MoDE和MoE-GS。前者通过联合优化将多个变形专家直接集成到可变形高斯点云渲染流程中，共享一个规范化的高斯表示；后者则独立优化各专家，并通过额外路由阶段进行组合，专家交互发生在非规范表示上。两种方法在整合约束下提供了不同的设计思路，提升了对复杂动态场景的适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D高斯点云方法通常采用单一变形模型，难以应对真实世界中多样且空间变化的运动特性，限制了其在复杂动态场景下的鲁棒性。因此需要更灵活的多变形建模机制以增强泛化能力。

Method: 从混合专家（MoE）视角出发，提出两种多变形建模方法：1）MoDE——联合优化多个变形专家，共享统一的规范高斯表示；2）MoE-GS——独立训练变形专家，并通过单独的路由模块组合，专家交互发生在非规范表示上。

Result: 实验表明，所提方法在多种动态场景下均优于单变形模型基线，展现出更强的泛化能力和重建精度。特别是MoE-GS在复杂运动模式下表现优异，验证了不同整合策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入双路径多变形建模框架，揭示了整合约束对变形专家设计与行为的影响，为动态3D场景重建提供了更灵活、鲁棒的解决方案。代码已开源。

Abstract: Dynamic scene reconstruction remains challenging due to the heterogeneous and spatially varying nature of real-world motion. Although recent 3D Gaussian Splatting methods have introduced diverse deformation formulations for dynamic novel view synthesis, each method typically relies on a single deformation model within its representation, which limits robustness across diverse dynamic scenarios. In this work, we study a fundamental problem-multi-deformation modeling for dynamic 3D Gaussian representations-under two distinct integration constraints that differ in when and how multiple deformation experts interact during training. From a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) perspective, we view multi-deformation modeling as the problem of combining multiple specialized deformation models within a unified 3D representation. We first introduce Mixture of Deformation Experts (MoDE), which integrates multiple deformation experts directly into the deformable Gaussian Splatting pipeline through joint optimization. In MoDE, experts operate on a shared canonical Gaussian representation, enabling multi-deformation modeling without introducing additional training stages or modifying the original optimization schedule. In contrast, we further present Mixture of Experts for Dynamic Gaussian Splatting (MoE-GS) under a different integration constraint, where deformation experts are optimized independently and combined through a separate routing stage. As a result, expert interaction occurs over non-canonical Gaussian representations after individual optimization. Together, these two approaches provide alternative strategies for multi-deformation modeling, clarifying how integration constraints shape the design and behavior of deformation experts in dynamic 3D Gaussian representations. Our code is available at: https://github.com/cvsp-lab/MoE-GS-studio.

### [38] [UniRef-UAV: A Multimodal Benchmark for Universal Referring in UAV Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08267)
*Haibin Tian,Huichao Xie,Xuelin Qian,Ruitao Lu,Junwei Han,Dingwen Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通用的无人机视觉定位任务Universal Referring，旨在解决现有基于文本的单目标定位方法在复杂空域场景中应用受限的问题。为此，研究构建了支持多模态查询（纯文本、纯图像、文本+图像）和可变输出数量的UniRef-UAV基准数据集，并设计了UAV-URNet检测式基线模型，通过统一查询空间实现多模态输入到可变目标集的映射。实验表明该模型在无目标识别、跨域泛化方面表现稳定且轻量高效，优于大型通用多模态大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉定位方法主要依赖文本查询且仅支持单目标输出，难以适应无人机在复杂空域中面对多模态指令、可能不存在目标或存在多个有效目标的实际需求。

Method: 提出UniRef-UAV多模态基准数据集，支持文本、图像及混合查询；设计UAV-URNet模型，采用集合预测机制将异构查询映射至共享空间并输出可变大小的目标集。

Result: UAV-URNet在多种查询模式下表现出稳定的无目标判别能力与良好的跨域泛化性能，模型更轻量、可复现性更强，且多模态查询有助于降低视觉查询歧义，提升查询与目标对齐的一致性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过构建通用无人机视觉定位任务与相应基准，验证了多模态查询与可变输出机制的有效性，为未来无人机智能感知研究提供了可复现的基准与轻量化解决方案。

Abstract: Unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) increasingly rely on visual grounding capabilities to localize task-relevant targets from diverse instructions in complex aerial scenes. Existing referring expression comprehension (REC) benchmarks and methods, however, are largely built around text-only queries and single-object outputs, which limits their applicability to practical UAV scenarios involving reference images, multimodal instructions, absent targets, and multiple valid target instances. To address this gap, we introduce \emph{Universal Referring}, a generalized UAV referring task that jointly expands the query modality and the output cardinality. We construct \emph{UniRef-UAV}, a multimodal benchmark that supports text-only, image-only, and text+image queries with modality-dependent target cardinality, where text-only and text+image queries admit no-target, single-target, and multi-target grounding while image-only queries focus on existence-aware single-instance grounding. It also provides in-domain and cross-domain evaluation protocols for visual-query generalization. We further present \emph{UAV-URNet}, a detection-style baseline that maps heterogeneous queries into a shared query space and predicts variable-size target sets through set prediction. Extensive experiments show that UAV-URNet provides a stable and reproducible baseline with more consistent no-target discrimination and a more lightweight, reproducible implementation than large general-purpose MLLMs. Additional domain analysis, query-representation analysis, and ablation studies demonstrate that multimodal queries help reduce visual-query ambiguity and promote a more unified query--target alignment space. The annotations, visual query crops/images, train/validation/test splits, evaluation scripts, and baseline code will be made publicly available to facilitate reproducible research.

</details>


### [39] [Progression as Latent Drift: Generative Forecasting of Slow-Evolving Pathologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08270)
*Yuxiang Feng,Juncheng Wang,Chao Xu,Wenlong Hou,Huihan Wang,Yijie Qian,Yang Liu,Baigui Sun,Yong Liu,Shujun Wan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出Latent Drift框架，通过在压缩语义空间中学习神经退行性疾病的进展动态，解决纵向MRI中微弱信号难以捕捉的问题。通过消除像素级身份依赖并引入有限标量量化抑制噪声，显著提升患者特异性预测性能，在生成保真度和临床相关指标上优于扩散模型与自回归Transformer基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型在低信号环境下因稳定基线解剖结构主导训练过程，且受样本特异性噪声干扰，难以有效捕捉缓慢演化的神经退行性疾病的真实进展信号，导致预测不可靠。

Method: 提出Latent Drift框架，将生成目标从全分辨率解剖结构转移至压缩的语义表示空间；结合有限标量量化技术，抑制高频小幅度噪声波动，保留一致的结构漂移特征。

Result: 在纵向3D脑部MRI数据上的实验表明，该方法在生成保真度和临床相关评估指标上均显著优于扩散模型与自回归Transformer基线，实现更准确的个体化神经疾病未来演化预测。

Conclusion: Latent Drift通过在语义空间中建模进展动态并抑制噪声，有效克服了身份坍缩与连续插值陷阱问题，为慢速演化的神经退行性疾病提供了更可靠的预测工具，具有重要临床应用潜力。

Abstract: Forecasting the future anatomy of slow-evolving neurodegenerative diseases could enable earlier, more targeted intervention and improve clinical trial design, but it remains challenging because true progression signals are subtle in longitudinal MRI. In this low-signal regime, transferring modern generative sequence models directly is unreliable: training is dominated by stable baseline anatomy and confounded by dense, sample-specific nuisance variation. We first provide a theoretical analysis that explains these failures through two modes. Identity collapse occurs when optimization is driven toward reproducing the current anatomy, which prevents the model from learning faint temporal change. The continuous interpolation trap arises when standard smooth networks cannot separate localized biological drift from pervasive noise, which leads to spurious changes that diffuse across the volume. To address both issues, we propose Latent Drift, a progressive generative framework that learns change in a compressed semantic representation rather than synthesizing full-resolution anatomy. This design removes pixel-level identity from the prediction target and concentrates model capacity on progression-relevant dynamics. We further apply Finite Scalar Quantization to the learned change representation, which suppresses small, high-frequency nuisance fluctuations while preserving consistent structural drift. Experiments on longitudinal 3D brain MRI show that Latent Drift improves patient-specific neuro-forecasting over diffusion and autoregressive transformer baselines across generative fidelity and clinically relevant evaluation metrics. Project page: \href{https://cutepkq.github.io/latent-drift}{https://cutepkq.github.io/latent-drift}.

</details>


### [40] [Enhancing the KidSat Model: Integrating Geographical Encoding and Data Quality Assessment for Childhood Poverty Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08281)
*Hou Hin Ip,Ka Nam Lam,Joshua Man Yu Ng,Makkunda Sharma,Seth Flaxman,Codie Gerlach-Wood,H Juliette T Unwin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的卫星图像贫困映射方法，通过优化数据预处理、图像质量评估和地理编码融合，显著提升了预测精度。通过重新聚合调查数据、引入两阶段质量筛选流程，并将DINOv2视觉嵌入与球谐函数（SH）位置特征融合，使平均绝对误差（MAE）从0.2167降至0.1759（相对降低18.83%）。在扩展至33个非洲国家时，最佳模型实现0.1658的总体MAE。研究表明，SH特征能持续提升性能，而更高容量的坐标增强（如SH+SIREN）需谨慎设计目标函数以避免性能下降。梯度提升树模型（如XGBoost/LightGBM）最有效利用了视觉-地理融合表示中的非线性关系。该方法仅依赖公开数据，具备可扩展性和理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有卫星图像贫困映射面临三大挑战：调查数据噪声大且稀疏、图像质量差（如云层遮挡）、以及纯图像模型缺乏显式空间结构。为克服这些问题，亟需一种更鲁棒、高精度的建模框架。

Method: 1. 通过重新聚合人口与健康调查（DHS）数据，将高基数类别降维（103→51），缓解数据稀疏性；2. 设计两阶段图像质量筛选流程，剔除受云层或损坏严重影响的样本；3. 融合DINOv2视觉嵌入与球谐函数（SH）地理编码特征，显式建模空间位置信息；4. 使用梯度提升树（XGBoost/LightGBM）建模非线性交互关系，对比不同坐标增强策略（如SH+SIREN）的效果。

Result: 在集群层面严重剥夺比例预测中，模型MAE由0.2167降至0.1759，相对减少18.83%；扩展至33个非洲国家后，整体MAE达0.1658。SH特征始终提升性能，而未经优化的SH+SIREN可能表现更差。梯度提升树在融合表示上表现最优。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一套可扩展、基于公开数据的精准卫星图像贫困映射方案，通过数据优化、质量控制与地理编码融合，显著提升预测性能，为发展中国家的社会经济监测提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Accurate poverty mapping using satellite imagery is often hindered by (i) noisy and sparse survey-derived supervision, (ii) image quality issues such as cloud cover and image corruption, and (iii) lack of explicit spatial structure in image-only models. Building on the KidSat framework, we develop an enhanced pipeline that improves predictive accuracy via refined data preprocessing, systematic image quality assessment, and mathematically defined geographic encoding. First, we refine the fine-tuning target matrix by resolving high-cardinality sparsity and reducing one-hot dimensionality from 103 to 51 via DHS re-aggregation. Second, we introduce a simple two-stage quality-screening procedure to filter heavily clouded or corrupted observations. Third, we fuse DINOv2 visual embeddings with Spherical Harmonics (SH) location features. Across extensive experiments, these changes reduce MAE from 0.2167 to 0.1759, corresponding to an 18.83% relative reduction on the cluster-level severe-deprivation proportion scale. When extended from 16 to 33 African countries, the best-performing configuration achieves an overall MAE of 0.1658. We find that SH features consistently improve performance over the image-only backbone, whereas higher-capacity coordinate Multi Layer Perception augmentation (SH+SIREN) can underperform without carefully designed objectives. Finally, gradient-boosted tree heads (XGBoost/LightGBM) most effectively exploit nonlinear interactions in the fused visual-geographic representation. These findings provide a scalable and principled recipe for improving satellite-based socioeconomic predictions using only publicly accessible data.

### [41] [ARGUS: Accelerated, Robust, General, and Unsupervised Cell Tracking Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08297)
*Noah Jaitner,Kandice Tanner,Ingolf Sack,Hossein S. Aghamiry*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ARGUS 是一种用于细胞追踪的加速、鲁棒、通用且无监督的框架，结合了自适应细胞检测、密集Farneback光流预测、帧间线性分配和序列级轨迹片段修复，可在无需训练数据或GPU的情况下实现高精度追踪（检测准确率0.905-0.971，追踪准确率0.897-0.964），运行时间仅需数秒至一分钟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化细胞追踪在时间序列显微成像中面临噪声、形态变化、细胞重叠及分裂/融合等动态事件的挑战，现有方法受限于对训练数据依赖或硬件要求，亟需一种高效、通用且无需标注数据的解决方案。

Method: ARGUS采用自适应细胞检测、密集Farneback光流预测、帧间线性分配与序列级轨迹修复相结合的方法，通过多阶段处理实现鲁棒追踪，具备模块化设计和可解释性。

Result: 在公开的Cell Tracking Challenge数据集上，ARGUS表现出优异的检测与追踪性能，准确率分别达到0.905–0.971和0.897–0.964，且单次处理耗时仅5–6秒（3帧），整体运行时间低于1分钟。

Conclusion: ARGUS是一种无需训练数据或GPU支持的通用、可扩展框架，适用于多种成像模态和生物应用场景，其代码已开源，便于科研人员使用与二次开发。

Abstract: Background and Objective: Quantitative analysis of cell dynamics is central to modern biological research, providing critical insights into immune cell interactions, disease progression, and drug mechanisms. Automated cell tracking in time-lapse microscopy remains challenging due to noise, morphological variations, overlapping cells, and dynamic events such as divisions and fusions.
  Methods: We present ARGUS, a framework for Accelerated, Robust, General, and Unsupervised Cell Tracking Solutions. ARGUS combines adaptive cell detection, dense Farneback optical-flow prediction, frame-to-frame linear assignment, and a sequence-level tracklet-refinement step that reconnects trajectory fragments across short temporal gaps.
  Results: On publicly available Cell Tracking Challenge datasets, ARGUS achieved detection accuracy of 0.905-0.971 and tracking accuracy of 0.897-0.964, with runtimes within 1 minute (5-6 seconds for 3 frames).
  Conclusions: ARGUS is a modular, interpretable framework that can be adapted to different imaging modalities and biological applications without training data or GPU infrastructure. The implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/Gitinc/argus

### [42] [Texture Representations in Deep Vision Models: Comparing CNNs, Vision Transformers, and Human Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08321)
*Ludovica de Paolis,Marco Baroni,Alessandro Laio,Eugenio Piasini*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了卷积神经网络（CNN）和视觉变压器（ViT）在纹理感知任务中的表现，发现ViT在纹理表示上与人类心理物理学数据更一致，且不同复杂度的纹理在ViT中形成相似表示，而CNN则表现不佳。结果表明，网络架构可能主导计算模型对纹理的表征方式，且ViT更接近人类视觉处理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注CNN在物体识别任务中与生物视觉的对齐性，但对纹理等非语义视觉任务的表征能力仍不明确。本文旨在探究不同深度学习模型在纹理感知任务中的表现，并评估其与人类视觉系统的相似性。

Method: 采用三种不同算法生成具有不同复杂度的纹理图像；利用基于秩的统计方法量化CNN和三种ViT模型内部表示的信息量；通过比较这些表示与人类心理物理学数据的相似性，评估模型与人类感知的一致性。

Result: ViT在纹理表示上表现出高度一致性，且其表示与人类行为数据相关性更高；而CNN与ViTs之间的纹理表示不一致；不同复杂度的纹理在ViTs中形成相似表示。

Conclusion: 视觉变压器（ViT）比卷积神经网络（CNN）更能忠实反映人类对纹理模式的视觉处理机制，且模型对纹理的表征受网络架构影响显著。

Abstract: In computational vision science, Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) have emerged as a popular model of biological vision because of the alignment they can exhibit with neural and behavioral data in humans and animals. However, it remains unclear to what extent this alignment persists for visual tasks that extend beyond the canonical object recognition paradigm based on well defined semantic content. In this study, we diverge from the common object-centric view by focusing on another aspect of vision: texture perception. We consider textures of different complexity generated with three different algorithms from the same source images. Using a rank-based statistic, we quantify the information encoded in the internal representations of a CNN and three Vision Transformers (ViTs), and we compare the similarity of these representations to those inferred from human psychophysics data. We find that the representation of textures is aligned in different ViTs, but not between the ViTs and the CNN; that ViTs form similar representations for textures of different complexity; that human performance in recognizing textures can be better predicted from ViTs representations rather than CNN representations. Taken together, these results suggest that ViTs may capture more faithfully than CNNs how texture patterns are visually processed by humans, and that the representations of texture stimuli in computational models may be driven by the network architecture.

### [43] [WCog-VLA: A Dual-Level World-Cognitive Vision-Language-Action Model for End-to-End Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08375)
*Xuerun Yan,Zhexi Lian,Nuoheng Zhang,Shiyu Fang,Haoran Wang,Chen Lv,Jia Hu,Binyang Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WCog-VLA提出一种双层次世界认知视觉-语言-动作框架，通过统一语义世界预测与生成式世界演化，实现主动自动驾驶。该框架在语义层面结合3D空间感知与代理标记以捕捉动态，并引入博弈论思维链（Game-CoT）推理；在生成层面采用对齐解耦扩散变换器（ADDT），高效生成物理合理多智能体轨迹。通过场景表示对齐减少去噪步骤，显著加速推理。构建包含8.5万条Game-CoT标注的大规模数据集，实验表明其在NAVSIM基准上达到92.9的SOTA PDMS分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
