Method: 提出WCog-VLA框架，包含两个层级：1）语义层：融合3D空间感知与代理标记，实现世界认知与推理统一，并引入博弈论思维链（Game-CoT）进行战略推理；2）生成层：设计对齐解耦扩散变换器（ADDT），生成物理合理的多智能体联合轨迹，通过场景表示对齐提升生成效率并加速推理。此外，构建大规模含85,000条Game-CoT标注的数据集以支持策略推理训练。

Result: 在NAVSIM基准测试中，WCog-VLA取得92.9的PDMS得分，达到当前最先进（SOTA）水平，验证了其在主动驾驶中的优越性能。

Conclusion: WCog-VLA成功实现了从被动反应到主动前瞻的转变，通过融合语义认知与生成式世界演化，显著提升了自动驾驶系统的预见性与决策能力，为未来智能交通系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have advanced end-to-end autonomous driving. However, existing methods either lack comprehensive world cognition or suffer from fragmented world foresight, inherently confining these models to reactive driving. To address this limitation, we propose WCog-VLA, a novel dual-level World-Cognitive VLA framework that successfully bridges semantic world forecasting with generative world evolution to achieve proactive autonomous driving. At the semantic level, WCog-VLA unifies world cognition and reasoning by incorporating 3D spatial perception and injecting agent tokens to capture the world dynamics, while concurrently enabling Game-theoretic Chain-of-Thought (Game-CoT) reasoning. At the generative level, we introduce the Aligned Decoupled Diffusion Transformer (ADDT) as a powerful generative world model that synthesizes physically-plausible joint multi-agent trajectories. Through scene representation alignment, ADDT reduces the number of denoising steps required and thus significantly accelerates inference. To facilitate strategic reasoning, we further construct a large-scale dataset featuring 85k Game-CoT annotations. Extensive experiments on the NAVSIM benchmark demonstrate that WCog-VLA achieves a State-Of-The-Art (SOTA) PDMS score of 92.9.

### [44] [Classical versus Deep Mirror-Symmetry Scoring: A Benchmark of Thirteen Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08379)
*Maximilian Woehrer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究对13种图像对称性评分方法进行了基准测试，涵盖从经典特征到冻结深度特征的方法，在单轴和多轴数据集上采用反射精确协议进行评估。结果显示，深度模型在单轴和复杂多轴任务中表现最佳，但经典HOG描述符仅以微小但显著的差距落后于最佳冻结网络读出，且运行速度比其快约300倍。研究表明，对称性判别主要集中在中等尺度的方向特征上，深度模型在浅层或中层达到峰值，而HOG在中等单元尺寸时表现最佳。因此，现有方法中，冻结深度特征相比优化后的经典描述符优势有限；任务训练的深度评分器是否能更好仍有待探索。研究还发布了开源工具imgsym，用于图像对称性检测与测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对称性评分方法缺乏统一、统计严谨的比较基准，限制了方法选择与应用优化。

Method: 采用反射精确协议，基于机会锚定和显著性检验的判别能力评估13种对称性评分方法，涵盖经典特征与冻结深度特征，在四个单轴和五个多轴数据集上进行测试。

Result: 深度模型在单轴和复杂多轴任务中表现最优；经典HOG描述符虽略逊于最佳冻结网络读出，但性能差异显著且运行速度快300倍；对称性判别集中于中等尺度方向特征，深度模型在浅/中层，HOG在中等单元尺寸达到峰值。

Conclusion: 冻结深度特征相比优化后的经典描述符并无明显优势；任务训练的深度评分器能否提升性能仍待研究。研究发布开源工具imgsym。

Abstract: Quantifying how mirror-symmetric an image is about a given axis (symmetry scoring) underpins applications from visual aesthetics to medical imaging, yet proposed scoring methods have never been compared on a common, statistically grounded protocol. We benchmark 13 scoring methods (nine collected from literature, four introduced here) spanning from classical features to frozen deep features, across four single-axis and five multi-axis datasets under a reflection-exact protocol with a chance-anchored, significance-tested discrimination skill. Deep backbones perform best on single-axis and harder multi-axis protocols. However, a classical histogram-of-oriented-gradients (HOG) descriptor trails the best frozen-network readout by a small (but significant) margin, is not statistically separable from the runner-up (a CNN-filter measure), and runs ~300x faster on CPU. Our results show that discrimination concentrates in mid-scale oriented features, where deep backbones peak at a low or mid stage, and HOG peaks at a mid cell size. Among existing methods, frozen deep features thus offer little over a tuned classical descriptor for measuring symmetry; whether task-trained deep scorers can do better remains open. We release the scorers and harness in imgsym, an open toolkit for image symmetry detection and measurement.

*Shun Liu,Nan Xi,Yang Liu,Tianyu Luan,Xuan Gong,David Doermann*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为ReferEndoscopy的大规模基准数据集，用于内窥镜图像分割（RIS），并引入了基于属性检索的端到端内窥镜图像分割框架AR-ERIS。该方法通过在高质量标注数据上预训练，有效捕捉内窥镜场景中的细粒度文本线索，在模拟和真实世界数据上均实现了最先进的性能，并展现出良好的泛化能力。

Motivation: 内窥镜图像分割面临标注数据稀缺、图像-文本关系复杂且领域特定的问题，现有视觉语言模型难以准确捕捉细粒度文本信息，导致性能不佳和泛化能力弱。

Abstract: Referring Image Segmentation (RIS) aims to segment image regions specified by natural language, enabling fine-grained and controllable visual understanding. Extending RIS to endoscopic imagery, however, presents unique challenges, including scarce high-quality annotations and complex, domain-specific image-text relationships. Although recent vision-language models demonstrate strong cross-domain alignment, they often fail to capture fine-grained textual cues in endoscopic settings, resulting in suboptimal performance and limited generalization. To address these challenges, we introduce ReferEndoscopy, a large-scale benchmark for RIS in the endoscopy field. Building on this dataset, we propose the Attribute Retrieval-based Endoscopic-RIS (AR-ERIS) framework for open-vocabulary endoscopic compositional referring segmentation. AR-ERIS leverages attribute retrieval for open-vocabulary endoscopic compositional referring segmentation and is pretrained on the curated ReferEndoscopy dataset, achieving state-of-the-art performance with strong generalization across both simulated and real-world endoscopic data. ### [46] [Swapping Faces, Saving Features: A Dual-Purpose Pipeline for Pedestrian Privacy in ITS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08402)

Provenly, Roop outperforms Ghost-v2 in various aspects, as will be discussed. Consequently, Roop is the face-swapping model to be used in the pipeline to strike the balance between pedestrian privacy via identity concealment and data usability via facial attribute preservation.

### [47] [Track2Map: Online Deformable SLAM with Motion-Aware Pose Optimization in Robotic Surgery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08408)
*Tianyi Song,Sierra Bonilla,Xinwei Ju,Evangelos Mazomenos,Danail Stoyanov,Adam Schmidt,Omid Mohareri,Sophia Bano,Francisco Vasconcelos*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Track2Map，一种在线3D高斯点云重建方法，可联合优化相机轨迹与可变形场景表示，无需依赖精确的相机轨迹先验，在无先验或先验噪声时仍能实现鲁棒的3D重建，具备类似SLAM的能力。通过基于密集2D点跟踪的锚定变形初始化和轨迹统计分析，有效缓解组织运动与模糊视觉线索带来的优化不稳定性，并在StereoMIS数据集上优于现有SLAM及非SLAM方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高斯点云方法多为离线处理且依赖精确的相机轨迹先验（如机器人运动学），当先验缺失或存在噪声时性能受限，限制了其在实际手术中的应用。因此需要一种不依赖先验、可在线运行并能同时估计相机轨迹与场景变形的重建方法。

Method: 提出Track2Map，采用在线3D高斯点云框架，联合优化相机轨迹与可变形场景表示；引入基于密集2D点跟踪的变形初始化，利用轨迹统计信息识别静止相机阶段，减少增量映射过程中的漂移，提升优化稳定性。

Result: 在StereoMIS数据集上，Track2Map在3D重建质量与相机轨迹估计方面均优于现有SLAM方法及依赖先验的非SLAM方法，证明其在无先验或低质量先验条件下的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Track2Map实现了无需精确相机轨迹先验的在线3D可变形重建，具备强鲁棒性和实用性，适用于真实手术环境，为机器人辅助微创手术中的实时三维可视化提供了新解决方案。

Abstract: Gaussian splatting is the current state-of-the-art for dense, deformable 3D anatomy reconstruction in robot-assisted minimally invasive surgery (RAMIS); however, most pipelines are offline and depend on accurate camera trajectory priors (often from robotic kinematics), limiting applicability when priors are missing or noisy. To address these limitations, we propose Track2Map, an online 3D Gaussian Splatting pipeline that jointly optimizes camera trajectory and 3D deformable scene representation directly from surgical video. Track2Map is therefore capable of robust 3D reconstructions when camera trajectory priors are either absent or noisy, and due to its online nature it effectively works as a Simultaneous Localisation and Mapping (SLAM) method. To stabilize optimization in the presence of tissue motion and ambiguous visual cues, we introduce a track-anchored deformation initialization using dense 2D point tracks. Track statistics are further utilized to disentangle camera motion from scene deformation by detecting static camera periods and reducing drift during incremental mapping. Experiments on StereoMIS show improved reconstruction quality and camera trajectory against competing SLAM methods, as well as compared to non-SLAM methods that utilize camera trajectory priors. The code is available at https://track2map.github.io/.

### [48] [DeltaV: Thinking with Visual State Updates in Unified Large Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08434)
*Pengjie Wang,Linger Deng,Zujia Zhang,Shaojie Zhang,Zhenbo Luo,Pei Fu,Jian Luan,Xiang Bai,Yuliang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DeltaV提出一种视觉更新机制，替代传统全图生成，通过增量预测紧凑的视觉变化令牌，减少冗余并增强关键状态转换的监督。引入时间相似性路由器（TSIM）动态控制令牌分配，提升效率。构建大规模多模态推理数据集StructCoT（1.05M样本），支持更广泛的任务。实验表明，该方法在保持重建质量的同时，视觉令牌生成量减少55.6%，多模态推理性能提升3.3%；DeltaV-2B在多个基准上优于更大模型和同规模Qwen3-VL-2B。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一大模型采用全图生成方式生成每个视觉状态，导致视觉令牌冗余严重，并削弱对稀疏但关键的状态转换的监督。需要更高效、精准的视觉表示机制以提升多模态推理能力。

Method: 提出视觉更新机制，基于历史视觉状态增量预测紧凑的视觉变化令牌；设计时间相似性（TSIM）路由器，根据边际重建增益动态停止令牌分配；构建大规模多模态推理数据集StructCoT以支持多样化任务训练。

Result: 视觉更新机制使新生成视觉令牌减少55.6%，重建保真度不变，多模态推理性能提升3.3%；DeltaV-2B在域内任务上超越更大开源模型8.4%，在外部基准上超越同规模Qwen3-VL-2B 5.9%。

Conclusion: DeltaV通过视觉更新与动态路由机制显著提升多模态推理效率与性能，结合大规模数据训练实现更强泛化能力，为高效统一多模态模型提供新范式。

Abstract: Current Unified Large Multimodal Models (ULMMs) support interleaved multimodal reasoning through textual reasoning and intermediate visual states, but typically generate each visual state as a full image. This full-image generation paradigm introduces substantial visual-token redundancy and dilutes supervision on sparse yet reasoning-critical state transitions. We propose DeltaV, a ULMM that replaces full-image generation with visual updates. Conditioned on historical visual states, DeltaV incrementally predicts compact update tokens that capture the visual changes across reasoning steps, avoiding repeated modeling of unchanged content. To align the token budget of each update with the magnitude of visual change, DeltaV introduces a temporal similarity (TSIM) Router, which stops allocating tokens once the marginal reconstruction gain falls below a threshold. To support more diverse and generalizable reasoning, we further construct StructCoT, a large-scale interleaved multimodal reasoning dataset with 1.05M samples spanning 44 task domains. Experiments show that the visual-update paradigm reduces newly generated visual tokens by 55.6\% on average without compromising reconstruction fidelity, and improves multimodal reasoning by 3.3\% over full-image generation. Trained with StructCoT and large-scale multimodal data, DeltaV-2B further outperforms substantially larger open-source models by 8.4\% on in-domain multimodal reasoning evaluations and surpasses the comparable-scale Qwen3-VL-2B by 5.9\% on external multimodal reasoning and understanding benchmarks. Code, models, and StructCoT will be released at https://github.com/Pengjie-W/DeltaV.

### [50] [VEGAS: Human-Aligned Video Caption Evaluation via Gaze](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08489)
*Shenghui Chen,Po-han Li,Ximeng Sun,Shijia Yang,Emad Barsoum,Zicheng Liu,Sandeep Chinchali,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VEGAS 是一种无需训练的视频字幕评估指标，利用测试时的眼动数据生成个性化的、与注意力对齐的文本。它通过跨模态信息论方法衡量候选字幕与观看者注意力的匹配程度，并在自定视角活动和教学幻灯片数据集上验证其有效性。实验表明，基于 VEGAS 选择的字幕能显著提升与人类注意力的一致性，并改善下游字幕到视频的检索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型生成的视频字幕通常无法反映个体观众的关注点，缺乏个性化注意力对齐。为解决这一问题，提出一种无需重训练即可在推理阶段融合观众注意力的评估方法。

Method: 提出 VEGAS（Video caption Evaluation via GAze Score），一种基于眼动数据的跨模态信息论评估指标，通过拒绝采样从候选字幕中筛选出与用户注视焦点更一致的描述，无需重新训练模型。

Result: 实验结果显示，使用 VEGAS 筛选的字幕在与人类注视行为的一致性上显著提升，同时增强了字幕到视频检索任务的性能。

Conclusion: VEGAS 证明了在推理阶段融入观众注意力可有效提升视频字幕的相关性和实用性，具有良好的应用前景。

Abstract: Vision-language models excel at video captioning, yet typically generate descriptions that fail to capture individual viewers' attention. We propose VEGAS (Video caption Evaluation via GAze Score), a training-free metric that leverages test-time gaze to sample personalized, attention-aligned text. It is a cross-modal, information-theoretic metric that quantifies how well a candidate caption matches a viewer's focus. To evaluate VEGAS, we curate a dataset of egocentric activities and instructional slides paired with synchronized gaze and reference annotations. We then select captions based on VEGAS via rejection sampling without model retraining. Experiments show that VEGAS-selected captions align significantly better with human focus and improve downstream caption-to-video retrieval, demonstrating the practical utility of incorporating viewer attention during inference.

### [51] [Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent for Multimodal Understanding, Generation, and Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08497)
*Feng Wang,Canmiao Fu,Zhipeng Huang,Chen Li,Jing Lyu,Ge Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种认知结构化的多模态智能体（Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent），通过将视觉信息外化到情景记忆中并选择性激活相关记忆片段，解决长时程多模态对话中的视觉令牌爆炸与跨轮次引用不可靠问题。该智能体包含感知抽象引擎、认知检索引擎和多模态执行控制器，并基于自动生成的带细粒度标注的多轮对话数据集，使用强化学习优化抽象与检索策略。构建了分难度层级的长时程视觉对话基准评估情景记忆召回能力。8B模型在20轮会话中达到91.4%检索准确率，优于32B基线8.2%，且每轮推理时间减半（23.1s→12.7s）。进一步推出CMA-Harness工具链，集成持久化多模态记忆、网络访问、图像生成/编辑/组合工具及OpenAI兼容服务，实现模块化决策与高效部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一多模态模型在长时程多模态对话中因反复输入全部历史视觉与文本信息，导致视觉令牌数量激增，影响效率并降低跨轮次引用可靠性。亟需一种更高效、可扩展的机制来支持长期记忆与上下文理解。

Method: 设计认知结构化多模态智能体，包括：1）感知抽象引擎用于结构化视觉信息提取；2）认知检索引擎实现跨轮次记忆检索；3）多模态执行控制器负责任务推断与动作规划。开发统一场景引擎生成带精细标注的多轮对话数据，用于强化学习训练。构建分层难度的长时程视觉对话基准进行评估。推出CMA-Harness工具链，集成记忆、工具与服务接口。

Result: 8B模型在20轮对话中实现91.4%的检索准确率，优于32B基线8.2%，每轮推理时间从23.1秒降至12.7秒，效率显著提升。实验验证了结构化记忆与模块化决策在长时程多模态交互中的有效性。

Conclusion: 基于认知结构的多模态智能体通过外部化视觉记忆与选择性重激活，实现了比单纯参数扩展更高效、可扩展的长时程多模态交互范式。结合工具增强与模块化架构，为未来智能体发展提供了新方向。

Abstract: Recent unified multimodal models show a single architecture can jointly perform vision/language understanding and image generation/editing. However, they repeatedly feed all historical visual and textual inputs into a shared context window, limiting long-horizon multimodal dialogue due to visual token explosion and unreliable cross-turn referencing. We propose a Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent that externalizes visual information into an Episodic Visual Memory and selectively reactivates relevant episodes during reasoning. The agent consists of a Perceptual Abstraction Engine for structured visual abstraction, a Cognitive Retrieval Engine for cross-turn memory retrieval, and a Multimodal Executive Controller for autonomous task inference and action planning. To address the lack of turn-level retrieval supervision in existing datasets, we develop a Unified Scenario Engine that programmatically generates structured multi-turn conversations with fine-grained retrieval annotations, enabling reinforcement learning to optimize abstraction and retrieval policies. We also construct a long-horizon visual-dialogue benchmark stratified by difficulty to evaluate episodic visual recall. Our 8B agent achieves 91.4% retrieval accuracy over 20-turn sessions, surpassing 32B baselines by +8.2% while nearly halving per-turn inference time (23.1s -> 12.7s). We further present the Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent Harness (CMA-Harness), a tool-augmented deployment of the same cognitive structure integrating persistent multimodal memory, web access, image generation/editing/composition tools, and OpenAI-compatible serving. Structured memory and modular decision-making offer a more scalable, efficient paradigm for long-horizon multimodal agents than monolithic parameter scaling. Code: https://github.com/caseclose/cma-harness ; Project page: https://caseclose.github.io/cma-harness/

### [52] [CT-CLIP Representations for Multimodal Lung Cancer Survival Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08503)

Method: 使用CT-CLIP作为预训练特征提取器，对242例肺癌患者的术前CT图像和临床变量进行特征提取。评估三种适应策略：冻结编码器、全微调和低秩适配；同时进行模态消融分析，并与临床及多模态基线模型进行比较。采用可训练的轻量级生存头部进行最终预测。

Result: 冻结的CT-CLIP模型配合可训练的轻量级生存头在生存预测任务上表现最佳，显著优于临床基线，且性能与或优于其他多模态方法。模型能有效划分出具有临床意义的高风险和低风险患者组。

Conclusion: 在数据受限的临床环境下，基于冻结的领域特定基础模型CT-CLIP进行特征提取，结合轻量级生存头部，是一种高效且有效的多模态生存预测策略，具备良好的临床应用潜力。

We assess the foundation model CT-CLIP as a feature extractor for pretreatment computed tomography images and clinical variables from 242 diagnosed lung cancer patients. The evaluation includes adaptation strategies based on frozen encoders, full fine-tuning, and low-rank adaptation, together with modality ablations and comparisons with clinical and multimodal baselines. The results show that a frozen CT-CLIP model combined with a trainable lightweight survival head outperforms the clinical baseline and achieves comparable or improved performance relative to other multimodal approaches, and separates patients into clinically meaningful high- and low-risk groups.

### [53] [Do Egocentric Video-Language Models Capture Both Hand- and Object-Centric Cues?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08514)
*Masatoshi Tateno,Alexandros Stergiou,Risa Shinoda,Yoichi Sato,Dima Damen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的手-物体交互（HOI）识别学习范式，通过手-物体掩码训练和HOI动态感知解码器，增强模型对手和物体外观及动态的鲁棒性。引入CI-HOI评估框架与DEHOI测试集，实现对线索独立推理能力的系统评测，验证了方法在多种任务上的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频-语言模型常依赖手、物体或环境之间的虚假关联，而非基于手和物体本身的外观与动态进行推理，导致泛化能力不足。为解决此问题，需提升模型对局部信息的敏感性与独立推理能力。

Method: 提出手-物体掩码训练以应对部分观察；设计HOI动态感知解码器，通过辅助预测手和物体的位置与语义，显式学习手-物体中心嵌入；构建DEHOI测试集，结合图像修复技术分离手与物体线索，支持线索隔离评估。

Result: 在DEHOI、标准动作识别、物体状态识别及机器人操作动作识别任务上均优于现有模型，证明所提方法能更有效地利用手与物体线索，提升整体HOI理解的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提学习范式显著提升了模型对手-物体交互中关键线索的独立感知与推理能力，为更可靠、可解释的视频理解提供了新方向。

Abstract: Hand-object interaction (HOI) recognition requires capturing both hand manipulations and object transformations. However, existing video-language models often fall into shortcuts by relying on spurious correlations among hands, objects, or environmental context, rather than reasoning from the appearance and dynamics of hands and objects themselves. To address this limitation, we propose a new learning paradigm that combines (i) hand-object masked training, which enables robust reasoning from partial hand or object observations, and (ii) an HOI-dynamics-aware decoder that explicitly learns hand- and object-centric embeddings through auxiliary predictions of their locations and semantics, enhancing sensitivity to both cues. To systematically evaluate such cue-specific reasoning, we introduce Cue-Isolated HOI (CI-HOI), a new evaluation that assesses models' ability to predict actions from hand- and object-related cues independently. To enable CI-HOI, we curate the DEHOI testbed, which separates hand- and object-related observations for disentangled HOI evaluation through inpainting. Using DEHOI, we demonstrate both quantitatively and qualitatively that our training strategy exploits hand- and object-centric information more effectively than existing models. Our approach improves over existing models on DEHOI, standard action recognition, object state recognition, and even robot manipulation action recognition, leading to more robust HOI understanding.

</details>


### [54] [Beyond wheelchairs and blindfolds: Investigating disability stereotypes in T2I models with INCLUDE-BENCH](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08515)
*Sophia Lichtenberg,Albert Gatt,Judith Masthoff*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 INCLUDE-BENCH，首个大规模评估文本到图像（T2I）模型中与残疾相关的偏见的基准测试。该基准包含11.9万张基于多维度偏见提示生成的图像，涵盖静态与动态情境。评估了15个开源和2个闭源模型，发现：所有模型对行动障碍和默认残疾提示均主要生成轮椅形象；带有残疾条件的生成图像多样性较低；刻板印象表现与文本提示关联更强；并引入‘刻板印象内容模型（SCM）得分’，表明T2I模型反映了现实世界中的刻板印象关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前T2I模型在社会偏见方面已有研究，但主要聚焦于性别、肤色和文化代表性，而对残疾群体的系统性探索不足。现有评估方法未能契合社会学定义的刻板印象，导致对残障人士表征伤害的评估缺乏原则性依据。因此，亟需一个全面、符合社会学框架的评估体系来揭示并量化此类偏见。

Method: 构建 INCLUDE-BENCH 基准测试，设计涵盖多个偏见维度的提示，生成11.9万张图像，覆盖静态与动态语境；评估15个开源与2个闭源T2I模型；使用定量分析与新提出的‘刻板印象内容模型（SCM）得分’衡量模型输出中的刻板印象强度与文本-图像对齐程度。

Result: （1）所有模型对行动障碍及默认残疾提示普遍生成轮椅图像；（2）残疾条件生成的图像多样性显著低于非残疾条件；（3）刻板印象图像与提示文本之间的对齐度更高；（4）通过SCM得分验证，模型反映真实世界中的刻板印象关联。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了当前T2I模型在残障表征上的深层系统性偏见，强调需要更严谨的社会学导向评估框架。INCLUDE-BENCH 为未来公平性评估提供了可扩展的基准工具，推动更具包容性的生成式AI发展。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) models have been shown to exhibit social biases. Prior work has mainly focused on gender, skin tone, and cultural representation within restricted occupational associations, and emerging benchmarks increasingly incorporate these dimensions. However, disability remains systematically underexplored. Current evaluation practices often fail to align with sociologically grounded definitions of stereotyping, limiting principled assessment of representational harms toward people with disabilities (PWD). To address this, we introduce INCLUDE-BENCH, the first large-scale benchmark for evaluating disability-related bias in T2I models. INCLUDE-BENCH comprises 119K generated images based on prompt design across multiple bias dimensions and both static and dynamic contexts. We evaluate 15 open-source and 2 closed-source models. Our key findings reveal that: (1) mobility-impaired and default disability prompts predominantly yield wheelchair depictions across all models; (2) disability-conditioned generations consistently exhibit less diversity; (3) stereotypical portrayals demonstrate stronger disability-text alignment; and (4) we introduce the Stereotype Content Model (SCM) Score, demonstrating that T2I models reflect real-world stereotypical associations.

### [55] [Whareformer: Learning to Track What is Where in Long Egocentric Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08537)
*Jacob Chalk,Saptarshi Sinha,Dima Damen,Yannis Kalantidis,Diane Larlus*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Whareformer 是首个基于学习的 OSNOM 任务解决方案，采用 Transformer 架构，结合可更新的记忆模块和前馈式轨迹分配机制，能有效跟踪遮挡或离视野物体，在小规模训练下实现 SOTA 性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OSNOM 任务要求在第一人称视频中持续追踪被佩戴者移动的物体，即使其离开视野或被严重遮挡，现有方法缺乏有效的学习型解决方案。

Method: 提出 Whareformer 模型，包含可更新的轨迹记忆和前馈式轨迹分配模块，联合推理物体外观（what）与 3D 位置（where），并引入新轨迹标记以识别新物体。

Result: 在仅 56 个训练视频上训练，模型在 260 个长视频测试集（EPIC-KITCHENS-100、IT3DEgo、HD-EPIC）上达到 SOTA 表现，显著优于先前方法。

Conclusion: Whareformer 通过相对距离建模和动态轨迹表示，实现了高效、鲁棒的在线物体追踪，为第一人称视频中的长期跟踪提供了新的学习范式。

Abstract: The recently established 'Out of Sight, Not out of Mind' (OSNOM) task for egocentric videos focuses on tracking objects that are moved by the camera wearer, online, maintaining knowledge of instance locations throughout the video even when they leave the field of view or become heavily occluded. In this paper, we propose the first learning-based solution to the OSNOM task: Whareformer, a transformer-based model with two components: an updatable memory of established tracks and a track assignment module that associates observations with existing tracks in a feed-forward manner. Whareformer jointly reasons over evolving object appearance (what) and updated 3D location (where), and employs a dedicated New Track token to reason about novel objects.
  Thanks to its design choices of using relative distances and evolving track representations, Whareformer is trained on a small set of 56 videos but achieves SOTA performance on 260 long test videos from three datasets: EPIC-KITCHENS-100 (unseen videos), IT3DEgo, and HD-EPIC, with significant absolute improvements over prior work.

</details>


### [56] [VocaDet: Sample-Driven Open-Vocabulary Object Detection and Segmentation via Visual Tokenization and Vector Database Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08541)
*ZhiXin Sun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VocaDet 是一种无需模型重训练即可从用户提供的正负样本中学习物体概念的开放词汇目标检测与分割框架。它通过将连续视觉表示转化为离散视觉词汇，并利用可扩展的向量数据库进行高效检索，实现了对任意物体的识别。该方法基于 DINOv3 提取视觉特征，采用自适应聚类敏感度的层次聚类生成多粒度视觉标记，并结合位置去偏表示和空间拓扑信息构建可扩展的对象记忆库。推理时，查询图像被转换为视觉标记并快速匹配存储的记忆库以实现定位与分割。此外，引入背景过滤机制以去除常见背景模式，减少固定摄像头场景下的冗余检索。在 UA-DETRAC 数据集上的实验表明，VocaDet 在无需传统检测器训练的情况下实现了有效的开放词汇检测性能，并支持随着新增样本持续扩展的识别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放词汇目标检测与分割方法通常依赖文本提示、有限视觉样例或昂贵的特征匹配过程，难以扩展至大规模且持续增长的物体库。因此，亟需一种无需重训练、可高效扩展的样本驱动框架。

Method: 使用 DINOv3 作为视觉特征提取器，通过自适应聚类敏感度的层次聚类生成多粒度视觉标记；结合位置去偏表示与空间拓扑信息构建可扩展的对象记忆库；将查询图像转为视觉标记后，在向量数据库中进行高效匹配；引入背景过滤机制减少冗余检索。

Result: 在 UA-DETRAC 数据集上，VocaDet 实现了无需传统检测器训练的有效开放词汇检测性能，具备随正负样本累积而持续扩展的识别能力，且在固定摄像头场景下表现出良好的鲁棒性与效率。

Conclusion: VocaDet 通过构建可扩展的视觉词汇与对象记忆库，提供了一种高效、无须重训练的开放词汇检测与分割解决方案，适用于大规模、动态更新的物体识别任务。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary object detection and segmentation aim to recognize arbitrary objects beyond predefined categories. Although recent vision-language and reference-based approaches have significantly advanced this field, they often rely on text prompts, limited visual examples, or expensive feature matching procedures, making them difficult to scale to large and continuously expanding object repositories. In this work, we propose VocaDet, a sample-driven open-vocabulary object detection and segmentation framework that learns object concepts directly from user-provided positive and negative sample collections without model retraining. The key idea is to transform continuous visual representations into discrete visual vocabularies and perform efficient retrieval-based recognition through a scalable vector database. Specifically, we employ DINOv3 as the visual feature extractor and apply agglomerative clustering with adaptive clustering sensitivity to generate multi-granularity visual tokens. These visual tokens, together with position-debiased representations and spatial topology information, are stored as expandable object memories in a vector database. During inference, query images are converted into visual tokens and efficiently matched against the stored object memories for object localization and segmentation. Furthermore, a background filtering mechanism is introduced to remove frequently occurring background patterns and reduce redundant retrieval operations in practical fixed-camera scenarios. Experiments on the UA-DETRAC dataset demonstrate that VocaDet achieves effective open-vocabulary detection performance without conventional detector training, while supporting continuously expandable recognition capability as additional positive and negative samples are accumulated.

</details>


### [57] [Switch-Reasoner: Learn When to Think in Multitask Mixtures via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08572)
*Yiyang Fang,Pei Fu,Jinjie Li,Jian Liang,Wenke Huang,Ruijie Luo,Shaojie Zhang,Jian Luan,Yi R. Fung,Mang Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Switch-Reasoner 是一种基于 GRPO 的框架，旨在让多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）自适应地选择推理模式。它将思考视为虚拟工具调用，允许模型直接回答或在回答前进行显式推理。通过双层调控机制，平衡整体和样本级别的思考与直接回答使用，提升训练稳定性。在 11 个多模态任务上的实验表明，该方法减少了不必要的推理，同时保持了强性能，实现了更好的准确率-效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的 MLLMs 采用固定的先思考后回答范式，在异构多任务场景中效率低下，因为简单输入无需复杂推理，而困难输入则需要。此外，后训练阶段的学习难以稳定，容易导致模型要么始终思考，要么始终直接回答。因此需要一种能够自适应判断何时思考的机制。

Method: 提出 Switch-Reasoner 框架，将思考视为虚拟工具调用，使模型可选择直接回答或先推理再回答。引入双层调控机制：全局层面平衡两种模式的使用比例；样本层面根据两种选择的相对收益提供监督信号，以稳定学习过程。

Result: 在 11 个多模态任务上，Switch-Reasoner 显著减少了不必要的推理，同时维持了高水平的准确性，实现了更优的准确率-效率权衡。

Conclusion: Switch-Reasoner 有效解决了 MLLMs 在多任务场景下推理决策不灵活、训练不稳定的问题，通过自适应选择推理模式提升了模型效率与性能平衡，为后续多模态智能系统设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) often follow a fixed Think-then-Answer paradigm, which is inefficient in heterogeneous multitask settings because simple inputs may not require explicit reasoning while difficult ones can benefit substantially from it. Learning when to think is also unstable during post-training, where imbalanced rollouts can drive the model toward always-thinking or always-direct behavior. We propose Switch-Reasoner, a GRPO-based framework that learns to adaptively select reasoning modes for MLLMs. It treats thinking as a virtual tool invocation and allows the model to either answer directly or invoke explicit reasoning before answering. To stabilize this decision, we introduce a dual-level regulation mechanism that balances the overall use of Thinking Mode and Direct Mode while providing sample-level supervision based on the relative benefit of the two choices. Experiments on 11 multimodal tasks show that Switch-Reasoner reduces unnecessary reasoning while maintaining strong performance, achieving a better accuracy-efficiency trade-off.

</details>


### [58] [When Structured Sparse Autoencoders Learn Consistent Concepts Across Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08605)
*Weiduo Liao,Yunqiao Yang,Ying Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出S^2AE，一种结构化稀疏自编码器，通过引入基于注意力相似性和空间邻近性的图像块分组及结构化稀疏正则化，提升视觉-语言模型中概念的一致性与可解释性。在Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct上，实现mIoU提升6.06%，表示效率提高（l0范数降低），同时保持99%以上的重建保真度，并在跨模态分析中显著增强单义性与语义一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有稀疏自编码器（SAEs）在视觉-语言模型中难以学习模态一致的概念，尤其在视觉模态中概念呈现碎片化分布，缺乏空间和语义一致性。为解决此问题，需引入结构化先验以促进概念的连贯性和可解释性。

Method: 将图像块根据Transformer注意力相似性和空间邻近性进行分组；设计结构化稀疏正则化，包含组间排他性稀疏以实现概念解耦，组内稀疏以保证组内概念一致性；在训练标准SAE时加入该正则化项，引导隐层神经元聚焦于具有明确语义的独立概念。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct模型上，平均语义对齐（mIoU）提升6.06%，表示效率（l0范数）显著降低至60.81，重建保真度（解释方差）超过99%；跨模态分析显示，视觉结构先验有效提升了神经元的单义性，语义一致性提升3.08%，单义性得分提升2.37%。

Conclusion: S^2AE通过引入视觉结构先验，成功增强了多模态模型中稀疏特征的语义一致性、空间连贯性和可解释性，为机制可解释性研究提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have emerged as a promising technique for mechanistic interpretability by learning a set of sparse latent features in large models, each of which encodes a distinct concept. However, in vision-language models (VLMs), vanilla SAEs struggle to learn modality-consistent concepts, with concepts often exhibiting fragmented coverage (i.e., disjoint regions) in the visual modality. To address this challenge, we propose a Structured Sparse AutoEncoder ($S^2AE$) that enforces concept consistency from both semantic and spatial perspectives in the visual modality. Specifically, we group image patches based on Transformer attention similarity and spatial proximity, and introduce a structured sparsity regularization when training the vanilla SAE. The regularization consists of exclusive sparsity for inter-group concept disentanglement and group sparsity for intra-group concept consistency, which drives the latent neurons by SAEs to specialize in distinct, semantically grounded concepts. Evaluated on the \texttt{Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct} model, the method achieves 6.06% average improvement in semantic alignment (mIoU) and 60.81 in representational efficiency (lower l0 norm) while maintaining near-perfect reconstruction fidelity with an Explained Variance above 99%. Cross-modal analysis further demonstrates that $S^2AE$ enhances neuronal monosemanticity by this visual structural prior, achieving a 3.08% average gain in semantic consistency and a 2.37% average gain in monosemanticity scores for both modalities of multimodal features, thereby fostering more coherent and disentangled representations.

### [59] [Do Transformations Reveal the Truth? Generative Residual Learning for Generalized AI-Generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08674)
*Kutub Uddin,Nusrat Tasnim,Awais Khan,Mohammad Umar Farooq,Khalid Malik*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI生成图像（AIGI）日益逼真，传统检测方法难以应对多样化的生成方式和细微伪造痕迹，亟需更鲁棒、泛化能力强的检测框架。

Method: 采用神经张量网络构建生成残差学习框架，引入可学习注意力机制聚合多源变换样本的关系特征，并使用PE-Core作为通用特征提取器以增强跨域表现。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上，GenRes++显著优于现有方法，具备更强的泛化能力与对未知生成方法的检测性能。

Conclusion: GenRes++通过细粒度关系建模与可学习注意力机制，有效提升了对复杂、多样化AI生成图像的检测能力，为深度伪造内容识别提供了新思路。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of generative AI has enabled the creation of highly realistic deepfake media, posing significant threats, including misinformation, digital identity theft, fraud, and manipulation of public opinion. AI-generated image (AIGI) detection is reliably challenging due to the diversity of generative methods and the subtle artifacts they leave behind. In this work, we propose GenRes, a novel framework for generative residual learning via a neural tensor network, which models fine-grained relational features between original and transformed samples to enhance generalization. To address scenarios involving multiple generative transformations, we introduce GenRes++, which employs a learnable attention mechanism to aggregate relational features across multiple transformed samples and enables the model to focus on the most informative cues. Both models leverage PE-Core as a feature extractor, providing generalized and semantically rich embeddings that improve cross-domain performance and enable the detection of AIGI generated by unseen methods. Comprehensive experiments on multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed GenRes++ approach outperforms existing methods.

### [60] [Multi-Resolution Feature Stem for Diabetic Retinopathy lesion segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08679)
*Indranil Dutta,Taehee Jeong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了输入分辨率对糖尿病视网膜病变（DR）不同病灶类型分割性能的影响，发现提高分辨率虽有助于微动脉瘤等细小病灶的识别，却可能降低大出血病灶的检测效果，挑战了‘分辨率越高越好’的普遍假设。为此提出一种多分辨率特征茎（Multi-Resolution Feature Stem），与UNet++结合，在不增加参数量的前提下并行处理多尺度信息，有效解决分辨率带来的矛盾，显著提升整体分割性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 糖尿病视网膜病变（DR）是全球可预防性失明的主要原因，需依赖深度学习模型实现病灶自动分割以实现早期检测和监测。然而，DR病灶在尺寸上差异巨大，从微小的微动脉瘤到较大的出血和渗出物，这种多样性对模型架构和输入分辨率提出了相互冲突的要求，导致现有方法难以兼顾所有病灶类型。因此，亟需理解输入分辨率对不同类型病灶的影响，并设计能够平衡多尺度特征捕捉能力的高效架构。

Method: 通过系统实验对比U-Net、UNet++、Vision Transformers、DeepLabV3+等多种模型在512×512和1024×1024两种输入分辨率下的表现，分析分辨率变化对不同病灶类型的影响。在此基础上，提出一种多分辨率特征茎（Multi-Resolution Feature Stem），作为输入级金字塔结构，与UNet++主干网络集成，实现多尺度特征的并行提取与融合，从而同时保留细节信息和上下文语义。

Result: 实验结果显示，提高输入分辨率显著提升了微动脉瘤等细小病灶的分割精度，但反而降低了大出血病灶的检测性能，揭示了分辨率影响的非线性与矛盾性。所提出的多分辨率特征茎架构在保持参数效率的同时，成功缓解了这一权衡问题，在多个数据集上实现了优于基线模型的整体性能提升，尤其在多尺度病灶联合分割任务中表现突出。

Conclusion: 本研究首次揭示了输入分辨率对不同大小糖尿病视网膜病变病灶具有相反影响的反直觉现象，证明单纯提升分辨率并非万能解法。提出的多分辨率特征茎架构通过并行多尺度处理，有效解决了分辨率与细节之间的矛盾，为复杂医学图像分割任务提供了新的设计思路与实用方案。

Abstract: Diabetic Retinopathy (DR) is a leading cause of preventable blindness worldwide, requiring automated lesion segmentation using deep learning models for early detection and monitoring. However, DR lesions vary dramatically in size from tiny microaneurysms to large hemorrhages and exudates. This variability creates conflicting demands on the model architecture and input resolution, posing a challenge for effective design. This work investigates the impact of input resolution on different lesion types. Through systematic experimentation with multiple architectures (U-Net, UNet++, Vision Transformers, DeepLabV3+) at $512 \times 512$ and $1024 \times 1024$ resolutions, we identify a critical, counter-intuitive phenomenon where increasing input resolution has opposing effects on different lesion types. We demonstrate that while higher resolution is essential for resolving fine-grained microaneurysms, it can unexpectedly degrade performance on larger hemorrhages. This finding challenges the common assumption that higher resolution is uniformly beneficial. To address this, we propose a novel Multi-Resolution Feature Stem, an input-level pyramid integrated with a UNet++ backbone. This architecture processes multiple scales in parallel, capturing fine-grained details without sacrificing contextual information. This work contributes crucial empirical evidence of this complex, resolution-dependent behavior and a practical, parameter-efficient architecture that successfully resolves this trade-off.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在多目标场景中需重复处理每个目标，导致帧率下降且延迟随目标数无界增长，亟需一种高效、低延迟的多目标视频分割方案。

Abstract: Modern Video Object Segmentation (VOS) involves tracking and segmenting user-specified targets. While recent approaches have achieved remarkable performance in single-target scenarios, extending them to multi-target settings typically involves replicating the single-target processing for each individual object, resulting in reduced frame rates (FPS) with unbounded latency as target count increases. Built upon Segment Anything 2 (SAM2), we propose SAM-MT, which addresses this by transforming the model into an interactive framework for real-time Multi-Target video segmentation. SAM-MT uses explicit queries to represent different individual targets, in parallel with a shared representation for global context. It employs decoupled masked attention to keep individual identities distinct from cross-target interference, and sparse memory for stable temporal evolution, along with specialized strategies for occlusion handling and overlap prevention. SAM-MT successfully decouples latency from the number of targets, achieving real-time speed on par with single-target baselines (>36 FPS for 10 targets) while maintaining SAM2's robust video segmentation performance.

Extensive benchmarks using state-of-the-art traditional detectors and Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) demonstrate the significant challenges of zero-shot generalization and fine-grained reasoning on HumanForge. Code and dataset will be publicly released.

Conclusion: 本研究提出的多模态重建框架有效整合了旧有DEM与图像数据，通过物理驱动的对齐机制大幅降低计算开销，实现了高精度、实时的3D地形重建，为大规模野火灾害应急响应提供了可靠的技术支持。

Abstract: Accurate 3D terrain maps are essential for emergency response when assessing wildfire hazards. However, wildfire-prone regions often span vast areas where conventional reconstruction methods underperform. Image-based methods offer a lower-cost alternative, but struggle due to sparse visual features and limited image overlap. We propose a multi-modal reconstruction framework leveraging outdated Digital Elevation Models (DEMs) as geometric priors for image-based 3D reconstruction. Our key innovation is physics-based pixel-pixel alignment between images and DEM data, dramatically reducing computational complexity by eliminating expensive feature matching procedures. To validate our approach, we developed a large-terrain simulator based on a real wildfire-prone area, generating realistic images enabling a comprehensive evaluation. Given posed images and legacy DEMs, our method produces high-fidelity depth maps while maintaining real-time performance. We find significant improvements in reconstruction accuracy and computational efficiency over existing techniques, offering a scalable solution for wildfire response.

### [64] [Pose-to-Biomechanics: Bridging 3D Human Pose Estimation and Biomechanical Attribute Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08725)
*Ayda Eghbalian,Kevin Desai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出BioModule，一种轻量级、可插拔的时序变换器，可附加在任意3D姿态估计算法下游，从标准17关节3D骨骼中预测生物力学属性。该方法无需修改上游模型，实现视觉姿态估计与生物力学分析之间的无缝衔接。为训练和评估，构建了大规模对齐数据集Human3.6Mplus，实现视频、3D关键点与生物力学标签的帧级对齐监督。在7个先进姿态估计算法上进行基准测试，首次系统分析上游姿态精度如何影响下游生物力学预测性能。结果表明BioModule是高效、模块化的桥梁，推动运动分析向物理可解释方向发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D人体姿态估计算法主要优化几何关键点精度，但康复、运动科学、人因工程等实际应用需要描述身体运动、受力和激活状态的生物力学量。当前缺乏将通用姿态估计与生物力学分析有效结合的方法，亟需一种轻量、通用且可扩展的解决方案。

Method: 提出BioModule，一个时序变换器模块，作为下游组件连接到任何3D姿态估计算法后。该模块基于标准17关节3D骨骼输入，预测多种生物力学属性。通过构建并验证Human3.6M与Human3.6Mplus数据集间的解剖坐标对应关系，实现跨模态帧级监督。利用对齐数据训练模型，并保持对上游姿态估计器的无侵入性。

Result: BioModule在多个主流3D姿态估计算法上表现优异，实现了高精度的生物力学属性预测。实验揭示了上游姿态误差对下游生物力学预测的影响规律。该模块具备良好的泛化能力与轻量化特性，可即插即用，显著提升视觉姿态估计在真实应用场景中的物理可解释性。

Conclusion: BioModule提供了一种通用、高效的框架，使现有姿态估计算法能够输出具有生物力学意义的运动分析结果。其模块化设计与对上游算法的无侵入性，使其适用于广泛的实际应用，为计算机视觉与生物力学交叉研究提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Recent progress in 3D human pose estimation has made markerless recovery of skeletal motion increasingly accurate and scalable. However, most pose estimators remain optimized for geometric keypoint accuracy, while many real-world applications in rehabilitation, sports science, ergonomics, and clinical movement analysis require biomechanical quantities that describe how the body moves, loads, and activates. In this work, we propose BioModule, a lightweight plug-in temporal transformer that attaches downstream of any 3D pose estimator and predicts biomechanical attributes from standard 17-joint 3D skeletons. BioModule is estimator-agnostic and requires no modification of the upstream pose model, enabling existing pose estimators to be extended toward physically interpretable motion analysis.
  To train and evaluate BioModule, we construct a large-scale aligned dataset pairing Human3.6M video and 3D keypoints with the biomechanical label space of Human3.6Mplus. We establish and verify anatomical correspondence between coordinate systems of the two datasets, enabling frame-accurate cross-modal supervision. Using this aligned supervision, BioModule predicts biomechanical quantities. We further benchmark BioModule across seven state-of-the-art 3D pose estimators, providing the first systematic analysis of how upstream pose estimation quality propagates to downstream biomechanical prediction fidelity. The results position BioModule as a compact, modular bridge between vision-based pose estimation and biomechanically meaningful human motion analysis.

### [65] [WaspMOT: A Benchmark for Long-Term Multi-Object Tracking of Trichogramma Wasps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08729)
*Tomasz Stanczyk,Yuan Gao,Hardik Agarwal,Seongroo Yoon,Tiantao Zhang,Vincent Calcagno,Francois Bremond*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WaspMOT introduces a new benchmark for long-term multi-object tracking using 10 sequences of Trichogramma wasps, each ~12,000 frames (8 minutes at 25 FPS), with dense annotations and oracle detections. It focuses on identity preservation over extended durations, featuring a closed-set scenario with no exits, challenging tracking methods with occlusions, abrupt movements, and similar appearances. Five state-of-the-art trackers were evaluated under a unified protocol; all suffered from severe trajectory fragmentation even with perfect detections. A simple spatial stitching baseline improved results, suggesting room for improvement. The benchmark is publicly available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing MOT benchmarks are dominated by short video sequences that fail to evaluate long-term identity preservation. This limits the ability to assess tracking robustness over extended durations, especially in scenarios involving occlusions, appearance changes, and abrupt motions. WaspMOT addresses this gap by introducing a controlled ecological experiment with long-duration tracking of wasps, enabling evaluation of sustained identity consistency.

Method: WaspMOT constructs a benchmark using 10 long video sequences (~12,000 frames each) of Trichogramma wasps in controlled experiments. It provides dense MOTChallenge-style annotations and oracle detections to isolate association performance. The dataset features a closed-set setting where all individuals remain present throughout. Five tracking-by-detection methods (ByteTrack, BoT-SORT, C-BIoU, OC-SORT, McByte) are evaluated under a unified protocol. A spatial tracklet stitching baseline is introduced to assess potential improvements.

Result: All tested tracking methods exhibited significant trajectory fragmentation despite perfect detections, indicating major challenges in long-term association. The simple spatial tracklet stitching baseline consistently improved performance, demonstrating that substantial gains are still possible through better association strategies. Results highlight limitations of current approaches not visible on standard benchmarks.

Conclusion: WaspMOT establishes a new benchmark for long-term multi-object tracking, revealing critical shortcomings in existing methods when faced with prolonged tracking demands. The dataset enables deeper study of identity persistence and opens avenues for future research focused on robust long-term association.

Abstract: Multi-object tracking (MOT) has achieved strong performance on benchmarks dominated by short video sequences. However, such datasets do not adequately evaluate long-term identity preservation, where objects must be tracked consistently over extended durations. We introduce WaspMOT, a benchmark designed to address this gap through long-duration tracking of Trichogramma wasps in controlled ecological experiments. The dataset contains 10 sequences of approximately 12,000 frames each (over 8 minutes at 25 FPS), with dense MOTChallenge annotations and oracle detections to isolate association performance.
  Unlike existing benchmarks, WaspMOT forms a closed-set tracking scenario where all individuals remain present throughout the sequence, requiring consistent identity assignment across thousands of frames despite abrupt jumps, occlusions, and highly similar appearance. We establish a benchmark by evaluating five tracking-by-detection methods, including ByteTrack, BoT-SORT, C-BIoU, OC-SORT, and McByte, under a unified protocol. Results show that all methods suffer from significant trajectory fragmentation, highlighting the difficulty of long-term identity preservation even with perfect detections. A simple spatial tracklet stitching baseline consistently improves performance, indicating that substantial gains remain possible.
  WaspMOT provides a new benchmark for studying long-term association and reveals limitations of current tracking approaches that are not observable on conventional datasets. The benchmark will be made publicly available at the project repository: https://github.com/tstanczyk95/WaspMOT/ .

However, existing video generators are primarily trained on general video corpora, still lacking diverse supervision and dedicated designs for CoF reasoning. To address this gap, we introduce OpenCoF, a framework comprising the OpenCoF-17K dataset, a reasoning video dataset spanning 11 task families, and Wan-CoF, a fine-tuned video model for studying whether diverse temporal supervision improves CoF behavior. Across four video reasoning benchmarks, Wan-CoF achieves considerable gains over the Wan2.2-I2V-A14B baseline. Building on this, we empirically explore more advanced designs for CoF capabilities, i.e., equipping the model with visual and textual reasoning tokens. This mechanism respectively captures low-level visual cues and high-level semantic priors for spatial and temporal reasoning. Through performance comparisons and attention analysis, we examine how these tokens contribute across model depth, denoising steps, space, and time. Our results suggest that stronger video reasoning requires both broad temporal supervision and explicit mechanisms for organizing intermediate reasoning state. We open-source the dataset, model, and code to facilitate future research on reasoning-oriented video generation.

### [67] [Enhancing In-context Panoramic Generation via Geometric-aware Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08765)
*Haoran Feng,Ruiyang Zhang,Longyi Zhang,Dizhe Zhang,Lu Qi*

Main category: cs.CV

To address the lack of large-scale, high-quality training data tailored to in-context panoramic tasks, we propose Canvas360Dataset, a collection of 1M high-quality paired panoramic samples for style transfer, inpainting, outpainting, and editing, enabling effective supervision across diverse in-context generation scenarios. On the modeling side, Canvas360 enhances text-to-panorama generation through parallel depth generation, velocity circular padding, and similarity loss regularization, enabling the model to learn geometry-aware representations, capture object distortion details, and improve geometric consistency and global coherence. Furthermore, empowered by strong panoramic priors, Canvas360 enables a unified in-context panoramic generation framework that supports diverse downstream tasks via token-level concatenation, surpassing prior methods in both task coverage and modeling flexibility. Extensive experiments show that Canvas360 improves panoramic image fidelity, achieving particularly strong performance on the panorama-specific FAED metric and competitive or leading results across the reported quantitative evaluations. More information can be found on our project page: https://zry000.github.io/Canvas360/

</details>


### [68] [OPSD-V: On-Policy Self-Distillation for Post-Training Few-Step Autoregressive Video Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08766)
*Hongyu Liu,Chun Wang,Feng Gao,Xuanhua He,Yue Ma,Ziyu Wan,Yong Zhang,Xiaoming Wei,Qifeng Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OPSD-V是一种用于后训练少步自回归视频扩散模型的在线策略自蒸馏范式，通过引入真实长视频数据作为时间上下文，在不改变原有推理路径的前提下，提供密集的轨迹级监督，有效缓解了长序列生成中的误差累积和运动动态弱化问题。实验表明，该方法在视觉质量、运动动态和长视频评估指标上均有显著提升，并在用户偏好测试中获得66.0%的偏好率（剔除平局后达82.5%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少步自回归视频生成模型虽能实现低延迟长视频生成，但在长时间自回归推理过程中仍面临误差累积和运动动态减弱的问题，亟需一种无需改变原有推理机制即可提升生成质量的方法。

Method: OPSD-V采用在线策略自蒸馏框架，学生模型遵循与推理时一致的生成路径，每一步基于自身生成的键值缓存进行预测；教师模型则在同一去噪状态评估，但使用更清洁的自回归一致性时间缓存，其中旧的历史信息被真实视频内容替代，从而提供密集的去噪级别修正目标。

Result: 在Self-Forcing和LongLive等代表性模型上应用后，OPSD-V显著提升了视频视觉质量、运动动态连贯性及VBenchLong评分；用户研究显示，66.0%的判断偏好该方法，剔除平局后为82.5%。

Conclusion: OPSD-V通过引入真实长视频作为时间上下文，在保持原生推理效率的同时有效抑制了长序列生成中的质量退化，是一种高效且兼容性强的后训练优化方案。

Abstract: We propose OPSD-V, an on-policy self-distillation paradigm for post-training few-step autoregressive (AR) video diffusion models. Existing few-step AR video generators can produce long videos with low latency, but still suffer from error accumulation and weakened motion dynamics during long autoregressive rollout. OPSD-V reduces long-horizon degradation while preserving the original few-step inference path. The key idea is to introduce real long-video data as temporal context during training and use it to provide dense trajectory-level supervision. Specifically, the student follows the exact inference-time rollout, generating each chunk conditioned on its own previously generated KV cache. In parallel, the teacher is evaluated at the same student-visited denoising states, but uses a cleaner AR-consistent temporal cache in which older history can be replaced by real-video context. This provides dense denoising-level corrective targets under on-policy AR cache dynamics, without changing the sampler, number of denoising steps, or inference-time cache mechanism. We apply OPSD-V to representative few-step AR video models, including Self-Forcing and LongLive. Experiments show consistent improvements in visual quality, motion dynamics, and VBenchLong scores. A user study with 10 participants comparing 20 video pairs shows that OPSD-V is preferred over the base models in 66.0% of overall-preference judgments (82.5% excluding ties).

</details>


### [69] [Geometry and Gradient-based Partitioning for Panoramic Outdoor Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08769)
*Weijian Chen,Weibo Yao,Yuhang Zhang,Xiaolin Tang,Guo Wang,Weijun Zhang,Xitong Gao,Yihao Chen,Hongde Qin,Lu Qi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PanoLOG提出了一种针对大规模全景3D高斯溅射（3DGS）重建的两阶段粗到精框架，通过几何与梯度结合的分区策略，解决全景图像中全局可见性导致的传统局部分区失效问题。该方法在全局粗略阶段利用天空球建模和全景单目深度监督获取可靠几何，在细化阶段通过视差驱动的不确定性构建自适应包围体积，并基于梯度重要性评分分配相机。此外，作者构建了首个大规模全景室外场景数据集Pano360。实验表明，G$^2$PS在保持可扩展块并行训练的同时实现了最先进的渲染质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将3D高斯溅射扩展到大规模户外场景面临数据采集和计算成本高的挑战。使用全景图像虽能减少采集负担，但其全向视野导致传统依赖局部相机锥体的分区策略失效，使块级优化退化为全局训练，亟需新的分区机制以实现高效、可扩展的重建。

Method: 提出PanoLOG两阶段框架：第一阶段采用天空球建模与全景单目深度监督进行全局几何估计；第二阶段引入G$^2$PS策略，基于视差驱动的不确定性生成自适应边界框，并通过梯度重要性评分动态分配相机，实现高效且稳定的块级并行优化。

Result: 所提方法在多个大型全景场景上实现了先进的渲染质量，同时保持了良好的可扩展性和块并行训练效率。构建的Pano360数据集为后续研究提供了基准支持。

Conclusion: PanoLOG通过创新的几何-梯度联合分区策略，成功解决了大规模全景3DGS中的分区失效问题，显著提升了重建效率与质量，为未来大场景三维重建提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Scaling 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to large outdoor scenes is costly in both data acquisition and computation. Adopting panoramic images with equirectangular projection (ERP) can reduce capture effort via their full $360^{\circ}$ field of view, yet the resulting omnipresent visibility invalidates existing partitioning strategies that rely on local camera frustums, causing block-wise optimization to degenerate into global training. Thus, we propose PanoLOG, a two-stage coarse-to-fine framework equipped with a Geometry and Gradient-based Partitioning Strategy tailored for large-scale panoramic 3DGS reconstruction. In the global coarse stage, PanoLOG leverages sky-sphere modeling and panoramic monocular depth supervision for reliable geometry, while in the refinement stage, G$^2$PS builds adaptive bounding volumes via parallax-driven uncertainty and assigns cameras via gradient-based importance scoring. Furthermore, we construct Pano360, the first benchmark on large-scale panoramic dataset for outdoor scene reconstruction. Extensive experiments demonstrate that G$^2$PS achieves state-of-the-art rendering quality while maintaining scalable, block-parallel training. Our models, training code, and dataset are publicly available.

Conclusion: LongE2V通过融合预训练视频先验与创新模块设计，在事件流视频处理中实现了高质量、高稳定性和强泛化能力的表现，为未来事件相机应用提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Recovering high-quality video from sparse event streams is a challenging task. Regression methods often blur textures, while existing generative models struggle with long-term stability. We propose LongE2V, a novel approach that leverages pre-trained video diffusion priors to jointly handle event-based video reconstruction, prediction, and frame interpolation. By fine-tuning a foundational video model, our approach achieves high data efficiency and superior perceptual quality. We introduce Autoregressive Unrolling and Adaptive Context Switching to mitigate temporal drift in extremely long sequences. We also propose Reencoding Alignment with Cross Residual Correction to ensure precise bidirectional consistency during frame interpolation. Furthermore, Event Voxel Density Augmentation ensures robustness across varying sensor resolutions. Extensive experiments on real-world benchmarks demonstrate that LongE2V outperforms state-of-the-art methods across all three tasks, exhibiting exceptional temporal coherence and zero-shot generalization. ### [71] [ZipDepth: Bringing Lightweight Zero-Shot Monocular Depth Anywhere, on Any Device](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08771)
*Fabio Tosi,Luca Bartolomei,Matteo Poggi,Stefano Mattoccia*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ZipDepth 是一个轻量级的单目深度估计网络，通过高效可重参数化的编码器-解码器结构与大规模知识蒸馏技术，结合大范围多领域训练数据，实现了在嵌入式和移动设备上的实时运行。其仅 6.1M 参数，在五个基准测试中表现出色，零样本精度与部署效率之间的平衡优于现有轻量级模型，性能接近参数量大 50 倍的基础模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 ZipDepth 模型，采用高效的可重参数化编码器-解码器结构，并通过从大型基础模型进行大规模知识蒸馏，利用涵盖多个领域的广泛数据集进行训练，从而在保持极低参数量（6.1M）的同时实现高性能。

Result: ZipDepth 在五个基准测试中均达到当前轻量级模型中最佳的零样本精度与部署效率平衡，推理速度覆盖从服务器GPU到低功耗设备，性能接近参数量大50倍的基础模型，显著提升了轻量级模型在真实场景中的实用性。

Conclusion: ZipDepth 成功弥合了高性能基础模型与轻量级实用模型之间的差距，为在资源受限设备上实现高精度、强泛化能力的单目深度估计提供了有效解决方案，是迈向边缘智能的重要一步。

Abstract: Monocular depth estimation has seen remarkable progress through foundation models achieving robust zero-shot generalization, yet their computational demands place them far beyond the reach of embedded and mobile platforms. Lightweight alternatives exist, but have been developed almost exclusively within single-domain, self-supervised paradigms, failing silently under domain shift. We present ZipDepth, a compact monocular depth network that bridges this gap by combining an efficient reparameterizable encoder-decoder with large-scale knowledge distillation from a foundation model over a large multi-domain training set. Comprising just 6.1M parameters, ZipDepth runs at real-time rates from server GPUs to power-constrained devices, achieving the best trade-off between zero-shot accuracy and deployment efficiency among lightweight models across five benchmarks, taking a significant step towards the accuracy of foundation models with 50x more parameters.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水下环境中的3D几何估计面临光衰减、散射以及缺乏大规模高质量3D标注的挑战，而现有依赖密集标注的方法在水下不可行，因此需要一种无需标注水下数据的迁移学习方法。

Method: 采用教师-学生架构的跨域半监督学习框架，利用大量未标注的真实水下视频进行训练，并设计跨视图一致性损失以补偿因水体衰减和散射导致的信息损失，从而实现从空气到水下的3D重建模型迁移。

Conclusion: Wat3R成功实现了无需任何标注水下数据的跨域3D重建迁移，显著提升了水下几何估计性能，同时推动了水下视觉评估标准的发展。

Abstract: Estimating 3D geometry in underwater environments presents unique challenges due to light attenuation, scattering, and the absence of large-scale, high-quality 3D annotations. Pioneering methods rely on massive dense annotations that are impractical in underwater settings. In this paper, we propose Wat3R, a cross-domain semi-supervised learning framework designed to adapt feed-forward 3D reconstruction models from air to underwater scenes. Uniquely, our method eliminates the need for any annotated underwater data following a teacher-student architecture, that learns robust geometry representations merely on abundant unlabeled real underwater video footage. We also design a cross-view consistency loss that leverages geometric cues from other views to compensate for the information degradation in the current view caused by water attenuation and scattering. Furthermore, considering the lack of comprehensive evaluation benchmarks, we construct Water3D, a diverse dataset covering various water bodies and underwater scenarios, designed for geometric task evaluation. Experimental results demonstrate that Wat3R outperforms current state-of-the-art methods in underwater multi-view depth estimation and point cloud reconstruction. The dataset and code are available at https://github.com/LSXI7/Wat3R .

By spotting these emotions, machine learning models help improve public opinion interpretation and trend forecasting. This paper examines the effectiveness of various machine learning and deep learning approaches. Designed for this use, the system evaluates logistic regression, random forest, naïve bayes, gradient boosting, and LSTM networks, among other algorithms applied in sentiment classification. ### [75] [DeepSearch-World: Self-Distillation for Deep Search Agents in a Verifiable Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07820)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在训练网页代理时面临挑战：监督微调依赖固定教师轨迹，而稀疏奖励强化学习则提供弱监督信号，难以支持长时程任务中的有效学习。因此，亟需一种能实现自我进化且无需依赖更强大模型指导的训练机制。

Method: 提出 DeepSearch-Evolve 自蒸馏框架，基于可复现、可验证的 DeepSearch-World 环境，包含 420K 多跳问答任务，支持进度验证、基于事实的反思与失败恢复等认知行为。通过迭代式轨迹生成、筛选、数据混合与微调流程，实现代理的持续优化。

Result: DeepSearch-World-9B 在无外部蒸馏的情况下，取得与开源模型相当甚至更优的表现：在 BrowseComp 上达 31.2%，GAIA 上为 61.5%，HotpotQA 上高达 93.4%。证明可验证环境支持大规模自我演化。

Conclusion: 可验证的环境是实现长时程网页代理自我演进的关键，DeepSearch-Evolve 框架展示了无需依赖更强模型即可实现性能提升的可能性，为未来自主智能代理的研究提供了重要基础。

Abstract: Training tool-use agents to improve from their own experience remains challenging, as supervised fine-tuning relies on fixed teacher-distilled trajectories, while sparse-reward reinforcement learning provides weak supervision for long-horizon interactions. We present DeepSearch-Evolve, a self-distillation framework for web agents built on DeepSearch-World, a deterministic and verifiable environment with reproducible search and page-reading tools. DeepSearch-World contains 420K multi-hop QA tasks constructed from entity-level random walks and supports key agentic cognitive behaviors useful for self-evolving, including progress verification, grounded reflection, and failure recovery. DeepSearch-Evolve iteratively performs trajectory generation, filtering, data mixing, and fine-tuning to train stronger agents. Without distillation from more capable models, DeepSearch-World-9B achieves competitive performance compared with open-source agents, reaching 31.2% on BrowseComp, 61.5% on GAIA, and 93.4% on HotpotQA, showing that verifiable environments enable scalable self-evolution for long-horizon web agents. We will release the environment, 420K training pool, validation set, model, and code to facilitate future research on self-improving deep search agents.

### [76] [How Do I Know What to Say Next? Barenholtz's Autogenerative Theory as an Enrichment of Harrisean Integrationism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07891)
*J. Mark Bishop,Stephen J. Cowley*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出，Elan Barenholtz的自生成语言理论可填补Roy Harris整合主义语言学的解释空白，包括符号的前瞻性开放机制、语言与非语言符号活动之间的连续性，以及过往整合积累档案的结构属性。该理论在不违背整合主义核心主张的前提下，丰富了其内容，并为自然语言处理和大语言模型设计提供了原则性解释，揭示了统计结构的本质及其局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 整合主义语言学虽批判了语言作为映射现实的代码的传统观点，但未能充分解释符号如何维持前瞻性开放、语言与非语言符号活动的连续性，以及过去整合经验的积累结构。这些问题限制了其理论的完整性。

Method: 通过分析Barenholtz的自生成理论，将其与Harris的整合主义进行融合，论证其在结构性机制、语义连续性和档案理论方面的补充作用。

Result: 自生成理论成功填补了整合主义的三个关键解释空白：提供符号前瞻性开放的结构机制；建立语言与非语言符号活动的计算对应关系；构建对历史整合积累的理论描述。同时，该合成框架保持了整合主义对情境化整合行为的本体优先性。

Conclusion: 整合主义与自生成理论的结合，不仅增强了理论解释力，也为大语言模型的设计与理解提供了更深层的哲学与计算基础，明确了其统计结构的优势与根本局限。

Abstract: Roy Harris's Integrationist linguistics offers a compelling critique of the referentialist tradition embedded deep at the heart of computational approaches to language, arguing that language is not a code that maps onto a pre-given world but a situated, bipartite activity oriented toward prospective joint action. Yet Integrationism leaves certain explanatory gaps: it does not fully account for the structural mechanism by which signs sustain prospective openness, it undertheorises the continuity between linguistic and non-linguistic semiotic activity, and it offers no detailed account of the structural properties of the accumulated archive of past integrations. This paper argues that Elan Barenholtz's autogenerative theory of language, developed in response to the behaviour of Large Language Models (LLMs), can fill precisely these gaps, enriching Integrationism without undermining any of its core commitments. Specifically, the autogenerative account provides: a structural mechanism for the prospective openness that Harris identifies as central to bipartite communication; a computational correlate for Harris's thesis of semiotic continuity between language and other sign-making activity; and a theory of the archive: what the accumulated residue of past integrations looks like and how new participants draw upon it. The synthesis preserves Harris's ontological primacy of the situated integrative act while adding explanatory content that Integrationism itself does not supply. For practitioners and researchers in natural language processing and large language model design, the argument offers a principled account of what the statistical structure that LLMs so effectively exploit actually is, and of what it cannot, by its nature, provide.

### [78] [When Debiasing Backfires: Counterintuitive Side Effects of Preprocessing-Based Stereotype Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07937)
*Yahan Zheng,John Guerrerio,Soroush Vosoughi,Weicheng Ma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Preprocessing-based stereotype mitigation methods in NLP often cause unintended side effects, such as increased stereotyping or counter-stereotyping for underrepresented groups, even across unrelated demographics.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Experiments on two model families (encoder-only and decoder-only), multiple preprocessing strategies (removing stereotypical sentences, removing group mentions, swapping group references), and both pre- and post-training at different data scales using Wikipedia data; attention-rollout analysis to examine attention flow changes.

Standard benchmarks failed to detect these shifts. Attention-rollout analysis showed little change in attention patterns, making mechanistic explanations difficult.

Conclusion: Current preprocessing-based mitigation methods can inadvertently harm other demographic groups. Evaluation frameworks must account for side effects, and future practices should prioritize transparency and holistic impact assessment.

Abstract: Preprocessing-based methods for stereotype mitigation, such as pre-/post-training on debiased corpora, are widely used in NLP. While these approaches reduce measurable stereotypes for targeted groups, we find they often induce unintended shifts-side effects, where stereotyping or counter-stereotyping can increase relative to neutral baselines for other demographics, including across unrelated demographic categories. We demonstrate these side effects across two model families (encoder-only and decoder-only), multiple preprocessing strategies (removing stereotypical sentences, removing group mentions, and swapping group references), and both pre- and post-training at different data scales on Wikipedia. Standard benchmarks frequently miss these shifts. Using attention-rollout analysis, we observe that such side effects are not accompanied by large changes in attention flow, complicating mechanistic explanations. We discuss implications for evaluation, provide actionable diagnostics, and argue for side-effect-aware, transparent mitigation practices.

### [79] [A Multi-cluster Boundary Learning Method for Out-of-Scope Intent Detection via MiniLM Embedding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07974)
*Yihong Xu,Mingyu Kang,Linyuan Lü*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用MiniLM嵌入（all-MiniLM-L6-v2）在单类分类框架下进行多聚类边界学习。通过分析训练语句生成的多聚类嵌入，学习其边界特征，进而判断输入语句是否属于已知意图范围，从而实现对出域意图的识别。

Result: 在CLINC150、StackOverflow和Banking77三个公开数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在OOS意图检测任务中表现优于现有基线方法，达到当前最优水平。消融实验进一步验证了MiniLM嵌入在该流程中的良好适应性。

Conclusion: 所提出的多聚类边界学习方法结合MiniLM嵌入，在单类分类框架下实现了高效、准确的OOS意图检测，具备良好的实用性和可扩展性，为实际系统部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Intent detection is a critical task that bridges human intents and system actions in human-machine interaction systems. However, there still exist challenges for detecting out-of-scope (OOS) intents. (i) The traditional methods view the OOS intent detection as a multi-class classification, then the detection accuracy decreases as the class number of the known intents increases; (ii) LLM-embedding methods require large parameters, that makes them difficult to train and practically deploy. Thus, this work proposes a multi-cluster boundary learning method to detect OOS intents via MiniLM embedding (i.e., all-MiniLM-L6-v2) in an one-class classification workflow. The method learns the boundaries of multi-cluster embeddings generated by MiniLM from the training utterances, and then rejects the out-of-domain utterances as OOS intents. Experiments are conducted on public CLINC150, StackOverflow and Banking77 datasets. The results show that the method achieves the state-of-the-art OOS intent detection performance compared the other baselines. Ablation studies are also conducted and the results show that the used MiniLM can better adapt to the workflow and utterance embedding requirements. The code is available at supplementary materials.

### [80] [When Implausible Tokens Get Reinforced: Tail-Aware Credit Calibration for LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07976)
*Xiuyi Lou,Zicheng Xu,Yu-Neng Chuang,Hoang Anh Duy Le,Zhaozhuo Xu,Guanchu Wang,Vladimir Braverman*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TACO提出了一种新的信用校准方法，以解决强化学习中因均匀信用分配导致的错误推理行为被错误强化的问题。通过引入尾部风险评分来区分异常罕见与不确定性探索，对高风险令牌的正向信用进行抑制，从而在保留有用稀有模式的同时抑制偶然噪声，提升训练稳定性和长时程性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有批评者缺失的强化学习方法依赖于均匀信用分配，导致低概率但错误的尾部令牌与合理的令牌获得相同正向奖励，造成错误推理行为的误强化。

Method: TACO首先计算结合局部生成上下文的尾部风险评分，评估每个令牌落入不可靠尾部的风险；然后基于该评分调整正向信用，对高风险令牌减少正向更新，同时保留梯度，使有用的稀有模式得以积累强化，而随机噪声逐渐被抑制。

Result: 在三种大语言模型和八个基准测试上，TACO均显著优于GRPO类基线方法，且提升了训练稳定性，支持长时程强化学习中的持续性能提升。

Conclusion: TACO有效缓解了正向信用污染问题，通过尾部感知的信用校准机制，实现了更精准、稳定的推理能力增强，为大语言模型的强化学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has achieved remarkable success in enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, widely used critic-free RL methods rely on uniform credit assignment, broadcasting the same advantage to all tokens regardless of their differences. We identify a critical failure mode of this design, which we refer to as Positive-Credit Contamination: low-probability tail tokens that are contextually erroneous receive identical positive credit to plausible ones within the same trajectory, resulting in the indiscriminate reinforcement of flawed reasoning behavior. To mitigate this issue, we propose Tail-Aware Credit calibratiOn (TACO), a method that calibrates uniform credit assignment to suppress undesirable positive updates. TACO first computes a tail-risk score that incorporates the local generation context to assess each token's risk of falling into the unreliable tail, distinguishing unexpected rarity from uncertainty-driven exploration. TACO then uses this score to tune positive credit for risky tokens without removing their gradients entirely, so that recurring useful rare patterns can accumulate reinforcement while incidental noise is progressively dampened. Experimental results across three LLMs and eight benchmarks show that TACO consistently outperforms GRPO-style baselines. Notably, TACO improves training stability, supporting sustained performance gains in long-horizon RL. The source code is available at: https://github.com/xiuyilou/TACO.

</details>


### [81] [A Reliability Assessment of LALM Audio Judges for Full-Duplex Voice Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07985)
*A. Sayyad,J. Emmons,S. Jones,T. Lin,H. Krishnan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究评估了Gemini系列模型（2.5 Flash、3.5 Flash、3.1 Pro）作为音频评判者，在直接从原始立体声波形评分全双工对话任务中的实证可靠性。以Gemini 2.5 Flash为基准，与三位校准人类评分员在209个立体声会话上进行对比，涵盖8个生产维度，包括152个全双工对话和57个注入缺陷的对抗性片段。结果显示：（i）在8个维度中，有5个维度的LALM-人类斯皮尔曼等级相关系数与人类-人类相关系数差异不超过0.07，且7个维度的95%置信区间重叠；（ii）在6个维度中，LALM与三人平均评分的偏差在1分以内，覆盖率为60%至92%；（iii）在45/48个（缺陷，维度）组合中，LALM的敏感度不低于或优于人类，但多数为统计功效不足的零假设。模型间排名能力可迁移：3.5 Flash在所有8个维度上达成更高一致性，而3.1 Pro虽保持良好秩相关，但在部分维度评分显著低于人类。研究强调模型替换需重新校准，不可仅依赖秩相关性推断。研究识别出四个需谨慎部署的领域，并估算人类评分成本约为LALM工作的百倍。结论是，当证据支持时，可将LALM作为替代或第四位评分员部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估大型音频语言模型（LALM）作为自动音频评判工具的可靠性，以减少对高成本人类评分的依赖，提升评估效率，并验证其在多维度语音质量评估中的有效性与可替代性。

Method: 采用Gemini 2.5 Flash作为基准模型，与三位校准人类评分员在209个立体声会话上进行对比，涵盖152个全双工对话和57个缺陷注入片段，评估8个生产维度。通过斯皮尔曼等级相关系数、置信区间重叠、评分一致性、敏感度分析（Newcombe-Wilson置信区间）等方法进行量化比较。进一步测试其他两个模型（3.5 Flash和3.1 Pro）的性能，评估其在不同维度上的表现及跨模型迁移能力。

Result: Gemini 2.5 Flash在多数维度上表现出与人类评分高度一致的性能：5个维度的LALM-人类相关性差异小于0.07，7个维度的95%置信区间重叠；6个维度中，LALM与人类均值的评分偏差在1点内，覆盖率达60%-92%；45/48个（缺陷，维度）单元中，LALM敏感度不低于或优于人类。3.5 Flash在所有8个维度上实现完全一致性；3.1 Pro虽有良好秩相关性，但部分维度评分显著偏低。研究证实人类评分成本约为LALM的百倍，表明使用LALM具有显著经济优势。

Conclusion: 在证据支持的维度上，可合理将大型音频语言模型（如Gemini 2.5 Flash）作为人类评分的替代或补充（第四位评分员）。然而，模型更换必须重新校准，不能仅依赖秩相关性推断。研究识别出四个需谨慎部署的场景，并证明自动化评分在效率与成本方面具有压倒性优势。

Abstract: We report the empirical reliability of Gemini models as audio judges that score full-duplex agent conversations directly from the raw stereo waveform, tested across three models in the Gemini family: 2.5 Flash, 3.5 Flash, and 3.1 Pro. Our primary evidence base uses Gemini 2.5 Flash as the ground-truth model, validated against three calibrated human raters on 209 stereo sessions, scored on 8 production dimensions: 152 full-duplex conversations across 13 accent-and-condition strata, together with 57 adversarial defect-injected clips. The evidence for Gemini 2.5 Flash is consistent across three tests. (i) On 5 of 8 dimensions the LALM-human Spearman rho departs from the pairwise human-human rho by at most 0.07, and on 7 of 8 dimensions the two quantities 95 percent bootstrap confidence intervals overlap. (ii) The LALM agrees with the three-rater human mean within 1 point on 60 to 92 percent of sessions on 6 of 8 dimensions. (iii) On 45 of 48 (defect, dimension) cells the LALM is as sensitive as humans or better under Newcombe-Wilson 95 percent confidence intervals, though most of these are underpowered nulls rather than demonstrated parity. Rank-ordering ability transfers across the Gemini family: 3.5 Flash improves simple agreement to 8 of 8 dimensions, while 3.1 Pro rates several dimensions markedly lower than humans despite comparable rank correlation. A model swap should be re-validated on calibration specifically, not assumed from rank-correlation alone. We identify four areas where deployment requires care, and we estimate that human rating alone for our current evaluation cadence costs roughly two orders of magnitude more than the equivalent LALM workload. The data presented here provides a defensible empirical basis for deploying the LALM as a substitute or fourth rater on the dimensions where the evidence supports it.

### [82] [Hallucination Self-Play: Bootstrapping Reinforced Detector via Evolved Generator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07993)
*Shiping Yang,Shining Liang,Weihao Liu,Wenbiao Ding,Linjun Shou,Lu Cheng,Angel X. Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Hallucination Self-Play（HSP）框架，通过迭代优化检测器与生成器，实现无需外部监督的幻觉检测能力提升，使小型语言模型性能媲美甚至超越大型语言模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖静态生成器合成训练数据，无法实现检测器的持续改进，且高质量标注数据稀缺，限制了幻觉检测的准确性与鲁棒性。

Method: HSP框架初始化两个角色：检测器与生成器，均源自同一基础模型。检测器先在人工标注数据上微调，再作为奖励模型，通过基于AI反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）训练生成器；生成器生成更具挑战性的幻觉样本，用于规则强化学习以进一步优化检测器，形成自进化闭环。

Result: 在RAGTruth基准及两个模型家族上的实验表明，该框架可逐步提升小规模语言模型的幻觉检测能力，使其性能达到或超过先进大模型水平，且无需外部监督。

Conclusion: HSP框架通过动态迭代的生成-检测循环，实现了幻觉检测系统的自我增强，为低资源环境下的高精度幻觉识别提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Identifying faithfulness hallucinations in LLM-generated outputs remains challenging due to the scarcity of high-quality annotated data. Recent work relies on advanced LLMs to synthesize training data, including rationales, labels, and hallucinated claims. However, these methods treat the generator as a static component, limiting iterative improvement of the detector. To address this limitation, we introduce Hallucination Self-Play (HSP), a novel framework that enables the detector to bootstrap with an evolved generator. HSP involves two roles initialized from the same base model, a detector that assesses the faithfulness of model outputs, and a generator that produces increasingly hard-to-detect hallucinated responses. Specifically, the detector is first fine-tuned on human-labeled data and then employed as a reward model to train the generator via reinforcement learning from AI feedback (RLAIF). In turn, the evolved generator synthesizes hallucination data to further optimize the detector through rule-based reinforcement learning. Experiments on RAGTruth benchmark and two model families demonstrate that the proposed framework can progressively enhance a small LLM to match or even outperform advanced LLMs without external supervision. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Hallucination-Self-Play-50B5 .

</details>


### [83] [From Execution to Education: A Bloom-Aligned Framework for Measuring Educational Control in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08009)
*Yi Zhang,Julia Rayz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于布卢姆分类学的框架，用于衡量大语言模型在教育任务中的控制能力，即在调整认知需求的同时保持教学意图。研究聚焦于计算机科学教育中的编程任务，比较了通用模型与代码专用模型在提升和降低任务难度、以及针对不同布卢姆层级的控制表现。结果发现，模型能有效提高认知需求，但难以降低；通用模型在中间层对任务难度和布卢姆控制的区分更明显，而代码模型在布卢姆控制上表现出更深的特征峰值。表明强大的执行能力并不等同于教育目标对齐的认知调控能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在教育应用中虽能完成任务，但缺乏对认知需求的精准控制，尤其在适应学习者水平方面存在不足。为实现真正意义上的教育适配，需要一种可量化、可操作的评估框架来衡量模型是否能按教学目标调整任务认知层次。

Method: 基于修订版布卢姆分类学构建认知需求操作化量表，设计两种干预场景：一般难度控制（提升或降低任务难易）与布卢姆层级控制（指向更高或更低认知层级）。使用匹配的Qwen3-Next-80B-A3B-Instruct与Qwen3-Coder-Next模型，在三个基准数据集共2520个编程任务上进行评估，并通过语义差分聚类与层间费雪判别比探针分析模型内部表示差异。

Result: 模型在增加认知需求时表现稳定，但在降低认知需求时效果显著不足，呈现明显的方向性不对称。通用模型在中间层对两类控制均有较好区分能力；代码模型在一般难度控制上区分度弱，但在布卢姆控制上出现更深的层内特征峰值，暗示其对高阶认知任务的敏感性更强。

Conclusion: 强大的任务执行能力并不能自动转化为符合布卢姆教育目标的认知调控能力。教育导向的模型设计需超越单纯性能优化，引入对认知层次精确控制的机制，以实现真正的个性化学习支持。

Abstract: We introduce a Bloom-aligned framework for measuring educational control in Large Language Models (LLMs): the ability to preserve a task's instructional intent while shifting its cognitive demand toward specified learning objectives. We apply this framework to programming tasks in computer science education to study the gap between solving tasks and adapting them for learners. Using revised Bloom's Taxonomy as an operational scale of cognitive demand, we evaluate two intervention settings: general difficulty control, where models are asked to make tasks harder or easier, and Bloom's control, where models are asked to target higher or lower Bloom's levels. We evaluate a matched Qwen3-Next model pair, comparing Qwen3-Next-80B-A3B-Instruct with Qwen3-Coder-Next across 2,520 tasks from three benchmarks. The framework reveals a robust directional asymmetry: both models reliably increase cognitive demand, but struggle to lower it. We further characterize these outcomes with semantic-delta clustering and layer-wise Fisher's Discriminant Ratio probing. Within this controlled comparison, the general model shows clearer middle-layer separability for both general difficulty and Bloom-control contrasts, whereas the coder model shows weaker separability for general difficulty and a deeper peak for Bloom-control contrasts. These results show that strong execution performance does not automatically entail Bloom-aligned educational control.

### [84] [Tool-Making and Self-Evolving LLM Agents in Low-Latency Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08010)
*Kalle Kujanpää,Ning Liu,Shahnawaz Alam,Yeshwanth Reddy Sura,Tianyu Yang,Kristina Klinkner,Shervin Malmasi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种代理工具生成管道，将重复的步骤编译为部署前已验证、版本化的工具，以减少生产环境中大语言模型代理的延迟和不可靠性。通过在运行时直接调用工具并仅在必要时回退到代码生成，显著提升了性能与可靠性。在实际应用中，工具调用使中位数延迟降低42%，错误率最多降低53%。此外，结构化输出简化了架构，进一步降低62%延迟，并增强可审计性与对数据漂移的检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生产环境中的大语言模型代理在每次请求时重复生成相同流程代码，导致延迟高且结果不稳定。需要一种方法来减少冗余计算，提升系统效率与可靠性。

Method: 构建一个代理工具生成管道，在部署前将重复的操作步骤（SOP）编译为已验证、版本化的工具；该过程基于实时执行轨迹、后端模式和值进行合成，生成候选工具并利用标注案例进行修复；运行时代理直接调用工具，仅在必要时才回退至代码生成。

Result: 在真实部署的警报诊断系统中，工具调用使中位数延迟降低42%，历史数据测试显示端到端错误率最高下降53%；结构化工具输出支持更简单的直接调用架构，进一步降低62%延迟；同时提升可审计性，揭示规范漏洞与上游数据漂移问题。

Conclusion: 自演化代理通过预编译工具可显著提升工业级大语言模型系统的速度、可靠性和可运维性，是实现高效、稳定生产的有效路径。

Abstract: Production LLM agents often waste latency and reliability by regenerating code for the same procedural steps on every request. We replace this inference-time coding loop with an agentic tool-making pipeline that compiles repeated SOP steps into validated, versioned tools before deployment. The tool-maker grounds synthesis in the live environment as it collects execution traces, observes backend schemas and values, generates candidate tools, and repairs them against labeled cases. At runtime, the production agent calls these tools directly and falls back to code generation only when needed. We deploy the approach in a Fulfillment Center alarm-triage system, where an agent diagnoses alarms against a 44-node SOP over heterogeneous metric backends. In production, tool calls reduce p50 latency by 42%. On 1,500 historical alarms, they reduce end-to-end error rate by up to 53% by suppressing run-to-run variance in repeated steps. Because tools return compact structured verdicts, they also enable a simpler direct-call architecture, reducing p50 latency by a further 62% in a controlled ablation. Versioned tools also improve auditability and expose specification gaps and upstream data drift. Our results show that self-evolving agents can make industrial LLM systems faster, more reliable, and easier to operate.
