### [117] [Towards the Explainability of Temporal Graph Networks via Memory Backtracking and Topological Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07716)
*Yazheng Liu,Xi Zhang,Sihong Xie,Hui Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于时间图网络（TGNs）的解释方法，通过拓扑归因树和记忆回溯树来追踪历史事件对模型预测的影响。该方法结合LRP确保事件贡献总和等于模型输出的logits，并设计优化目标以克服top-k选择在非线性映射下的不准确性。在九个时间图数据集上的实验表明，该方法能提供忠实且优于现有基线的解释结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有解释方法忽视了TGN中的记忆模块，而该模块是记录和更新节点历史的核心组件，因此无法全面理解历史事件对预测的影响。

Method: 提出拓扑归因树以捕捉邻居及其记忆向量的影响，再通过记忆回溯树量化历史事件如何塑造节点记忆向量；采用LRP保证事件贡献总和等于模型logits，并设计优化目标识别关键事件。

Result: 在九个时间图数据集上，所提方法在节点属性预测、链接预测和图分类任务中均实现了更忠实的解释效果，显著优于现有先进方法。

Conclusion: 本文方法有效揭示了历史事件对TGN预测的影响，增强了模型可解释性和可信度，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Temporal graphs are ubiquitous in real-world applications and Temporal Graph Networks (TGNs) have achieved superior predictive accuracy. Understanding which historical events drive model predictions can enhance trustworthiness of TGNs. Existing explanation methods overlook the memory module, the core component that records and updates node histories, leaving the influence of past events unexplored. To address this, we attribute TGNs predictions through the topology attribution tree and memory backtracking tree. The topology attribution tree captures the influence of neighbors and their memory vectors, then the memory backtracking tree quantifies how historical events shape node memory vectors. We apply the LRP in TGNs, ensuring that the total contribution of events equals the logits of model. Finally, top-k selection may be unfaithful due to the nonlinear mapping from logits to probabilities, we design optimization objectives to identify the important events. Experiments on nine temporal graph datasets, spanning node property prediction, link prediction tasks and graph classification tasks, show that our method provides faithful explanations and outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. The code is available at https://github.com/yazhengliu/MemExplainer

</details>


### [118] [Who Gets Missed in the Tail? Thresholded Subgroup Underdiagnosis in Long-Tailed Chest X-ray Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07717)
*Ha-Hieu Pham,Hai-Dang Nguyen,Dang P. M. Cao,Thanh-Huy Nguyen,Min Xu,Trung-Nghia Le,Ulas Bagci,Huy-Hieu Pham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究胸部X光（CXR）分类中长尾分布导致的罕见阳性患者漏诊问题，提出通过诊断阶梯分析类别级长尾损失、子群感知加权、群体鲁棒性与阈值选择。在VinDr-CXR和MIMIC-CXR/CXR-LT数据集上，采用组尾加权与尾部感知阈值化方法显著降低尾部FNR（从0.665降至0.269），性别和年龄最差群体的FNR也大幅下降，同时宏观mAP略有提升。但在MIMIC-CXR/CXR-LT上仍存在较高的残余漏诊率。配对引导对比验证了阈值优化效果，而GroupDRO实验表明仅提升整体群体鲁棒性无法消除罕见子群漏诊。结论指出：罕见标签公平性依赖于病灶类型、子群属性与操作阈值的共同作用，而非仅由标签频率或排序指标决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在胸部X光分类任务中，尽管模型整体排名性能良好，但罕见阳性患者仍可能因长尾分布问题被遗漏，尤其在特定子群中。该问题在部署前评估阶段影响公平性，亟需系统性审计机制来识别并缓解此类漏诊风险。

Method: 提出诊断阶梯框架，分解长尾损失、引入子群感知权重、设计尾部感知阈值策略，并结合配对Bootstrap对比与GroupDRO基准进行验证。

Result: 在VinDr-CXR上，尾部FNR从0.665降至0.269，性别最差组FNR从0.705降至0.157，年龄最差组从0.822降至0.133，宏-mAP从0.611升至0.635；在MIMIC-CXR/CXR-LT上尾部FNR从0.866降至0.741，各子群最差组FNR均下降，但仍有较高残余漏诊率。

Conclusion: 罕见标签的公平性不能仅通过标签频率或排序性能衡量，而是由病灶类型、子群特征与操作阈值共同决定，需联合优化三者以实现真正公平的临床决策支持。

Abstract: In chest X-ray (CXR) classification, acceptable ranking performance can still leave rare-positive patients below threshold, especially within subgroups. We study this pre-deployment fairness problem as an audit question: after a long-tailed multi-label CXR model is converted from scores into decisions, who is missed? Across VinDr-CXR and MIMIC-CXR/CXR-LT, we use a diagnostic ladder to separate class-level long-tail losses, subgroup-aware weighting, group robustness, and threshold selection. On VinDr-CXR, group-tail weighting followed by tail-aware thresholding reduces tail FNR from 0.665 to 0.269, sex worst-group FNR from 0.705 to 0.157, and age worst-group FNR from 0.822 to 0.133, while macro-mAP increases from 0.611 to 0.635. On MIMIC-CXR/CXR-LT, the same score-to-threshold comparison reduces tail FNR from 0.866 to 0.741 and lowers worst-group FNR across sex, age, race, and insurance; residual missed-positive rates nevertheless remain high. Paired bootstrap contrasts on VinDr support the thresholded FNR reductions, and GroupDRO reference runs indicate that aggregate group robustness alone does not remove rare subgroup misses in this setting. The study supports a narrow audit claim: rare-label fairness in CXR depends jointly on the finding, subgroup, and operating threshold, not on label frequency or ranking metrics alone.

</details>


### [119] [LLT: Local Linear Transformer for PDE Operator Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07718)
*Oded Ovadia,Eli Turkel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为局部线性Transformer（LLT）的新神经算子，用于解决偏微分方程（PDE）的求解映射学习问题。该方法结合了线性全局注意力与局部空间混合，并引入坐标和几何信息，有效克服了传统Transformer在计算复杂度和局部交互建模上的局限性。在弹性、塑性、机翼流、管道流、达西流等多类PDE问题上进行了评估，涵盖多种数值离散化方式与结构/非结构网格。实验表明，LLT在精度和计算效率方面均优于或媲美现有神经算子与Transformer基线方法，训练迭代时间加速1.8至2.5倍；且成功扩展至包含32,186个非结构网格点的三维汽车气动数据集，展现了良好的可扩展性与通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准注意力机制在应用于偏微分方程（PDE）求解时存在两个主要问题：一是计算复杂度随节点数呈二次增长，二是缺乏对局部物理交互的显式建模偏好。这限制了其在大规模、复杂几何场景下的应用效率与准确性。因此需要一种兼具高效性与物理一致性的人工智能框架来学习PDE解映射。

Method: 提出局部线性Transformer（LLT），其核心结构包括：1）线性全局注意力模块，以降低计算复杂度；2）局部空间混合模块，显式建模邻域交互；3）嵌入坐标与几何信息的输入表示，增强模型对空间结构的理解能力。整体架构兼顾长距离依赖捕捉与局部物理规律遵循。

Result: LLT在多个典型PDE问题（如弹性、塑性、空气动力学、管道流动、达西流）上表现出色，相对L2误差低于或接近现有最优方法。在相同结构化网格条件下，每轮训练耗时减少1.8至2.5倍，相较于Transolver显著提升效率。此外，在包含32,186个非结构网格点的三维汽车气动数据集上成功部署，验证了其在高维、复杂网格下的可扩展性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: LLT是一种高效且准确的神经算子，适用于不同离散方式、网格类型及问题设置下的PDE求解。它通过融合线性注意力与局部混合机制，有效平衡了计算效率与物理一致性，为加速科学计算提供了强有力的新工具。

Abstract: Neural operators have become a common approach for learning PDE solution maps and accelerating numerical simulations. Transformer-based neural operators are of particular interest, since attention can learn long-range dependencies in the computational domain. However, standard attention has two major limitations when applied to PDEs: it scales quadratically with the number of computational nodes, and it lacks an explicit bias toward local interactions. To address these issues, we introduce Local Linear Transformer (LLT) for PDE operator learning. The architecture combines linear global attention with local spatial mixing, and incorporates coordinate and geometry information. We evaluate LLT on several PDE problems, including elasticity, plasticity, airfoil flow, pipe flow, and Darcy flow. The reference data for these problems span finite-element, finite-volume, and finite-difference discretizations on structured and unstructured meshes. Compared with other neural-operator and transformer baselines from prior studies, LLT achieves competitive or lower relative $L_2$ error across these problems. On matched structured discretizations, wall-clock time per training iteration is reduced by factors of 1.8 to 2.5 relative to Transolver. We also scale the approach and apply it to a three-dimensional car aerodynamics dataset with 32,186 unstructured mesh points per sample. Together, these results indicate that LLT provides an accurate and computationally efficient operator for PDE problems across discretizations, mesh types, and problem settings.

</details>


### [120] [ReCoLoRA: Spectrum-Aware Recursive Consolidation for Continual LLM Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07719)
*Wentao Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ReCoLoRA 是一种谱感知的持续微调框架，通过递归整合低秩适配器来缓解任务间遗忘问题。它基于随机SVD初始化适配器，每层使用肘部法则选择有效秩，并优先适应主子空间，再开放残差容量。在每次新任务前，重新分解当前有效权重，而非原始权重，使模型从已吸收前序任务的状态开始。在六个任务的持续GLUE序列上，ReCoLoRA在四个7-8B模型中三个取得最佳平均得分，同时训练参数更少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LoRA-style方法在持续微调中因不断叠加低秩更新导致任务间遗忘，即新任务覆盖旧任务的知识。如何在保持参数效率的同时实现稳定、可累积的学习是核心挑战。

Method: ReCoLoRA采用谱感知策略：1）基于随机SVD初始化适配器；2）使用肘部法则确定每层有效秩；3）优先更新主子空间，再启用残差容量；4）在每个新任务前，对当前有效权重进行递归重分解，生成冻结残差、缓慢更新的主成分和全新适配器。

Result: 在六任务持续GLUE任务序列上，ReCoLoRA在四个7-8B大模型中的三个上优于LoRA、PiSSA、AdaLoRA和DoRA基线，且训练参数更少；其基于最优路由的任务库变体作为全任务隔离的上限基准。

Conclusion: ReCoLoRA通过递归整合机制实现了高效且稳定的持续微调，在保持低参数量的同时显著提升多任务学习性能，为参数高效持续学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning adapts a large language model to one task cheaply, but across a task sequence LoRA-style methods keep stacking low-rank updates on the same frozen weight, so each new task tends to overwrite the previous ones. We present ReCoLoRA (Recursive Consolidation of Low-Rank Adapters), a spectrum-aware framework for continual fine-tuning: adapters are initialized from a randomized SVD of the pretrained weight, per-layer effective ranks are selected by an elbow criterion, and the principal subspace is adapted before residual capacity is opened. Before each new task, ReCoLoRA re-decomposes the current effective weight, rather than the original one, into a frozen residual, a slowly updated principal component, and a fresh adapter (recursive consolidation), so every task starts from the model that has already absorbed its predecessors. On a six-task continual GLUE sequence over four 7-8B backbones, ReCoLoRA attains the best final average score on three of the four backbones against rank-swept LoRA, PiSSA, AdaLoRA, and DoRA baselines while training fewer parameters; an oracle-routed task-bank variant serves as an upper bound under full task isolation. Code: https://github.com/bhqy666/ReCoLoRA.

</details>


### [121] [Omni-Sleep: A Sleep Foundation Model via Hierarchical Contrastive Learning of CNS--ANS Dynamic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07720)
*Zhoujie Hou,Song Wang,Kexin Lou,Mo Wang,Chen Wei,Quanying Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Omni-Sleep 是一个基于中枢神经系统（CNS）与自主神经系统（ANS）生理结构先验的睡眠基础模型，通过拓扑约束表示学习，利用多模态睡眠数据（如EEG、ECG、呼吸等）进行结构化表征。其核心方法包括系统内一致性、系统间同步性以及潜在空间的掩码时序建模，以捕捉脑-体动态和长时程睡眠规律。在超过10万小时的多中心数据上预训练后，该模型在睡眠分期和多疾病分类任务中表现优异，具备更强的标签效率、跨数据集泛化能力及对缺失模态的鲁棒性，验证了生理层次结构在可泛化睡眠表征学习中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有睡眠基础模型通常以拓扑无关的方式融合异构生物信号，忽略了神经与自主神经系统之间的生理组织结构，导致表征学习缺乏生物学意义。因此，需要引入生理先验来提升模型的可解释性和泛化能力。

Method: Omni-Sleep 采用 CNS/ANS 分区作为生理先验，设计三种学习目标：1）系统内一致性，提取神经与心肺信号中的共享子系统因子；2）系统间同步性，对齐不同系统的子系统轨迹以建模脑-体动态；3）潜在空间的掩码时序建模，捕捉长期睡眠动态。模型在大规模多中心多模态睡眠图谱数据上预训练。

Result: Omni-Sleep 在多个数据集和模态缺失设置下均优于现有强基线模型，表现出更高的标签效率、更强的跨数据集泛化能力以及对缺失模态的鲁棒性，证明了生理层次结构对于构建通用且稳健的睡眠表征学习至关重要。

Conclusion: 将生理组织结构（如CNS/ANS分区）作为先验信息融入模型设计，能够有效促进睡眠表征学习的结构化、可解释性和泛化性能，为未来智能睡眠分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: Sleep physiology arises from the coordinated dynamics of the central nervous system (CNS) and autonomic nervous system (ANS), as reflected by multimodal polysomnography signals including EEG, EOG, EMG, ECG, and respiration. However, existing sleep foundation models often fuse heterogeneous biosignals in a topology-agnostic manner, overlooking their physiological organization. We introduce Omni-Sleep, a sleep foundation model that uses the CNS/ANS partition as a physiological prior for topology-constrained representation learning. Omni-Sleep learns structured representations through three objectives: intra-system consistency, which captures shared subsystem-level factors within neural and cardio-respiratory signals; inter-system synchronization, which aligns subsystem trajectories to model brain--body dynamics; and latent-space masked temporal modeling, which captures long-horizon sleep dynamics. Pre-trained on over 100,000 hours of multi-center multimodal PSG data, Omni-Sleep is evaluated on sleep staging and multi-disease classification. Across datasets and modality-ablation settings, Omni-Sleep outperforms strong foundation-model baselines, showing improved label efficiency, cross-dataset generalization, and robustness to missing modalities. These results highlight the value of physiological hierarchy for generalizable sleep representation learning. Code is available at https://github.com/AutoBrain-sleep/OmniSleep.

</details>


### [122] [Uncertainty-gated selection for block-sparse attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07724)
*Thomas Rossi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于信息价值的路由机制，用于改进块稀疏注意力（Block-sparse attention）中因贪心选择前k个关键块而导致的信息丢失问题。该方法通过评估每个查询的顶部k选择的确定性，对置信度低的查询扩大保留块数量，从而显著提升召回率。在LongBench-v2中，该方法相比传统top-k策略提升28个百分点（p<0.01），接近密集注意力性能，并在多个模型和长上下文场景下保持高效运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统块稀疏注意力采用贪心的top-k选择，当第k个与第(k+1)个块得分相近时，会错误丢弃可能包含重要答案证据的块，且无法恢复，导致信息损失。需要一种更智能的机制来判断是否应保留更多候选块。

Method: 设计了一个值-信息（value-of-information）路由器，评估每个查询的前k选择的决策置信度（即得分差距），对得分差距最小（最不确定）的查询，将其保留块数加倍；该方法与现有块评分方法如Quest兼容，可无缝集成。

Result: 在LongBench-v2 medium数据集上，router-on-Quest实现配对召回率0.75，相较top-k基线（0.47）提升28个百分点（p<0.01）；在128K上下文长度下，Qwen2.5-7B-1M和Qwen3.6分别保持了0.81和0.89的稠密注意力精度，而计算效率分别为0.62x和0.80x稠密运行时间。

Conclusion: 所提出的值-信息路由器能够有效缓解块稀疏注意力中的信息丢失问题，显著提升长上下文建模能力，同时保持较高的计算效率，适用于多种模型架构。

Abstract: Block-sparse attention scales long-context language models by replacing the O(N^2) softmax with a per-query top-k selection over key blocks. This cutoff is myopic: when the k-th and (k+1)-th blocks are nearly tied in score, the selector commits without spending extra budget, and a dropped block carrying answer evidence is unrecoverable downstream. We propose a value-of-information router that measures, for each query, how decisively the top-k cut was made, and doubles the kept set for the queries where that gap is smallest; the rule is backbone-agnostic and stacks with existing block-scoring methods such as Quest. On LongBench-v2 medium at n=215 (the entire dataset subset), router-on-Quest reaches paired recall 0.75 vs. top-k 0.47 -- +28 pp over the SSA-style baseline (McNemar p<0.01) -- and lands within 2 pp of dense on RULER NIAH multikey at the same context. The lift reproduces on four models from three architectures (Qwen2.5, Mistral-Nemo, Qwen3.6). At 128K, the router preserves 0.81 and 0.89 of dense accuracy on Qwen2.5-7B-1M and Qwen3.6 (vs. SSA-style top-k at 0.09 on the former) while the fused selection-plus-kernel pipeline runs at 0.62x and 0.80x dense wall time.

</details>


### [123] [SHIFT: Survival Prediction from Incomplete and Heterogeneous Genomic Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07725)
*Muhammet Sami Yavuz,Ayhan Can Erdur,Sabri Mustafa Kahya,Benedikt Wiestler,Jana Lipkova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SHIFT 是一种针对基因组数据中缺失特征的生存预测模型，通过自注意力机制和特征可用性掩码，在不进行测试时插补的情况下直接从不完整基因组输入中进行预测。该方法在胶质母细胞瘤和肺鳞状细胞癌的多中心数据上表现出良好的泛化能力，优于传统基线和基于插补的方法，并能统一处理不同特征集。此外，训练时纳入部分观测数据可提升外部验证性能，表明不完整队列可被用于模型构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基因组预测模型在跨机构迁移时因测序面板差异导致特征结构缺失，现有方法如限制共享基因、排除不完整患者或依赖测试时插补，均会降低鲁棒性并限制多中心数据利用。因此需要一种能直接处理不完整输入的模型。

Method: 提出 SHIFT 模型，采用单独表示每个基因组特征，结合掩码自注意力与特征可用性掩码，确保预测仅基于观测到的输入；训练时引入可变率特征掩码以增强对异质缺失模式的鲁棒性。

Result: SHIFT 在多个队列（包括严重跨队列面板不匹配）中表现出强泛化能力，优于标准生存基线和插补方法，且使用单一模型处理不同特征集；训练时包含不完整队列可提升外部性能。

Conclusion: 缺失感知建模是精准肿瘤学中多中心生存预测的一种实用策略，能够有效利用不完整但有价值的多中心数据。

Abstract: Genomic prediction models often fail to transfer across institutions because sequencing panels differ across sites, creating structural feature missingness at deployment. Existing approaches to this challenge typically restrict analysis to genes shared across cohorts, exclude patients with incomplete profiles, or rely on test-time imputation, all of which can reduce robustness and limit the use of multi-center data. We propose Survival prediction Handling Incomplete Features using Transformer (SHIFT), a missingness-aware survival model that directly predicts from incomplete genomic inputs without test-time imputation. SHIFT represents each genomic feature separately and uses masked self-attention, along with a feature-availability mask, so that predictions are based only on observed inputs. Further, we introduce variable-rate feature masking during training to improve robustness to heterogeneous missingness patterns. We evaluate the approach on glioblastoma and lung squamous cell carcinoma with external validation across multiple cohorts, including a challenging setting with severe cross-cohort panel mismatch. Across these settings, SHIFT shows strong generalization and compares favorably with standard survival baselines and imputation-based approaches, while using a single model across differing feature sets. We also find that incorporating patients from incomplete cohorts during development can improve performance on external data, suggesting that partially observed cohorts need not be excluded from model building. These results support missingness-aware modeling as a practical strategy for multi-center survival prediction in precision oncology.

</details>


### [124] [Jet-Long: Efficient Long-Context Extension with Dynamic Bifocal RoPE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07740)
*Haozhan Tang,Zerui Wang,Yuxian Gu,Song Han,Han Cai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Jet-Long 是一种无需微调的零样本长上下文扩展方法，通过动态调整长程窗口的缩放因子，在保持短上下文精度的同时实现高效的长上下文外推。其双焦点架构结合了局部 RoPE 保真窗口与自适应长程窗口，采用包含-排除注意力融合和实时 RoPE 修正旋转，几乎无推理开销。在 H100 上，长上下文预填充速度最高达 FA2 的 1.39 倍，单批次生成延迟增加不超过 4%。在 Qwen3 系列模型上，Jet-Long 在 128K 上显著优于 RULER 基线，提升 2.03~4.79 个百分点，并在 HELMET-RAG 和 PG-19 任务中表现最优。该方法可无缝扩展至混合注意力架构（如 Jet-Nemotron），且对超参数不敏感，便于部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 Jet-Long 方法，利用局部 RoPE 保真窗口与动态缩放的长程窗口构建双焦点注意力结构；通过包含-排除注意力融合与实时 RoPE 修正旋转，实现近乎零开销的推理集成；所有操作被融合进单一 CuTe 内核，优化硬件利用率。

Result: 在 Qwen3-1.7B/4B/8B 模型上，Jet-Long 在 128K 上分别领先 RULER 4.79、2.18、2.03 个百分点；在 HELMET-RAG 基准上达到最佳准确率，在 PG-19 上取得最低困惑度；长上下文预填充速度达 FA2 的 1.39 倍，生成延迟增加 ≤4%；适用于混合注意力架构且无需重训练，对超参数鲁棒。

Conclusion: Jet-Long 实现了无需微调的高效零样本长上下文扩展，兼具高精度、低延迟与强泛化能力，是当前长上下文部署的理想解决方案。

Abstract: Modern LLMs are increasingly deployed in long-context applications such as retrieval-augmented generation, repository-level coding, and agentic workflows whose accumulated reasoning and tool traces routinely push the input an order of magnitude past the pretraining window, making zero-shot context extension the dominant deployment path for open-weight checkpoints. Most existing zero-shot methods fix a single rescaling factor up front, so an aggressive factor sacrifices short-context fidelity while a conservative one breaks down at long contexts. We propose Jet-Long, a tuning-free zero-shot method that pairs a local RoPE-faithful window with a long-range window whose rescaling factor adapts dynamically to the current sequence length, recovering the base model exactly at short inputs while extrapolating cleanly at long ones. An inclusion-exclusion attention merge and an on-the-fly RoPE correction rotation make the bifocal construction essentially free at inference; fused into a single CuTe kernel, long-context prefill reaches up to $1.39\times$ FA2 throughput on H100 (approaching the Hopper-only FA4), and single-batch generation incurs $\le 4\%$ overhead at every length. On Qwen3-1.7B/4B/8B up to 128K context, Jet-Long leads RULER by $+4.79$/$+2.18$/$+2.03$~pp over the strongest baseline at 1.7B/4B/8B, achieves the best overall accuracy on HELMET-RAG (a benchmark identified by HELMET as the most efficient predictor of downstream long-context performance) and attains the lowest PG-19 perplexity. Jet-Long also generalizes to hybrid attention architectures such as Jet-Nemotron for further long-context improvement without retraining, and remains hyperparameter-resilient for ease of deployment.

### [125] [Architecture Generalization with MetaNCA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07743)
*Meet Barot,Daniel Berenberg,Sina Khajehabdollahi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MetaNCA 是一种新型框架，通过学习局部更新规则来实现人工神经网络权重的自组织。该方法利用基于线性注意力的 Weight Transformer 架构，在仅依赖局部信息交互的情况下迭代更新任务网络权重。训练完成后，规则网络可生成不同架构的网络（如 MLP、CNN、ResNet），且无需反向传播。在 MNIST 和 CIFAR-100 上验证了其有效性，支持高达 200 万参数的网络，并展现出对未见架构的良好泛化能力，且训练中引入架构多样性有助于提升泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受生物神经元通过局部相互作用实现高效学习和自适应的启发，旨在设计一种能够通过局部规则自组织人工神经网络权重的框架，以实现无需反向传播的动态网络生成与适应性优化。

Method: 提出 Meta Neural Cellular Automata (MetaNCA)，采用 Weight Transformer 作为规则网络，利用线性注意力机制聚合邻近权重与隐藏状态的信息，通过迭代局部更新机制调整任务网络权重，从而实现网络结构的自组织生成。

Result: MetaNCA 成功在 MNIST 与 CIFAR-100 数据集上生成适用于 MLP、CNN、ResNet 的有效权重，支持高达 200 万参数的网络；具备对未见过的网络架构的泛化能力，且训练阶段引入架构多样性显著增强泛化性能。

Conclusion: MetaNCA 展现了通过局部规则实现神经网络权重自组织的强大潜力，为无反向传播的神经网络生成与动态适应提供了新范式，具有良好的可扩展性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Self-organization is an emergent property of life, driven by the collective behavior of individual components acting on local information. Biological neurons, through local interactions transmitted through synapses, are able to learn efficiently and can adapt their connections over an organism's lifespan. Motivated by these desirable properties of adaptability and local interaction, neural cellular automata (NCA) models have been successful at learning morphogenesis solely through local update rules, demonstrating stability over many updates and robustness to perturbations. In this work, we introduce Meta Neural Cellular Automata (MetaNCA), a framework that learns local rules which self-organize the weights of artificial neural networks. A learned rule network iteratively updates the weights of a task network using only local interactions on the computation graph. We propose a novel Weight Transformer architecture for the local rule network, which uses linear attention to aggregate signals from neighboring weights and hidden states. Once trained, the rule network generates task networks of diverse architectures without backpropagation. We show that MetaNCA generates weights for feedforward MLPs, CNNs, and ResNets on MNIST and CIFAR-100, scaling to networks of 2 million parameters. We further show that MetaNCA generalizes to architectures not seen during meta-training, and that architectural diversity in the training phase strengthens this generalization.

### [126] [LiST: Lipschitz Scaling Training for Robust and Calibrated Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07745)
*Arthur Chiron,Franck Mamalet,Thomas Massena,Thomas Deltort,Mathieu Serrurier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Lipschitz Scaling Training (LiST)的新训练范式，通过理论和实证揭示了Lipschitz约束与温度缩放（Temperature Scaling）之间的联系，发现存在一个最优的Lipschitz常数L*，可使模型在无需额外校准的情况下实现良好校准。LiST通过迭代调整全局Lipschitz常数，构建出完全校准的准确率-鲁棒性帕累托前沿，支持用户在保持校准的同时灵活权衡准确率与鲁棒性，并可在收敛后重新引入校准数据以提升样本效率。实验在CIFAR-10/100和Tiny-ImageNet上验证了其优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前神经网络的准确性、鲁棒性和校准性通常被分别研究，但同时满足三者仍是挑战。虽然Lipschitz约束模型能保证鲁棒性，但其约束参数L的选择影响准确率-鲁棒性权衡，且校准性能未被充分探索。因此需要一种能够统一优化三者的机制。

Method: 提出LiST方法，利用训练损失中的边际参数动态调整全局Lipschitz常数，基于校准作为选择最优操作点的指导原则，构建完全校准的帕累托前沿，并允许在训练后期重用校准数据。

Result: 在CIFAR-10/100和Tiny-ImageNet上，LiST实现了与约束及非约束基线相当甚至更优的准确率和鲁棒性，且无需额外校准即具备良好校准能力，同时提升了样本效率。

Conclusion: LiST成功将校准作为设计准则，实现了准确率、鲁棒性和校准性的协同优化，为构建可靠神经网络提供了一种新范式。

Abstract: While accuracy, robustness, and calibration are all essential for reliable neural networks, they are often studied separately; developing models that satisfy all three simultaneously remains a central challenge. Lipschitz-constrained models guarantee robustness by design, yet the manual selection of the Lipschitz constraint L governs the resulting accuracy-robustness trade-off, and their calibration properties remain largely underexplored. In this work, we highlight a theoretical and empirical link between the enforced Lipschitz constraint and Temperature Scaling, a state-of-the-art calibration method. Specifically, we find that for a given training scheme, there exists a non-trivial value L* that yields an out-of-the-box calibrated network, and that calibration acts as a principled criterion to select a well-defined operating point on the accuracy-robustness Pareto front. Leveraging these insights, we introduce Lipschitz Scaling Training (LiST), a novel training paradigm that iteratively adjusts the global Lipschitz constant to reach this operating point. Through a margin parameter in the training loss, LiST further enables the construction of a fully calibrated Pareto front, allowing users to navigate the accuracy-robustness trade-off while remaining calibrated throughout. At convergence, LiST also enables the reintegration of calibration data into training, improving sample efficiency without sacrificing calibration. We validate LiST on CIFAR-10/100 and Tiny-ImageNet, demonstrating competitive accuracy and robustness against constrained and unconstrained baselines, while remaining calibrated out of the box. Code is available at GitHub.

</details>


### [127] [Selective Left-Shift: Turning Test-Time Compute and Difficulty-based Curation into Training Data for Low-Resource Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07748)
*Didula Samaraweera,Anjana Supun,Srinath Perera*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在高资源语言（如Python、Java）上表现良好，但在低资源编程语言（LRPLs）如Julia上性能急剧下降。现有小语言模型改进方法面临三难困境：监督微调受限于数据稀缺，推理时扩展成本过高，从零开始的强化学习几乎无收益。

Method: 提出三阶段流水线：1）通过迭代编译器与测试反馈的离线数据合成引擎生成验证过的训练样本；2）在合成数据上微调小语言模型以获得强语法先验；3）应用基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），使用语言无关的输入/输出测试作为奖励信号，结合微调前的先验知识引导探索方向，防止语法错误。

Result: 在MultiPL-E和Agnostics LiveCodeBench上，相比当前最佳结果，Julia的pass@1分别提升7.6和14.2点；仅使用1/3的数据量和1/6的计算成本。在Ballerina上达到49.7%的MultiPL-E Pass@1，证明方法对缺乏预训练表示的语言具有强泛化能力。消融实验表明SFT阶段和执行基础奖励均对稳定训练至关重要。

Conclusion: 所提出的三阶段流水线有效解决了小语言模型在低资源编程语言上的性能瓶颈，通过解耦语法与推理、利用合成数据与可验证奖励，实现了高性能、低成本、强泛化的代码生成能力，且具备良好的跨语言迁移潜力。

Abstract: Large Language Models achieve strong code generation for high resource languages like Python and Java but suffer sharp performance drops on Low-Resource Programming Languages~(LRPLs) such as Julia. Improving Small Language Models~(SLMs) for these languages faces a trilemma: Supervised Fine-Tuning~(SFT) is bottlenecked by data scarcity, inference-time scaling is too expensive for deployment, and Reinforcement Learning from scratch yields near zero advantages. We propose a three-phase pipeline that resolves this trilemma by decoupling syntax acquisition from algorithmic reasoning. First, we \emph{left-shift} inference-time compute to an offline data synthesis engine that uses iterative compiler and test feedback to generate verified training examples. Second, we fine-tune an SLM on this synthetic, verified data to embed strong syntactic priors. Third, we apply Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward~(RLVR) grounded by language-agnostic Input/Output tests, where the SFT prior constrains exploration away from syntax errors. Applied to Qwen3-8B, our pipeline improves pass@1 by up to +7.6 points on MultiPL-E and +14.2 points on the Agnostics LiveCodeBench for Julia compared to SOTA results. Furthermore, the pipeline only used $\frac{1}{3}$ data and $\frac{1}{6}$ cost over the previous state-of-the-art. We further demonstrate that the pipeline generalizes to Ballerina achieving 49.7\% MultiPL-E Pass@1, a language with near-zero pretraining representation. Ablations confirm that both the SFT phase and execution-grounded rewards are necessary for stable training.

### [128] [A Transdiagnostic Space of Disorder Like Phenotypes in Reinforcement Learning Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07753)
*Hari Prasad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究将心理障碍建模为可调控的认知评估信号，在一个基于评估引导的PPO代理中，以七个精神障碍（焦虑、躁狂、强迫检查、抑郁、冲动、成瘾和创伤后应激）作为单一控制旋钮进行模拟，每个症状通过预注册的测量工具进行量化。在超过一千次实验运行中，所有障碍均表现出非控制组无法复制的剂量-反应关系。研究发现：障碍自发形成二维情感空间，躁狂与焦虑相互映射；移除特定旋钮可缓解奖励扭曲型障碍（如躁狂、成瘾），但无法缓解回避型障碍（如焦虑、PTSD），后者可通过渐进暴露训练恢复；两个同时激活的旋钮产生非加性交互作用，支持共病预测。此外，三个障碍旋钮（抑郁、成瘾、焦虑）可在三维像素环境（MiniWorld）中转移至标准卷积代理，且跨任务验证了分离效应，表明该框架不局限于网格世界或PPO的评估批评器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常通过手动调整奖励函数诱发单一或双个精神障碍，行为标签为事后判定，且仅报告单次运行结果，缺乏系统性和可重复性。本研究旨在建立一种可调控、可量化的计算精神病学模型，实现对多种精神障碍的精确模拟，并探索其内在机制与治疗潜力。

Method: 采用基于评估引导的PPO强化学习框架，将七种精神障碍建模为可调节的认知评估权重旋钮，结合预注册的测量指标（如症状评分、行为模式）来量化各障碍表现。通过多轮实验（10个随机种子、4个对照组）分析剂量-反应关系，评估不同障碍间的交互与转移能力。

Result: 所有障碍均呈现单调递增的剂量-响应曲线，且无控制组能复现此现象；障碍自发聚类于二维情感空间，躁狂与焦虑具有相似特征；移除某些旋钮可缓解奖励扭曲型障碍但不影响回避型障碍，后者可通过暴露训练恢复；双障碍协同时出现非加性交互，支持共病假设；部分障碍旋钮可在不同环境和架构间转移，且跨任务验证了症状分离。

Conclusion: 认知评估权重可构成一个可控的精神障碍表型空间，同一参数既能诱发障碍也能模拟治疗过程。该框架具备良好的泛化性与可解释性，为计算精神病学提供了统一、可扩展的建模平台。

Abstract: Modelling psychological disorders in artificial agents offers both a testbed for computational psychiatry and a lens on the failure modes of affective control. Prior work induces one or two disorders in a reinforcement learning (RL) agent by hand-tuned reward shaping, labels the behaviour post hoc, and reports single runs. We recast disorder modelling as dose-controllable manipulation of cognitive appraisal signals in an appraisal-guided PPO agent, expressing seven disorders (anxiety, mania, obsessive-compulsive checking, depression, impulsivity, addiction, and post-traumatic stress) each as a single knob grounded in a computational psychiatry account, with each symptom measured by a preregistered assay mapped to a recognised paradigm. Across more than a thousand runs (10 seeds, four controls, 95% confidence intervals) every disorder shows a graded, monotone dose-response that no control reproduces. Beyond these induced effects, three findings emerge that were not written into the reward: the disorders self-organise into a two-dimensional affective space in which mania mirrors anxiety; removing a knob remits reward distortion disorders (mania, checking, addiction) but not avoidance disorders (anxiety, PTSD), which instead recover under a graded exposure curriculum; and two simultaneous knobs interact nonadditively, yielding testable comorbidity predictions. Appraisal weights thus parameterise a controllable space of affective phenotypes in which the same knobs that induce a disorder can model its treatment. We also show that three disorder knobs (depression, addiction, anxiety) transfer to a three-dimensional pixel environment (MiniWorld) with a standard convolutional agent and no appraisal critic, with cross-assay dissociation confirmed across both domains, indicating the framework is not specific to grid worlds or to PPO's appraisal critic.

### [129] [Image classification via a quantum-inspired strategy involving a mixture of experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07754)
*Kumari Jyoti,Rohith Babu,Apoorva D. Patel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受量子启发的混合经典-量子框架，用于图像模式识别。该方法利用幅度编码、局部酉操作卷积、多专家并行处理及量子稳定子码提取特征，结合经典全连接网络进行分类。在MNIST和Fashion-MNIST数据集上，该方法显著优于单一专家模型，预测失败率降低约一半，且在GPU工作站上的计算开销适中，具备实际应用潜力，并可进一步部署于量子处理器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合经典-量子架构：量子部分包括图像幅度编码、局部酉操作实现卷积、多个专家以不同参数并行处理同一图像、利用量子稳定子码提取特征；经典部分通过全连接网络融合各专家输出，完成图像分类。

Conclusion: 所提出的量子启发式混合框架在图像分类任务中表现优异，兼具高性能与实用性，是一种对现有经典方法的有效补充，未来可拓展至真实量子硬件实现。

Abstract: Pattern recognition problems arise in a variety of physical image processing situations, and convolutional neural networks are a popular scheme for the required feature extraction and classification tasks. The classical networks use diffusion-based smearing and block-wise pooling to downsample the image data and capture important structural features. In this work, we propose and demonstrate a more efficient quantum-inspired strategy involving a mixture of experts. It is a hybrid classical-quantum framework. The quantum part consists of amplitude encoding of the images, convolution using local unitary operations, multiple experts processing the same image with different parameters, and feature extraction using quantum stabiliser codes. The classical part then jointly processes the features extracted by different experts using a standard fully connected neural network for image class prediction. Using MNIST and Fashion-MNIST datasets as benchmarks, we demonstrate that the joint expert analysis outperforms the individual expert one, as well as reduces the failure rate of image class prediction by around a factor of two. The overhead of our quantum-inspired strategy is only moderate on GPU workstations, which makes our proposal a practical alternative to existing classical schemes. We also point out how the quantum part of our framework can be executed on a quantum processor.

Motivation: 表格数据领域仍被视为深度学习的未攻克之地，现有方法多采用简单的MLP作为编码器，效果有限；为提升多模态学习性能，需探索更强的表格编码器。

Conclusion: 编码器的选择对多模态学习至关重要，应重视表格数据专用强编码器的应用，未来研究应解决标签依赖等限制，推动多模态学习在复杂数据场景中的发展。

Abstract: Multimodal learning usually requires a dedicated encoder per modality. When a tabular modality is involved, prior work has been mostly using a \emph{plain MLP} as the encoder. Yet if it were a strong encoder, the tabular domain would not be ``the last unconquered castle for deep learning''. This study evaluates state-of-the-art tabular models as encoders in the image-tabular setting for the first time. An obstacle stands out. In-Context Learning models, among the best performing methods in the tabular domain, require labels to process instances, making it non-trivial to embed training and test instances the same way. ### [133] [Unlocking Temporal Generalization in Hamiltonian Video Dynamics Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07763)
*Eli Laird,Corey Clark*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种改进连续时间世界模型在非保守环境下的时间泛化能力的方法。针对哈密顿生成网络（HGN）在外部驱动、耗散系统中因步长超出训练范围而导致的预测失败问题，识别出两个主要故障机制：由不受约束的动作-力映射引起的潜在量级增长，以及积分器分辨率不足导致的全局截断误差累积。论文提出了针对性修复方案，并验证了在远超训练分布的时间分辨率下仍能稳定预测动态行为。研究还为连续时间视频生成中的时间泛化提供了多项建议。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 分析HGN在非保守环境中的两种失效机制：1）动作-力映射未受约束导致隐状态量级失控；2）积分器分辨率不足引发全局截断误差积累。提出分别针对这两个机制的修正方法，包括对动作-力映射施加约束和使用更高精度积分器。通过实验验证改进后的模型在广泛时间分辨率下仍保持稳定预测。

Result: 改进后的模型在超出训练时间步长的多种分辨率下均表现出稳定的动态预测能力，显著提升了时间泛化性能。实验表明，通过约束动作-力映射和优化积分器，可有效抑制潜在量级增长与误差累积，实现可靠的时间尺度外推。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了连续时间世界模型在非保守环境下时间泛化的关键障碍，并提供了有效的修复策略。结果表明，通过合理约束模型结构和改进数值积分，可实现跨时间尺度的稳定动态预测，为连续时间视频生成等应用提供了重要技术支撑。

Abstract: World models are typically trained to predict discrete-time physical dynamics with a fixed step size baked into the model weights, preventing prediction at variable temporal resolutions. This matters for hierarchical planning, sim-to-real transfer, and scientific or game-engine applications that must query the same dynamics at multiple timescales. Hamiltonian Generative Networks (HGN) offer a principled path forward, grounding predictions in a continuous-time energy function that is, in principle, independent of the observation frame rate. In practice, however, their temporal generalization breaks down in non-conservative settings. We show that in externally forced, dissipative environments, HGN rollouts at step sizes beyond the training regime fail due to distinct failure modes, including latent magnitude growth driven by an unconstrained action-force map, and global truncation error accumulation from an under-resolved integrator. We identify a targeted fix for each mechanism and demonstrate stable dynamics prediction at temporal resolutions well outside the training distribution. In a detailed analysis, we recommend several strategies for enabling temporal generalization in continuous-time video generation.

### [135] [Graph-Regularized Deep Learning for EEG-Based Emotion Recognition with Psychologically-Grounded Label Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07773)
*Dongyang Kuang,Zizheng Ma,Yushan Zhang,Xiaocong Zeng*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法将情绪类别视为孤立标签，忽略了其在心理学上的内在关联性，导致模型预测可能违背情绪之间的实际接近性，影响识别性能与可解释性。

Method: 构建情绪图结构，基于维度情绪理论定义节点间边权；引入三种图正则化策略：图标签平滑（软标签）、基于图拉普拉斯的通行距离（谱图理论）、切片沃尔什距离（最优传输），以惩罚偏离情绪拓扑的预测。

Conclusion: 所提图正则化框架有效融合情绪的心理学先验知识，提升了情绪识别的准确性与合理性，为未来脑机接口与心理健康监测提供了更可靠的技术路径。

Abstract: EEG-based emotion recognition is critical for mental health monitoring and affective brain-computer interfaces, yet existing deep learning approaches often treat emotion classes as isolated labels, ignoring their psychological interdependencies. We propose a graph-regularized learning framework that conceptualizes emotions as nodes in a graph where edges encode proximity based on dimensional emotion theories. We adapt three complementary regularization strategies--Graph Label Smoothing (intuitive soft labeling), Commuting distance on graph via Graph Laplacian (spectral graph theory), and Sliced Wasserstein Distance (optimal transport on graph)--ordered by increasing computational complexity. These strategies penalize model predictions that deviate from the established emotion topology. Our framework is evaluated across three representative backbone architectures: AudioTransformer (pure transformer), Conformer (CNN-transformer hybrid), and DCGNN (causal graph neural network), demonstrating architecture-agnostic benefits. Experiments on SEED-IV (4 classes) and SEED-V (5 classes) datasets show consistent improvements: best case up to +5.42% accuracy and 39% reduction in psychologically implausible misclassifications. Ultimately, our framework help raise the upper bound of performance achievable with standard approaches. Code will be released.

### [136] [A law of robustness for two-layer neural networks with arbitrary weights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07778)
*Yitzchak Shmalo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文证明了Bubeck、Li和Nagaraj关于两层神经网络在拟合噪声标签时的Lipschitz常数下界猜想，针对连续分段线性激活函数（如ReLU），在高维球面或高斯数据分布下，即使权重无界，也成立该下界，仅差一个对数因子。关键在于使用函数空间覆盖替代参数空间覆盖，并引入刚性引理控制分段线性函数的拐点系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究两层神经网络在拟合带噪声标签时的内在泛化能力限制，特别是当权重无界时，如何刻画其Lipschitz常数的下界。此前的工作受限于参数有界假设，而实际中权重可能无界，因此需要新的分析框架。

Method: 采用函数空间覆盖代替传统的参数空间覆盖，以应对无界权重带来的挑战；核心是提出并证明一个‘刚性引理’：在高维空间（d≥3）中，不同超平面上的拐点无法在通用点处相互抵消，从而使得每个标准拐点的系数受函数的Lipschitz常数控制。

Result: 对于从单位球面$\mathbb{S}^{d-1}$（d≥3）或标准高斯分布$N(0,I_d/d)$中采样的数据，标签噪声水平为$σ^2>0$，任意宽度为$m$的两层网络（含偏置和跳接连接），若其误差低于噪声水平$\varepsilon$，则其Lipschitz常数满足：$\mathrm{Lip}(f) \ge c\,\varepsilon\sqrt{n/(\bar m\log(C\bar m nd/\varepsilon))}$，其中$\bar m = (K-1)m+1$。此外，若函数具有至多$n$个不同拐点超平面，则下界可依实际拐点数调整，与冗余隐藏单元无关。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在无权重有界假设下证明了两层神经网络的Lipschitz下界猜想，揭示了高维数据中函数复杂度与泛化能力之间的深层制约关系。刚性引理表明，在高维中拐点不可抵消，这是实现下界的关键。而在二维情况下刚性失效，存在低Lipschitz常数的插值解，说明维度在其中起决定性作用。

Abstract: Bubeck, Li and Nagaraj conjectured that, for generic data, any two-layer neural network with $m$ neurons that fits $n$ noisy labels must have Lipschitz constant at least of order $\sqrt{n/m}$, with no restriction on the size of the weights. Bubeck and Sellke proved a universal version of this law for Lipschitz-parameterized classes, but under a polynomial bound on the parameters; at depth three that boundedness hypothesis is genuinely necessary. The two-layer unbounded-weight case requires a different argument. We prove the conjectured law, up to one logarithmic factor, for every continuous piecewise-linear activation, in particular for ReLU networks. For data drawn uniformly from $\mathbb{S}^{d-1}$, $d\ge3$, or from $N(0,I_d/d)$, labels in $[-1,1]$ with noise level $σ^2>0$, and any width-$m$ two-layer network with arbitrary real weights, biases and affine skip connection, fitting the data $\varepsilon$ below the noise floor forces $\mathrm{Lip}(f)\ge c\,\varepsilon\sqrt{n/(\bar m\log(C\bar m nd/\varepsilon))}$, $\bar m=(K-1)m+1$, with high probability. A realized-kink-count version holds on the same event: every realized two-layer piecewise-linear function with $k(f)\le n$ distinct kink hyperplanes obeys the bound with $\bar m$ replaced by $k(f)+1$, irrespective of how many redundant hidden units parameterize it. The proof replaces parameter-space covering, impossible for unbounded weights, by a function-space covering. The central deterministic ingredient is a rigidity lemma: on $B_2$, and on $\mathbb{S}^{d-1}$ for $d\ge3$, the coefficient of each canonical kink is controlled by the Lipschitz constant of the realized function, because kinks on distinct hyperplanes cannot cancel at generic points. Rigidity genuinely fails at $d=2$, and an explicit two-layer ReLU interpolant with $O(1)$ Lipschitz constant at width $2n$ matches the law at the overparameterized endpoint.

</details>


### [137] [Predicting Pseudo-nitzschia harmful algal blooms along the Portuguese Coast using satellite-derived predictors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07834)
*Ayman Bnoussaad,El Khalil Cherif,Ligia Pinto,Ramiro Neves,Alexandra D. Silva,Alexandre Bernardino*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究开发并评估了一个时空机器学习框架，用于预测葡萄牙大西洋沿岸的有害藻华（HAB）发生情况，仅使用卫星遥感数据作为预测因子，并在现实预报约束条件下进行验证。研究覆盖了9个牡蛎养殖区（L1-L9），基于5,882个观测数据，重点分析了两个热点区域（L1-L2）的环境与生物变异。利用2013-2023年共1,440个观测数据和超过1,000个卫星衍生变量（如海表温度、上升流指数、叶绿素a和浮游植物功能类型），通过河流感知的空间聚类方法将采样点划分为生态上合理的子区域。采用严格的时空交叉验证策略，同时剔除整年和空间聚类，防止信息泄露并贴近真实预报场景。结果表明，HAB事件具有中等可预测性，集成树模型表现最佳：随机森林在仅使用环境变量时达到0.74±0.05的性能；加入生物变量后，极端随机树模型提升至0.77±0.06。特征重要性分析显示，季节结构、空间背景和滞后环境条件是模型决策的关键因素，而生物指标则在物理适宜期进一步细化藻华可能性。该框架为东部边界上升流海岸的卫星支持型HAB早期预警系统提供了实际应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Pseudo-nitzschia藻华对葡萄牙大西洋沿岸的海洋生态系统和贝类养殖构成持续威胁，亟需高效、实时的预测工具。传统监测手段受限于时空覆盖和成本，难以满足早期预警需求。因此，迫切需要一种基于卫星数据的可操作、可扩展的预测框架，以实现对有害藻华事件的提前预警，保障食品安全与渔业可持续发展。

Method: 采用机器学习方法构建时空预测模型，整合十年（2013–2023）的卫星遥感数据，包括海表温度、上升流指数、叶绿素a及浮游植物功能类型等超过1,000个变量。通过河流感知的空间聚类划分生态子区域，使用严格的时空交叉验证策略（同时剔除整年和空间簇）防止信息泄露。比较多种模型（如随机森林、极端随机树等）在不同特征组合下的表现，并进行特征重要性分析以揭示关键驱动因子。

Result: HAB事件具有中等可预测性。集成树模型表现最优：随机森林在仅使用环境变量时达到0.74±0.05的准确率；加入生物变量后，极端随机树模型性能提升至0.77±0.06。特征重要性分析表明，季节结构、空间上下文和滞后环境条件是主要决定因素，生物指标在物理适宜期内进一步提高预测精度。该框架具备实际操作潜力，适用于东部边界上升流海岸的卫星支持型早期预警系统。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了一个基于卫星数据的时空机器学习框架，能够有效预测葡萄牙沿海地区Pseudo-nitzschia藻华的发生，具备良好的操作性和推广前景。该系统可为沿海管理机构提供科学依据，支持早期预警与风险防控，尤其适用于类似东部边界上升流系统的全球沿海区域。

Abstract: Pseudo-nitzschia diatoms pose recurrent risks to coastal ecosystems and shellfish harvesting along the Portuguese Atlantic coast. Here we develop and evaluate a spatio-temporal machine-learning framework to predict harmful algal bloom (HAB) occurrence using exclusively satellite-derived predictors under realistic forecasting constraints. We characterised environmental and biological variability across shellfish production zones (L1-L9) using 5,882 observations, providing system-wide context. Predictive models were developed for zones L1-L2, a hotspot for Pseudo-nitzschia and domoic acid events, using a decade-long dataset (2013-2023; 1,440 observations; more than 1,000 satellite-based predictors including sea surface temperature, an upwelling index, chlorophyll-a, and plankton functional types). Sampling locations were partitioned into ecologically meaningful sub-regions using a river-aware spatial clustering scheme. A stringent spatio-temporal cross-validation strategy that simultaneously withholds entire years and spatial clusters prevents leakage and closely mimics real-world forecasting conditions. HAB occurrence proved moderately predictable across model classes and feature configurations. Ensemble tree-based methods achieved the strongest discrimination: Random Forest reached 0.74 +/- 0.05 with environmental predictors; Extra Trees reached 0.77 +/- 0.06 with biological variables added. Feature-importance analyses revealed that seasonal structure, spatial context, and lagged environmental conditions dominate model decisions, while biological indicators refine bloom likelihood within physically favourable periods. The framework demonstrates operationally relevant skill for satellite-supported HAB early-warning systems along eastern boundary upwelling coasts.

### [138] [Explaining Near-Zero Hessian Eigenvalues Through Approximate Symmetries in Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07845)
*Marcel Kühn,Bernd Rosenow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了深度神经网络训练损失的海森矩阵中大量趋近于零的特征值的来源，提出这些特征值源于网络参数化中的连续对称性被弱破坏后产生的伪戈尔德斯通模式。在深度线性网络中，这些对称性产生精确的平坦方向和零特征值；引入ReLU非线性作为微小扰动后，对称性被弱破坏，但特征向量仍主要位于对称子空间内。高曲率方向与对称子空间正交，而大部分特征值则集中在对称子空间中。通过两层ReLU学生-教师模型和CIFAR-10训练网络验证了该机制，并扩展至卷积网络，揭示了海森矩阵的“主体”部分与弱破坏对称性的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解深度神经网络损失函数的海森矩阵中大量近零特征值的来源，现有理论无法解释其成因，尤其是这些低频模式的几何意义。

Method: 分析深度线性网络中的精确对称性及其导致的零特征值；引入ReLU非线性作为微扰，研究对称性如何被弱破坏；通过解析构造特征向量、分解谱结构、对比高曲率方向与对称子空间的关系，进行实证验证。

Result: 发现海森矩阵的大多数小特征值对应于弱破坏的伪戈尔德斯通模式，其特征向量几乎完全位于对称子空间中；高曲率方向与之正交；该机制在全连接与卷积网络中均成立。

Conclusion: 海森矩阵的主体部分来源于网络参数化中连续对称性的弱破坏，其本质是伪戈尔德斯通模式，这为近零特征值提供了清晰的几何解释。

Abstract: The Hessian of the training loss governs the local geometry of the loss landscape, yet despite existing explanations for its largest eigenvalues, the origin of the vast multitude of vanishingly small eigenvalues remains elusive. We argue that the bulk consists of the weakly lifted pseudo-Goldstone modes of the continuous symmetries of the network parametrization. In deep linear networks these symmetries are exact: they generate flat directions and hence exact zero modes, whose eigenvectors we construct explicitly. Introducing a ReLU nonlinearity as a perturbation, we show that it breaks these symmetries weakly and explicitly. Resolving the spectrum at the level of eigenvectors, we find that the high-curvature directions are orthogonal to the symmetry subspace, while the bulk lies almost entirely within it. We demonstrate the mechanism in a two-layer ReLU student--teacher model and in a network trained on CIFAR-10. A convolutional example demonstrates that the same diagnostic extends beyond fully connected layers. Together, these results link the Hessian bulk to weakly broken symmetries and clarify the origin of near-zero modes.

### [139] [When Does Continual Learning Require Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07847)
*Anne Harrington,Nayan Saxena,Michael Murphy,Anastasia Borovykh,Zeyu Yun,Sridhar Kamath,Ara Eindra Kyi,Trevor Darrell,Jitendra Malik,Yutong Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出，持续学习不仅是缓解遗忘和管理上下文的问题，更核心在于模型随世界变化而提升能力。作者从空间（新领域出现）和时间（数据漂移）两个维度重新定义持续学习，并在真实场景下评估多种方法：提示法（如GEPA、ACE）快速适应但后续退化；基于蒸馏的方法稳定积累知识但难以更新过时信息；上下文压缩提升效率但对学习新任务帮助有限；在线强化学习最能适应知识更新但对噪声奖励敏感。结果表明，不同环境变化模式需要不同的更新策略，决定了是应内化于模型权重还是通过外部支持实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前持续学习研究主要聚焦于上下文管理和遗忘缓解，但这一框架不完整，无法充分应对现实世界中动态变化的复杂性，如新领域出现、事实过期及智能体交互累积状态等。因此亟需一个更全面的视角来理解并设计有效的持续学习机制。

Method: 将主流LLM基准测试重构为序列问题，引入一种机制无关的评估协议，系统比较提示法（GEPA、ACE）、监督学习（SFT、SDFT）、强化学习（GRPO、SDPO）以及上下文压缩（Cartridges、In-place TTT）等多种方法在真实持续学习场景下的表现。

Result: 提示法快速适应新阶段但性能在后续任务中下降；蒸馏方法知识积累稳定但难以更新过时信息；上下文压缩提升效率但未显著增强学习新任务的能力；在线强化学习对知识更新适应性最强，但受噪声奖励影响大。不同方法在不同变化模式下表现各异，说明持续学习并非单一能力。

Conclusion: 持续学习的本质是应对环境变化以提升模型能力，其成功依赖于根据变化类型选择合适的更新策略——有些需内化于模型权重，有些可通过外部架构实现。未来系统设计应基于此认知，针对性地融合多种机制。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) become increasingly capable, the next question is how can we enable models to continually learn? Today, the field largely frames this as a problem of context management and mitigating forgetting. We argue this framing is incomplete: continual learning is fundamentally about increasing model competence as the world changes. We disentangle this change along two axes -- space, where the model encounters new domains, and time, where the underlying data drifts under a fixed task. This framing lets us study continual learning under realistic conditions: new domains arrive over time, facts drift past their training cutoff, and agentic interactions accumulate state across episodes. To evaluate methods under this setting, we recast widely used LLM benchmarks as sequential problems and introduce a single mechanism-agnostic protocol that compares prompt-based methods (GEPA, ACE), supervised learning (SFT, SDFT), reinforcement learning (GRPO, SDPO), and context compression (Cartridges, In-place TTT). Prompt-based methods fit each new stage quickly but degrade on future tasks. Distillation-based methods accumulate knowledge stably but struggle to update outdated facts. Context compression improves efficiency without substantially improving the ability to learn new tasks. Online reinforcement learning adapts most effectively to knowledge updates but remains sensitive to noisy reward signals. Overall, our results suggest that continual learning is not a single capability: different patterns of environmental change require fundamentally different update behaviors, determining when adaptation must be learned inside model weights and when it can be achieved through external scaffolding. We hope that understanding where each method succeeds and fails will guide the design of stronger continual learning systems.

</details>


### [140] [NFTR: From Provable Mode-Averaging to Geodesic Subgoal Selection in Offline Goal-Conditioned RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07855)
*Erdemt Bao,Xing Lei,Jun Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NFTR提出了一种基于归一化流的子目标选择方法，通过三角松弛重加权机制解决传统方法中的乐观偏差和模式崩溃问题，确保在随机动态下仍保持稳定性与最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离线目标条件强化学习方法在子目标选择时依赖值函数优势，易产生乐观偏差和模式崩溃，尤其在多模态分布下退化为单一高斯均值，导致不可达区域的问题。

Method: 采用条件归一化流替代传统高斯策略，利用闭式模式平均结果证明归一化流是最小生成类；引入基于三角不等式的三角松弛评分，乘性修正优势权重以抑制路径代价过高的子目标；设计RWDR目标函数，保持群体级单调改进并支持三部分次优性分解。

Result: 所提方法有效避免了高斯模式崩溃，在随机环境中保持稳定，且理论上保证了子目标选择的合理性与可组合性。

Conclusion: NFTR通过归一化流与三角松弛重加权相结合，实现了鲁棒、稳定的子目标选择，显著提升了离线目标条件强化学习在复杂环境中的性能与可靠性。

Abstract: Hierarchical Implicit Q-Learning (HIQL), an offline goal-conditioned RL method, selects subgoals by value-function advantages alone. This rule has two coupled failure modes. Optimistic bias treats lucky stochastic outcomes as skillful choices, and mode collapse reduces a multi-modal subgoal distribution to a single Gaussian mean that often falls in unreachable regions. We propose NFTR (Normalizing Flows subgoal policies with Triangle-slack Reweighting). A conditional Normalizing Flow replaces the Gaussian policy, and a closed-form mode-averaging result identifies NFs as the minimal generative class for AWR-based subgoal selection. A triangle slack score, built on the architectural triangle inequality without relying on distance accuracy, multiplicatively corrects the AWR weight to downweight subgoals whose detour cost exceeds average reachability. Triangle-slack vanishes on geodesics in deterministic MDPs and remains a conservative upper bound on composability violation under stochastic dynamics. The RWDR objective preserves AWR's population-level monotonic improvement and admits a three-term suboptimality decomposition. Together, these two ingredients yield subgoal selection that provably avoids the Gaussian collapse described above and remains stable under stochastic dynamics. GitHub page: https://github.com/erdemtbao/NFTR

</details>


### [141] [Physics-Informed Machine Learning Under Small-Data Constraints: Lessons from Abrasive Waterjet Milling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07863)
*Sarah Grewe,Jörg Frochte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对小样本、高成本的物理主导加工过程，本文提出三项方法论贡献：区分物理数据清洗与统计数据整理，将后者视为可竞争的建模假设；发现单次划分评估结果不稳定，建议采用10折交叉验证以获得更可靠模型排序；研究不同层次的物理信息融合方式，发现基于紧凑物理基线的残差学习对高斯过程（GP）表现优异，但会损害树基模型；贝叶斯超参数调优提升梯度提升与支持向量回归等敏感模型性能，却对多阶段混合模型产生负面影响。此外，GP的不确定性区间近似校准。整体表明，在小样本工艺数据中，可靠的模型比较需明确数据整理假设、稳健评估策略及谨慎的物理信息融入方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理主导的加工过程中，实验数据量小、成本高且材料特定，因此数据处理、评估设计和物理信息整合方式的重要性不亚于学习算法本身。如何有效利用有限数据并确保模型可靠性成为关键挑战。

Method: 采用155个Inconel 718材料的磨料水射流铣削数据集，系统对比了不同数据预处理策略、评估方法（单次划分与10折交叉验证）、物理信息融合方式（从完全依赖数据到残差学习结合物理基线），并应用贝叶斯超参数优化改进多种模型。

Result: 1. 统计数据整理作为可竞争的建模假设优于隐式预处理；2. 单次划分评估结果不稳定，10折交叉验证更可靠；3. 残差学习在高斯过程上表现良好，降低方差且可解释性强，但在树基模型中效果下降；4. 贝叶斯调优提升参数敏感模型，但削弱多阶段混合框架；5. 高斯过程的不确定性区间具有良好的校准性（实际覆盖率86%，名义90%）。

Conclusion: 对于小样本、高成本的工艺数据，模型比较的可靠性依赖于显式的数据整理假设、稳健的评估流程以及物理信息的合理整合方式。应避免隐式预处理，优先使用交叉验证，并根据模型类型选择合适的物理融合策略。

Abstract: In physically dominated machining processes, experimental datasets are small, expensive, and material-specific; in this regime, data curation, evaluation design, and the form of physics integration can matter as much as the learning algorithm. Using an abrasive waterjet milling dataset ($n{=}155$, Inconel\,718), we make three methodological contributions. First, we separate physics-based data \emph{cleaning} from statistical \emph{curation} and treat the latter as competing modelling hypotheses rather than silent preprocessing. Second, we find that model rankings from a 15-point hold-out set can be unstable: the single-split winner drops from rank~1 to rank~7 under 10-fold cross-validation, while Gaussian Process (GP) variants occupy the top ranks. Third, we study a spectrum of physics integration levels and find that residual learning on a compact physics baseline is competitive for GP, yielding lower variance and an interpretable decomposition, but degrades tree-based models. Bayesian hyper parameter tuning improves parameter-sensitive baselines such as gradient boosting and SVR, yet harms multi-stage hybrid pipelines at this sample size. GP uncertainty intervals are approximately calibrated ($86\%$ empirical coverage at nominal $90\%$). The resulting picture is methodological: for small, expensive process datasets, our results suggest that, in this setting, reliable model comparison benefits from explicit curation hypotheses, robust evaluation, and careful choices about how physics enters the model.

### [142] [Optimal Learning Rate Scaling Depends on Data in Deep Scalar Linear Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07884)
*Yedi Zhang,Peter E. Latham,Leena Chennuru Vankadara,Andrew Saxe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了深度标量线性网络的梯度下降动态，发现即使在最简模型中，最优的学习率缩放也依赖于数据；数据无关的缩放规则无法跨深度泛化。在数据依赖的最优缩放下，学习动态与数据无关且对深度弱依赖，所有深度（包括无穷）均保持恒定的线性收敛速率。类似的数据依赖效应也在带残差连接的深度标量线性网络中被观察到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究深度标量线性网络中学习率缩放与数据的关系，揭示数据依赖性对学习动态的影响，并验证其在不同网络结构中的普适性。

Method: 通过解析求解深度标量线性网络的梯度下降动态，分析不同学习率缩放策略下的收敛行为，并扩展至带残差连接的网络结构进行验证。

Result: 数据依赖的最优学习率缩放可使学习动态与数据无关、对深度弱依赖，实现所有深度下的恒定线性收敛速率；残差结构中亦存在类似现象。

Conclusion: 学习率的最优缩放必须考虑数据特性，数据无关的规则无法跨深度有效迁移；数据依赖的缩放能实现稳定且一致的优化性能，适用于各种深度结构。

Abstract: In this short note we consider the gradient descent dynamics of deep scalar linear networks, $f(x) = \prod_{l=1}^L w_l x$, which enjoy exact time-course solutions for any integer depth. We show that even in this minimal model, the optimal depth-wise learning rate scaling depends on data, whereas data-agnostic scaling rules fail to transfer across depths. Under the data-dependent optimal scaling, the learning dynamics is independent of data and weakly dependent on depth, resulting in a constant linear convergence rate across all depths including infinity. We further show similar data-dependent effects in deep scalar linear networks with residual connections.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分布式架构，对数据集的分区子集分别进行小波映射，各节点独立计算局部OLS估计器，最终通过平均合并结果。基于固定设计假设，推导并分析平均估计器的理论误差。

Result: 在子集协方差差异较小的条件下，所提方法的额外损失与传统全数据集映射方法相当，证明其在降低计算成本的同时仍能保持良好的统计性能。

Conclusion: 通过对分块子集进行分布式小波映射，可在显著降低计算开销的前提下，实现与全数据集映射相媲美的估计精度，尤其适用于协方差结构相近的大规模数据场景。

Abstract: This paper studies distributed sketching for ordinary least squares (OLS) regression, an approach that distributes small sketches of a large data set over multiple machines to separately construct OLS estimators and average them. Unlike prior studies that consider sketching on the whole data set, we consider sketching on partitioned subsets to further reduce computational cost. Under the fixed design setting, we characterize the exact excess loss of the averaged OLS estimator. Results show that this loss is comparable to the established loss for sketching on the whole data set when the divergence among subset covariances is small.

### [144] [Multimodal Unlearning Across Vision, Language, Video, and Audio: Survey of Methods, Datasets, and Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07907)
*Nobin Sarwar,Shubhashis Roy Dipta,Zheyuan Liu,Vaidehi Patil*

TL;DR: 该综述系统性地探讨了多模态遗忘（multimodal unlearning）技术，针对视觉、语言、音频和视频等模态，提出了一种统一的系统视角，以应对大型多模态模型中因训练数据带来的敏感、版权、偏见或不安全跨模态关联问题。通过构建分类框架，清晰比较不同模型架构与模态间的权衡，涵盖删除强度、保留能力、效率、可逆性与鲁棒性等关键指标，并指出当前开放问题与实际部署挑战。作者还发布了开源资源库以支持后续研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着视觉-语言模型（VLMs）、扩散模型（DMs）、大语言模型（LLMs）和音频-视觉模型（AFMs）的广泛应用，这些模型可能在共享表示中隐含敏感、版权、偏见或不安全的跨模态关联。重新训练以响应删除请求或政策更新往往不切实际，且知识分布广泛，导致针对性遗忘困难。因此需要一种可选择性地跨模态删除特定知识但保持整体性能的方法。

Method: 提出一个系统性的多模态遗忘分类框架，整合近期进展，涵盖不同模态（视觉、语言、音频、视频）的遗忘机制，分析其在删除强度、保留能力、效率、可逆性和鲁棒性之间的权衡。结合具体案例与方法对比，实现跨模型、跨模态的系统化评估。

Result: 建立了一个可比较的多模态遗忘分析体系，揭示了现有方法的优势与局限；明确了关键性能指标间的权衡关系；为未来研究提供了明确方向与实用建议。同时发布了一个持续更新的精选资源库，促进领域发展。

Conclusion: 多模态遗忘是保障模型安全性、合规性与可解释性的关键技术，亟需更高效、可靠且可扩展的解决方案。本综述为该领域的理论研究与工程实践提供了坚实基础，并呼吁进一步探索通用遗忘机制与实际应用场景的融合。

Abstract: With the growing adoption of VLMs, DMs, LLMs, and AFMs, these multimodal foundation models can inadvertently encode sensitive, copyrighted, biased, or unsafe cross-modal associations that originate from their training data. Retraining after deletion requests or policy updates is often impractical, and targeted forgetting remains difficult because knowledge is distributed across shared representations. Multimodal unlearning addresses this challenge by enabling selective removal across modalities while retaining overall utility. This survey offers a unified, system-oriented view of multimodal unlearning across vision, language, audio, and video, grounded in recent advances, emerging applications, and open problems. Our taxonomy enables systematic comparison across model architectures and modalities, clarifying trade-offs among deletion strength, retention, efficiency, reversibility, and robustness. This survey highlights open problems and practical considerations to support future research and deployment of multimodal unlearning. We release a curated repository: https://smsnobin77.github.io/Awesome-Multimodal-Unlearning/

### [145] [Efficient Safety Alignment of Language Models via Latent Personality Traits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07918)

Method: 采用心理学人格量表中的66个无害陈述作为训练样本，通过对抗训练稳定其潜在表示，利用人格特征与危害规避之间的潜在结构关联，间接约束被攻击者利用的子空间。

Abstract: Current safety methods for large language models are known to be vulnerable to adversarial attacks, motivating research into robust alternatives. Latent Adversarial Training (LAT) is among the most effective defenses, but can degrade utility and requires training on large datasets of harmful prompts. We introduce Latent Personality Alignment (LPA), which replaces explicit harm refusal with adversarial training on just 66 harm-agnostic statements drawn from psychometric personality literature. We hypothesize that personality-anchored representations share latent structure with harm avoidance, so adversarially stabilizing them implicitly constrains the subspace exploited by jailbreak attacks. LPA achieves near-zero attack success rates on HarmBench across direct requests and five jailbreak methods, despite never seeing harmful content during training and no loss of performance on standard benchmarks. Moreover, the training process is lightweight; the entire procedure completes in minutes on a single GPU and uses 75x fewer examples than standard LAT. Extensive ablations demonstrate the robustness, efficiency, and generalization of our method.

### [146] [path_boost: A Python Package for Interpretable Graph-Level Prediction using Path-Based Gradient Boosting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07935)
*Claudio Meggio,Johan Pensar,Riccardo De Bin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: path_boost 是一个用于图结构数据可解释监督学习的 Python 包，实现 PathBoost 算法，通过自动发现图中具有预测能力的标签路径进行建模。该方法利用梯度提升迭代选择和扩展路径，避免穷举所有路径，生成可解释的加性模型，支持回归与二分类任务，并兼容 scikit-learn 工作流，具备并行训练、自定义基学习器与重要性分析等功能。在过渡金属化合物分子性质预测等任务中表现优异，优于现有 GNN 与图核方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统图神经网络缺乏可解释性，而路径特征虽具解释性但需枚举所有路径导致计算成本高。本文旨在开发一种既能保持高预测性能又具备强可解释性的图学习方法，通过自动发现关键路径来揭示预测依据。

Method: 提出 PathBoost 算法，基于梯度提升框架，迭代选择具有高预测力的路径并扩展其长度，构建加性模型；使用路径作为特征，结合弱学习器形成强集成模型；引入自动起始节点选择、并行训练及变量重要性计算机制。

Result: 在六种分子数据集上，PathBoost 在预测性能上优于或相当于是图神经网络与图核方法，且能明确揭示影响预测的关键子结构路径，在可解释性方面显著优于黑箱模型。

Conclusion: PathBoost 为图结构数据提供了一种高效、可解释的监督学习方案，尤其适用于需要理解预测依据的科学领域，如药物设计与材料发现。

Abstract: We present path_boost, a Python package for interpretable supervised learning on graph-structured input data. The package implements PathBoost, a gradient boosting algorithm that automatically discovers predictive labeled paths within graphs during the learning process. Unlike graph neural networks, which are generally difficult to interpret, PathBoost produces an additive prediction model over path-based features that explicitly reveals which substructures drive predictions. To avoid an exhaustive enumeration of all possible paths, the algorithm iteratively selects and extends paths during learning based on their predictive power, using boosting to combine weak learners into a strong ensemble. The package supports both regression and binary classification. Key features include compatibility with scikit-learn workflows, support for custom base learners and selectors, automatic starting node selection, parallel training across anchor nodes, and built-in variable importance computation. We demonstrate PathBoost on molecular property prediction of transition metal compounds, where atoms serve as nodes and bonds as edges, and further benchmark PathBoost against an established graph neural network and a graph kernel method across six molecular datasets. The package is available on PyPI and GitHub under an open-source license.

### [147] [Evaluating the Generalizability of Foundation Models for Extreme Environmental Events: Case Study of California Wildfire PM2.5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07951)
*Yongcan Huang,Li Jiang,Ze Yu Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地比较了六种时间序列基础模型（TSFM）配置与全训练基线模型在预测加州12年（2013–2025）期间1,375次野火事件中每小时PM₂.₅浓度方面的表现，采用留一事件外（LOIO）评估策略，涵盖6、12、24小时预测范围。结果表明，尽管微调后的TSFMs性能显著提升，但所有基础模型均未超越传统训练好的循环神经网络（如BiLSTM）在所有指标上的表现，尤其在极端污染事件（如危害级>225.5 μg/m³）的预测上，其F1得分最高仅为0.63，而零样本模型普遍表现不佳，甚至出现严重误差波动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前野火烟雾导致的极端PM₂.₅浓度对公共健康构成重大威胁，但准确预测罕见且危险的浓度峰值仍是关键挑战。尽管时间序列基础模型（TSFMs）在通用基准上表现优异，但其在极端分布外条件下的行为尚不明确，亟需系统评估其在真实环境灾害场景中的适用性。

Method: 构建了一个覆盖1,375次野火事件、79个监测站点、12年（2013–2025）的高分辨率小时级PM₂.₅数据集；采用留一事件外（LOIO）协议评估模型对未见火灾事件的泛化能力；对比六种TSFM配置（包括零样本和LoRA微调版本）与传统模型（LSTM、BiLSTM、Transformer）及朴素持续性方法；使用MAE、RMSE和超过美国环保署空气质量指数（AQI）阈值的超出事件F1分数作为评价指标，覆盖6、12、24小时预测窗口。

Result: BiLSTM在所有预测时长和指标上表现最佳，达到最低MAE（5.16 μg/m³）和最高的超出事件F1，尤其在危害级污染（>225.5 μg/m³）下达0.63，优于任何基础模型（最高0.54）。零样本TSFMs仅小幅优于持续性预测，其中零样本Chronos-2表现出严重的尾部误差不稳定（RMSE达23.4 μg/m³，R²为负），而LoRA微调显著改善了性能并修复了稳定性问题，但仍未超越训练过的循环模型。

Conclusion: 研究挑战了‘更大预训练模型在环境预测中必然占优’的假设，揭示了当前基础模型在极端事件预测中的局限性，并为野火空气质量管理中的模型部署提供了实证指导：在关键公共卫生应用中，仍应优先考虑经过充分训练的传统模型，而非直接依赖零样本或轻量微调的基础模型。

Abstract: Wildfire smoke events produce extreme PM$_{2.5}$ concentrations that pose severe public health risks, yet forecasting rare, hazardous-level spikes remains a fundamental challenge. Time series foundation models (TSFMs), pretrained models offering zero-shot inference and efficient adaptation, perform strongly on general benchmarks, but their behavior under extreme out-of-distribution conditions is poorly understood. We present the first systematic benchmark comparing six TSFM configurations (zero-shot TimesFM, Chronos-2, Moirai-2, and Time-MoE, plus LoRA fine-tuned Chronos-2 and Time-MoE) against fully-trained baselines (LSTM, BiLSTM, Transformer) and naive persistence on a 12-year (2013--2025) hourly PM$_{2.5}$ dataset covering 1,375 wildfire incidents across 79 California monitoring sites. A leave-one-incident-out (LOIO) protocol evaluates generalization to unseen fires, using MAE, RMSE, and exceedance F1 at EPA AQI thresholds across 6-, 12-, and 24-hour horizons. Results reveal a consistent hierarchy. The BiLSTM achieves the lowest MAE ($5.16\,μg/m^3$) and the highest exceedance F1 at every threshold, including the Hazardous band ($>225.5\,μg/m^3$), reaching 0.63 versus at most 0.54 for any foundation model. Zero-shot TSFMs improve on persistence only modestly, and zero-shot Chronos-2 exhibits severe RMSE tail instability ($23.4\,μg/m^3$, negative $R^2$) from sporadic large errors. LoRA fine-tuning substantially improves both adapted families and largely repairs this instability, yet no foundation model surpasses the trained recurrent baselines on any metric. These findings challenge the assumption that larger pretrained models universally dominate environmental forecasting and provide actionable deployment guidance for wildfire air quality prediction.

### [148] [Linear Attention Architectures: Mechanisms, Trade-offs, and Cross-Layer Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07953)
*Tommaso Cerruti,Tim Rieder,George Rowlands,Lingfeng Jin,Imanol Schlag*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究对比了softmax注意力与四种新型循环线性注意力架构（DeltaNet、Gated DeltaNet、Kimi Delta Attention、Gated DeltaNet-2），通过统一的循环记忆表示揭示其在表达能力、记忆衰减、擦除与写入控制、训练吞吐量及实现复杂度上的差异。实验基于3.5亿参数模型在150亿标记数据上进行，涵盖优化器与学习率比较、混合栈与纯栈对比、序列长度运行时测试、更大规模的DeltaNet模型（13亿和30亿参数）以及少量下游评估。结果表明，在相同设置下，Kimi Delta Attention配合Muon优化器达到最低验证损失；纯Gated DeltaNet栈使用AdamW具有最高训练吞吐量；混合栈通常以牺牲吞吐量换取更低损失；Muon相比AdamW在多数情况下进一步降低验证损失。研究还引入轻量级跨层路由机制，发现将低层的写入误差传递至高层值目标无提升效果，而将写入值传入对齐隐藏流（即跨层值路由，CLVR）可带来小幅性能改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自注意力机制虽能捕获全局上下文信息，但其二次方时间复杂度限制了长序列的训练与推理效率。为突破这一瓶颈，亟需高效且可扩展的替代方案。本文旨在系统评估几种新兴的线性注意力架构，揭示其内在机制差异，并探索提升性能的有效策略。

Method: 将五种注意力机制（softmax注意力与四种线性注意力）统一表述为循环记忆形式，分析其在表达能力、记忆管理、训练效率等方面的特性；通过大规模语言模型训练实验（3.5亿参数，150亿标记），对比不同架构、优化器、栈结构与超参数配置；引入跨层路由机制（如CLVR），评估其对模型性能的影响。

Result: Kimi Delta Attention配合Muon优化器在3.5亿参数模型中取得最低验证损失；纯Gated DeltaNet栈使用AdamW实现最高训练吞吐量；混合栈结构在损失上优于纯栈但代价是吞吐量下降；Muon优化器普遍优于AdamW；跨层值路由（CLVR）在匹配实验中对DeltaNet和Gated DeltaNet均带来轻微性能提升。

Conclusion: 尽管各类线性注意力架构在效率上具备优势，但其性能表现仍受优化器与结构设计影响显著。通过合理选择优化器（如Muon）和引入有效的跨层路由机制（如CLVR），可在保持高训练吞吐量的同时有效提升模型精度。该研究为长序列建模提供了实用的架构与训练策略参考。

Abstract: Self-attention lets each token retrieve information from the full context, but its quadratic cost in sequence length limits training and inference at long context. This paper presents a comparative study of softmax attention and four recent recurrent linear-attention architectures: DeltaNet, Gated DeltaNet, Kimi Delta Attention, and Gated DeltaNet-2. We express these mechanisms in a common recurrent-memory notation, making explicit how they differ in expressivity, memory decay, erase and write control, training throughput, and implementation complexity. Our experiments center on 350M-parameter models trained for 15B tokens, and include optimizer and learning-rate comparisons, hybrid-versus-pure stack comparisons, sequence-length runtime measurements, larger DeltaNet runs at 1.3B and 3B parameters, and a small set of downstream evaluations. The reported speed results measure training throughput and iteration time; we do not provide an empirical inference-speed benchmark. Within the reported 350M-parameter, 15B-token sweep, Kimi Delta Attention with Muon reaches the lowest final validation loss, a pure Gated DeltaNet stack trained with AdamW has the highest normalized training throughput, hybrid stacks generally improve loss at a throughput cost, and Muon consistently lowers final validation loss relative to AdamW in the matched architecture settings we evaluate. We introduce and evaluate lightweight cross-layer routing mechanisms for DeltaNet-style memories. The most natural DeltaNet-inspired formulation, forwarding a lower layer's delta-rule write error into the next layer's value target, does not improve over matched baselines. Routing into the aligned hidden stream and forwarding the write value instead yields a modest improvement in the matched runs we report: Cross-Layer Value Routing (CLVR) lowers final validation loss for both DeltaNet and Gated DeltaNet.

### [149] [KronQ: LLM Quantization via Kronecker-Factored Hessian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07964)
*Donghyun Lee,Yuhang Li,Ruokai Yin,Priyadarshini Panda*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KronQ提出一种新的后训练量化框架，通过引入梯度协方差打破传统方法仅依赖输入激活统计的假设。它在双向不相干性处理和跨层混合精度分配方面实现改进，显著提升量化性能，在LLaMA-3-70B 2-bit量化下达到7.93困惑度，远超GPTQ和GPTAQ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有二阶后训练量化方法（如GPTQ）仅基于输入激活统计构建量化目标，假设所有输出通道对重建贡献相同，忽略了梯度信息的影响，导致量化质量下降，尤其在极端低比特下易出现发散或退化。

Method: KronQ基于克罗内克积近似赫斯蒂安矩阵，联合利用激活协方差与梯度协方差构建量化损失；提出双向不相干处理（扩展随机旋转至输出维度），并设计基于梯度与激活赫斯蒂安迹的新敏感性度量用于混合精度分配。

Result: 在LLaMA-3-70B 2-bit权重量化下，KronQ实现7.93的困惑度，而GPTQ和GPTAQ出现发散（>2000困惑度），证明其在极低比特压缩下的优越稳定性与精度。

Conclusion: KronQ通过融合梯度协方差，有效提升了后训练量化在极端低比特条件下的性能与鲁棒性，为大模型压缩提供了新范式。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) is a widely adopted technique for compressing large language models (LLMs) without retraining. Existing second-order PTQ methods, including GPTQ, construct quantization objectives exclusively from input activation statistics, effectively assuming that all output channels contribute equally to the layer-wise reconstruction objective. We propose KronQ, a PTQ framework that challenges this assumption by introducing the gradient covariance into the quantization pipeline. Under the Kronecker-factored Hessian approximation, the quantization loss depends jointly on both the activation and gradient covariances, and KronQ exploits this at two complementary levels. (1) KronQ introduces bidirectional incoherence processing, extending the existing input-side random rotation to the output dimension using the gradient covariance, reducing weight magnitude variance across both input and output dimensions. (2) KronQ derives a new sensitivity metric for inter-layer mixed-precision allocation, driven by the gradient and activation Hessian traces. Notably, in the case of 2-bit weight-only quantization on LLaMA-3-70B, while GPTQ and GPTAQ diverge or produce degenerate quantizations (>2000 perplexity on WikiText-2), KronQ achieves 7.93 perplexity.

### [150] [Provably Optimal Learning Algorithms for Assistance Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08012)
*Nivasini Ananthakrishnan,Mark Bedaywi,Michael I. Jordan,Stuart Russell,Nika Haghtalab*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了辅助博弈框架的在线变体，其中知情代理（人类）和非知情代理（助手）在 $T$ 个时间步中反复交互以优化共同奖励函数。知情代理观察世界隐状态，而非知情代理仅观察人类的动作。本文提出了首个可证明高效的在线学习算法，引入了‘辅助遗憾’概念，衡量实际交互累积效用与最优联合策略（映射隐状态到动作对）之间的差距。提出去中心化算法，使人类和助手均达到 $(1-1/e)$-近似遗憾率 $\widetilde{O}(T^{3/4})$，且运行时间在动作和状态空间大小上为多项式。该算法具有通用性，可兼容任意无遗憾算法。证明了优于 $(1-1/e)$ 的近似因子在计算上不可行。此外，通过共享随机串，可将算法调整至伪去中心化设置，实现 $\widetilde{O}(T^{1/2})$ 的最优遗憾率（对数因子内）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在人机协作场景中，人类通常掌握完整环境信息，而机器助手仅能观察人类行为。如何设计高效、可证明性能的协作学习机制，使双方在长期交互中逼近最优联合策略，是关键挑战。现有方法缺乏理论保障，尤其在动态、不确定环境下。因此需要构建一个兼具理论严谨性和实用性的在线学习框架，以应对实际应用中的信息不对称问题。

Method: 提出基于辅助遗憾的分析框架，设计去中心化学习算法，利用无遗憾学习机制更新人类与助手的策略；引入共享随机字符串实现伪去中心化，降低遗憾率；通过组合优化与概率分析证明算法的近似性能边界。

Result: 实现了 $(1-1/e)$-近似辅助遗憾率 $\\widetilde{O}(T^{3/4})$，在伪去中心化设置下达到最优的 $\\widetilde{O}(T^{1/2})$ 遗憾率；证明了优于 $(1-1/e)$ 的近似因子在计算上不可行，表明算法性能已达到理论极限。

Conclusion: 本文首次建立了在线辅助博弈的可证明高效学习框架，提供了具有理论保证的去中心化与伪去中心化算法，揭示了性能上限，并展示了其在人机协作中的广泛适用性。

Abstract: This paper studies an online variant of the assistance games framework, where an informed agent and an uninformed agent repeatedly interact over $T$ timesteps to optimize a common reward function. While the informed agent (the human) observes a latent state of the world, the uninformed agent (the assistant) observes only the human's actions. We provide the first provably efficient learning algorithms for repeated assistance games. We introduce the notion of assistance regret: the gap between the cumulative utility of interactions and that of the optimal joint policies in hindsight, which map latent states to action pairs. We present decentralized algorithms for both the human and the assistant that achieve a $(1-1/e)$-approximate assistance regret rate of $\widetilde{O}(T^{3/4})$, with runtime polynomial in the size of the action and state spaces. These algorithms are general; in particular, they accommodate any no-regret algorithm for the assistant. We prove that achieving a regret approximation factor better than $(1-1/e)$ is computationally intractable. Furthermore, we demonstrate how these generic no-regret algorithms can be tailored to a pseudo-decentralized setting -- using a shared random string -- to achieve a rate of $\widetilde{O}(T^{1/2})$, optimal up to logarithmic factors.

</details>


### [151] [Collate: Collaborative Neural Network Learning for Latency-Critical Edge Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08013)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习优化主要关注训练效率，但忽视了在真实边缘系统中因设备异构性导致的推理延迟问题，尤其在存在严格延迟约束时表现不佳。因此需要一种能同时满足多系统延迟要求并保持高精度的新方法。

Method: 设计动态零化-恢复机制以自适应调整本地模型结构，使其在特定延迟约束下保持高精度；提出原型修正的联邦聚合策略，实现对异构模型的有效聚合，仅需一次训练过程即可适配多种延迟需求。

Result: 实验表明，在延迟约束条件下，相比现有最优方法，扩展模型平均提升1.96%准确率，压缩模型平均提升3.09%准确率，且训练开销几乎不变。

Conclusion: Collate成功实现了在异构边缘系统中协同训练满足延迟约束的多样化模型，兼顾推理速度与精度，为实际部署中的联邦学习提供了高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) empowers multiple clients to collaboratively learn a model, enlarging the training data of each client for high accuracy while protecting data privacy. However, when deploying FL in real-time edge systems, the heterogeneity of devices among systems has a severe impact on the performance of the inferred model. Existing optimizations on FL focus on improving the training efficiency but fail to speed up inference, especially when there is a latency constraint. In this work, we propose Collate, a novel training framework that collaboratively learns heterogeneous models to meet the latency constraints of multiple edge systems simultaneously. We design a dynamic zeroizing-recovering method to adjust each local model architecture for high accuracy under its latency constraint. A proto-corrected federated aggregation scheme is also introduced to aggregate all heterogeneous local models, satisfying the latency constraint of different systems with only one training process and maintaining high accuracy. Extensive experiments indicate that, compared to state-of-the-art methods and under a latency constraint, our extended models can improve the accuracy by 1.96% on average, and our shrunk models can also obtain a 3.09% accuracy improvement on average, with almost no extra training overhead. The related codes and data will be available at https://github.com/ntuliuteam/Collate

Method: 提出PGD-NO神经算子，采用预计算几何分解策略，通过迭代几何分解算法提取几何令牌，实现特征提取与解查询的解耦，降低运行时内存开销，提升可扩展性。

Abstract: While neural PDE solvers have demonstrated significant potential for accelerating engineering simulations, existing architectures remain constrained by high memory consumption and the single node bottleneck, where the maximum processable mesh resolution is strictly limited by the VRAM of a single compute unit. To address these challenges, we propose PGD-NO, a neural operator with Precomputed Geometry Decomposition, that relocates the computational overhead of geometric encoding to a deterministic pre-computation phase. By utilizing an iterative geometry decomposition algorithm to extract geometry tokens, our model decouples feature extraction from solution querying. This architecture enables linear memory scalability, allowing high fidelity learning on meshes exceeding 10 million nodes, a scale where existing architectures typically encounter memory exhaustion. PGD-NO demonstrates competitive predictive accuracy across diverse industrial benchmarks and provides intrinsic interpretability through attention mechanisms. By effectively overcoming traditional mesh-size constraints, PGD-NO offers a robust and efficient solution for the next generation of large-scale, high-fidelity industrial design applications.

### [153] [Rethinking Small VLM Quantization: From Component-Wise Analysis to Hardware-Aware Edge Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08029)
*Hyeju Shin,Chorwon Kim,Ryangsoo Kim,Hark Yoo,Jaein Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种系统评估框架，针对六种量化配置在Jetson Orin NX和AGX平台上的五个假设进行实证验证。研究发现：（1）量化敏感性由结构范式（MoE vs. dense）决定而非规模；（2）SigLIP编码器在Jetson Ampere上导致显著的INT8延迟，是部署相关的硬件-内核-编码器交互问题；（3）LLM的INT4量化虽降低显存占用但增加解量化开销，减慢生成速度；（4）复合量化误差基本可加，但模态对齐路径存在架构依赖性；（5）能效比因内存带宽限制在不同平台上差异显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前小型视觉语言模型在设备端部署中快速发展，但组件级量化机制缺乏深入理解，制约了最优部署性能。为解决这一瓶颈，需系统评估量化策略对多模态模型各组件的影响。

Method: 构建系统评估框架，分离视觉编码器、投影模块与大语言模型主干网络，分别测试五种量化配置在两种边缘计算平台上的表现，并分析量化敏感性、延迟、能耗及误差传播特性。

Result: 量化敏感性主要受模型结构范式影响（如MoE优于密集结构），特定硬件组合下存在非预期延迟（如SigLIP+Jetson Ampere），INT4量化虽节省显存但引入解量化开销，复合误差近似可加但模态对齐路径例外，能效比受内存带宽显著影响。

Conclusion: 量化策略的选择必须结合模型结构、硬件平台和任务需求综合权衡，不能仅依赖参数规模或通用量化规则。未来部署应考虑硬件-模型协同优化。

Abstract: The emergence of vision language models with fewer than 3 billion parameters has accelerated the implementation of on-device multimodal intelligence. However, a detailed understanding of component-wise quantization remains a bottleneck for optimal deployment. This paper presents a systematic evaluation framework for empirically validating five hypotheses across six quantization configurations on the Jetson Orin NX and AGX. By separating the vision encoder, projector, and large language model backbone yields the following results: (1) Quantization sensitivity is governed by the structural paradigm (MoE vs. dense) rather than scale alone, with MoE backbones mitigating INT4 noise where dense backbones degrade; (2) SigLIP encoders incur disproportionate INT8 latency on Jetson Ampere--a deployment-specific encoder-kernel-hardware interaction, not a SigLIP flaw; (3) Although INT4 quantization of LLMs greatly reduces VRAM consumption, it also causes slower token generation due to dequantization overhead; (4) Composite quantization errors are largely additive, except along the modality-alignment path, which is architecture-dependent; (5) The intelligence-per-joule profile varies significantly across platforms owing to memory bandwidth constraints.
