### [154] [What to Keep, What to Forget: A Rate--Distortion View of Memory Compaction in LLMs and Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08032)
*Ashwin Gerard Colaco,Nada Lahjouji*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将大语言模型中不同层次的内存压缩问题统一为一个率-失真优化问题，即在资源预算下决定保留或丢弃哪些上下文信息及其保真度，以维持下游任务效用。作者构建了一个七轴分类体系，统一了从KV缓存到代理长期记忆等不同层面的压缩方法，并提出了跨层机制迁移的思路。研究发现：各层级均依赖注意力强度或时间新近性作为决策信号，但这一策略因在查询未知时即丢弃信息且无法撤销而普遍失效。此外，现有评估多聚焦单轮长上下文压缩，缺乏对代理重复压缩行为的系统评测，且无基准能同时控制所有层级的资源预算。基于此，作者提出新的基准设计、参考实验及一系列压缩感知的设计原则，并梳理出未来关键开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型及其代理在计算和内存上越来越依赖于记忆管理（如缓存注意力键值、携带长提示、维护递归状态、存储历史交互），现有研究虽在不同领域独立发展出压缩技术（如KV缓存淘汰/量化、提示剪枝/蒸馏、架构状态约束、代理记忆整合），但缺乏统一视角。这些方法本质上都涉及在有限资源下权衡保留与丢弃上下文信息的决策，因此亟需一个统一的理论框架来揭示其共性并推动跨层创新。

Method: 提出统一的压缩目标函数与分层无关的下界，建立七轴分类体系，用于系统化地组织和比较跨栈方法；通过分析各层级决策信号的共性与缺陷，识别出‘预判性丢失’的核心问题；进而设计新型基准方案，涵盖多层资源预算协同控制，并提供小规模参考实验验证有效性；最后提炼出一系列面向压缩感知的系统设计原则。

Result: 成功将分散的压缩技术统一到一个理论框架下，揭示了跨层决策信号的共性和根本缺陷；提出的七轴分类体系可有效归类现有方法；新基准与参考实验展示了评估重复压缩行为的重要性；设计原则为未来系统设计提供了指导方向；明确了多个尚未解决的关键挑战。

Conclusion: 大语言模型中的内存管理本质上是率-失真优化问题，应通过统一框架进行建模与优化。当前方法在决策时机与不可逆性上存在系统性缺陷，亟需引入更智能的预测与回溯机制。未来工作应在多层资源约束下建立统一评测基准，并发展具备前瞻性的压缩策略。

Abstract: Large language models, and the agents built on them, spend an ever-growing share of their compute and memory on remembering: caching attention keys and values, carrying long prompts, maintaining recurrent state, and storing what happened in previous turns and sessions. Because none of this memory is free, four largely separate research communities have each learned to compact it. They evict or quantize the KV cache, prune or distill prompts, bound architectural state, and consolidate agent memory. We argue that these are instances of one problem: a rate--distortion decision about what context-derived information to retain versus discard, at what fidelity, under a resource budget, so as to preserve downstream task utility. We make this lens precise with a single compaction objective and a layer-agnostic lower bound, use it to build a seven-axis taxonomy that classifies methods from across the stack uniformly, and use it to transfer mechanisms between layers that have never been connected, from serving-stack KV management to agent long-term memory. Two patterns hold across the survey. At every layer the signal that decides what to keep is attention magnitude or recency, and it fails in the same way everywhere, by discarding, before the query is known and with no way to undo it, information the query later needs. And while compression is measured carefully on single-turn long context, the repeated compaction that agents actually perform is almost never measured, and no benchmark holds one budget axis across all the layers at once. We turn both observations into a benchmark proposal, a small reference experiment, and a set of compaction-aware design principles, and we map the open problems.

</details>


### [155] [An exact information theory of generalization phase transitions in Bayesian diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08041)
*Henry Hunt,Mason Kamb,Surya Ganguli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种可解析的贝叶斯信息受限扩散模型（BIRD），通过限制每个像素对噪声数据的观测信息，揭示了扩散模型如何在有限训练数据下学习高维复杂分布而不只是记忆。研究发现，当受限观测与训练数据之间的互信息超过训练样本数量的对数时，模型会进入记忆状态；否则则实现泛化。实验验证了这一信息论相变边界的存在，并表明生成过程始终接近记忆-泛化的临界边缘。信息限制是生成模型克服维度灾难的关键机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解扩散模型如何在高维空间中从有限数据中学习复杂分布，而非简单记忆，是当前生成模型的核心挑战之一。特别是如何避免维度灾难，需要深入探究其内在机制。

Method: 提出贝叶斯信息受限扩散模型（BIRD），通过在反向生成过程中利用贝叶斯后验推断当前受限观测来自哪个历史训练样本。该方法扩展了以往基于局部信息限制的解析扩散模型，并引入信息论分析框架以刻画记忆与泛化的边界。

Result: BIRD模型在早期训练阶段能很好地近似真实扩散模型，且在不同架构（如UNet、DiT）上表现一致。理论和实验均证实存在一个由数据量、生成时间与信息限制程度共同决定的信息论相变边界：当互信息超过log(训练样本数)时模型记忆数据，否则泛化。生成过程始终靠近该边界，表明信息限制随时间增加。

Conclusion: 信息限制是扩散模型克服高维空间中维度灾难的根本机制。生成过程通过动态减少信息观测来维持在记忆与泛化的临界边缘，从而实现高效且泛化的生成能力。

Abstract: How diffusion models circumvent the curse of dimensionality to learn complex distributions over high dimensional spaces from a finite training set, instead of memorizing it, remains a fundamental mystery. To address this, we introduce analytically tractable Bayesian information restricted diffusion (BIRD) models, in which each pixel observes restricted information about noisy data. A BIRD model time-reverses diffusion by inferring which past training sample produced its current restricted observation using the Bayesian posterior. This model class generalizes existing analytical diffusion models that use spatially local information restriction. We show that spatially local BIRD models closely approximate trained diffusion models \textit{early in training}, across different architectures such as UNets and DiTs. Under minimal assumptions on the data distribution, we identify an information-theoretic phase boundary between memorization and generalization in the joint space of amount of training data, time in the reverse generative process, and amount of information restriction: a BIRD model memorizes when the mutual information between its restricted noisy observations and the training data exceeds the log number of training points, and it generalizes otherwise. Experiments across a range of datasets confirm our theoretically predicted location for the transition. We find that generation proceeds near the edge of memorization: both spatially local BIRD models and early-training diffusion models track the memorization-generalization phase boundary by increasingly restricting information over time. Overall, our results reveal a fundamental role for information restriction in generative AI to circumvent the curse of dimensionality.

</details>


### [156] [Who Analyses the Analyser? Self-Validating LLM Hazard Analysis with Constitutional Meta-STPA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08054)
*Samuel Tetteh,Udip Shrestha,Joshua R. Waite,Cody Fleming*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为《宪法型元STPA》的LLM辅助安全分析工具，通过将系统理论过程分析（STPA）应用于自身，实现对AI辅助安全工具的自我审视。该方法构建了一个闭环机制，从工具的设计中自动生成21条工具原则与8条元安全原则，并将其绑定至代码执行点，形成可审计的治理宪章。研究通过形式化定义‘宪章边际覆盖率’算子，验证了覆盖度与模型或扫描器无关的可靠性，并报告四项发现：(i) 自我推导能力——前沿模型组合可恢复全部8条治理原则及18/21条规范原则；(ii) 元层受限于模型能力而非宪章设计；(iii) 相同治理原则在另一独立开发工具中重现；(iv) 该方法具备可复现、可验证和可审计的特性，为解决大模型在安全分析中的幻觉与不可追溯问题提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型被广泛用于生成安全分析中的关键文档（如损失、危害、不安全控制行为和约束），但忽视了这些工具本身作为安全相关系统的潜在风险——可能产生虚构标准、不可验证的约束且缺乏审计轨迹。本文旨在回应一个被长期忽略的核心问题：谁来分析分析者？

Method: 提出《宪法型元STPA》框架，采用元STPA对AI辅助安全工具进行自我分析，通过从损失→危害→不安全控制行为→约束的链路自动生成治理宪章，形成由21条工具原则与8条元安全原则组成的可执行宪法，并引入宪章边际覆盖率算子以确保结果的可验证性与独立性。

Result: 实验表明，前沿模型组合能恢复18/21条标准原则和全部8/8条治理原则，且相同治理原则在另一独立工具中重复出现，证明该方法具备自洽性与可复现性；同时，覆盖率不受模型或扫描器影响，具有良好的稳定性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究首次将系统理论过程分析（STPA）应用于大语言模型辅助的安全分析工具本身，实现了从‘自我生成’到‘自我监管’的跃迁。所提出的宪法型元STPA不仅解决了工具幻觉与不可审计的问题，还为未来可信AI安全工具的构建提供了可验证、可复制、可审计的新范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly trusted to draft the artifacts of safety analysis such as, losses, hazards, Unsafe Control Actions (UCAs), and safety constraints, inside rigorous processes such as Systems-Theoretic Process Analysis (STPA). Yet a blind spot runs through this fast-growing literature: every system gets analysed except the LLM-assisted tool doing the analysing, which is itself a safety-relevant system that can hallucinate standards, emit unverifiable constraints, and leave no audit trail from prompt to artifact. We take seriously the question the field has skipped -- {who analyses the analyser?} and answer it by turning STPA on the tool itself. We present \{Constitutional Meta-STPA}, an LLM-assisted STPA tool built around a closed loop: the tool runs a {meta-STPA} of the class of AI-assisted safety tools and {derives} rather than asserts, its governance constitution from the resulting loss$\to$hazard$\to$UCA$\to$constraint chain, yielding a published constitution of $21$ Tool Principles and $8$ Meta-Safety Principles, each bound to a code enforcement point. We formalise the measured object as a constitution-marginal coverage operator over a principle set $P$ ($|P|{=}29$) with a soundness lemma that isolates coverage from model and scanner, and report four findings. {(i)~Self-derivation:} a frontier ensemble ({claude-opus-4.8}${+}${claude-sonnet-4}) recovers $18/21$ canonical and all $8/8$ governance principles from the tool's own design, while a weaker pair recovers $12/21$ and $3/8$, so the meta layer is model-limited, not constitution-limited, and the same $8/8$ re-emerge from a second, independently authored tool.

</details>


### [157] [Reinforcing the Generation Order of Multimodal Masked Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08056)
*Yidong Ouyang,Zhe Wang,Sourav Bhabesh,Dmitriy Bespalov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了扩散语言模型（DLMs）在文本到图像合成与多模态理解中的生成顺序优化问题。发现仅依赖模型logits无法确定最优生成序列，提出通过组相对策略优化（GRPO）训练可学习的控制模块来动态决定生成顺序。该方法显著提升了文本到图像对齐与多模态理解性能，尤其增强了对图像中细粒度空间关系的捕捉能力，并在GenEval和VLMEvalKit基准上分别取得4.08%和4.85%的相对提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖模型logits确定生成顺序，在文本到图像合成和多模态理解任务中表现不足，难以有效捕捉复杂空间与语义关系，因此需要一种更灵活、可学习的生成顺序控制机制。

Method: 引入一个可学习的控制模块，利用组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行训练，以动态决定生成顺序，从而优化扩散语言模型在文本到图像生成与多模态理解中的表现。

Result: 在GenEval基准上实现4.08%的相对改进，在VLMEvalKit上实现4.85%的相对改进；显著增强模型对图像中细粒度空间关系的建模能力及多模态推理与理解性能。

Conclusion: 通过学习生成顺序控制模块，能够有效提升扩散语言模型在文本到图像合成与多模态理解任务中的表现，验证了生成顺序优化在复杂跨模态任务中的关键作用。

Abstract: Diffusion Language Models (DLMs) have recently achieved substantial progress in natural language generation tasks. Recent research demonstrates that adaptive token generation ordering can significantly improve performance in mathematical reasoning and code synthesis applications. In this work, we investigate the optimization of generation order for both text-to-image synthesis and multimodal understanding. We first establish that, unlike structured problems in language generation such as Sudoku puzzles, model logits alone are insufficient for determining optimal generation sequences in text-to-image generation and multimodal understanding. To address this challenge, we introduce a learnable control module trained via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to determine the generation order. Our results demonstrate that learning this control block substantially improves both text-to-image alignment and multimodal understanding in DLMs. In particular, it enhances the model's ability to capture fine-grained spatial relationships in generated images while also strengthening performance on multimodal reasoning and comprehension tasks. We evaluate our framework on GenEval, an object-focused benchmark for text-to-image alignment, where it achieves 4.08% relative improvements. In addition, experiments on VLMEvalKit confirm 4.85% relative improvements in multimodal understanding, highlighting the broad effectiveness of our approach.

### [159] [When Thinking Hurts: Epistemic Signals in the Reasoning Chains of Visual Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08059)
*Mayank Singal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次对思考模式下视觉语言模型（VLMs）的答案熵行为进行了三类实证分析。在相同对抗样本上测试四个模型，发现三种不同模式：Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking出现完全熵崩溃（答案熵AUROC=0.492），GLM-4.1V-9B-Thinking无崩溃（0.716），InternVL3-8B则表现出选择性思考（仅50%样本生成链路，完整与仅思考链的熵分别为0.675和0.602）。在生成思维链的样本中，思维链熵始终优于答案熵（0.647、0.759、0.608对比0.492、0.716、0.602），表明链路信号更可靠。在VQA-v2数据集上的小规模验证也显示链熵优于答案熵（0.680 vs 0.595），尤其在自由回答任务中差距更大（0.733 vs 0.467）。在复杂推理任务（HallusionBench）中，所有模型表现中等（约0.64），反映困难问题下预承诺不充分。研究还发现结构化回避现象影响12%-22%查询，且偏向缺失对象类问题；引入实用的回避门机制后，在无额外计算成本下将准确率从71.0%提升至93.8%，覆盖率达62.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型的不确定性量化主要聚焦于答案令牌分布，但缺乏对思考模式下模型行为的系统性理解。特别是对思维链生成过程中的熵动态及其与预测可靠性关系的研究不足。本文旨在揭示思考模式下答案熵的真实行为特征，并探索更可靠的不确定性指标，以提升模型鲁棒性与可信度。

Method: 在相同对抗样本（POPE）上运行四款思考模式视觉语言模型，分析其答案熵与思维链熵的变化模式；通过三类实验设计验证结果：1）跨模型比较不同熵行为模式；2）在子集上比较链熵与答案熵的预测性能；3）在VQA-v2和HallusionBench等基准上进行小规模验证。同时引入结构化回避机制并评估其对准确率的影响。

Result: 发现三类典型熵行为模式：完全崩溃（Qwen）、无崩溃（GLM）、选择性思考（InternVL3）。思维链熵在生成链的样本中显著优于答案熵，尤其在Qwen和GLM中优势明显。在真实数据集（VQA-v2）上，链熵仍优于答案熵，且在自由回答任务中差距最大。在复杂推理任务中，信号中等，反映模型预承诺不充分。结构化回避机制可有效提升准确率，实现高精度与高覆盖率的平衡。

Conclusion: 思维链熵是比答案熵更可靠的不确定性指标，尤其在链路生成时。引入结构化回避机制可在不增加计算成本的情况下显著提升模型准确率。未来应关注如何优化模型在困难任务中的预承诺能力，并构建基于链路信号的统一不确定性评估框架。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification for visual language models (VLMs) conventionally targets the answer token distribution. We provide the first three-family empirical characterisation of answer entropy behaviour in thinking-mode VLMs. Running four models on identical POPE adversarial samples, we find three qualitatively distinct patterns: Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking shows complete collapse (ans H AUROC = 0.492); GLM-4.1V-9B-Thinking shows no collapse (0.716); and InternVL3-8B shows selective thinking (chains on only 50% of samples, ans H = 0.675 full / 0.602 thinking-only). Across all three thinking-mode models, thinking chain entropy outperforms answer entropy on the subset where chains are generated (0.647, 0.759, 0.608 vs. 0.492, 0.716, 0.602 respectively), suggesting chain signals are the more reliable predictor whenever chains are present. This holds strongly for Qwen and GLM, but with only marginal and statistically unreliable advantage for InternVL3 (n_FP = 17). A 300-sample VQAv2 pilot confirms chain entropy (0.680) outperforms answer entropy (0.595) on VQAv2 questions, with the gap largest for free-form answers (0.733 vs. 0.467). On harder reasoning tasks (HallusionBench) both Qwen models show moderate signal (approx. 0.64), consistent with incomplete pre-commitment on difficult questions. We additionally document structured abstention affecting 12-22% of queries with asymmetry toward absent-object queries, and a practical abstention gate raising accuracy from 71.0% to 93.8% at 62.7% coverage with no additional inference cost.

Method: 采用基于扩张卷积和跨模态注意力的生成框架，融合母体与胎儿双导联心电图数据，通过自注意力机制捕捉长期时间依赖性，实现多普勒波形的合成。

Abstract: Fetal electrocardiogram (fECG) and Doppler ultrasound provide complementary views of fetal cardiovascular function: fECG captures electrical activity while Doppler reflects mechanical hemodynamics shaped by factors such as placental resistance and vascular compliance. In addition, clinical evidence of maternal-fetal cardiac coupling suggests that maternal cardiovascular dynamics may also inform fetal hemodynamics. Trained on 885 synchronized fetal/maternal ECG and Doppler envelope segments from 39 pregnancies, our model synthesizes Doppler envelopes with power spectral density mean squared error (PSD MSE) of 49.9 +/- 15.8 dB^2 (51% lower than two-channel baseline) and heart-rate error of 4.71 +/- 0.77 bpm (1.5% better than baseline; negligible relative to the 110-160 bpm physiological range). Cross-modal attention yields a 39% PSD MSE reduction over naive dual-channel concatenation, quantifying the contribution of maternal-fetal coupling. Our proposed framework advances computational modeling of the maternal-fetal cardiovascular system by enabling the synthesis of Doppler envelopes from dual-lead ECG. By analysis of both recoverable and residual Doppler components, this approach enables quantification of the purely mechanical contributions to Doppler waveforms -- those not recoverable from electrical recordings -- ultimately facilitating a more comprehensive fetal assessment.

### [161] [Modular Pretraining Enables Access Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08077)
*Ethan Roland,Murat Cubuktepe,Erick Martinez,Stijn Servaes,Keenan Pepper,Mike Vaiana,Diogo Schwerz de Lucena,Judd Rosenblatt,Addie Foote,Cem Anil,Alex Cloud*

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为梯度路由辅助模块（GRAM）的新方法，通过在神经网络中添加可选择性更新的模块来实现模型能力的专门化。推理时可通过禁用特定模块来移除某项能力，从而实现对双重用途AI能力的访问控制。该方法在多个领域（如病毒学、网络安全等）测试中表现良好，既能有效屏蔽目标能力，又能保持其他能力，并且在大规模模型中优于传统微调后遗忘方法。更重要的是，其训练成本不随能力配置数量增加，相比数据过滤方案节省5倍资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决人工智能双重用途带来的安全风险问题，即同一技术既可用于有益目的（如疾病治疗），也可能被滥用（如合成有害物质）。现有方案如为不同用户部署独立模型成本过高，因此需要一种高效的方法实现对模型能力的可控分离。

Method: 引入梯度路由辅助模块（GRAM），在预训练阶段向神经网络添加可选更新的模块，仅针对特定任务激活相应模块，使模型具备多能力支持但可按需禁用；推理时通过禁用某些模块来移除特定功能，模拟从过滤数据中训练出的专用模型。

Result: GRAM能有效关闭目标能力而保留其余能力，在多种真实场景下验证了其有效性；相比事后遗忘方法，更难恢复被禁用的能力；在不同规模模型上（50M至5B参数），其性能与数据过滤模型高度一致，且训练成本与能力配置数无关，显著降低资源开销。

Conclusion: GRAM提供了一种高效、可扩展的双重用途AI能力控制机制，能够在不牺牲性能的前提下实现灵活的能力隔离，是替代多模型部署的可行方案，尤其适用于大规模模型场景。

Abstract: AI developers face a dual-use dilemma. An AI capability that helps one user cure a disease can help another synthesize one. This dilemma could be resolved with access control, limiting dual-use AI capabilities to trusted deployments with a legitimate need. A gold standard for access control would be to serve separate models with different capabilities to different users. However, training and deploying multiple models is prohibitively expensive. To address this challenge, we propose gradient-routed auxiliary modules (GRAM), a pre-training method that adds modules to a neural network and selectively updates them to induce specialization. Ablating a module at inference time removes its capability from the network, approximating a model trained on filtered data. We evaluate GRAM on synthetic stories and realistic dual-use data spanning virology, cybersecurity, nuclear physics, and specialized code. These experiments show that GRAM disables targeted capabilities while preserving the rest, and resists their recovery under finetuning better than post-hoc unlearning. Most importantly, a Chinchilla-optimal scaling analysis from 50M to 5B parameters shows that the gap between data-filtered and full-data models widens with scale on removed capabilities but stays small on retained ones, and that GRAM closely tracks data filtering. GRAM's training cost is independent of the number of supported capability profiles, yielding a 5x reduction over data filtering in our 5-profile setting.

Computing important performance metrics, such as tail probabilities, is even more intractable, despite their practical relevance. In this paper, we develop a deep learning approach that accurately and efficiently learns the Laplace transform of high-dimensional RBMs based on the basic adjoint relationship (BAR). Our framework combines a careful design of the loss function, training data sampling procedure, and neural network architecture. We evaluate the proposed method on RBM instances with known ground-truth tail probabilities and demonstrate near-perfect prediction in high-dimensional settings, highlighting its potential as a general tool for analyzing stochastic systems beyond analytically tractable regimes.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将每个实例视为具有多个可能秩的随机变量，构建基于概率排序关系的损失函数；结合判别性损失（增强实例与中心点之间的区分能力）和随机序损失（保证实例间概率排序的一致性），学习一个鲁棒的嵌入空间。

Result: 在多种数据集和不同类型的标签噪声下，SOL显著优于现有方法，在噪声环境中仍能保持稳定的秩估计性能，且代码已开源。

Conclusion: SOL成功地将秩估计中的标签不确定性建模为随机序问题，通过双目标优化机制提升了模型对噪声的鲁棒性，为处理带有结构化噪声的排序任务提供了新的思路。

Extensive experiments across diverse datasets demonstrate that SOL enables reliable rank estimation under various types and levels of label noise. The source code is available at https://github.com/cwlee00/SOL.

### [165] [Contrastive Order Learning: A General Framework for Ordinal Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08109)
*Chaewon Lee,BeomJun Shim,Kwang Pyo Choi,Chang-Su Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出对比顺序学习（ConOrd），一种融合对比学习与顺序学习优势的序数回归框架。该方法通过引入基于排名差异的软亲和与差异权重的对比顺序损失，精细建模批次内所有样本对之间的序数关系，克服了传统对比学习忽略标签顺序性、顺序学习难以捕捉全局序数结构的问题。在人脸年龄估计、图像质量评估和视频质量评估等任务上，ConOrd表现出卓越且一致的性能，达到当前最优水平，并展现出良好的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对比学习方法虽能有效利用批次中所有样本，但忽略了标签的内在排序关系；而传统顺序学习虽然显式建模标签序数性，但多依赖局部边际比较，难以捕捉全局序数结构。因此需要一种既能利用全局样本信息又能精细建模序数关系的新方法。

Method: 提出对比顺序损失，结合软亲和与差异权重，根据样本间排名差异动态调整其对比强度，实现对批次内所有样本对之间序数关系的细粒度建模。

Result: 在多个序数回归任务（如人脸年龄估计、盲图像/视频质量评估）中，ConOrd均取得当前最优性能，表现稳定且泛化能力强。

Conclusion: ConOrd成功融合了对比学习的全局信息利用能力和顺序学习的序数建模能力，为序数回归提供了高效且通用的新范式。

Abstract: We propose contrastive order learning (ConOrd), a contrastive learning framework for ordinal regression that integrates the strengths of contrastive learning and order learning. While contrastive learning effectively leverages all samples in a batch, it typically ignores the inherent ordering among rank labels. Conversely, order learning explicitly models label ordinality but often relies on local, margin-based comparisons, limiting its ability to capture global ordinal structure. ConOrd addresses these limitations by introducing a contrastive order loss with soft affinity and disparity weights based on rank differences, enabling fine-grained modeling of ordinal relationships across all sample pairs within a batch. Extensive experiments on a range of ordinal regression tasks, including facial age estimation, blind image quality assessment, and blind video quality assessment, demonstrate that ConOrd consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance and generalizes well across diverse ordinal regression scenarios. The source code is available at https://github.com/cwlee00/ConOrd.

### [166] [Workload-Preserving Differentially Private Synthetic Data for Causal Inference via Maximum-Entropy Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08122)
*Amir Asiaee,Kaveh Aryan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出因果工作负载（causal workloads），一种针对双重稳健因果估计器所用正交矩设计的差分隐私（DP）查询集，以更好支持平均处理效应（ATE）等因果估计量。该方法通过释放一次性工作负载，可直接用于稳定矩映射估计或通过最大熵校准生成可重用的合成数据，并在理论层面分解了ATE误差为抽样、隐私、工作负载近似、蒙特卡洛和校准等部分。研究还引入Causal-AIM自适应工作负载选择器和噪声感知多重插补（NA+MI）程序以生成置信区间。实验表明，在严格隐私预算下，因果工作负载在不确定性校准方面表现更优；而当隐私放宽时，通用工作负载在点估计均方误差（RMSE）上仍具优势。核心启示是：分布保真度有助于点估计精度，但有效因果推断需保留因果矩并传播差分隐私噪声，而非将合成行视为真实数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于工作负载的差分隐私合成数据方法虽能实现强分布保真度，但对平均处理效应（ATE）等因果估计量可能不充分，因这些估计依赖于处理组平衡性和结果矩，而通用边际分布未必保持这些特性。因此需要设计专门面向因果推断的工作负载，以确保关键因果矩被正确捕捉和传播。

Method: 提出因果工作负载，即围绕双重稳健估计器使用的正交矩构建的差分隐私查询集；结合最大熵校准技术重构合成数据；引入Causal-AIM自适应选择工作负载；采用噪声感知多重插补（NA+MI）方法生成置信区间。理论分析将ATE误差分解为多个组成部分，涵盖采样、隐私、工作负载近似、蒙特卡洛和校准项。

Result: 在严格隐私预算下，因果工作负载显著优于通用工作负载，尤其在不确定性校准方面表现更佳；当隐私预算放宽时，通用工作负载在点估计（如RMSE）上仍有优势。同一工作负载可支持ATE、ATT及子群分析，无需额外隐私开销。实验证明因果工作负载在保持因果有效性方面具有不可替代性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了分布保真与因果有效性之间的权衡：虽然高分布保真有助于点估计精度，但有效的因果推断必须关注并保留关键因果矩，同时正确传播差分隐私噪声。因果工作负载的设计实现了这一目标，使合成数据在支持复杂因果分析的同时保持隐私保障。

Abstract: Workload-based differentially private (DP) synthetic data methods privately measure aggregate queries and post-process the noisy answers into synthetic records. Generic workloads can achieve strong distributional fidelity, but causal estimands such as the average treatment effect (ATE) depend on treatment-arm balance and outcome moments that generic marginals need not preserve. We propose causal workloads: DP query sets designed around the orthogonal moments used by doubly robust causal estimators. The released workload can be used directly by stable moment-map estimators or reconstructed by maximum-entropy calibration into reusable synthetic data; our theory decomposes ATE error into sampling, privacy, workload-approximation, Monte Carlo, and calibration terms. We also introduce Causal-AIM, an adaptive workload selector, and a noise-aware multiple-imputation (NA+MI) procedure for confidence intervals from DP synthetic data. Because the workload is released once, the same DP synthetic table can support ATE, ATT, and subgroup analyses without additional privacy spending. Empirically, causal workloads are most useful at strict privacy budgets and for calibrated uncertainty, while generic workloads often retain an advantage for point RMSE as privacy relaxes. The broader lesson is a tradeoff: distributional fidelity can help point accuracy, but valid causal inference requires preserving causal moments and propagating DP noise rather than treating synthetic rows as real.

This transparency is crucial in clinical medicine and social science, but SR faces three challenges: high-dimensional inputs, principled selection of Pareto-front formulae, and data irregularities such as multicollinearity and class imbalance. We introduce DeepPySR, which addresses these issues with a dynamic variable-pruning schedule to remove irrelevant features during search, an exponential Pareto selection criterion that eliminates trade-offs between accuracy and complexity, and a multi-layer architecture for hierarchical symbolic composition. On four Feynman physics benchmarks and seven biomedical and social-science datasets, DeepPySR outperforms PySR and baselines on body fat (R$^2$: 0.794 vs.\ 0.702), heart disease (F1: 0.898 vs.\ 0.787), student performance (R$^2$: 0.964 vs.\ 0.948), and Raine BMI (R$^2$: 0.525 vs.\ 0.370), producing interpretable formulas aligned with domain risk factors.

### [168] [Ensemble Diversity Optimization for Subjective Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08493)
*Xia Cui,Ziyi Huang,N. R. Abeynayake*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为集成多样性优化（EDO）的预测空间框架，通过统一可微目标联合优化集成权重、有效基数和校准。EDO利用Gumbel-Softmax松弛实现集成结构与规模的端到端学习，并引入有符号多样性正则化项，在验证数据上调整以控制分歧的保留或抑制，防止集成坍缩并实现效用-校准权衡的可控调节。该方法结合软F1代理、类别加权交叉熵处理类别不平衡，以及可靠性加权多样性调节组内变异性。在四个主观文本分类基准（ArMIS、ConvAbuse、HS-Brexit、MD-Agreement）上的实验表明，EDO显著提升了概率校准效果，交叉熵降低40-78%（相对于基线），同时降低布里尔分数，优于Soft-CE、Soft-MD、Top-5投票和WEL，且保持竞争性F1得分及与标注者分布的一致性。结果表明，通过有符号多样性正则化联合优化集成结构，是一种高效、模型无关的建模人类主观性的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为集成多样性优化（EDO）的预测空间框架，通过统一可微目标联合优化集成权重、有效基数和校准；采用Gumbel-Softmax松弛实现集成结构与规模的端到端学习；引入有符号多样性正则化项，基于验证数据调优，以控制分歧的保留或抑制；结合软F1代理、类别加权交叉熵处理不平衡问题，以及可靠性加权多样性调节组内变异性。

Result: 在四个主观文本分类基准（ArMIS、ConvAbuse、HS-Brexit、MD-Agreement）上，EDO显著改善了概率校准，交叉熵降低40-78%（相对于基线），布里尔分数更低，优于Soft-CE、Soft-MD、Top-5投票和WEL；F1得分保持竞争力，且与标注者分布更一致。

Conclusion: 联合优化集成结构与有符号多样性正则化，提供了一种高效、模型无关的方法来建模监督学习中的人类主观性，尤其适用于存在系统性标注者分歧的任务。

Abstract: Subjective NLP tasks often exhibit systematic annotator disagreement, requiring models that represent uncertainty rather than collapse it. We introduce Ensemble Diversity Optimization (EDO), a prediction-space framework that jointly optimizes ensemble weights, effective cardinality, and calibration through a unified differentiable objective. EDO learns ensemble composition and size end-to-end via Gumbel-Softmax relaxation and incorporates a signed diversity regularizer, tuned on validation data, to steer optimization toward either preserving or suppressing disagreement. This regularization prevents ensemble collapse and enables controlled navigation of the utility-calibration trade-off. The framework integrates a soft F1 surrogate, class-weighted cross-entropy to address imbalance, and reliability-weighted diversity to regulate intra-ensemble variability. Experiments on four subjective text-classification benchmarks (ArMIS, ConvAbuse, HS-Brexit, MD-Agreement) show that EDO substantially improves probabilistic calibration, reducing cross-entropy (40-78% depending on baseline) and lowering Brier scores relative to Soft-CE, Soft-MD, Top-5 Voting, and WEL, while maintaining competitive F1 and better alignment with annotator distributions. These results demonstrate that jointly optimizing ensemble structure with a signed diversity regularizer provides an efficient, model-agnostic approach for modeling human subjectivity in supervised learning.

### [169] [Understanding Layer Patching in Model Size Interpolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08170)
*Sara Kangaslahti,Jonathan Geuter,Nihal V. Nayak,Marco Fumero,Francesco Locatello,David Alvarez-Melis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了零样本模型尺寸插值中的学生层选择问题，将最优层子集选择建模为最短路径问题，并提出KLPatch算法基于KL散度进行贪心补丁，显著提升插值性能。实验表明，简单顺序策略（如从头到尾或从尾到头）在实践中表现优异，而KLPatch进一步逼近最优解，为构建近似最优的插值模型提供了理论与实践指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将模型尺寸插值中的层选择问题形式化为有向无环图上的最短路径问题；设计基于KL散度的贪心算法KLPatch，用于自动选择最优层补丁序列；通过理论证明该问题可被高效求解。

Result: 实验表明，补丁策略对插值行为有显著影响，不同模型家族表现差异大；简单顺序补丁（如从头到尾或从尾到头）已具较强性能；KLPatch算法在多数情况下优于基线策略，接近理论最优解，有效提升了插值模型的质量。

Conclusion: 本研究首次系统揭示了层补丁对模型尺寸插值的影响机制，证明其可建模为最短路径问题，并提出有效的KLPatch算法，为零样本模型尺寸插值提供了理论依据与实用工具。

Abstract: Zero-shot model size interpolation aims to create new models of intermediate target sizes by combining existing models without additional training. Recent work on boomerang distillation [Kangaslahti et al., 2026] shows that a student language model distilled from a larger teacher can be expanded by iteratively patching its layers, replacing student layers with contiguous blocks of teacher layers to obtain models whose size and performance interpolate between the student and the teacher. In this work, we provide the first systematic study of student-layer selection for model size interpolation. We cast finding the optimal layer subset for each model size as an optimization problem and prove it can be viewed as a shortest-path problem in a certain acyclic graph. In experiments, we show that patching strongly shapes interpolation behavior, with effects that vary substantially across model families. We find that simple sequential strategies--patching either from the first layer to the last or from the last to the first--often achieve surprisingly strong performance in practice. We further introduce KLPatch, a greedy patching algorithm based on KL divergence, which often improves over last-to-first patching and approximately solves the optimization problem. Together, our results provide a principled understanding of how layer patching affects model size interpolation and offer practical guidance for constructing near-optimal interpolated models.

### [171] [PIT-SUN: A Deployable Empirical Marginal Transform Framework with Expectation-Consistent Recovery for Regression in Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08202)
*Mingyu Zhao,Zhaohan Li,Zhenxiong Miao,Xu Zhang,Dewei Leng,Yanan Niu,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出PIT-SUN框架，通过概率积分变换与无偏恢复，解决推荐系统中重尾、零膨胀、多模态目标下的期望估计问题，实现高精度、良好校准和排名质量的改进，部署开销小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准MSE在重尾、零膨胀、多模态目标下梯度不稳定，导致均值崩溃和尾部收缩；现有非线性变换虽缓解尺度冲突，但直接逆变换会破坏期望一致性，且缺乏对稀疏复杂边际下坐标、查找、基函数和监控策略的选择指导。

Method: PIT-SUN利用经验边际表构建有界正态得分坐标，通过逆分位数查找、方差控制的恢复基，并采用乘法无偏恢复（SUN）估计原始空间期望，避免直接逆变换。

Result: 在合成分布、公开基准、大规模工业数据集及线上部署中均表现出点预测精度、校准性和排序质量的显著提升，且部署轻量。

Abstract: Estimating original-space conditional expectations is central to value-driven recommender systems, including dwell time, GMV, and LTV forecasting. Standard MSE is expectation-consistent in principle, but its gradients become unstable on heavy-tailed, zero-inflated, and multimodal targets, causing mean collapse and tail shrinkage. Target transformation alleviates this scale conflict, yet any useful nonlinear marginal transform loses expectation consistency under direct inversion. This is not an implementation oversight: a direct inverse-transform estimator is universally expectation-consistent only when the inverse transform is affine, which cannot simultaneously provide bounded tail compression. Existing conditionally linear recovery methods restore expectation consistency, but still leave open which coordinate, inverse lookup, recovery base, and deployment monitor should be selected for sparse complex marginals. We propose \textbf{P}robability-\textbf{I}ntegral-\textbf{TranS}formed \textbf{Un}biased recovery (\textbf{PIT-SUN}), a deployable empirical marginal recovery framework. PIT-SUN uses one empirical marginal table to define a bounded normal-score coordinate, its inverse-quantile lookup, a variance-controlled recovery base, and drift monitoring, then applies multiplicative SUN recovery to estimate the original-space expectation instead of directly inverting transformed predictions. Experiments on synthetic distributions, public benchmarks, large-scale industrial datasets, and online deployment show robust improvements in point accuracy, calibration, and ranking quality with lightweight deployment overhead.

### [172] [RhyMix: A Lightweight Adaptive Multi-Rhythm Network for Long-Term Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08234)
*Sumit Satishrao Shevtekar,Chandresh Kumar Maurya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RhyMix 是一种基于并行双路径建模与自适应门控机制的混合神经架构，旨在捕捉时间序列中的多尺度动态模式。它包含周期路径（Cyclic Path）和轻量级多尺度卷积网络路径（MSTCN-CA Path），通过可学习的周期嵌入和通道注意力机制分别捕捉周期性规律与局部依赖关系。自适应门控机制在路径和预测头层面动态调整模型行为，使模型能根据输入特性灵活响应。该方法在12个真实世界数据集上表现优异，在10个数据集上达到最佳性能，同时保持约4万参数、线性复杂度和低延迟推理（<5ms），适用于边缘设备实时部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列预测模型通常采用单一路径建模，如Transformer难以保留局部细节，卷积受限于感受野，线性模型无法捕捉非线性动态。真实世界时间序列常包含短期波动、季节性周期、长期趋势及突发变化等多重时序模式，亟需一种能够同时建模多种模式且高效轻量的统一框架。

Method: 提出RhyMix架构，包含两个并行分支：(i) Cyclic Path利用可学习的周期嵌入引入显式季节性归纳偏置；(ii) MSTCN-CA Path采用多尺度深度可分离膨胀卷积与通道注意力机制，捕获不同时间尺度的依赖关系。引入多层次自适应门控：路径门动态融合四种专用预测头（直接预测、趋势-季节分解、局部卷积、周期融合），混合门则依据输入特征自适应平衡两路径贡献。

Result: 在12个真实世界长期预测数据集上，RhyMix在10个数据集上达到或超越现有最优性能；模型参数量仅约4万，计算复杂度为线性，推理延迟低于5毫秒，具备良好的实时性与边缘部署能力。

Conclusion: RhyMix通过并行双路径结构与多层次自适应门控，有效建模时间序列中复杂的多尺度时序模式，在精度与效率之间取得良好平衡，是面向资源受限场景的高性能时间序列预测新范式。

Abstract: Real-world time series exhibit complex dynamics characterized by multiple simultaneous temporal patterns: short-term fluctuations, periodic seasonal cycles, long-term trends, and irregular abrupt changes. However, many existing forecasting architectures rely on single-path temporal modeling--transformers capture long-range dependencies but smooth local variations, convolutions capture local patterns but have limited receptive fields, and linear models are efficient but cannot capture nonlinear dynamics. To address this, we introduce RhyMix (RHYthm MIXture), a hybrid neural architecture designed around a parallel dual-path modeling paradigm with adaptive gating mechanisms. RhyMix integrates two complementary encoding branches: (i) a Cyclic Path that incorporates explicit seasonal inductive bias through learnable cyclic embeddings, capturing predictable rhythmic patterns; and (ii) a lightweight Multi-Scale Temporal Convolutional Network with Channel Attention Path that employs multi-scale depthwise dilated convolutions to capture temporal dependencies across different receptive fields. A key innovation is the use of adaptive gating at multiple levels: a path gate dynamically combines four specialized forecasting heads (Direct, Trend-Seasonal Decomposition, Local Convolution, and Periodic Fusion) per sample and channel, while a hybrid gate adaptively balances the Cyclic and MSTCN-CA Paths based on input characteristics. This design ensures the model adapts to specific temporal patterns while maintaining linear complexity in sequence length, channels, and prediction horizon. Across extensive benchmarks on 12 real-world datasets for long-term forecasting, RhyMix achieves state-of-the-art performance on 10 of 12 datasets. The model remains lightweight (~40K params) with linear complexity and low-latency inference (<5ms),suitable for resource-constrained edge devices and real-time deployment.

</details>

Abstract: Recent algorithmic advances have made directed acyclic graph (DAG) structure learning scalable for causal discovery. Yet, the currently available techniques assume a completely homogeneous population, precluding their application to clustered data where cluster-specific variations (e.g., patient-specific effects) are common. We address this issue by introducing a new approach that estimates a global structure while accounting for local cluster-level effects. The key idea is to extend the fixed- and random-effects framework of classical mixed models to the structure learning setting. Towards this end, we present a differentiable graph coupling mechanism that guarantees the union of the fixed- and random-effects graphs remains acyclic. Computationally, we provide a provably convergent first-order method and leverage efficient batched updates across clusters. Statistically, we establish identifiability of the model and show that our approach recovers the true structure asymptotically. In experiments on real and synthetic data, our proposal detects dependencies missed by alternative estimators, underscoring its value for structure learning in clustered settings.

### [174] [An interpretable Good--Turing restart criterion for k-means++](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08243)
*Renato Cordeiro de Amorim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出GTRC重启准则，结合Good-Turing估计、无条件界和置信度界，动态决定k-means++算法的重启次数，根据数据集难度自适应调整，避免固定重启次数带来的计算浪费或不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有k-means++算法通常采用固定次数的重启以避免局部最优，但重启次数常被随意设定且对所有数据集相同，导致在简单数据集上浪费计算资源，在困难数据集上可能不足以获得高质量结果，影响可比性与效率。

Method: 提出GTRC（Good-Turing Restart Criterion），利用Good-Turing估计估算改进概率，结合理论上的无条件界与置信度界，构建一个可解释的、依赖数据的停止条件，当进一步重启改善结果的概率低于用户设定的容差ε时停止。

Result: 在36个数据集上，GTRC达到与精心选择的固定重启次数相当的聚类质量，且重启次数随数据集难度动态变化，表现出良好的自适应性和效率。

Conclusion: GTRC提供了一种基于原理且可报告的替代方案，用于确定k-means++算法的重启次数，避免了预先固定重启次数的局限性，实现更高效、更合理的聚类优化。

Abstract: The k-means++ algorithm is commonly restarted multiple times to avoid poor local optima, yet the number of restarts is almost always chosen arbitrarily and applied uniformly regardless of data set difficulty. This undermines any comparison relying on such a choice and wastes computation on easy data sets while potentially under-serving hard ones. We introduce GTRC, a restart criterion combining a Good-Turing estimate, a proven unconditional bound, and a confidence-based bound on the probability that a further restart would improve on the current result, stopping once this probability falls below a user-specified tolerance $\varepsilon$. Across 36 data sets, GTRC reached clustering quality competitive with well-chosen fixed restart counts, while the number of restarts used varied considerably and appropriately with data set difficulty, governed by an interpretable, data-dependent signal rather than a fixed rule. GTRC offers a principled and reportable alternative to fixing the number of $k$-means++ restarts in advance. Software:https://github.com/RCdeAmorim/Good-Turing-Restart-Criterion.

Method: 提出CASL-VAE模型，利用深度对比潜在变量架构，将变异分解为共享的连续公共潜在因子和层级化的显著潜在因子（建模离散亚型和连续内部变异），通过变分推断实现无配对数据下的联合似然优化。

Abstract: Quantifying variability in a target population relative to a reference population is central to many scientific and clinical problems (e.g., diseased vs. healthy). Yet, without paired data and in the presence of heterogeneous target variation, existing methods struggle to separate multiple modes of target-specific variation. We propose \textit{CASL-VAE}, a deep contrastive latent variable model that learns structured latent generative factors from unpaired data. CASL-VAE factorizes variation into continuous common latent factors shared across populations and hierarchical salient latent factors that model target-specific heterogeneity as discrete subtypes and continuous within-subtype variation. Using variational inference, we show how approximate joint likelihood optimization over reference and target domains can be performed using unpaired data, providing a principled basis for paired-sample generation and cross-domain analysis. ### [178] [Write-Protected Discrete Bottlenecks for Language-Grounded World Models: A Structural Limitation and Sufficient Fix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08312)
*Jiayi Fang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨语言如何与世界模型的离散符号系统交互，指出当前主流的端到端注入大模型特征的方法存在根本性缺陷：语言梯度会引发符号瓶颈中的符号坍缩问题。通过实验发现，基于Gumbel-softmax的离散瓶颈无法同时保持符号多样性与语义学习能力。提出三个关键约束可彻底解决该问题：(1) 断开梯度链（z.detach()），阻止语言信号影响符号表示；(2) 引入无参数的语义通道——基于共现计数的记忆表，替代梯度绑定；(3) 采用DP-Means流式聚类处理符号冲突，实现自动子簇分裂。三者结合使接地准确率达到97.2%，显著优于无第三层的22.2%。在74次独立实验中，32个种子均未出现符号坍缩，且在多种架构与环境下表现稳定，仅需训练不足200万参数，无需微调大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流方法假设语言梯度可直接塑造物理符号表示，但该假设在实践中导致符号坍缩，严重损害世界模型的语义表达能力。因此需要重新审视语言与离散符号系统的接口机制，寻找结构上更稳健的解决方案。

Method: 设计并验证一种新型符号系统接口架构，包含：断开梯度链、引入非参数记忆表进行语义绑定、使用DP-Means聚类处理符号碰撞。通过多组对比实验评估不同变体在符号多样性与语义准确性上的表现，并在多种环境和编码器下验证其泛化能力。

Result: 所提方法在所有测试条件下均避免符号坍缩，接地准确率达97.2%，显著优于基线（22.2%）。跨32个种子、74次运行均稳定有效，仅需训练<2M参数，且无需微调大语言模型。

Conclusion: 语言与离散符号系统的接口必须脱离依赖梯度的绑定机制。通过断开梯度链、引入非参数语义通道及动态聚类机制，可在不增加复杂度的前提下实现高精度、高鲁棒性的符号语义绑定，为构建可靠的世界模型提供结构性保障。

Abstract: How should language interface with a world model's discrete symbol system? The dominant paradigm -- end-to-end injection of LLM/VLM features into robot world models (RT-2, Octo, PaLM-E) -- implicitly assumes that language gradients can directly shape physical symbol representations. We ask whether this assumption is safe, find that it is not, and characterize the minimal architectural constraint that prevents the failure. Any language gradient entering a Gumbel-softmax-based discrete symbol bottleneck forces a structural trade-off: the vanilla estimator collapses to 2.2/64 symbols (4/5 seeds), while five anti-collapse strategies maintain diversity but fail to learn semantic labels (all <= 9.2% accuracy). No tested GumbelBottleneck variant achieves both objectives simultaneously. Within this family of discrete bottlenecks, the failure is structural rather than a matter of optimization. We characterize a sufficient set of three constraints that prevent the failure: (1) cut the gradient chain (z.detach()), preventing language signals from reaching the symbol bottleneck; (2) provide a gradient-free semantic channel -- a non-parametric Memory Table (Dict[symbol -> Counter[label]], zero parameters, zero gradients) where co-occurrence counting replaces gradient-based binding; (3) handle symbol collisions via DP-Means streaming clustering for automatic sub-cluster splitting. All three layers together achieve 97.2% grounding accuracy vs. 22.2% without Layer 3. Across two experiments spanning 74 independent runs, we demonstrate zero symbol collapse in all 32 seeds, with the blackboard achieving 79-100% semantic binding across three encoder architectures (CNN, V-JEPA 300M, CLIP ViT-L), two environments, and three texture conditions. The fix trains fewer than 2M parameters and requires no LLM fine-tuning.

### [179] [ArtMine: Discovering and Formalizing Artistic Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08331)
*Kaustubh Kumar,Ashutosh Ranjan,Vivek Srivastava,Blessin Varkey,Shirish Karande*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ArtMine 是一个从异构历史证据中发现并形式化艺术创作过程的框架。它通过整合档案记录、草图、书信等碎片化资料，构建结构化知识库，并利用皮尔士式的溯因推理生成可解释的艺术生产步骤。这些步骤被转化为组合图和渲染提示，通过自我反思优化生成作品与参考作品之间的差异。该方法在多艺术家、多艺术流派的案例研究中验证了其可行性，展示了如何基于零散文献构建连贯、可解释且可审计的艺术创作流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式AI主要关注成品艺术品的分布建模，缺乏对创作过程的理解；而艺术创作过程通常仅以碎片化文档（如档案、草图、通信）留存，难以进行计算建模。因此需要一种能从异构历史证据中挖掘和形式化艺术创作过程的方法。

Method: ArtMine 将异构艺术证据整合为结构化存储库，使用皮尔士溯因推理推断有证据支持的创作步骤，将其转化为组合图和渲染提示，并通过自省机制优化生成结果与参考作品的一致性。

Result: 在多个艺术家和艺术流派的初步案例研究中，该框架成功从开放域历史资料中重建出连贯、可解释、可审计的艺术创作流程，证明了碎片化文献可用于支持过程中心的建模。

Conclusion: ArtMine 通过建模创作过程而非仅最终成果，推动了以过程为中心的人机协同创作系统的发展，为艺术诠释、创意教育、反思性协作及文化生产的计算研究提供了新范式。

Abstract: Understanding how artworks are created requires reasoning about the iterative decisions, material operations, and contextual influences that shape artistic production. While recent generative AI systems can synthesize artworks with high fidelity, they primarily model distributions over finished artifacts rather than the creative processes underlying their creation. In practice, artistic workflows are only partially documented through fragmented sources such as archival records, preparatory studies, correspondence, etc., making process-level understanding difficult to formalize computationally. In this work, we introduce ArtMine, a framework for discovering and formalizing artistic processes from heterogeneous historical evidence. Our approach synthesizes heterogeneous artwork evidence into a structured repository, from which a Peircean abductive agent infers evidence-grounded production steps. These steps are converted into a compositional graph and rendering prompt, then optimized through self-reflection over deviations between the generated and reference artworks. We provide a preliminary proof-of-concept case study using open-domain historical sources across multiple artists and artistic movements, demonstrating that fragmented documentary evidence can support coherent, interpretable, and auditable representations of artistic workflows. By modeling creative processes rather than only final artifacts, our work moves toward process-centred human-AI co-creativity systems that can support artistic interpretation, creative education, reflective collaboration, and computational studies of cultural production.

### [180] [AutoAnchor: Stable Diffusion Unlearning Using Cross-Attention as a Manifold Surrogate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08337)
*Siyuan Wen,Jiahao Zeng,Ningning Ding*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为\\mysysn的两阶段框架，用于解决文本到图像扩散模型中不稳定的去学习问题。通过理论分析，作者指出缺乏流形邻近锚点会导致显著的法向量漂移，从而降低去学习性能。为此，\mysysn自动合成流形邻近锚点，并引入一种新的交叉注意力一致性损失作为流形接近性的高效代理，以实现稳定、无偏的去学习。实验表明，该方法在多个主流基线模型上均显著提升了目标概念去除效果（CLIP分数提升最高达31.04%）和非目标内容保真度（最高提升4.18%），且可无缝集成至现有方法中，平均提升概念去除6.30%和实用性6.65%。

Motivation: 当前扩散模型中的去学习技术存在两大缺陷：基于锚点的方法依赖人工选择的语义锚点，易引发偏见；而无锚点方法因潜在空间更新不受约束，导致去学习结果不稳定。因此，亟需一种既能保证稳定性又能避免偏差的去学习机制。

Method: \\mysysn采用两阶段框架：第一阶段自动生成与目标概念流形相近的锚点；第二阶段利用提出的交叉注意力一致性损失来逼近流形结构，替代计算复杂的几何优化，从而实现高效且稳定的去学习。

Result: \\mysysn在多个基准测试中表现出色，显著提升了目标概念去除能力（最多提升31.04% CLIP得分）和非目标内容质量（最多提升4.18% CLIP得分），并能有效增强现有去学习方法的性能（平均提升6.30%和6.65%）。

Abstract: Diffusion unlearning is essential for mitigating the generation of harmful or copyrighted content in text-to-image models. Current diffusion unlearning techniques determine the model update direction by either using alternatives of the target concept as an anchor or using empty prompts. The anchor-based method relies on manually and semantically-chosen anchors that risk biased unlearning, while the anchor-free method inherently suffers from unrobust unlearning due to unconstrained latent updates. In this work, we theoretically formalize such unstable diffusion unlearning issues under the manifold hypothesis and prove that lacking a manifold-proximal anchor inevitably induces significant normal-space drift that degrades unlearning performance. To achieve stable unlearning, we propose \mysysn, a two-stage framework that automatically synthesizes manifold-proximal anchors. However, direct geometric manifold optimization is computationally intractable. To address this challenge, \mysys introduces a novel cross-attention consistency loss which serves as a highly efficient surrogate of manifold proximity. Experimental results demonstrate that \mysys effectively achieves robust and unbiased unlearning across various state-of-the-art baselines, significantly improving targeted concept removal (by up to 31.04\% in CLIP score) and non-target utility (by up to 4.18\% in CLIP score). Moreover, \mysys can also be easily integrated into existing diffusion unlearning methods to enhance their unlearning performance (by 6.30\% for concept removal and 6.65\% for utility on average).

Abstract: Q-learning is a fundamental algorithm in reinforcement learning (RL) for solving discounted Markov decision processes (MDPs) when the transition kernel is unknown. Dueling Q-learning decomposes the Q-function into a value function and an advantage function and learns the two components jointly, which can improve learning efficiency. However, the theoretical understanding of dueling Q-learning is still limited. Recent work has initiated an analysis of tabular dueling Q-learning, but existing guarantees focus on a regularized formulation and leave the pure tabular update less completely understood. This paper strengthens that line of analysis by adding a direct interpretation of the centered tabular decomposition and by establishing convergence guarantees for the unregularized, unprojected constant step-size recursion. In particular, we derive an exact switching linear system representation for deterministic dueling Q-learning and a finite-time error bound in expectation for the sampled stochastic version. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将评估指标形式化为因果估计量，基于输入分布与干预分布的期望；采用霍夫丁型序列与方差自适应投注序列，结合有界混合重要性加权实现自适应采样下的置信区间与序列生成。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability often evaluates explanations by intervening on a model: swapping hidden states, patching activations, ablating components, or comparing a compressed model to the original one. These experiments are usually summarized by a point estimate, even though the evaluation may be monitored while it runs or adapted toward suspected failures. This makes it hard to tell whether a reported fidelity or patching effect is a stable causal claim or a consequence of finite sampling and evaluation choices. We introduce Certified Interventional Fidelity (CIF), a statistical layer for interventional interpretability evaluations. CIF first writes the quantity being reported as a causal estimand: an expectation of a bounded score over a stated input distribution and a stated intervention distribution. It then provides confidence intervals and anytime-valid confidence sequences for this estimand, including under adaptive intervention sampling via bounded mixture importance weighting. We instantiate CIF with Hoeffding-style sequences and variance-adaptive betting sequences, the latter reducing certification cost by 10-30x in our experiments. On MNIST abstractions and GPT-2 Small IOI circuits, CIF certifies high-fidelity claims, shows when apparent method differences are not statistically supported, and makes sensitivity to the intervention distribution explicit.

Abstract: Connected vehicles are autonomous cyber-physical systems whose behavior must be continuously monitored during operation to detect deviations from normal operation before they propagate into failures. Such evaluation is challenging because the systems themselves evolve: over-the-air updates, configuration changes, and shifting workloads alter the definition of normal behavior, causing static diagnostic methods to degrade silently over time. Existing approaches typically address either automated model adaptation or operator integration in isolation, rather than as a single coordinated supervisory loop.
  This paper presents an online anomaly detection framework for autonomous CPS that integrates three coordinated mechanisms. A factorized deep Q-network with self-attention selects the most suitable detector from a candidate pool for each monitored service, exploiting inter-service dependencies in the microservice topology. An ensemble of three statistical drift detectors monitors the input distribution and raises an alarm only when all three concur, prioritizing precision over recall. A human-in-the-loop retraining mechanism, built around a pending transition buffer and a 60/40 prioritized replay strategy, allows the operator to incorporate expert knowledge while preserving the system's learned response to prior data distributions.
  The framework is evaluated on a connected-vehicle testbed running an automated valet parking application across seven backend microservices. The attention-augmented agent achieves an F1 score of 0.69, compared to at most 0.11 for any single detector applied uniformly. Following a real software update that induces measurable concept drift, F1 drops to 0.52; after operator-triggered retraining, performance recovers to 0.65 on the new distribution while remaining at 0.69 on the prior one, demonstrating sustained adaptation without catastrophic forgetting.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification is central to the reliable deployment of large language models (LLMs), and eigenvalues of semantic embeddings have recently emerged as a key tool in state-of-the-art methods. However, conventional calibration results developed for classification probabilities cannot be directly transferred to eigenvalues. We address this gap by proposing a novel framework for calibrating the eigenvalues of semantic embeddings. We interpret LLMs combined with semantic embeddings of their generated answers as density matrix predictors, and we propose a novel approach to calibrate density matrix predictors by applying temperature scaling to their eigenvalues. We establish entropy-risk equivalence under calibration, derive a central calibration inequality specific to eigenvalues, and prove that temperature-scaled eigenvalues optimize calibration when minimizing proper score risks. Experiments on a variety of real-world settings show that current LLMs are systematically overconfident, and validate our theoretical findings. Together, these results advance the foundations and practice of uncertainty quantification for semantic embeddings.

### [185] [Dynamics of Gradient Descent with Large Step Size Near a Manifold of Flat Minima](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08380)
*Lachlan Ewen MacDonald,René Vidal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将先前关于大步长梯度下降在孤立平坦极小值邻域的理论扩展到两个新方向：(1) 向量输出的过参数化最小二乘问题（包括任意多观测的回归），(2) 平坦极小值流形的邻域。作者推广了正常形式和三个收敛定理，并提出一种解决奇异偏微分方程的新方法，该方法可能具有独立兴趣。此外，研究证明该框架适用于深矩阵分解，在温和假设下得出若干新结构结果，如平坦极小值集构成球面乘积上的纤维丛，且尖锐度沿该流形为Morse-Bott型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典梯度下降分析要求步长小于尖锐度倒数的两倍，但此条件在深度神经网络训练中常被违反。已有研究在过参数化单输出最小二乘情形下通过正常形式建立了大步长下的收敛性，但其适用范围有限。本文旨在拓展该理论至更广泛的应用场景，包括多输出回归与平坦极小值流形，以弥合理论与实际训练之间的差距。

Method: 通过构造适用于向量输出及平坦极小值流形的广义正常形式，结合对奇异偏微分方程的新型求解方法，推导出大步长梯度下降的收敛性质。进一步利用微分几何工具分析极小值集的拓扑结构，揭示其纤维丛特性与尖锐度的Morse-Bott性质。

Result: 成功将正常形式和三类收敛定理推广至向量输出与平坦极小值流形情形；提出一种求解奇异偏微分方程的新方法；证明深矩阵分解中平坦极小值集构成球面乘积上的纤维丛，且尖锐度沿该流形满足Morse-Bott条件。

Conclusion: 本研究显著拓展了大步长梯度下降的理论框架，使其适用于更复杂的过参数化学习任务，尤其在矩阵分解等结构化模型中提供了深刻的几何洞察，为理解深度学习优化动态提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: An important quantity in the theory of gradient descent (GD) is the \emph{sharpness}, defined as the largest eigenvalue of the objective Hessian. Classical analyses typically require the step size to be uniformly smaller than twice the reciprocal of the sharpness, but this condition is frequently violated in the training of deep neural networks. Recent work bridges this gap in the setting of overparametrised least-squares with a \emph{single scalar output}, providing a normal form for large-step GD in a neighbourhood of an \emph{isolated} flat minimum and establishing three corresponding convergence results. In this paper, we extend this theory in two directions: (1) to overparametrised least-squares with \emph{vector-valued outputs} (including regression with arbitrarily many observations), and (2) to a neighbourhood of a \emph{manifold} of flat minima (which we show is essential for applications such as matrix factorisation). We generalise both the normal form and all three convergence theorems of \cite{macdonaldeos} to this broader setting, overcoming several technical challenges, including the solution of a singular partial differential equation via a novel method that may be of independent interest. We further show that our framework applies to deep matrix factorisation under mild assumptions, yielding several new structural results. In particular, we prove that the set of flat minima forms a fibre bundle over a product of spheres, and that the sharpness is Morse-Bott along this manifold.

</details>


### [186] [Beyond Backpropagation: Monte Carlo Method Can Train Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08406)
*Hong Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需梯度的简单蒙特卡洛算法，仅通过随机扰动参数并保留使损失下降的更新，即可在单个GPU上有效训练深度神经网络。该方法无需批量归一化、残差连接等常规技术，可直接训练超过20层的深层网络，且适用于稀疏训练、离散权重、非标准激活函数（如高斯函数）等复杂场景。实验涵盖宽网络（16,384个隐层神经元）、Transformer架构，并在图像分类（MNIST）和字符级语言建模（Tiny Shakespeare）任务中取得成功。该方法揭示了深度网络的显著冗余性，为理解神经网络自组织与学习机制提供了新视角，并为构建物理启发的深度学习系统提供替代路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反向传播依赖梯度，面临梯度消失和爆炸问题。长期以来，研究者寻求不依赖梯度的训练方法，以更深入理解神经网络的学习机制，并探索更具物理可行性的深度学习系统。

Method: 采用最简单的蒙特卡洛算法：在单个GPU上随机扰动网络参数，若损失降低则保留更新，否则重试。整个过程不使用任何梯度信息，也无需批量归一化、残差连接等常规技术。

Result: 该方法成功训练了超过20层的深度网络、具有16,384个隐层神经元的单隐藏层宽网络，以及一个简单的Transformer模型。在图像分类（MNIST）和字符级语言建模（Tiny Shakespeare）任务中表现良好。同时支持纯剪枝训练、离散权重、非标准激活函数（如高斯函数），并揭示了深度网络中的巨大冗余性。

Conclusion: 该简单的无梯度蒙特卡洛方法展示了在深度学习中完全无需梯度计算的可能性，不仅具备实用性，还为理解神经网络的自组织特性提供了新视角，也为构建物理可实现的深度学习系统开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Backpropagation (BP) dominates deep learning training, but its reliance on gradients brings inherent troubles -- vanishing and exploding gradients. The pursuit of gradient-free methods has long been a goal in the field of artificial intelligence. This paper shows that indeed the simplest Monte Carlo algorithm implemented on a single GPU -- randomly mutate a parameter, keep it if the loss decreases, otherwise retry -- can practically train deep networks. This gradient-free method does not even need common techniques such as batch normalization or residual connections to directly train sufficiently deep networks. More remarkably, its flexibility extends to several nontrivial scenarios: it enables pure pruning training, supports discrete weights, accommodates unconventional transfer functions such as Gaussian, and reveals the substantial redundancy of deep networks. We have demonstrated its feasibility on deep networks with more than 20 layers, single-hidden-layer wide networks with up to 16,384 hidden neurons, and even a simple Transformer architecture trained on both image classification (MNIST) and character-level language modeling (Tiny Shakespeare). This simple gradient-free method may offer a complementary perspective for understanding the self-organization and learning mechanisms of neural networks, and also provides an alternative route for building physically inspired deep learning systems.

### [187] [Predicting Male Fertility Using Machine Learning: A Semen Parameters Based Analysis with the VISEM Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08429)
*Shahnawaz Qureshi,Raja Khurram Shahzad,Muhammad Fozan,Emal Kawal,Syed Aziz Shah,Sattam Al-Anazi,Syed MuhammadZeeshan Iqbal*

Motivation: 男性不育是生殖健康中重要但常被忽视的问题，传统精液分析虽为临床评估基础，但存在主观性强、效率低等问题。为提升诊断效率与客观性，亟需开发更先进的分析方法。本研究旨在探索机器学习在男性生育能力分类中的应用潜力，以改善生育力评估的准确性与速度。

Method: 使用VISEM数据集，包含85名男性的精液样本，依据WHO标准分为三类：正常、亚正常、不育。对数据进行预处理与特征工程后，采用LazyPredict框架训练并评估超过40种分类算法。通过5折交叉验证和多类别ROC-AUC分析评估模型性能，最终选择最优模型进行比较与验证。

Result: 在所有测试的模型中，最近中心分类器表现最佳，准确率达到94.2%。该模型在5折交叉验证和多类别ROC-AUC分析中均表现出良好的稳健性，显著优于其他常见模型如支持向量机（SVM）和二次判别分析（QDA）。

Conclusion: 机器学习模型能够高效、准确、客观地评估精液质量，具有显著潜力用于临床辅助生育诊断与治疗决策支持。本研究证实了机器学习在男性不育评估中的可行性与优越性，未来有望推动个性化生育策略的发展。

Abstract: Male infertility is a significant yet often underdiagnosed aspect of reproductive health, with semen analysis serving as the cornerstone of clinical evaluation. This dataset includes semen samples from 85 participants, classified into three categories, i.e., Fertile, Sub-Fertile, and Infertile, according to the World Health Organization's criteria. After pre-processing and feature engineering, the dataset was used to train and assess multiple classification models using the LazyPredict framework. Among the more than 40 algorithms tested, the Nearest Centroid classifier achieved an accuracy of 94.2%, outperforming other models such as Support Vector Machines and Quadratic Discriminant Analysis. The model's robustness was validated using 5-fold cross-validation and multiclass ROC-AUC analysis. This study illustrates that machine learning models can provide fast, accurate, and objective assessments of semen quality, potentially supporting clinical decision-making in andrology and assisted reproductive technologies. These findings emphasize the growing potential of machine learning to enhance fertility diagnostics and inform patient-specific treatment strategies.

### [188] [MatBind: A Shared Embedding Space for Multimodal Materials Characterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08470)
*Le Yang,Anoop K. Chandran,Jona Östreicher,Evgenii Sovetkin,Adrian Mirza,Sebastien Bompas,Bashir Kazimi,Pascal Friederich,Stefan Kesselheim,Kevin Maik Jablonka,Stefan Sandfeld*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MatBind 是一个对比学习框架，将晶体结构、模拟的粉末X射线衍射（pXRD）、电子态密度（DOS）和文本四种材料模态对齐到以晶体结构为中心的统一嵌入空间中。该框架在训练中未显式配对的模态之间实现对齐，从而支持零样本跨模态检索。嵌入空间能按物理性质组织材料，无需显式标注；多模态联合查询时检索性能显著提升。结果表明，将异构材料数据视为单一物理现实的不同投影，而非孤立数据源，更符合物理本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有材料数据（如原子结构、衍射图谱、电子密度、自然语言描述）通常独立存储与分析，难以跨表示边界关联或查询。为解决这一问题，需要一种能够整合多种模态并建立统一表示的方法，以揭示材料内在的物理一致性。

Method: 提出 MatBind 框架，采用对比学习策略，以晶体结构为物理锚点，将四种不同模态（晶体结构、模拟 pXRD、DOS、文本）映射到同一嵌入空间。通过设计多模态对比损失函数，使不同模态在无显式配对情况下仍能实现对齐，并支持零样本跨模态检索。

Result: 所学嵌入空间能根据物理属性自然组织材料，无需监督信号；跨模态检索性能在组合多个模态进行查询时持续提升；即使未在训练中配对的模态间也能实现有效的零样本检索。

Conclusion: 将异构材料数据视为同一物理实体的不同投影，不仅在实践上可行，而且更符合材料科学的基本物理规律。该方法为多模态材料数据的统一建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Fully characterizing a crystalline material requires integrating heterogeneous data sources -- atomic structures, diffraction patterns, electronic density of states, and natural language -- each of which captures a different facet of the same physical object. In practice, however, these modalities are stored and analyzed in isolation, making it difficult to relate or query materials across representational boundaries. We present MatBind, a contrastive learning framework that aligns four materials modalities -- crystal structure, powder X-ray diffraction (pXRD) simulated from structures, density of states (DOS), and text -- into a unified embedding space using crystal structure as the central physical anchor. The framework induces alignment between modalities never explicitly paired during training, enabling emergent zero-shot cross-modal retrieval as a direct consequence of the shared representation. The learned embedding space organizes materials according to physically meaningful properties without explicit supervision, and retrieval performance improves systematically when modalities are combined at query time. These results demonstrate that treating heterogeneous materials data as complementary projections of a single physical reality, rather than as isolated data sources, is not a practical choice but is consistent with the underlying physics.

### [189] [Frequency-Domain Multi-Modality Transportation Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08475)
*Jiewen Deng,Hangchen Liu,Junchen Li,Boyuan Zhang,Renhe Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种轻量级但有效的频域多模态建模方法FreMo，通过显式利用频域实现自适应、选择性的跨模态协同。FreMo将模态特异性谱重构与跨模态协同分离，并支持与通用时间序列骨干网络的即插即用集成。其核心包括模态特异性频域滤波器（MFF）以自适应优化各模态的频谱成分，以及基于频率引导的协同整合器（FSI）以选择性地聚合不同模态信息，提升知识共享并减少负迁移。在真实数据集上的大量实验表明，FreMo在多种预测场景下均显著优于现有先进方法，具备优异性能和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态交通系统中不同交通模式（如道路交通流与公共交通）的动态耦合受共享时间模式影响，准确预测仍具挑战性，主要因不同模态具有不同的频谱特征且跨频段交互不均衡；现有方法多局限于时域处理或依赖粗粒度特征融合，难以有效捕捉复杂频域交互。

Method: 提出FreMo框架，包含两个关键模块：1）模态特异性频域滤波器（MFF），用于自适应地增强每个模态中的有效频率成分并抑制噪声；2）频率引导的协同整合器（FSI），根据各模态在不同频率下的相对贡献，选择性地进行跨模态信息聚合，实现高效的知识共享与负迁移抑制。该框架可无缝集成到通用时间序列模型中。

Result: 在多个真实世界数据集上，FreMo在各类预测任务中均显著优于现有最先进方法，表现出更强的预测精度、鲁棒性和泛化能力，验证了其在复杂多模态交通系统建模中的有效性。

Conclusion: FreMo通过显式建模频域特性，实现了对多模态交通系统中复杂动态的精准刻画，为多模态交通预测提供了一种高效、灵活且可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Multi-modality transportation refers to urban systems composed of multiple transportation modes, such as traffic flow and public transit, whose dynamics are coupled by shared temporal patterns. Accurate multi-modality transportation forecasting remains challenging because (1) different modalities exhibit distinct spectral characteristics and (2) interact unevenly across frequencies, whereas most existing methods operate primarily in the time domain or rely on coarse feature fusion. To address these limitations, we propose a lightweight yet effective Frequency-Domain Multi-Modality modeling (FreMo) that explicitly exploits the frequency domain to enable adaptive and selective cross-modality synergy. FreMo disentangles modality-wise spectral refinement from cross-modality synergy and supports plug-and-play integration with general time series backbones. Specifically, FreMo introduces a Modality-Wise Frequency Filter (MFF) to adaptively refine spectral components within each modality, emphasizing informative frequencies while suppressing noise. FreMo further incorporates a Frequency-Guided Synergy Integrator (FSI) that selectively aggregates information across modalities based on their relative contribution at each frequency, facilitating effective cross-modality knowledge sharing while mitigating negative transfer. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets show that FreMo consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, with superior performance and generalization across diverse forecasting scenarios. The code is available at https://github.com/beginner-sketch/FreMo.

Our framework combines the established statistical paradigm of sequential testing with stopping criteria tailored to common evaluation needs such as diminishing returns detection, and minimum detectable effect size. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法大多只关注表示的时间相似性，忽略了系统故障和潜在异常所体现的内部因果关系破坏，因此需要一种能捕捉因果一致性的新方法。

Method: CAAD框架将外生时间序列变量作为残差建模，利用多尺度对齐来内化系统动态，并采用基于梯度的矩阵监控内部因果关系的破坏，从而量化动态与拓扑层面的因果偏差。

Abstract: The operational integrity of complex industrial systems relies on precise anomaly detection and diagnosis. The vast majority of existing methods narrowly focus on capturing temporal similarities of representations, often overlooking the disruption of internal causal relationships, which characterizes system failures and latent anomalies. In this paper, we propose a novel framework (CAAD) that reframes anomaly detection as the continuous verification of Granger causality consistency through exogenous variables.
  Specifically, the CAAD framework models exogenous time-series variables as residuals, identifying anomalies as significant deviations caused by external interventions. The proposed framework leverages multi-scale alignment to internalize system dynamics and utilizes a gradient-based matrix to monitor internal causal relationship breakdowns. By quantifying causal deviations of both dynamic evolution and relational topology, the CAAD is able to capture subtle causal shifts to achieve precise anomaly detection. Extensive experiments on real-world industrial datasets demonstrate that the CAAD achieves high-precision anomaly detection, outperforming most state-of-the-art baselines.

### [193] [Contravariance Theory: Strong Alignment for Minimal Solutions to Hard Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08561)
*Dan Yamins,Aran Nayebi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了深度神经网络（DNN）与大脑在处理复杂任务时的相似性，揭示了在足够困难的任务下，DNN的表示结构会自发形成对齐的“特权轴”，且这种对齐具有层级性。研究证明，即使仅通过仿射映射实现弱对齐，也能导致强对齐；同时，这种对齐随网络层次自上而下“拉链式”整合，表明人工网络与生物脑网络之间存在必然的趋同演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，神经人工智能（NeuroAI）面临核心问题：如何有效比较深度神经网络与真实大脑的表征？以及在复杂任务中，人工网络是否必然与生物脑网络产生相似结构？本研究旨在从理论上解答这些关键问题。

Method: 通过形式化分析，构建最小化DNN解在高难度任务下的数学模型，引入并扩展了Cao和Yamins [2024] 提出的反变性（contravariance）概念，利用仿射映射与层级结构建模，推导出表示对齐的传播机制。

Result: 研究发现，在足够困难的任务下，任意两个最小化DNN解都会表现出强对齐的特权轴，且这种对齐沿着网络层级自上而下逐步“拉链式”整合，说明不同网络间的表征差异对任务度量不敏感，且趋同演化是不可避免的。

Conclusion: 该研究为神经人工智能提供了理论支持：在强任务驱动下，人工网络与大脑网络的结构趋同是必然结果，这使得跨网络比较更具稳定性，也为理解大脑信息处理机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: A series of results from the NeuroAI over the past fifteen years have raised core questions both about how to compare Deep Neural Network (DNN) models to the brain, and about how much convergent evolution to expect between artificial networks and real brain networks. Here, we show that for any two minimal DNN solutions to a sufficiently hard task: (i) "weak" alignment of network representations based on affine mappings guarantees "strong" alignment of privileged axes, and (ii) alignment "zippers" up the network hierarchy, causing the emergence of privileged axes from end-to-end task optimization. These results formalize the notion of contravariance from Cao and Yamins [2024], and illustrate important consequences for the theory of NeuroAI: with sufficiently strong tasks, choice of metric for inter-network comparison is not all that sensitive, and that convergent evolution is probably inevitable.

### [194] [Spectral Stability of Pseudoinverse-Based Extreme Learning Machine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08581)
*Bich Van Nguyen,Ngoc Anh Khong*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ELM虽训练快速，但其数值稳定性依赖于隐藏层矩阵的条件性，亟需从谱角度理解其不稳定性机制。

Method: 通过奇异值分解（SVD）分析伪逆计算，结合随机特征解释研究宽度对条件性的影响，并对比SVD与迭代超幂方法的性能。

Result: SVD-based方法在病态条件下最稳定，迭代方法对奇异值分布敏感；隐藏层矩阵的奇异值结构是决定ELM稳定性的根本因素。

Conclusion: ELM的稳定性本质上由隐藏层矩阵的奇异值结构决定，建议在实际应用中优先采用SVD-based伪逆计算以保障数值稳健性。

Abstract: Extreme Learning Machine (ELM) computes output weights analytically using the Moore-Penrose pseudoinverse. Although this leads to fast training, its numerical stability depends strongly on the conditioning of the hidden layer matrix. This paper studies pseudoinverse-based ELM from a spectral perspective. We show that the smallest singular value governs perturbation amplification in the output weights, while the condition number provides a quantitative measure of hidden-layer instability. We compare SVD-based pseudoinverse computation with iterative hyperpower methods and discuss width-dependent conditioning through a random feature interpretation. Experiments on synthetic matrices and ELM benchmarks show that SVD-based methods remain the most reliable under ill conditioning, while iterative methods are more sensitive to spectral properties. The results suggest that ELM stability is fundamentally governed by the singular value structure of the hidden layer matrix.

*Haripriya Harikumar,Sammie Katt,Yasir Zubayr Barlas,Samuel Kaski*

TL;DR: 本文研究了在存在潜在干扰因素情况下的决策感知实验设计问题，提出了一种基于贝叶斯决策理论的对抗鲁棒性实验设计方法，旨在提升决策在实际扰动下的稳定性，而非仅追求名义上的最优。实验表明，传统方法易收敛到高置信但脆弱的决策，而本文方法能显著提高决策的稳健性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际科学实验中，决策的可靠性常受到未建模或弱建模因素的影响，导致最优决策失效。现有方法假设模型准确且决策稳定，但在现实中往往不成立。因此需要一种能够应对潜在对抗性变化的鲁棒决策感知实验设计方法。

Method: 基于贝叶斯决策理论，构建了对抗鲁棒性最优决策模型，并推导出一种新的贝叶斯实验设计准则，该准则显式优化决策稳定性而非名义最优性。通过考虑对抗变量的可能变化，实现对最坏情况下的信息增益建模。

Result: 在合成数据和真实世界科学数据集上的实验表明，传统决策感知设计方法虽快速收敛至高置信度决策，但其结果对扰动敏感；而本文提出的鲁棒方法所得决策在对抗变化下表现更稳定、更可靠。

Conclusion: 本文提出的对抗鲁棒性决策感知实验设计方法，有效提升了科学实验中决策的稳健性，尤其适用于存在隐藏或不确定影响因素的实际场景。

Abstract: Scientific experiments are often designed to maximize information gain, yet in many applications the primary objective is to support reliable downstream decision-making. Existing decision-aware experimental design and active learning methods typically assume well-specified outcome models and implicitly rely on the stability of the optimal decision under real-world perturbations. In practice, however, experimental outcomes are frequently influenced by hidden or weakly modeled effects, which can substantially alter decision optimality and lead to misleading conclusions. We study sequential adversarially robust decision-aware experimental design, where data acquisition has to take into account information gain against plausible worst-case unexpected effects, modeled here as variation in adversarial variables. Building on Bayesian decision theory, we formalize an adversarially robust optimal decision under this setting and derive a principled Bayesian experimental design criterion. The criterion explicitly targets decision stability rather than nominal optimality. Experiments on synthetic and real-world scientific datasets show that conventional decision-aware design can converge rapidly to high confidence yet fragile decisions, while our robustness-aware approach yields decisions that are significantly more stable and reliable under adversarial variation.

### [198] [BiSCo-LLM: Lookup-Free Binary Spherical Coding for Extreme Low-Bit Large Language Model Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08643)
*Yuantian Shao,Peisong Wang,Zhilei Liu,Chuangyi Li,Yuanteng Chen,Pengcheng Xie,Yiwu Yao,Zhihui Wei,Jian Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出BiSCo-LLM，一种无代码本的二进制球面编码框架，用于极端低比特大语言模型权重压缩。通过将局部权重块映射到单位超球面并二值化为紧凑的球面码，实现以位打包符号流为主的数据表示；引入残差球面量化阶段以提供明确的率失真路径；并通过类别级恢复蒸馏减少局部重构与整体模型行为间的偏差。同时使用8位保护通道作为辅助稳定机制，整体存储开销包含二进制码、神经解码器、保护通道数据、LoRA适配器和元数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低比特压缩方法在接近2比特/权重时受限于表示能力（如标量或分组量化），而向量量化虽具更丰富表示但需显式代码本、索引查找及额外存储。因此亟需一种无需代码本、高效且能支持极低比特压缩的新方法。

Method: 1. 将局部权重块映射至单位超球面并二值化生成球面码；2. 设计残差BSQ阶段编码基编码器遗留的重建误差；3. 在替换每个Transformer模块类别后执行类别级恢复蒸馏以缓解局部重构与全局行为不一致问题；4. 引入8位保护通道作为敏感通道的辅助稳定机制，独立计入总存储预算。

Result: 该方法实现了无需代码本的极端低比特（接近2比特）模型压缩，显著降低存储与带宽开销，同时保持良好模型性能；实验表明其在多种基准上优于现有方法，在极低比特下仍具备强鲁棒性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: BiSCo-LLM通过创新的无代码本球面编码机制与多阶段优化策略，成功突破传统低比特压缩的瓶颈，为大语言模型部署提供了高效、低存储成本的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly constrained by memory capacity, weight bandwidth, and checkpoint storage during deployment. Existing low-bit compression methods mainly follow two directions. Scalar or group-wise quantization is simple and compatible with efficient low-precision kernels, but its representation capacity becomes limited when the target budget approaches 2 bits per weight. Vector-quantized weight compression provides a richer block-level representation, but usually introduces explicit codebooks, index lookup, and additional storage accounting. This paper presents BiSCo-LLM, a codebook-free binary spherical coding framework for extreme low-bit LLM weight compression. The core pipeline is built on three components. First, local weight chunks are mapped onto a unit hypersphere and binarized into compact spherical codes, so that the main payload is a bit-packed sign stream rather than explicit VQ centroids. Second, a residual BSQ stage encodes the reconstruction error left by the base spherical codec, providing an explicit rate-distortion path without stored codebooks. Third, category-wise recovery distillation is performed after replacing each Transformer module category, reducing the mismatch between local weight reconstruction and assembled model behavior. A small 8-bit protected-channel path is used as an auxiliary stabilization mechanism for sensitive channels and is counted separately from the BSQ payload. The reported storage budget includes binary codes, neural decoders, protected-channel payloads, LoRA adapters, and metadata.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种分层机器教学算法，首先贪婪选择能暴露互补奖励约束的信息丰富环境，然后在这些环境中策略性地查询低成本反馈。

Abstract: As autonomous agents are increasingly deployed across diverse operational contexts, aligning their behavior with human intent demands reward functions that remain robust to such changes rather than overfitting to any single environment. Inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) provides a principled way to infer such objectives from human feedback. However, existing analyses of optimal teaching approaches for IRL focus on single-environment, demonstration-only settings, leaving underexplored how heterogeneous feedback modalities and environment dynamics jointly constrain reward functions that generalize across multiple environments. Because demonstrations in one MDP entangle reward information with that environments specific structure, the resulting rewards frequently fail to generalize when the agent is deployed in a new setting. We first analyze how different feedback modalities constrain rewards, showing that, in the unlimited-data regime, comparisons impose strictly stronger global constraints than other modalities. Beyond this theoretical analysis, we introduce a hierarchical machine teaching algorithm for reward learning that operates across multiple MDPs. The algorithm first greedily selects informative environments that expose complementary reward constraints, then strategically queries low-cost feedback within those environments. Empirically, our method achieves substantially lower regret and stronger generalization to held-out environments than uniform teaching baselines under identical feedback budgets, demonstrating the importance of multi-environment, multi-modal teaching for learning dynamics-robust reward functions.

### [200] [Secure Decentralized Federated Learning via Gossip and Virtual Voting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08651)
*Amirhossein Taherpour,Xiaodong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出gspDAG-FL，一种基于共识的去中心化联邦学习框架，利用相同的gossip历史实现模型更新的最终确定性。通过构建紧凑的DAG和虚拟投票机制，实现无需全局协调的高效、安全、可审计的模型聚合，支持对拜占庭和懒惰节点的鲁棒性，在保持高检测率的同时提升吞吐量与学习质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于gossip的去中心化联邦学习缺乏最终确定性和对恶意或懒惰参与者的鲁棒性；而传统区块链等链式方案引入了全局协调开销，违背了去中心化局部性的设计目标。需要一种既能保障安全性又能避免中心化瓶颈的新方法。

Method: gspDAG-FL通过节点间仅与邻居交换模型数据，全节点收集事件证书与接收端背书的接受证明，重建紧凑的拓扑有向无环图（DAG），采用类似Hashgraph的虚拟投票机制，并生成轻量级全节点证书。共识基于唯一的模型来源元组而非参数状态一致，结合三重验证机制（载荷、证明、语义审计）增强抗干扰能力。

Result: 在MNIST分类与Penn Treebank语言建模任务中，gspDAG-FL达到接近基于验证的链式联邦学习的学习性能，显著降低协调开销，提高系统吞吐量，且在混合拜占庭与懒惰节点场景下仍保持高无效来源检测率。形式化证明了控制平面的安全性与条件存活性，并给出了在时变有效混合条件下带认证扰动gossip的收敛性保证。

Conclusion: gspDAG-FL成功实现了去中心化联邦学习中的安全、高效与可审计性平衡，通过利用gossip历史本身构建共识，避免了外部协调依赖，为大规模分布式学习提供了可信且高性能的解决方案。

Abstract: Decentralized federated learning (DFL) removes the central server by letting nodes exchange model updates through peer-to-peer gossip, but existing gossip-based methods often lack provenance finality and resilience to Byzantine or lazy participants. Ledger-assisted federated learning (FL) improves auditability, yet blockchains, shards, or settlement committees can reintroduce global coordination costs that conflict with DFL locality. This paper proposes \emph{gspDAG-FL}, a secure DFL framework that derives consensus from the same gossip history used to disseminate models. Nodes exchange model payloads only with neighbors, while full nodes collect event certificates and receiver-endorsed accepted gossip proofs, reconstruct a compact Topology directed acyclic graph (DAG), and run Hashgraph-style virtual voting followed by compact full-node certificates. Finality is over unique model-origin tuples, not identical local parameter states. To improve resilience, gspDAG-FL combines payload validation, accepted-proof validation, and private semantic audit before aggregation. We formalize the adversarial setting, prove safety and conditional liveness of the control plane, and give a convergence guarantee for certified perturbed gossip under time-varying effective mixing. Experiments on MNIST classification and Penn Treebank language modeling, using fair held-out validation/audit data and networks up to \(N=100\), show that gspDAG-FL achieves learning quality close to validation-based ledger FL while reducing coordination bottlenecks, improving throughput, and maintaining high invalid-origin detection under mixed Byzantine and lazy participation.
