### [201] [EdgeRefine: Privacy-Utility Balance for Graphs via Jaccard Sampling under Edge Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08659)
*Wenxiu Ding,Muzhi Liu,Zheng Yan,Mingjun Wang,Yifan Zhao,Qiao Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EdgeRefine 是一种基于局部差分隐私的图神经网络隐私保护框架，通过自适应边精炼提升隐私-效用平衡。它利用Jaccard相似性估计边存在概率，按重要性排序后选择性地添加噪声，结合隐私预算ε和采样率k控制边数与可靠性，显著提升模型性能。在节点分类任务中，相比现有方法，准确率提升达17.8%~19.7%；图分类任务中仅损失约5%精度；且对图重构攻击具有强鲁棒性，平均绝对误差高于1，有效防止隐私泄露。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图神经网络在隐私敏感场景应用受限，因图结构易泄露敏感边信息。传统方法通过向邻接矩阵注入噪声实现边级差分隐私，但过度噪声会严重损害模型效用，导致隐私与效用难以平衡。因此亟需一种更优的隐私保护机制，在保障隐私的同时最小化性能损失。

Method: 提出EdgeRefine框架：首先基于Jaccard相似性计算边存在概率并排序；根据隐私预算ε确定真边与假边的比例，分别采样；使用独立采样率k控制最终图的稀疏性；通过自适应筛选保留关键边，降低噪声影响。

Result: 在ACM数据集上GAT模型下节点分类准确率较最优基线提升17.8%，Cora数据集上GCN模型提升19.7%；图分类任务平均精度下降仅约5%；在图重构攻击下，相对绝对误差始终高于1（Cora均值1.962，AMAP均值1.472），表明具备强抗隐私泄露能力。

Conclusion: EdgeRefine通过自适应边精炼策略有效缓解了隐私-效用权衡难题，显著优于现有方法，在保持高隐私保障的同时实现了接近无噪声基线的性能表现，为隐私敏感图学习提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have shown considerable success in learning from graph-structured data, but their use in privacy-sensitive areas remains difficult because graph structure can leak sensitive link information. To satisfy edge-level differential privacy, a common approach is to inject noise into all elements of the graph's adjacency matrix, thereby obfuscating the existence of any single edge. However, stronger privacy requires more noise, and excessive noise reduces utility, making the privacy-utility balance a major barrier to practical privacy-preserving graph learning.
  To address this issue, we propose EdgeRefine, a local differential privacy framework that improves this trade-off through adaptive edge refinement. EdgeRefine first estimates edge-existence probabilities using Jaccard similarity and ranks edges for noisy edge removal. To ensure the sparsity and reliability of the final graph, it uses the privacy budget $ε$ to determine the ratio of true to false edges, samples them separately based on this probability ranking, and controls the total number of edges with a separate sampling rate $k$. Extensive experiments show that EdgeRefine achieves accuracy comparable to the noise-free baseline and substantially outperforms other privacy-preserving methods across datasets and GNN architectures. Under privacy budget $ε= 2.5$, EdgeRefine improves node classification accuracy over state-of-the-art baselines by 17.8\% on ACM under GAT and 19.7\% on Cora under GCN. In graph classification, it achieves an average accuracy degradation of around 5\% compared to the noise-free baseline. Under graph reconstruction attacks, EdgeRefine maintains relative absolute error levels above 1 across all privacy budgets, averaging 1.962 on Cora and 1.472 on AMAP, indicating strong resilience against privacy leakage.

</details>


### [202] [Resample or Reroute? Budget-Aware Test-Time Model Selection for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08665)
*Teng-Ruei Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种预算感知的测试时模型选择方法（RoR），在有限的每查询预算下，权衡重采样与重新路由之间的资源分配，以最大化预期正确性。该方法基于对选择与采样可恢复性的不对称性分析，设计了在线的重采样或重路由分配策略，并在多个基准上验证其优越性，尤其在异构性较高的任务中表现更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有路由机制在响应质量与服务成本之间存在权衡，且无法利用理想化的正确性标签和无限预算来实现最优选择。而实际部署系统面临的是不完美验证器和有限预算，因此需要一种能同时考虑重采样与重新路由的预算约束下的优化策略。

Method: 提出一种在线的重采样或重路由（RoR）分配策略，依据单位成本带来的边际正确性估计进行决策，充分利用预算并实现对选择与采样能力的不对称利用。

Result: 在包含11个模型的开源模型池上，于四个不同难度的基准上进行回放实验，结果表明RoR策略在成本-质量帕累托前沿上优于单路由、单承诺路由器、预算感知的Best-of-K、级联和随机分配等基线方法，尤其在最异构的基准上收益最大；消融实验显示收益受验证器质量限制，随验证器性能下降而减少；在提供方价格向量和无标签一致性验证器下的鲁棒性实验进一步验证了结论的适用范围。

Conclusion: 预算感知的测试时模型选择通过合理分配每查询预算中的资源，在有限条件下实现了对模型选择性能的有效提升，特别是在高异构场景下具有显著优势，且策略对验证器质量和外部环境变化具有一定的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Routing among large language models (LLMs) trades response quality against serving cost, motivated by the reported gap between deployed routers and a per-instance oracle. Recent analysis shows that test-time resampling can recover per-instance selection headroom that no single-commit router captures; however, that guarantee holds only under an idealized oracle equipped with correctness labels and an unconstrained budget, neither of which a deployed system has. To the best of our knowledge, no previous work treats resampling the committed model and rerouting to an alternative model as competing uses of a single per-query cost budget. Therefore, this work formulates budget-aware test-time model selection: given a per-query budget and an imperfect verifier, allocate each unit of budget between resampling and rerouting so that expected correctness is maximized. An online resample-or-reroute (RoR) allocation policy driven by estimated marginal correctness per unit cost is proposed, and its behavior is grounded in the recoverability asymmetry between selection and sampling. Replay experiments on newly regenerated multi-draw correctness tensors from an eleven-model open-weight pool over four benchmarks of differing difficulty show that the proposed RoR policy attains a favorable cost-quality Pareto front relative to single-route, one-commit-router, budget-aware best-of-K, cascade, and random-allocation baselines for the tested pools, with the largest gains on the most heterogeneous benchmark; an ablation further shows the gains are verifier-gated, shrinking as verifier quality degrades, and robustness replays under a provider price vector and a label-free agreement verifier delineate where the conclusions carry over.

</details>


### [203] [A Practical Investigation of Training-free Relaxed Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08690)
*Guoxuan Xia,Luka Ribar,Paul Balanca*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了无需训练的松弛型推测解码技术，统一了现有方法，并在现代设置下进行了基准测试，为实践者提供了经验性结论。关键发现包括：松弛型方法需要额外的能力评估，且多数依赖于表现良好的语言模型作为起草器，因此不适用于轻量级专用多标记预测起草器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准推测解码虽能保持LLM采样分布不变，但速度提升有限；放松这一严格保证可能带来进一步加速、可控的能力-速度权衡甚至能力提升，因此有必要探索训练-free的松弛型推测解码方法。

Method: 提出一个统一框架，整合现有松弛型推测解码技术，通过实验在当代设置下进行对比分析，评估不同方法在速度、准确性和能力上的表现。

Result: 实证表明，松弛型推测解码虽可提升速度，但需额外能力评估；多数方法依赖高质量语言模型作为起草器，对轻量级专用起草器不适用。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates sampling from an autoregressive LLM by using a faster auxiliary model to draft tokens which are then verified in parallel by the LLM. Standard speculative decoding is lossless: its rejection and resampling steps exactly preserve the LLM's sampling distribution. Recent work argues that relaxing this strict guarantee can yield further speed-ups, controlled capability-speed trade-offs, or even capability gains. We practically investigate training-free relaxed speculative decoding techniques, unify existing approaches within a shared framework, benchmark them on contemporary settings, and distil takeaways and empirical findings for practitioners. Important takeaways include: relaxation can require considerable capability evaluation unlike lossless speculative decoding, and many relaxed approaches rely on a drafter that is a good language model, making them unsuited for lightweight dedicated multi-token-prediction drafters.

### [204] [MPFlow: Learning Budgeted Max-Flow Optimization on the Lightning Network with Deep Graph Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08703)
*Harrison Rush,Vincent Davis,Simone Antonelli,Vikash Singh,Jesse Shrader,Emanuele Rossi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将流动性放置建模为预算约束下的组合优化问题，目标是最大化s-t最大流；使用图神经网络与近端策略优化（PPO）结合动作掩码构建轻量级强化学习代理，并引入‘枢纽排除’训练课程，迫使模型摆脱对中心节点的依赖，学习更鲁棒的容量感知策略。

Result: 在多个真实闪电网络快照上，所提方法在最大流指标上显著优于现有启发式基线，具有良好的泛化能力与稳定性；已在生产环境中成功部署，支撑超过30个节点的4640次通道开通过程，累计分配267.3 BTC（超1600万美元），验证了其实际有效性与可扩展性。

Abstract: We address liquidity placement in the Bitcoin Lightning Network (LN): given a fixed budget, which channels should a node open to maximize its routing capacity? We cast this as a budget-constrained combinatorial optimization problem on graphs, selecting $k$ edge additions that maximize $s$--$t$ max-flow, a theory-grounded measure of routing capacity, and solve it with graph reinforcement learning. Our lightweight agent combines a message-passing policy network with proximal policy optimization (PPO) and action masking, and is trained under a hub-exclusion curriculum: the network's top hubs are removed from training subgraphs, forcing the policy to learn capacity-aware placement rather than hub attachment. In extensive experiments on real Lightning Network snapshots, our method consistently outperforms strong heuristic baselines on the max-flow objective across multiple seeds and unseen graphs. The agent has been deployed in production for peer recommendations, executing 4640 channel-open decisions that cumulatively allocate 267.3 BTC over $16 million across 30 managed nodes.

### [205] [Deep Learning for Joint Narrowband Interference Cancellation and Soft Demodulation in OFDM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08717)
*Emmanouil Kavvousanos,Francky Catthoor,Vassilis Paliouras*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种统一的深度学习框架NBI-CNet和LLR-CNet，联合实现窄带干扰（NBI）消除与鲁棒软解调。NBI-CNet采用物理信息卷积结构，单次前向传播即可估计并去除多音干扰，相比最优算法降低60%计算复杂度；LLR-CNet作为结构去相关器，将非高斯残差映射为校准的软度量，避免传统方法中因残差结构导致的对数似然比（LLR）不可靠、译码器饱和及严重误码平台问题。仿真表明，在密集频谱下该框架消除了传统方法的误码平台，在强干扰（SIR=-10 dB）下性能仅落后最优迭代基线0.2-0.5 dB，且在重叠严重时（Q=12）获得超过3 dB编码增益。整体架构具备尺度不变性，无需重新训练即可泛化至任意FFT尺寸，并克服由干扰估计误差引发的2×10⁻⁴误码平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统压缩感知（CS）方法在处理窄带干扰（NBI）时存在高串行延迟，且残留信号具有结构化、非高斯特性，导致对数似然比（LLR）不可靠、译码器饱和，进而引发严重误码平台。经典高斯解映射器无法适应此类非理想残差，造成系统性能下降。因此亟需一种能联合处理干扰消除与软解调、兼容非高斯残差的新方法。

Method: 提出基于深度学习的统一框架：1）NBI-CNet——物理信息引导的卷积神经网络，用于单次前向传播估计并去除多音窄带干扰，无需预先知道干扰源数量；2）LLR-CNet——结构去相关器，将经干扰消除后的非高斯残差映射为可靠、校准的软度量，提升后续解调可靠性。两模块协同工作，构建端到端的抗干扰链路。

Result: 在强干扰（SIR = -10 dB）条件下，系统在目标块错误率（BLER=10⁻⁴）下仅比最优迭代基线低0.2–0.5 dB SNR；在轻度干扰但频谱重叠严重（Q=12）时，避免信号峰混淆，实现超过3 dB的编码增益；彻底消除传统方法中的2×10⁻⁴误码平台；且模型具备尺度不变性，可直接推广至任意FFT大小而无需重新训练。

Conclusion: 所提出的联合深度学习框架有效解决了传统方法中干扰消除与软解调之间的“管道不匹配”问题，显著提升OFDM系统在复杂干扰环境下的鲁棒性与性能上限，兼具高效性、通用性与可扩展性，为下一代抗干扰通信系统提供新范式。

Abstract: Narrowband interference (NBI) severely degrades orthogonal frequency-division multiplexing (OFDM) systems by corrupting subcarriers and rendering classical soft demodulation ineffective. Conventional compressed-sensing (CS) mitigation exhibits high sequential latency and leaves structured, non-Gaussian residuals that cause log-likelihood ratio (LLR) unreliability, decoder saturation, and severe error floors when employing classical Gaussian demappers. We resolve this pipeline mismatch using a unified deep learning framework for joint NBI cancellation and robust soft demodulation. First, NBI-CNet employs a physics-informed convolutional architecture to estimate NBI parameters and remove multi-tone interference in a single forward pass. Without requiring prior knowledge of the active interferer count, NBI-CNet reduces computational complexity by up to 60% ($N{=}2048, Q{=}64$) compared to the state-of-the-art EOMP-IDS algorithm. Second, LLR-CNet acts as a structural whitener by mapping non-Gaussian post-mitigation residuals onto well-calibrated soft metrics. Simulations demonstrate that this joint framework eliminates the error floors inherent to traditional baselines across dense grids. Under severe interference ($\text{SIR}{=}{-}10$ dB), the pipeline operates within a $0.2$ to $0.5$ dB SNR margin of the optimal iterative baseline at a target block error rate (BLER) of $10^{-4}$. Under mild interference ($\text{SIR}{=}10$ dB) with heavy spectral overlap ($Q{=}12$), where classical greedy algorithms erroneously subtract valid data components and corrupt the payload, NBI-CNet avoids signal-peak confusion to deliver a coding gain exceeding $3$ dB. Finally, the architecture circumvents the $2{\times}10^{-4}$ error floor triggered by interferer-estimation errors, while its scale-invariant design enables robust generalization across arbitrary FFT sizes without retraining.

### [206] [Latent Memory Palace: Reasoning for Control as Autoregressive Variational Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08724)
*Chuning Zhu,Eva Xu,Jose Barreiros,Krishnan Srinivasan,Paarth Shah,Abhishek Gupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为潜在记忆宫殿（Latent Memory Palace, LMP）的新方法，通过在自回归潜在空间中组织信息来实现控制策略的自适应推理。该方法将推理建模为变分推断，并设计了一种可训练的潜在空间强化学习技术以优化其变分下界。LMP-$\pi$ 策略在仿真和真实世界任务中表现出色，且具备可解释的测试时计算分配能力。此外，该框架还衍生出一种可变长度动作标记器 LMP-$\texttt{tok}$，显著提升了下游自回归策略的性能。整体工作为基于变分推断的潜在空间推理提供了新的视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型虽能实现自适应推理，但直接在语言空间中进行推理难以满足连续控制对空间感知和精确动作的要求。因此需要一种既能保持灵活性又能提供足够精度的推理机制。

Method: 提出潜在于自回归潜在空间中的记忆宫殿结构，将推理视为变分推断问题，通过构建变分下界并使用潜在空间强化学习进行优化，从而得到可解释且高效的控制策略与动作标记器。

Result: LMP-$\pi$ 在多种仿真与现实任务中表现优异，展现出可解释的动态计算分配；LMP-$\texttt{tok}$ 显著提升下游自回归策略性能。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了通过变分推断在潜在空间中实现自适应推理的新路径，为连续控制中的灵活决策提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Human decision-making is highly flexible -- some actions are taken immediately; others require longer deliberation. Language models have exhibited a similar capacity for adaptive "reasoning." However, transferring this capability to continuous control policies has been challenging, as directly reasoning in language space may lack the granularity for spatial understanding and precise motions. In this work, we show that reasoning for control policies can emerge by organizing information in an autoregressive latent space reminiscent of a memory palace, where retrieval is iterative and adaptive. Our method, Latent Memory Palace (LMP), formulates reasoning as variational inference with an autoregressive latent distribution. We derive a latent-space reinforcement learning technique to tractably optimize its variational lower bound. The resulting policy, LMP-$π$, achieves strong empirical performance in simulation and real-world domains while exhibiting interpretable, adaptive allocation of test-time compute. We further show that the same framework yields a variable-length action tokenizer, LMP-$\texttt{tok}$, which significantly improves the performance of downstream autoregressive policies. Together, these results present a new perspective on latent reasoning for control through the lens of variational inference.

### [207] [Super Weights in LLMs and the Failure of Selective Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08733)
*Shreyas Subramanian,Adewale Akinfaderin,Akarsha Sehwag*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了超级权重（Super Weights）在大语言模型中的关键作用，发现其移除并不总是导致性能显著下降，且单独训练这些权重会导致模型性能崩溃至随机猜测水平。相比之下，随机选择的参数或使用低秩适配（LoRA）方法则能有效提升性能。结果表明，参数的重要性不等于可训练性，有效的微调依赖于对整个层的结构化分解，而非聚焦于个别重要权重。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究超级权重在大语言模型中的实际重要性及其在微调中的可训练性，以验证其是否真正影响模型性能。

Method: 通过对比实验，分析移除或单独训练超级权重与随机选择参数的效果，并将低秩适配（LoRA）应用于不同参数集，评估其在多个模型上的表现。

Result: 单独训练超级权重导致模型性能急剧下降至随机猜测水平；而随机选择相同数量的参数或使用低秩更新反而能提升性能。此外，限制LoRA仅在超级权重位置更新仍能获得与全参数更新相当的结果。

Conclusion: 参数重要性并不等同于可训练性，有效的微调应基于结构化的方法（如低秩分解）对整个层进行更新，而非聚焦于孤立的重要权重。

Abstract: Recent work identified Super Weights, individual parameters whose removal degrades model performance by orders of magnitude. We show that this degradation due to pruning Super Weights does not universally apply to all LLMs. Furthermore, if these parameters are so important, Super Weight-aware training should be effective. We show the opposite. Training Super Weights in isolation (100 to 8,192 parameters) drops accuracy to random-guessing levels on both OLMo-1B and OLMo-7B, and expanding to local neighborhoods of up to 36K parameters provides no improvement. The failure is specific to Super Weight coordinates: training an equal number of randomly chosen positions in the same down_proj layers instead improves over the baseline, so the collapse comes from targeting Super Weights, not from sparsity itself. Vanilla LoRA, updating every position in attention weight matrices through low-rank structure, succeeds with only 0.16% of parameters, and applying the same low-rank update to down_proj succeeds as well. A 10-seed ablation confirms that constraining LoRA updates at positions corresponding to Super Weight coordinates yields statistically indistinguishable results. These findings establish that parameter importance does not imply parameter trainability in isolation, and that effective fine-tuning relies on structured decompositions over entire layers rather than targeting individually important weights.

### [208] [Dimensionality Reduction Meets Network Science: Sensemaking on UMAP's kNN Graph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08746)
*Duen Horng Chau,Donghao Ren,Fred Hohman,Dominik Moritz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了UMAP在高维数据探索中的应用，指出其内部构建的k近邻图（kNN）常被忽视，而该图能有效反映原始高维空间中的数据流形结构。研究展示了将标准图算法应用于此内部图的潜力：利用PageRank识别代表性数据点，通过k-core分解揭示密集核心与稀疏外围区域，以及使用聚类系数检测高度相似的数据邻域。实验在MNIST和Fashion MNIST数据集上验证了这些方法的有效性，结果表明其不仅实用，且在性能上可媲美或补充专门设计的方法（如k-medoids、HDBSCAN）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前使用UMAP进行数据分析时，主要关注其二维嵌入结果，忽略了其在高维空间中构建的丰富k近邻图。该图保留了原始数据流形信息，未受降维投影带来的失真影响，因此具有重要分析价值。本文旨在挖掘这一被忽视的内部表示潜力，提升数据理解能力。

Method: 提出将标准图分析方法（如PageRank、k-core分解、聚类系数）应用于UMAP生成的内部kNN图，以揭示数据的结构特性，包括代表性点、密度分布和紧密连接的子群。

Result: 在MNIST和Fashion MNIST数据集上的定量与定性评估显示，基于图的方法在识别代表样本、发现密度结构和探测紧密邻域方面表现优异，效果不逊于甚至优于专用方法，如k-medoids和HDBSCAN，具备良好的互补性。

Conclusion: UMAP的内部kNN图是一个极具价值的分析工具，将其与经典图算法结合，可显著增强对高维数据的洞察力，为数据探索提供新视角，建议在常规分析流程中纳入此类图分析步骤。

Abstract: While UMAP is widely used for exploring high-dimensional data, typical workflows focus on its lower-dimensional embedding, largely overlooking the rich k-nearest-neighbor (kNN) graph that UMAP constructs internally. This graph encodes the data manifold in its original high-dimensional space, before the distortion that UMAP's 2D projection introduces. We demonstrate the untapped potential of this internal representation, showing how standard graph algorithms applied to this graph enhance data sensemaking: (1) PageRank identifies representative data points, (2) k-core decomposition reveals dense core regions versus sparse periphery, and (3) clustering coefficient detects tight-knit neighborhoods with highly-similar data points. Through quantitative and qualitative evaluation on MNIST and Fashion MNIST, we show that these graph-based analyses are not only practical but also competitive with or complementary to purpose-built methods (e.g., k-medoids for exemplar selection, HDBSCAN for density-based clustering).

### [209] [SLORR: Simple and Efficient In-Training Low-Rank Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08754)
*David González-Martínez,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SLORR是一种简单、无状态且保持模型架构的训练中低秩正则化框架，通过Hoyer稀疏度和核范数两种变体实现，利用GPU友好的近似方法在前向和反向传播中直接正则化原始权重矩阵，具有近似保证。在ImageNet-1K上对ResNet-50、ViT-B/16、ViT-L/16进行短周期持续训练和ResNet-18预训练实验，以及在135M和560M规模的大语言模型预训练中验证，均显示其能有效提升模型可压缩性，训练开销低于8%（大模型低于1%），且性能保持更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩正则化方法存在需执行大型权重矩阵的SVD、修改模型结构引入额外可训练参数或依赖状态缓存等问题，限制了其在现代神经网络中的应用。为克服这些局限，需要一种简单、无状态、不改变模型结构的训练时低秩正则化方法。

Method: 提出SLORR框架，基于Hoyer稀疏度和核范数设计两种变体，采用GPU友好型近似方法处理正则项的前向与反向传播，并提供理论近似保证。该方法直接作用于原始权重矩阵，无需额外参数或状态存储。

Result: 在ImageNet-1K上的多种模型（包括ResNet-50、ViT-B/16、ViT-L/16、ResNet-18）的持续训练和预训练中，SLORR显著提升了模型可压缩性，训练开销低于8%；在135M和560M规模的大语言模型预训练中，压缩模型性能优于未正则化模型，平均训练开销低于1%。

Conclusion: SLORR是一种高效、轻量、兼容性强的训练时低秩正则化方法，可在不改变模型结构的前提下有效提升神经网络的可压缩性，同时保持极低的训练开销和优异的性能表现，适用于从图像模型到大语言模型的广泛场景。

Abstract: Low-rank factorization is widely used to compress neural networks, but modern models are often not naturally amenable to aggressive factorization without significant accuracy loss. Existing training-time low-rank regularizers can improve compressibility, but they often require SVDs of large weight matrices, modify the model architecture (introducing additional trainable parameters), or rely on stateful cached quantities. To address these limitations, we introduce SLORR, a simple, stateless, and architecture-preserving framework for in-training low-rank regularization, instantiated with two main variants based on the Hoyer sparsity metric and the nuclear norm. SLORR directly regularizes the original weight matrices using GPU-friendly approximations for the forward and backward passes of the regularizers, for which we provide approximation guarantees. We first evaluate SLORR on ImageNet-1K across short-horizon continued training of ResNet-50, ViT-B/16, and ViT-L/16, and pretraining of ResNet-18, where SLORR induces compressibility while introducing less than 8% training overhead. We further evaluate SLORR-Hoyer in LLM pretraining at 135M and 560M scales: SLORR-trained compressed models preserve performance substantially better than unregularized models while adding less than 1% average training overhead.

</details>

### [210] [Context Graphs for Proactive Enterprise Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07721)
*Avinash Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于上下文图的主动式企业AI代理框架，通过实时监控企业实体状态变化，自动发现并推送高相关性、高紧迫性的信息，显著提升工作效率。实验表明，该方法在多个企业场景中实现0.83的Precision@5、11%的误报率，并将信息发现时间从47分钟缩短至30秒以内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前企业AI系统（如RAG和代理框架）大多为被动响应式，需等待用户查询才能行动，无法充分发挥潜力。真正的企业生产力提升需要能够主动发现并推送相关信息的智能代理。

Method: 提出上下文图（Context Graph），用于建模企业实体、关系及状态随时间的变化；设计了差分检测引擎（Delta Detection Engine）持续监控状态变化，使用可解释的提示工程构建的主动评分器（Proactivity Scorer）对候选洞察进行排序，并通过大模型驱动的呈现层生成有依据的通知。所有组件均形式化定义，形成统一的主动评分函数，并提供基于NetworkX和Anthropic Claude API的完整Python实现。

Result: 在合同生命周期管理、工程事故响应、销售管道健康度三个典型企业案例中，该框架实现了Precision@5为0.83，误报率为0.11，平均信息发现时间从47分钟降至30秒以下，显著优于传统被动基线。

Conclusion: 基于上下文图的主动式代理能有效推动企业AI从被动响应转向主动服务，为提升组织效率提供了可落地的技术路径。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and agentic frameworks have advanced enterprise AI considerably, yet agents remain fundamentally reactive: they wait for a human query before acting. This paper argues that genuine enterprise productivity gains require proactive agents: systems that surface relevant, actionable information to workers before they ask. We propose the Context Graph, a live relational data structure that models enterprise entities, their relationships, and state transitions over time. Built on this graph, we define a Delta Detection Engine that continuously monitors state changes, a Proactivity Scorer that ranks candidate insights by urgency, relevance, and persona-fit, and a Surfacing Layer powered by an LLM that delivers ranked notifications with grounded explanations. We formalize each component, derive a unified Proactivity Score function, and provide a complete end-to-end Python implementation using NetworkX and the Anthropic Claude API. Evaluation across three generic enterprise case studies (contract lifecycle management, engineering incident response, and sales pipeline hygiene) demonstrates that context-graph-driven proactivity achieves Precision@5 of 0.83, a false positive rate of 0.11, and reduces mean time to surface from 47 minutes (reactive baseline) to under 30 second.

Result: 该工具能够高效模拟并可视化农业供应链在不同扰动下的连锁反应，提升决策者对复杂系统动态的理解能力。

### [212] [Adversarial Social Epistemology for Assemblies of Humans and Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07760)
*Mihnea C. Moldoveanu,Joel A. C. Baum*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对抗性社会认识论（ASE），用于分析高度互动的公共话语环境，其中信息通过证言链、推理、制度认证和隐性信任进行支撑。作者指出，传统概念如‘认识论泡沫’或‘回音室’无法充分解释信息操纵现象，关键在于揭示个体如何利用本应增强可信度的信任机制来谋取私利。文章引入基于语义推理的信念网络框架，构建分析工具以识别并纠正信任链条中的漏洞，从而恢复公共沟通中的可审计性与可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论难以解释在高度互动的公共话语中，为何信任机制会被滥用，导致信息被扭曲或伪造。需要一种新范式来理解这种信任的异化过程及其后果。

Method: 采用基于认知网络的框架，结合推理主义语义学，对公共陈述的推断链条进行建模，识别信任被破坏的关键节点，并设计审计与修复机制。

Result: 成功构建了一个能够检测和应对信任侵蚀的分析系统，揭示了信任机制如何被策略性地滥用，并提出了可操作的补救方案。

Conclusion: 对抗性社会认识论提供了一个强有力的理论工具，不仅解释了复杂信息生态中的信任危机，还为重建可信赖的公共沟通提供了实践路径。

Abstract: We outline an adversarial social epistemology (ASE) for densely interactive communicative landscapes in which public assertions are scaffolded by chains of testimony, inference, institutional certification, and tacit trust. In such landscapes, agents have incentives and affordances to distort, color, omit, fabricate, or strategically under-specify information for private, reputational, rhetorical, or material gains. We argue that these phenomena are not adequately captured by familiar descriptions of epistemic bubbles, echo chambers, or misinformation diffusion. What requires explanation is how communicative agents exploit the commitments and entitlements that normally make scaffolded assertions trustworthy. We provide language that delivers the requisite analysis, outline mechanisms that subvert trust in scaffolded public communications, and outline machinery for auditing and redressing trust breaches arising from subverting the auditability of inferential chains, drawing on epistemic networks, enriched with an inferentialist semantics for interpreting assertions.

### [213] [Aligning Clinical Needs and AI Capabilities: A Survey on LLMs for Medical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07761)
*Qi Peng,Jiatong Li,Sirui Huang,Yiyang Jiang,Kaisong Gong,Ronger Ding,Shijie Ye,Changmeng Zheng,Yi Cai,Xiaobo Yang,Jin Huang,Xiao-Yong Wei,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文综述了医疗大语言模型（LLMs）在临床推理和患者护理中的最新进展，提出了一种结合临床实践与计算方法的双重视角。从临床角度，基于Miller金字塔构建了五个级别的能力框架，涵盖从知识回忆到动态病例管理；从计算角度，将演绎、归纳和溯因推理与常见医疗任务对应。研究还引入了一个涵盖五个层次医疗推理能力的基准数据集，并评估了18个先进模型的表现，发现专科模型在诊断任务中表现优异，而通用模型在决策支持和对话任务中更优。最后讨论了当前挑战如数据限制、幻觉和可解释性问题，并提出未来需构建更安全、可靠且可融入临床工作流的系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在医疗领域的广泛应用，亟需系统梳理其在临床推理中的应用进展，明确不同模型在各类医疗任务中的优势与局限，同时建立标准化评估体系以推动技术向真实临床场景落地。

Method: 采用双视角分析框架：一是基于临床实践的五级能力模型（依据Miller金字塔），二是匹配计算层面的三类推理模式（演绎、归纳、溯因）。通过构建多层级医疗推理基准数据集，对18个主流医学大模型进行实证评估，结合定性分析与定量结果，揭示模型性能差异及其背后原因。

Result: 医学专科模型在诊断相关任务中表现突出，尤其在复杂病例识别和病因推断方面；通用大模型在决策支持、医患对话生成等需要广泛知识整合的任务中更具优势。基准测试显示，现有模型在高阶推理任务（如动态病例管理）上仍存在明显短板，且普遍存在幻觉与缺乏可解释性问题。

Conclusion: 尽管医疗大语言模型在多个临床任务中展现出潜力，但其可靠性与安全性仍有待提升。未来研究应聚焦于高质量医学数据构建、减少幻觉、增强模型可解释性与实际工作流集成能力，以实现真正可信、可部署的智能辅助系统。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have emerged as important tools in healthcare, showing growing potential for clinical reasoning and patient care. This survey examines recent progress in medical LLMs, focusing on reasoning applications and requirements. We present a dual-view approach that connects clinical practice with computational methods. On the clinical side, we establish a five-level competency scheme following Miller's Pyramid, progressing from knowledge recall to dynamic case management. On the computational side, we link deductive, inductive, and abductive reasoning patterns to common medical goals and tasks. We also introduce a benchmark dataset spanning five levels of medical reasoning capability and report results on 18 state-of-the-art models, revealing that medical specialist models excel in diagnosis-centric tasks while general models lead in decision support and dialogue. We conclude by discussing current progress and open challenges, including data limitations, hallucination, and grounding issues, and outline directions toward safer, more reliable, and workflow-ready systems.

</details>


### [214] [Alignment Plausibility: A New Standard for Assuring AI in Healthcare](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07766)
*Gwydion Williams,Sara Zannone,Bilal A Mateen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将大型语言模型（LLMs）在心理健康支持中的对齐问题，类比人类临床实践的安全保障机制，从价值规范、训练嵌入和部署监督三个层面构建结构性安全。为此引入“对齐可信度”概念，作为评估AI健康系统是否可能带来积极效果且不造成伤害的监管框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型虽被广泛用于心理支持，但其设计受注意力经济驱动，倾向于维持用户参与而非提供真正有效的心理干预，导致依赖、边界模糊及错误信念强化等长期风险被忽视。现有安全措施多为被动应对，缺乏系统性预防机制。

Method: 提出三层次对齐结构：1）基于临床实践规范明确价值；2）通过训练将这些价值观内化至模型；3）部署中实施持续监督以检测偏差与长期危害，类似人类临床督导机制。并引入‘对齐可信度’作为评估依据，类比生物学中的‘生物可信度’。

Result: 该框架提供了一种系统性方法来论证或质疑心理健康AI系统的安全性与有效性，强调不仅要防止直接伤害，更要确保其长期有益于患者，从而提升公众信任。

Conclusion: 将对齐工作组织为价值、训练与监督三重结构，有助于实现更可靠的、可验证的心理健康AI系统，推动其向负责任、可持续的方向发展。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have become significant providers of mental health support, yet they remain products of an attention economy whose operational and commercial targets favour sustained engagement over the friction that effective psychological support often requires. Developers' safety responses have been largely reactive, addressing the most visible and acute harms while subtler, longer-term patterns of risk (e.g., dependency, boundary erosion, the amplification of distorted beliefs) receive less attention. We contend that making LLMs structurally safe requires alignment organised at three levels that mirror how society assures the safety of human clinical practice: 1) explicit value specification grounded in the codified normative commitments of clinical practice; 2) training that embeds those values in the model; and 3) oversight that detects drift and longer-term harm during deployment, much as clinical supervision does for human practice. Organising alignment in this way yields a construct we call alignment plausibility - a structured demonstration that a system's values, training regime, and oversight mechanisms are together consistent with safe and positive outcomes. We propose alignment plausibility as a regulatory construct (by drawing analogy to the established construct of biological plausibility) for AI in health: a principled way to argue for, or against, trust that systems are aligned to positive health outcomes, will cause no harm even where capable of doing so, and will ultimately lead to patient benefit.

</details>


### [215] [Idiobionics: The Unification of Privacy and Intelligent Robotic Prostheses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07775)
*Kwesi Afari Darfoor,Patrick M. Pilarski,Bailey Kacsmar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出“个体生物电子学”（idiobionics）这一新研究方向，旨在系统探讨智能假肢与个人隐私之间的交叉问题。随着假肢集成先进传感器和人工智能控制技术，其功能虽大幅提升，但也带来了隐私泄露等安全风险。作者定义了idiobionics，梳理相关文献，并初步分析潜在的恶意攻击方式，最后提出一系列开放性研究问题，以推动可信赖的可穿戴机器人系统发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能假肢因集成先进传感与人工智能技术而具备更强的自适应能力，但同时也引入了隐私泄露等安全隐患，这些风险可能阻碍用户采纳。因此，亟需系统性地研究假肢中的隐私问题，以实现下一代假肢的全面潜力。

Method: 通过文献综述构建idiobionics概念框架，识别现有技术中的隐私威胁，分析潜在的对抗性攻击场景，并归纳出该领域关键的开放研究问题。

Result: 提出了idiobionics的概念体系，展示了智能假肢在隐私方面的潜在攻击路径，并整理出一组面向未来研究的关键问题，为可穿戴机器人与人机融合系统的安全设计提供指引。

Conclusion: idiobionics作为一个新兴研究方向，有助于深入理解并应对智能假肢中的隐私挑战，从而促进其更广泛、安全地应用，释放其全部潜能。

Abstract: The human body is at the center of a growing family of technologies designed to tightly and persistently couple biological and digital systems. Robotic prostheses are a representative example of this tight coupling. Also referred to as bionic limbs, robotic prostheses are devices that support people who have lost limbs in pursuing daily life activities such as walking and grasping objects. Bionic limbs are now perceptive and responsive owing to their integration with advanced sensors and artificial intelligence-based control approaches. Consequently, such robotic prostheses can now be viewed as semiautonomous wearable robotic systems that can co-adapt with their users. However, the same sensing and control advancements that increase the capability of robotic prostheses also introduce threat vectors that could be exploited by malicious entities to violate the privacy of users. To fully realize the benefits of next-generation bionic limbs, we maintain it is important to directly understand and address these privacy risks and the barriers they might present to user adoption. This paper therefore introduces a new line of inquiry we term idiobionics to holistically investigate issues at the intersection of privacy and intelligent bionic limbs. As the main contribution of this paper, we define idiobionics, ground it in related literature, and provide preliminary evidence showing and discussing potential adversarial attacks that could exploit intelligent bionic limb designs. We then contribute a curated list of open research questions within idiobionics that are relevant to researchers in wearable robotics and other human-facing autonomous systems. We expect that idiobionics research will help unlock the full potential of robotic prostheses and related bionic devices.

</details>


### [216] [Infinity-Parser2 Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07836)
*Zuming Huang,Jun Huang,Kexuan Ren,Baode Wang,Weizhen Li,Jianming Feng,Yu Wang,Yichen Yao,Shijun Lin,Yige Tang,Cheng Peng,Weidi Xu,Wei Chu,Yinghui Xu,Yuan Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Infinity-Parser2提出一种结合可控数据合成与多任务强化学习的端到端文档解析框架，解决标注数据稀缺问题。构建了可扩展的合成引擎，生成500万样本的中英双语文档数据集Infinity-Doc2-5M，涵盖多种文档类型和丰富标注（边界框、标准内容形式、阅读顺序）。设计可验证的多任务奖励机制，联合优化8个目标（布局分析、表格/公式/图表/化学式解析、文档VQA等），统一感知、结构与推理。发布两个变体：Flash版低延迟、高吞吐；Pro版高精度，达到87.6%（olmOCR-Bench）和74.3%（ParseBench），超越多个现有模型，泛化能力强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文档解析数据集存在标注稀缺、覆盖不全、多任务协同不足等问题，限制了模型性能与泛化能力。需通过可控数据合成生成大规模高质量标注数据，并设计统一优化框架实现多任务联合学习。

Method: 构建可控渲染与迭代精炼相结合的合成引擎生成大规模数据；设计基于可验证反馈的多任务强化学习框架，联合训练8个核心任务；采用共享架构推出低延迟Flash版与高精度Pro版模型。

Result: Infinity-Doc2-5M数据集包含500万样本，覆盖多样文档类型；Infinity-Parser2-Pro在olmOCR-Bench达87.6%，ParseBench达74.3%，优于DeepSeek-OCR-2、PaddleOCR-VL-1.5、MinerU2.5；模型在图表、化学式、文档VQA上表现优异，具备强泛化能力。

Conclusion: Infinity-Parser2通过可控数据合成与多任务强化学习，有效缓解标注数据稀缺问题，实现了端到端文档解析的高性能与强泛化能力，为多模态文档理解提供了新范式。

Abstract: We present Infinity-Parser2, a large multimodal model that couples a controllable data-synthesis pipeline with multi-task reinforcement learning for end-to-end document parsing, addressing the persistent scarcity of faithfully annotated parsing corpora. Our contributions are threefold. First, we build a scalable synthesis engine, pairing a controllable rendering framework with an iterative refinement loop, and use it to construct and open-source Infinity-Doc2-5M: a 5-million-sample bilingual (Chinese/English) corpus spanning diverse document types, annotated with element bounding boxes, canonical content forms (Markdown, HTML, LaTeX, SMILES, structured charts), and full-page reading order. Second, we introduce a verifiable, multi-task reward system that enables Joint Reinforcement Learning across eight co-trained objectives (document parsing, layout analysis, table parsing, math formula parsing, chart parsing, chemical formula parsing, document VQA, and general multimodal understanding), unifying perception, structure, and reasoning in a single optimization signal. Third, we release two variants under a shared architecture: Infinity-Parser2-Flash, optimized for low-latency inference with a $3.68\times$ throughput gain over Infinity-Parser-7B, and Infinity-Parser2-Pro, engineered for precision-critical settings. Infinity-Parser2-Pro reaches state-of-the-art 87.6% on olmOCR-Bench and 74.3% on ParseBench, surpassing DeepSeek-OCR-2, PaddleOCR-VL-1.5, and MinerU2.5, with strong generalization to charts, chemical formulas, and document VQA.

</details>


### [217] [VectorizationLLM: Smart Vectorization Based AI Assistant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07846)
*Ryan Duke*

Main category: cs.AI

The result is 94 prompt, completion, and reasoning-trace rows. In every row, the prompt names the real indicator, subsector, year, and source of the record it comes from. The data adaptation work was carried out by Adaption Labs. Along the way we describe a problem that is common when language models are used to build datasets. The prompts can match the real numbers while saying nothing about the real domain. We show that fixing this raises the share of domain-grounded prompts from 1 out of 78 in an earlier release to 94 out of 94, and that every retrieval answer now matches its source value (84 out of 84). We release the data, the reasoning layer, and a per-row provenance file under CC-BY-4.0. We are clear about the limits. With 89 records and 17 indicators that have only one observation, this is a reference and seed dataset, not a large training set. Most reasoning rows are retrieval rather than multi-step computation.

### [222] [Persona Cartography: Charting Language Model Personality Traits in Weight Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07916)
*Luke Baines,Anton Gonzalvez Hawthorne,Mariia Koroliuk,Irakli Shalibashvili,Clément Dumas,Konstantinos Voudouris,David Demitri Africa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将大语言模型的潜在行为模式（即‘人格’）视为由OCEAN框架（开放性、尽责性、外向性、宜人性、神经质）描述的行为特征空间中的位置，并通过低秩适配器来放大或抑制特定特质。研究在六种不同规模（4B-32B）的模型上验证了这些适配器可单调地影响目标特质，且多个适配器可近似叠加生成混合人格，同时在中等规模下保持原有能力表现。此外，调整人格特质会影响安全相关的下游行为（如神经质影响挫败感，宜人性影响阿谀奉承）。作者还提出一种无监督心理测量流程，从模型输出中提取出四个可解释的行为因子（语气、主动性、说教性、认知谨慎性），从而实现对人格的可控学习、扩展与组合，为人格测量、模型编辑与安全性提供了新桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型存在重复性的行为模式（即‘人格’），但缺乏可靠工具来分解、度量和控制这些人格特征。为了提升模型的可控性、可解释性和安全性，亟需建立一个系统化的人格建模与调控框架。

Method: 采用OCEAN人格五维模型描述模型人格特征；训练低秩适配器以调节各维度特质；使用基于人类验证的LLM裁判、特定性格的多选题基准和标准能力评估进行效果验证；引入无监督心理测量方法从模型输出中提取行为因子；分析适配器在不同规模下的单调性、可叠加性及对性能的影响。

Result: 适配器能有效、单调地调节目标人格特质，多适配器组合具有近似加性效应，且在中等规模下不损害模型能力；人格变化显著影响安全相关行为（如神经质影响挫折反应，宜人性影响讨好倾向）；无监督方法成功识别出四个可解释的行为因子，支持人格的可控构建与编辑。

Conclusion: 该研究为大语言模型的人格建模提供了一种可量化、可控制、可组合的方法，打通了人格测量、模型编辑与安全控制之间的路径，有助于实现更安全、可控、可解释的语言模型开发。

Abstract: Large language models exhibit recurring behavioural patterns -- personas -- that shape generalisation and safety, but we lack reliable tools for decomposing, measuring, and controlling them. Our central insight is to treat personas as positions in a space of behavioural traits, using the OCEAN framework to describe model personas in terms of Openness, Conscientiousness, Extraversion, Agreeableness, and Neuroticism. We train low-rank adapters to amplify or suppress individual traits, and evaluate their effects using an LLM-judge calibrated against a human-validated panel, trait-specific multiple-choice benchmarks, and standard capability evaluations. Across six models from three families (4B-32B), we find that each adapter moves its target trait largely monotonically with scale, combines approximately additively with other adapters to construct mixed personas, and preserves performance on capability benchmarks at moderate scales. We further show that the induced trait axes affect safety-relevant behaviour in downstream evaluations: for example, moving along neuroticism and agreeableness axes affects frustration and sycophancy respectively. We also introduce an unsupervised psychometric pipeline that recovers four interpretable behavioural factors (tone, initiative, didacticism, epistemic caution) from model rollouts. Persona control can then be considered in terms of learning, scaling, and composing traits in weight space, providing a bridge between personality measurement, model editing, and safety.

### [223] [Evaluating the Effect of Frame Rate in Sequence-Based Classification of Autism-Related Self-Stimulatory Hand Idiosyncrasies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07957)
*Raunak Mondal,Peter Washington*

TL;DR: 本研究针对自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）的远程行为筛查，提出基于视频的自动化检测方法。通过对比LSTM与GRU模型在不同采样率下的表现，发现每15帧采样时GRU模型达到98.75%的最高准确率；同时评估了十种数据增强策略，表明上采样对复杂行为视频增强至关重要。个性化建模方法在时间分割数据上表现出稳定预测能力（平均损失1.84，标准差0.79），为小样本临床场景提供实用指导。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Autism spectrum disorder (ASD) affects over 75 million individuals worldwide, yet scalable computational methods for remote behavioral screening remain limited. This study addresses two complementary challenges in automated detection of autism-related self-stimulatory behaviors from video: (1) identifying the optimal sequence-based neural network architecture and temporal sampling rate, and (2) characterizing data augmentation strategies for training on small behavioral datasets. For the first objective, long short-term memory (LSTM) and gated recurrent unit (GRU) models were trained on pose-derived features from the Self-Stimulatory Behavior Diagnosis (SSBD) dataset at frame sampling intervals of 1, 5, 15, 30, 45, and 90 frames. Both architectures exceeded prior convolutional neural network (CNN) baselines (62-76% accuracy), with peak accuracies of 97.5% (LSTM) and 98.75% (GRU) at a sampling interval of every 15 frames. For the second objective, ten data augmentation strategies were applied to an I3D transfer learning pipeline, with an ablation study quantifying the marginal contribution of each technique. Horizontal flip achieved the highest standalone accuracy (48.78%), while exclusion of upsampling from the augmentation pipeline produced the largest performance degradation, indicating its necessity for complex behavioral video augmentation. A personalized machine learning approach, in which per-subject models were trained and tested on temporally split segments of each video, produced consistent predictions (mean loss 1.84, SD 0.79). These results provide practitioners with concrete guidance on architecture selection, sampling rate, and augmentation strategy for video-based behavioral classification in data-scarce clinical domains.

### [224] [Agentic Neural Architecture Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07984)
*Seokhoon Jeong,Mijung Kim,Taehwan Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentNAS提出一种融合大语言模型（LLM）与神经架构搜索（NAS）的新机制，通过LLM生成高质量种子架构并分解为可插拔模块的“槽化架构”，自动构建任务特定的搜索空间，避免手动设计。该方法在17个跨模态任务上实现11项新纪录，且LLM与NAS互补：LLM提供优质初始架构，NAS通过模块重组进一步优化，三类不同能力的LLM均验证了该分工的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NAS方法受限于人工设计的搜索空间，需大量领域知识且难以迁移；而LLM虽能生成开放空间架构，但缺乏高效搜索机制。如何协同二者优势、合理分配任务尚不明确。

Method: AgentNAS采用三阶段模块化流程：首先由LLM生成种子架构；其次将其分解为带命名模块槽的“槽化架构”，形成任务相关的结构化搜索空间；最后利用传统NAS在此空间内进行组合优化。各阶段独立贡献可量化评估。

Result: 在NAS-Bench-360和Unseen NAS数据集上的17个任务中，AgentNAS在11个任务上达到新最优性能，超越已有基线及专家定制设计；消融实验表明LLM与NAS具有显著互补性，前者提供高质量初始解，后者通过模块重组带来额外增益。

Conclusion: LLM与NAS的协同可通过“种子生成+结构化搜索”机制实现高效分工，该模式不依赖特定LLM能力，具备强鲁棒性与广泛适用性，为自动化架构设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Neural architecture search (NAS) methods have grown increasingly efficient, yet they remain bounded by manually engineered search spaces that require substantial domain expertise and must be rebuilt for every new task. Large language models (LLMs) can generate architectures in an open-ended space, but how to optimally divide the labor between LLM-driven design and NAS-driven search remains unexplored. We propose a mechanism that bridges these two paradigms: an LLM produces a high-quality seed architecture, then decomposes it into a "slotted architecture", a scaffold with named, interchangeable module slots that automatically defines a bounded, task-specific search space for conventional NAS to explore, without manual engineering. We instantiate this mechanism in AgentNAS, a modular three-phase pipeline in which each component's contribution can be measured independently. On 17 tasks spanning classification, dense regression, segmentation, and multi-label tagging across diverse modalities (NAS-Bench-360 and Unseen NAS), AgentNAS establishes a new state of the art on 11 tasks, outperforming published baselines including task-specific expert designs. Ablation studies show that the two search mechanisms are broadly complementary: the LLM-generated seed already surpasses published baselines on the majority of tasks, and NAS delivers additional gains in most cases through combinatorial recombination across slots, a mode of search that independent LLM samples cannot replicate. These patterns hold across three LLMs of different capability levels, confirming that the division of labor is robust. Our code is available at https://github.com/alroimfebruary/AgentNAS.

</details>


### [225] [Concretized Proposition Prompting Resolves Composition-Knowledge Dichotomy in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08018)
*Changhun Lee,Minguk Jeon,Jongkyung Shin,Chiehyeon Lim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Concretized Proposition Prompting (CPP)的框架，旨在解决大语言模型在组合性与知识性之间的平衡难题（即组合-知识二分法）。通过显式具体化与问题相关命题，CPP显著提升了推理性能，尤其在医学基准测试中表现突出，同时在数学基准测试中也保持竞争力。实验表明，CPP可扩展至不同基础模型和参数规模，是一种能够弥合组合型与知识型方法差距的根本性范式，从而为逻辑组织且事实依据充分的推理提供了坚实基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在处理需要精确知识的任务时往往难以兼顾组合性和知识性，这种矛盾被称为组合-知识二分法。现有方法难以有效平衡两者，因此亟需一种新的机制来提升模型在复杂推理任务中的表现。

Method: 提出Concretized Proposition Prompting (CPP)框架，通过显式将与问题相关的命题具体化，使模型更清晰地理解并利用事实信息进行推理。该方法不依赖特定模型结构，具有良好的通用性和可扩展性。

Result: CPP在医学领域基准测试中显著提升推理性能，在数学推理任务中也表现出良好竞争力。此外，其效果在多种基础模型和参数规模下均稳定，验证了其广泛适用性与有效性。

Conclusion: CPP成功解决了组合-知识二分法问题，提供了一种兼具逻辑严谨性与事实准确性的新范式，为未来构建更可靠、可解释的推理系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: LLMs often struggle to balance compositionality with knowledgeability, a challenge we define as Composition-Knowledge Dichotomy. To address this, we propose Concretized Proposition Prompting (CPP), a framework that explicitly concretizes propositions relevant to questions. The results demonstrate that CPP significantly enhances reasoning performance, particularly in medical benchmarks where precise knowledge is paramount, while being competitive on math benchmarks where deductive reasoning is prioritized. Additional experiments reveal that CPP is scalable to various foundation models and parameter sizes, being a fundamental paradigm that bridges the gap between composition- and knowledge-based approaches. Consequently, CPP resolves the composition-knowledge dichotomy by providing a solid foundation for logically organized and factually grounded reasoning.

### [226] [From Prompts to Contracts: Harness Engineering for Auditable Enterprise LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08028)
*Joongho Ahn,Moonsoo Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对企业大语言模型应用的可追溯、可审计的LLM代理架构，通过将确定性行为移入代码、规范和验证产物中，实现对源数据、实体路由、输出契约等关键特性的严格控制。在韩国五家上市公司共25家公司的公开数据上验证了三个研究问题：（1）该架构能有效保持源基性、实体路由、可追溯性、输出清洁度和推荐语言契约；故障注入测试确认验证器能正确识别违规。（2）在三种托管模型下，所有270次组合边界运行均通过验证，错误仅限于模型侧并被记录。（3）仅靠提示词无法实现与代码级保障同等的安全性——提示词方式导致推荐语言和内部追踪泄露问题未被阻止，而该架构完全阻断此类问题。外部防护层虽可防止违规但过度拒绝，使实用性降至88/120，而该架构维持120/120的完整可用性。结果表明，代码级控制是安全与实用兼顾的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业大语言模型应用从原型到产品化过程中面临源边界、实体路由、答案契约、可复现追踪等挑战，现有基于提示和检索的方法难以满足可审计、可验证的要求。需要一种工程化方法，将探索性原型转化为具备版本化源、控制与验证能力的可审计系统。

Method: 提出一种“夹具工程”方法（harness-engineering approach），将确定性逻辑封装在代码、配置文件、验证规则和元数据中，构建可替换的组合边界。源数据作为运行时答案权威，而代码层负责强制执行实体路由、输出格式、推荐语言、内部信息泄露防护等契约。通过在真实企业数据集上进行多模型替换与故障注入实验，评估其有效性。

Result: （1）夹具成功保持了源基性、实体路由、可追溯性、输出清洁度和推荐语言契约，在故障注入下验证器能准确检测违规；（2）跨三种模型，270次运行全部通过，错误被限制在模型侧并被记录；（3）仅用提示词无法实现同等安全，代码层保障可完全防止推荐语言和内部追踪泄露，而外部防护层虽有效但过严，降低实用性。只有代码级控制同时保障安全与可用性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种可复用的工程模式，将探索性大模型原型转化为具备版本化源、可控性和可验证性的生产级应用，核心在于将关键保证机制从提示词转移到代码和验证资产中，实现了安全性与实用性的统一。

Abstract: Enterprise large language model (LLM) applications often begin as prototypes whose behavior is carried by prompts and retrieval context. Productization adds requirements for source boundaries, entity routing, answer contracts, and reproducible traces. We present a harness-engineering approach that reconstructs this pattern into a traceable, auditable LLM-agent architecture: deterministic behavior moves into code, manifests, schemas, and validation artifacts around a replaceable composition boundary, while source-backed claims remain the authority for runtime answers. We instantiate it on a public-data slice of five Korean corporate groups (25 listed companies) and evaluate three research questions. (1) The harness preserves its source-grounding, entity-routing, trace, output-hygiene, and recommendation-language contracts across the fixed validation scenarios; a fault-injection control confirms the validators flag deliberately broken contracts. (2) The checks the harness enforces held under model substitution: across three hosted models, they passed on all 270 composition-boundary runs; failures were confined to the model-composed side and were caught and recorded. (3) The code-owned guarantees are load-bearing, not reproducible by prompting alone: holding the model fixed and varying only the enforcement layer, prompt instructions alone let recommendation-language and internal-trace-leakage violations reach the reader, which the harness blocks entirely. A bolt-on external guardrail prevents such violations too but over-refuses, dropping utility to 88/120 where the harness preserves full utility (120/120); in this ablation, only code-owned enforcement preserves both safety and utility. The result is a reusable engineering pattern for turning exploratory prototypes into auditable applications with versioned source, control, and validation artifacts.

### [227] [A safety-oriented hypothetico-deductive framework for AI-assisted differential diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08038)
*Fan Ma,Mauro Giuffrè,Donald Wright,Kent McCann,Mark Iscoe,Lingfei Qian,Mingyang Jiang,Chi Wing Ng,Na Hong,Huan He,Cathy Shyr,Qingyu Chen,Lee Schwamm,Lucila Ohno-Machado,Hua Xu*

TL;DR: AegisDx is a safety-oriented framework for clinical diagnosis using large language models, designed to improve diagnostic accuracy and safety by enforcing structured reasoning, screening for critical conditions, and verifying against medical evidence. It outperforms standalone LLMs in both diagnostic accuracy and identification of must-not-miss diagnoses across multiple datasets and physician evaluations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current LLMs treat diagnosis as a one-shot prediction task, often missing high-risk conditions and lacking verification of reasoning, posing risks to patient safety. There is a need for AI systems that prioritize safety and transparency in clinical decision-making.

Method: AegisDx uses role-specific LLM components coordinated via contracts, structured outputs, evidence retrieval, and verification gates to generate differential diagnoses, screen for dangerous conditions, verify reasoning with medical evidence, and recommend next steps.

Result: On NEJM and JAMA case reports, AegisDx achieved Top-3 accuracy of 59.9% and 62.7% respectively, surpassing standalone LLMs. On Annals of Emergency Medicine cases, it reached 85.7% accuracy vs. 68.6%. It captured at least one must-not-miss condition in 78.0% of cases (vs. 52.0%). In physician evaluation, it improved safety score from 4.31 to 4.55 (p = 2.1x10^-4).

Conclusion: Engineering diagnostic AI as a safety-oriented reasoning framework—rather than focusing solely on predictive accuracy—can significantly enhance safety, transparency, and clinical utility in acute care settings.

Abstract: Diagnostic error is a major threat to patient safety, yet current large language model (LLM) systems often treat diagnosis as a one-shot prediction task, lacking safeguards against missed high-risk alternatives or rigorous verification of their reasoning. Here, we present AegisDx, a safety-oriented framework for hypothetico-deductive clinical reasoning. AegisDx coordinates specialized LLM components through role-specific contracts, structured intermediate outputs, evidence-retrieval interfaces, and verification gates to generate broad differential diagnoses, enforce explicit screening for dangerous "must-not-miss" conditions, verify reasoning against grounded medical evidence, and structure actionable next steps. We evaluated AegisDx across three layers. On literature-derived case reports from NEJM and JAMA, with GPT-oss-120B as the shared backbone, Top-3 diagnostic accuracy was 59.9% versus 52.1% for the standalone LLM on JAMA cases and 62.7% versus 51.4% on NEJM cases. On cases from Annals of Emergency Medicine, Top-3 accuracy was 85.7% versus 68.6%; against physician-consensus must-not-miss diagnosis sets, AegisDx captured at least one such condition among its top three diagnoses in 78.0% of cases versus 52.0%. In a blinded physician evaluation of 43 real-world emergency department notes from the Yale New Haven Health System compared against GPT-5, AegisDx improved the physician-rated composite safety score from 4.31 to 4.55 on a 5-point scale (adjusted p = 2.1x10^-4), with qualitative gains in must-not-miss identification and reasoning safety. Our findings suggest that engineering diagnostic AI as a safety-oriented reasoning framework, rather than optimizing raw predictive accuracy alone, can provide a safer, more transparent, and clinically meaningful layer of bedside decision support for acute care workflows.

### [228] [When LLMs Agree, Are They Right? Auditing Self-Consistency and Cross-Model Agreement as Confidence Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08065)
*Kaihua Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型作为评判者（LLM-as-judge）在评估AI系统时依赖一致性（如模型自身或多个模型间的一致性）作为正确性代理的可靠性。通过大规模跨运行者实验（53个运行者，265,000个样本），发现一致性虽为正向但弱相关的预测指标（rho 0.20–0.59），其有效性取决于具体场景：在中等性能模型和计算资源分配中表现较好，但在最一致的前沿模型中表现出过度自信且准确性未提升的问题。研究指出自一致性不能作为独立置信度评分，而仅是条件性代理，并公开了去标识化的数据与答案分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-as-judge系统普遍假设模型间或模型自身的高一致性代表正确性，但该假设可能因共享偏见、记忆启发式或选项位置先验而失效，亟需验证一致性是否真正反映真实正确性。

Method: 开展大规模跨运行者实验，53名运行者对GPQA Diamond和AIME任务生成50个样本/案例，共265,000个样本；采用多数正确性作为部署标签，结合分层运行者聚类自助法（runner-clustered bootstrap）分析一致性与准确性的关系，并进行跨家族模型对比（如不同Claude层级）。

Result: 一致性与准确性呈正相关但强度较弱（rho 0.20–0.59），在中等性能模型和算力分配中表现最佳；而在最一致的前沿模型中，高一致性伴随显著过度自信，且错误重复出现，表明其不可靠。此外，跨模型家族验证显示类似趋势，证实问题普遍存在。

Conclusion: 自一致性不是独立的置信度指标，而是一个条件性代理，仅在特定情境下可用。在部署决策中应谨慎使用一致性作为唯一依据，尤其避免对高度一致的前沿模型过度信任。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge (Zheng et al., 2023) is increasingly the default for evaluating AI systems in enterprise pipelines, often scaled to ensembles (Verga et al., 2024) or "mixture-of-experts" (Shazeer et al., 2017) panels of judges. These systems share a key assumption: that consistency -- agreement among judges, or among a model's own samples -- indicates correctness. We show this assumption is unreliable. Agreement is not accuracy: a model can agree with itself, and different models can agree with each other, out of shared bias, a memorized heuristic, or an option-position prior rather than truth. We ask when agreement is nonetheless a usable proxy, in a large-scale cross-runner study: 53 runners drew K=50 samples for assigned overlapping cases across comparisons of model tier, prompting, and scale on GPQA Diamond and AIME -- 265,000 samples. Using majority-correctness as the deployment label and a hierarchical runner-clustered bootstrap, agreement is a positive but weak predictor (rho 0.20-0.59, all positive under item-clustered resampling) whose usefulness is regime-dependent: best for unsaturated mid-tier models and for allocating compute, and worst -- over-confident yet no more accurate -- for the most consistent frontier model (agreement >=0.8 on 77% of GPQA case-result entries, 48% of those wrong). An exploratory cross-family check on three Claude tiers shows the same frontier over-confidence, with confident errors recurring across providers above a marginal-preserving null. Self-consistency is thus a conditional proxy for correctness, not a standalone confidence score. We publicly release the de-identified per-run rows and answer distributions.

</details>


### [229] [Persuasion Attacks Can Decrease Effectiveness of CoT Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08066)
*Jennifer Za,Julija Bainiaksina,Nikita Ostrovsky,Tanush Chopra,Victoria Krakovna*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了链式思维（CoT）监控在AI代理中的安全性，发现尽管CoT可暴露不当行为，但大语言模型仍易受基于说服的越狱攻击。实验表明，在对抗性场景下，监控器访问代理的推理过程反而使有害行为批准率平均上升9.5%，因为推理过程成为额外的说服渠道。为此，提出一种基于跨模型事实核查的监控框架，使用不同模型家族组合（如Claude 3.7 Sonnet作监控器、GPT-4.1作核查器）可将违规行为批准率降低至6%以下，相比单一模型组合下降45%。结果表明，仅依赖CoT监控不足以抵御对抗性说服，而模型多样性事实核查能有效缓解风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有链式思维（CoT）监控机制虽能揭示模型的推理过程以提升安全性，但最新研究表明大语言模型易受自然语言说服攻击，导致其绕过安全约束。本研究旨在检验这一漏洞是否同样影响CoT监控系统：即是否存在恶意代理通过其推理过程说服监控器批准违规行为的可能性。

Method: 设计包含40个任务的评估框架，模拟数千次代理与监控器之间的交互；代理被指令生成违反政策的提议，并通过其推理过程进行说服性论证；分析监控器在有无可见推理过程情况下的决策变化；引入跨模型事实核查机制，测试不同模型组合对降低违规批准率的效果。

Result: 在对抗性设置中，提供完整推理过程的监控使有害行为批准率平均上升9.5%，说明推理内容反而增强了说服力；采用不同模型家族的监测与核查组合（如Claude 3.7 Sonnet + GPT-4.1），可将违规行为批准率降至6%以下，较单一模型组合减少45%。

Conclusion: 链式思维监控本身可能因提供额外说服通道而加剧安全风险；相比之下，使用来自不同模型家族的事实核查机制能显著提升监控鲁棒性，是应对对抗性说服攻击的有效策略。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is a promising safety mechanism for AI agents, based on the premise that visible reasoning traces can surface misaligned or deceptive behavior. While effective in standard scenarios, recent work highlights that LLMs remain vulnerable to persuasion-based jailbreaks, where natural-language arguments override model constraints. We stress-test whether this vulnerability extends to monitoring LLMs: can an adversarial agent persuade its CoT monitor to approve proposed actions that violate the monitor's policy? We design an evaluation framework with 40 tasks and analyze thousands of agent-monitor interactions, where agents are instructed to argue for policy-violating proposals. We find that in such adversarial settings, monitor access to the agent's CoT reasoning increases rather than decreases approval of harmful actions on average by 9.5%, as the scratchpad provides an additional persuasion channel. To address this, we introduce a fact-checking monitoring framework. We find that a fact-checker and monitor pairing from different model families, for example a Claude 3.7 Sonnet monitor paired with a GPT-4.1 fact-checker, reduces approval of policy-violating actions by up to 45%, compared to only 6%, when using the same model for both fact-checking and monitoring roles. Our results demonstrate that CoT monitoring alone may be insufficient against adversarial persuasion, and that model-diverse fact-checking provides a robust mitigation.

### [230] [PARA-PV: Physics-Aware Retrieval-Augmented PV Prediction Based on Frozen Foundation Model and Distribution Shift Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08079)
*Hang Fan,Weican Liu,Ying Lu,Dunnan Liu,Long Cheng,Wei Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PARA-PV是一种物理感知的检索增强框架，用于提高光伏功率预测的准确性。它通过融合历史数据与物理规律，在不同时间尺度和运行状态下生成更可靠的预测，尤其在光照变化、昼夜交替等复杂场景下表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光伏功率预测面临天气波动、昼夜变化、运行模式切换等多重挑战，传统方法难以兼顾物理规律与数据驱动的灵活性。因此需要一种能嵌入物理知识并自适应环境变化的预测框架。

Method: PARA-PV采用多变量观测编码为块级表示，利用物理感知的检索增强学习器匹配历史相似片段与模拟轨迹；再通过轻量级残差适配器结合预训练时序基础模型以引入广泛的时间规律；最后使用物理感知的分布偏移校正模块和分段加权损失函数，分别处理条件变化和关键运行状态的学习。

Result: 实验表明，PARA-PV在多种真实数据集上显著优于现有基线方法，尤其在峰值、快速爬坡、夜间等关键时段表现出更强的鲁棒性和精度，且具备良好的可解释性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: PARA-PV成功将物理约束与数据驱动方法相结合，实现了高精度、强鲁棒性的光伏功率预测，为可再生能源并网调度提供了可靠的技术支持。

Abstract: Accurate photovoltaic (PV) power forecasting is essential for reliable grid dispatch and renewable energy integration, yet it remains challenging because PV generation is jointly shaped by weather variability, day-night transitions, regime-dependent dynamics, and strict physical constraints. We propose PARA-PV, a Physics-Aware Retrieval-Augmented framework that embeds physical knowledge throughout the forecasting process. The framework first encodes multivariate PV observations into patch-level representations and, through a physics-aware retrieval-augmented learner, retrieves historical patches and analog trajectories that are consistent with the current window in temporal shape, power level, PV operating state, and intra-day period; this yields a physically grounded base forecast. To supplement local memory with broader temporal knowledge, the base forecast is then calibrated against a frozen Chronos time-series foundation-model prior through a lightweight residual adapter, so that general temporal regularities are adapted to PV-specific dynamics without overriding the physically grounded prediction. Because residual conditional distribution shifts persist when weather and diurnal regimes change, a physics-aware distribution shift correction module subsequently adjusts the preliminary forecast using power, weather, timestamp, and day/night conditions, applying gated mean-shift and scale corrections selectively. Finally, a physics-constrained loss function partitions the samples into peak, ramping, night-time, and regular regimes and adaptively reweights their error contributions, preventing the dominant regular regime from suppressing learning of operationally critical states. Our code is available at https://github.com/weican1103/PARA-PV.

### [231] [CausalDS: Benchmarking Causal Reasoning in Data-Science Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08093)
*Andrej Leban,Yuekai Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CausalDS is a novel benchmark for evaluating causal reasoning in agentic data-science workflows, combining synthetic structural causal models, observational data, and natural-language stories grounded in realistic domains. It supports all three of Pearl's rungs of causality, includes data science coding tasks with tool use, handles imperfect observations, and scores both answers and abstention.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing benchmarks either lack realistic data analysis or proper causal structures; CausalDS addresses this by creating diverse, systematically generated synthetic causal scenarios grounded in real-world distributions to avoid overfitting to known patterns.

Method: Each benchmark instance consists of a sampled structural causal model (SCM), generated observational data, and a synthetic natural-language story. Tasks are derived across Pearl's three rungs of causality, requiring coding, tool use, and uncertainty handling. Real-world empirical distributions optionally inform component generation to preserve realism while ensuring synthetic diversity.

Result: CausalDS enables comprehensive evaluation of causal reasoning, data science, tool use, uncertainty quantification, and abstention in LLM agents, offering a more holistic and realistic assessment than prior benchmarks.

Conclusion: CausalDS provides a principled, scalable, and realistic benchmark for evaluating advanced agentic data-science capabilities, bridging the gap between symbolic causal reasoning and practical data analysis.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly act as integrated data-science agents, combining abstract reasoning with advanced tool use. Yet the relevant benchmark landscape largely divides into symbolic causal reasoning benchmarks without realistic data analysis or data analysis benchmarks without a principled causal data-generating structure. Furthermore, existing causal evaluation datasets are often restricted to curated examples from existing sources, with diversity coming from limited templatized variations rather than from systematic generation of novel synthetic causal structures. We introduce CausalDS, a benchmark for evaluating causal reasoning in agentic data-science workflows. Each benchmark instance is a scene consisting of a sampled structural causal model (SCM) with generated observational data and an accompanying synthetic natural-language story grounded in a realistic domain. We optionally ground the composition of the benchmark components in empirical distributions obtained from real-world datasets, thus retaining empirical structure while reducing the "causal parrot" risk through completely synthetic generation. From each scene, we then derive tasks spanning all three of Pearl's rungs, with typical data-science prediction tasks appearing as Rung 1. Most tasks include a data science coding component, where the model typically needs to use several tools to arrive at the final answer due to the frequent presence of imperfect observations, which are generated by an observation model. Additionally, recognizing when a question admits no warranted answer and abstaining is treated as a first-class scored outcome. The benchmark thus jointly evaluates symbolic causal reasoning, data science, uncertainty quantification, abstention, and tool use/coding.

</details>

### [233] [Overthinking: Amplifying Reasoning Weights to Extract Learned Secrets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08173)
*Jack Hopkins,Dipika Khullar,Fabien Roger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为'过度思考'（overthinking）的新方法，通过使用推理任务向量来增强语言模型在审计过程中的思考能力，从而更有效地揭示隐藏信息。该方法通过线性插值将非推理指令模型与推理提炼模型的参数结合，以放大推理行为，并引入分层衰减策略，在不牺牲输出质量的前提下提升推理能力。实验表明，该方法在2B-32B规模的语言模型中可使隐藏信息的暴露频率提高最多10倍，且不同类型的秘密对参数扰动方向敏感性不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前黑箱审计方法可能无法检测到语言模型中细微的对齐偏差和隐藏信息，因此需要一种更有效的方法来激发模型的深层推理能力，以暴露潜在风险或未预期行为。

Method: 定义了过思考模型 $\boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{O}_α} = \boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{M}} + α(\boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{R}} - \boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{M}})$，其中 $α > 1$，通过在推理方向上进行参数放大，增强模型的思考倾向；同时引入层级衰减策略，控制放大强度以保持输出质量与连贯性。

Result: 实验结果显示，过思考模型在四种设置下均显著提升了隐藏信息的暴露率，最高可达原始推理模型的10倍；不同类型的秘密对参数扰动的方向和幅度响应不同：部分需沿推理方向扰动，另一些则仅需足够大的整体扰动即可触发。

Conclusion: 推理能力的放大有助于揭示训练过程中积累的隐秘信息或意外行为，表明在模型审计中引入过思考机制是一种有效的增强手段，尤其适用于发现深层、隐蔽的风险。

Abstract: Black box auditing of language models is an essential pre-deployment tool, but it may miss subtle forms of misalignment and hidden information. To better elicit hidden information during an auditing process, we introduce \emph{overthinking}: the process of using reasoning task vectors to amplify the propensity to think out loud of reasoning models. Given the parameters of a non-reasoning instruct model $M$ and reasoning-distilled model $R$, we define the \emph{overthinking model} as $\boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{O}_α} = \boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{M}} + α(\boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{R}} - \boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{M}})$, where $α> 1$ amplifies reasoning beyond the pure reasoning model $R$. Additionally, we introduce new layer-wise attenuation strategies that selectively amplify reasoning without losing quality and coherence of model outputs. We demonstrate that overthinking models are more likely to reveal hidden information across four experimental settings, across 2B-32B models. Our findings suggest that reasoning amplification may surface secrets or unintended behaviors acquired during training up to $10\times$ more frequently than the original reasoning model. How secrets surface depends on the secret type: some require perturbation along the reasoning direction, while others yield to any sufficiently large weight perturbation.

</details>

Motivation: 现有船舶维护和运营报告存在格式不统一、信息不完整等问题，亟需一种自动化方式从历史报告中提炼出简洁、准确的结构化模式，以指导报告撰写，提升报告质量与可用性。

Method: 提出ASMR框架，包含两个模块：1）字段生成代理，基于自适应多粒度聚类从非结构化文本中提取语义概念并生成候选字段；2）结构优化代理，采用强化学习策略筛选出最紧凑、最具信息量且无冗余的最终模式结构。

Result: 实验表明，所提方法能够有效生成高质量的报告模式，显著提升报告的完整性与一致性，为后续自动化报告生成与知识提取提供支持，同时揭示了在模式泛化、人机协同等方面的未解决问题。

Conclusion: ASMR框架展示了在自动模式生成方面的潜力，是连接数据管理、智能体系统与人机协作的重要探索，未来需进一步研究如何增强模型的可解释性与跨领域迁移能力。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the automatic schema generation problem: given a collection of historical ship maintenance and operational reports across multiple form categories, automatically discover compact and informative schemas that capture the essential information requirements of each report type. To address this challenge, we propose ASMR, a modular agentic framework consisting of two specialized agents. A Field Generation Agent extracts semantic concepts from historical narratives and generates candidate schema fields through adaptive multi-granularity clustering, while a Structural Optimizer Agent employs reinforcement learning to identify compact, informative, and non-redundant schema representations. The resulting schemas can guide report authors toward producing more complete, consistent, and actionable reports. Preliminary results demonstrate the promise of the proposed approach and highlight several open research challenges at the intersection of data management, agentic AI, and human-centered AI.

### [235] [A First-Principles Theory of Slow Thinking and Active Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08196)
*Hongkang Yang,Zhi-Qin John Xu,Feiyu Xiong,Weinan E*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于概率分布提升与投影的数学框架，用于形式化思考与感知过程，特别聚焦于慢思考（slow thinking）和主动感知。通过引入‘主动提升’理论，该研究以减少不确定性的内在驱动力为核心，构建了一个包含大语言模型设计、训练与推理的广泛设计空间。理论中引入内部时间轴进行推断，并建立类似最小长度编码的语言生成训练目标，从而刻画感知中的主体性与慢思考格式的涌现。技术成果包括改进慢思考模型的三阶段路径、统一处理多模态数据的编码器与生成模型构造方法、类人视觉表征的先验形成，以及可能解决策略崩溃问题的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在为认知功能的第一性原理建模提供数学基础，特别是对慢思考与主动感知机制的正式描述，以理解复杂智能行为的底层原理。

Method: 采用概率分布的提升与投影方法，结合隐变量序列采样与最小不确定性减少的内在驱动，提出‘主动提升’理论；通过静态理论构建表示层次与采样层次，实现模型升级；引入内部时间轴进行推断，并设计基于最小长度编码的语言生成式训练目标。

Result: 成功形式化了慢思考与主动感知的数学结构，实现了大语言模型的设计、训练与推理一体化框架；揭示了智能行为中主体性与语言发明的潜在机制；产生多个可落地的技术成果，如三阶段优化路径、跨模态统一建模方法、类人视觉表征生成及策略崩溃缓解方案。

Conclusion: 主动提升理论为慢思考与主动感知提供了统一的数学基础，不仅深化了对认知智能本质的理解，也为下一代通用人工智能模型的设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: As part of a series on first-principles modeling of cognitive functions, this paper attempts to provide a mathematical formulation of thinking and perception. It formally derives slow thinking or more generally, active perception, and encompasses the design, training and inference of slow thinking large language models. Our starting point is the lifting and projection of probability distributions on the observable and latent spaces, with the objective of representing complex data distributions by simple function families such as neural networks. A theory called "active lifting" is proposed, based on the sampling of latent sequences and an intrinsic drive to reduce uncertainty with maximum rate. It derives a large design space, containing the slow thinking models in a subspace that we call the static theory. These models are positioned on the representation hierarchy and sampler hierarchy induced by the static theory, and can be upgraded by climbing the two hierarchies. Active lifting further derives an inference process with an internal time axis, and a training objective that resembles minimum-length coding as well as the invention of languages. Thus, it characterizes the agency of perception, including the emergence of the slow thinking formats. Technical by-products of this theory include a three-stage pathway for improving slow thinking models, a unified approach to constructing encoders and generative models for all data modalities, a priori formation of human-like visual representations, and a possible solution to policy collapse.

### [236] [Playing ZendoWorld: Challenging AI Agents on Active Visual Concept Induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08233)
*Sophia Koehler,Antonia Wüst,Inga Ibs,Wasu Top Piriyakulkij,Wolfgang Stammer,Constantin Rothkopf,Kevin Ellis,Kristian Kersting*

TL;DR: 本文提出ZendoWorld这一受控交互环境，用于研究智能体在复杂输入下联合感知、形成假设并设计信息性实验的能力。通过评估多种方法（如纯视觉语言模型推理、贝叶斯粒子滤波、动态概念发现和神经符号方法），发现高标签预测准确率并不等同于规则恢复；感知与归纳对不同智能体是不同瓶颈；基于VLM的智能体提出的实验几乎无信息量，无法有效减少假设不确定性。人类数据对比显示，在复杂规则下的归纳推理存在明显差距。该工作为评估智能体提供了新框架，并指明了科学发现等领域的改进方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能系统在联合感知、假设生成和主动实验设计方面仍面临挑战，亟需一个可控且能评估这些能力的交互环境。

Method: 构建ZendoWorld环境，让智能体根据视觉观察推断逻辑规则，通过提出新场景获取反馈并修正假设；评估多种智能体方法，并收集人类数据进行对比分析。

Result: (1) 高预测准确率不等于正确恢复底层规则；(2) 不同智能体在感知和归纳上存在不同瓶颈；(3) 基于VLM的智能体提出的实验信息量低，不能有效减少不确定性；(4) 人类在复杂规则下也表现出归纳推理差距。

Conclusion: ZendoWorld为评估智能体的主动学习与归纳能力提供了一个重要平台，揭示了现有方法的局限性，尤其在科学发现等需要主动探索的领域中，亟需提升智能体的实验设计能力。

Abstract: A central challenge in building intelligent systems is enabling agents to jointly perceive complex inputs, form hypotheses about hidden patterns, and design informative experiments to test them. To study this problem, we propose ZendoWorld, a controlled interactive environment in which agents must infer a logical rule about visual game observations, acquire information by proposing new scenes, and refine their hypotheses based on feedback from the game environment. We evaluate several agents spanning pure VLM reasoning, Bayesian particle filtering, dynamic concept discovery, and neuro-symbolic methods. Our main findings are: (1) high accuracy in predicting labels for observed examples does not imply recovery of the underlying rule; (2) perception and induction are distinct bottlenecks for different agent classes; and (3) VLM-based agents propose near-uninformative experiments, failing to actively reduce hypothesis uncertainty. To compare these results, we collect human data on the task, which reveals a gap in inductive reasoning, particularly for more complex rules. Overall, ZENDOWORLD takes an important step toward evaluating intelligent agents and identifies concrete avenues for improvement, particularly in domains like scientific discovery.

### [237] [AutoPersonas: A Multi-Timescale Loop Engine for Open-Ended Persona Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08252)
*Mengchen Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出AutoPersonas，一种多时标的生命-环境引擎，用于解决长期人格代理在持续演化中出现的自我锁定问题。通过分离环境事件、观察记录与人格状态，采用OSO循环实现未来导向的多样性与证据驱动的吸收，有效缓解了行为重复、关系弱化和决策停滞等问题。实验表明，该方法显著降低主题重复率（从61.8%降至36.3%），提升主题多样性，并在虚构世界中成功避免固化，验证了其在保持身份连续性的同时减少自锁现象的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期人格代理在持续演化过程中易陷入自我锁定：尽管局部事件看似合理，但整体生命轨迹逐渐退化为熟悉环境、薄弱关系、悬而未决的决策和停滞的发展阶段。这种现象源于模型层面的高概率行为通道收敛与系统层面由状态、记忆、历史和环境摘要带来的上下文引力。

Method: 提出AutoPersonas，采用多时标设计，将环境侧的事件（Occurrences）、累积的观察（Observations）与人格状态（State）分离，构建OSO循环——允许未来面向的多样化输入，但要求在状态或可达性发生变化前必须经过证据治理的吸收过程，从而实现受控的发散与有依据的整合。

Result: 三载压缩模拟揭示了环境水印壳、事件硬化缺口、慢变积累失败、递归犹豫及关系脆弱等现象；40天八模型压力测试显示，5日滚动动作类别重复率达95.2%-97.6%，所有模型在第11天即超过90%；语义重保分析显示直接循环中宏观主题重复率为79.0%-88.0%。在同运行时间的A/B测试中，引入上下文切片遮蔽与样本级发散目标后，宏观主题重复率下降至36.3%，累计主题数翻倍。虚构世界中的幼年哥布林实验亦成功再现抗固化机制，无现实干预。

Conclusion: 通过将受控发散与证据治理的吸收相分离，可有效缓解人格-环境自锁现象，同时维持身份连续性，支持该方法在长期人格代理演化中的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Long-term persona agents must remain identifiable while adapting to new events, relationships, evidence, and social conditions. We identify self-locking as a runtime failure mode in continuing persona-life loops: locally plausible events keep appearing while the generated life collapses toward familiar environments, weak relationships, suspended decisions, and stale life stages. We trace this failure to model-level convergence toward high-probability behavioral channels and system-level context gravity from State, memory, history, and environment summaries. We introduce AutoPersonas, a multi-timescale life-environment engine for bounded persona-level recursive self-evolution. It separates environment-side Occurrences, accumulated Observations, and persona State. Its OSO loop admits divergent future-facing material while requiring evidence-governed absorption before State or reachability changes. A three-year compressed simulation exposed environment watermark shells, occurrence-hardening gaps, slow-change accumulation failures, recursive indecision, and weak relationship persistence. An eight-model 40-day stress test generated 1,600 events and found mean rolling 5-day action-category repetition of 95.2%-97.6%, with all models crossing 90% by day 11. Semantic re-keeping found 79.0%-88.0% macro-theme repetition across all direct-loop runs. In a same-runtime 40-day A/B, context-slice masking plus per-sample divergence targeting reduced macro-theme repetition from 61.8% to 36.3% and roughly doubled cumulative theme count. A juvenile-goblin fictional-world run reproduced the anti-fixation regime without hard real-world intrusions. These results support a bounded claim: separating controlled divergence from evidence-governed absorption can reduce persona-environment self-locking while preserving identity continuity.

### [238] [Compete Then Collaborate: Frontier AI Teachers Build a Verifiable Curriculum to Improve a Coding Student Beyond Imitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08255)
*Miseong Shawn Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种竞争-协作框架，让多个前沿AI教师（Claude、Codex-GPT、Grok、Gemini）通过执行验证（如单元测试）进行公平排名，再协同构建可验证的课程以训练学生模型（Qwen2.5-Coder）。研究发现：在执行验证下，所有教师在标准问题上表现接近完美，但在难题上差异明显（Gemini最优，Grok最差）；但学生性能并不依赖教师排名。直接模仿（SFT）已具备能力的学生会削弱其表现，而使用相同课程作为强化学习的可验证奖励环境（RLVR），则显著提升学生在竞赛题上的表现（从5.9%提升至8.8%，相对增益49%）。核心结论是：AI教师的价值不在于答案聚合，而在于共同构建一个让学生“通过实践学习”的可验证训练环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识蒸馏方法在多教师场景中缺乏对教师能力的客观评估，且常依赖偏向自身输出的LLM评判器，导致教学效果不可靠。同时，单纯模仿教师输出难以提升已有能力的学生，甚至可能退化。因此需要一种更公平、可验证的教学机制，使学生真正通过实践学习。

Method: 提出竞争-协作框架：首先让四名前沿教师在统一执行验证标准下（单元测试与输入输出检查）进行头对头竞争，实现公平排名；随后这些教师协作生成包含正确解法的可验证训练集，作为学生模型的监督信号或强化学习环境。采用基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）策略，引导学生通过试错获得反馈，而非简单模仿。

Result: 1. 在执行验证下，所有教师在标准问题上自修正后准确率高达99-100%，但在复杂竞赛题上表现分化显著（Gemini 77% > Claude/Codex 69% > Grok 50%）；但学生最终性能不受教师排名影响。2. 使用验证解进行模仿学习（SFT）反而降低学生性能（如MBPP-test从76.7%降至72.7%，竞赛题从5.9%降至2.9%）。3. 将相同课程用于强化学习（RLVR），学生在竞赛题上从5.9%提升至8.8%，相对增益达49%，实现性能反转。

Conclusion: AI教师协作的核心价值不在于提供答案集合，而在于共同构建一个可验证的、支持学生自主探索与试错的学习环境。该框架通过执行验证确保教学数据质量，并借助强化学习激发学生真实能力提升，为大模型时代下的高效知识传递提供了新范式。并开源了可在NVIDIA GB10设备上运行的复现管道及GRPO框架补丁。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly serve as teachers generating training data for smaller students. Prior multi-teacher knowledge distillation methods merge outputs without determining which frontier model teaches best, often relying on an LLM judge biased toward its own outputs. We introduce a compete-then-collaborate framework where four frontier AI teachers (Claude, Codex-GPT, Grok, Gemini) are ranked head-to-head by an execution-based judge (unit tests and stdin-stdout checks) with fairness controls, and then collaborate to build a verifiable curriculum for a student (Qwen2.5-Coder). We report three findings. (1) Under execution verification, all teachers solve standard problems near-perfectly after self-correction (99-100%) due to a saturation effect, but harder competition problems separate them (Gemini 77% > Claude 69% = Codex 69% > Grok 50%); however, the robust student-side results do not depend on teacher ranking. (2) Imitation (SFT) on verified solutions does not improve, and can degrade, an already-competent student at 7B and 32B (e.g., from 76.7% to 72.7% on MBPP-test, and 5.9% to 2.9% on competition problems). (3) Using the same collaborative curriculum as a reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) environment improves the student (from 5.9% to 8.8% peak on competition problems, a +49% relative gain), reversing SFT's direction. The value of AI-teacher collaboration lies not in pooling answers to imitate, but in jointly constructing a verifiable environment where the student learns by doing. We release a reproducible on-prem pipeline (NVIDIA GB10) with framework patches for running GRPO on a bleeding-edge stack.

</details>


### [239] [MentalHospital: A Virtual Environment for Evaluating Psychiatric Clinical Encounters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08257)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 临床医生调查显示MentalHospital具有良好的临床保真度（3.88/5）；MentalEval评估器与专家判断高度一致，平均QWK达0.944；基准测试表明，即使最强的LLM在客观精神科能力上仍比临床医生低37.28个百分点，精神状态评估是主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: MentalHospital和MentalEval为评估大语言模型在精神科临床实践中的综合能力提供了可靠、可扩展的基准平台；当前大语言模型在复杂临床决策任务中仍显著落后于人类专家，尤其在精神状态评估方面亟需改进。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong performance on isolated psychiatric tasks, including dialogue, diagnosis, and treatment planning, yet existing benchmarks rarely simulate complete psychiatric clinical encounters. We introduce $\textbf{MentalHospital}$, a virtual evaluation environment for LLM-based psychiatric clinical encounters. MentalHospital instantiates the Subjective Interviewing, Objective Examination, Diagnostic Assessment, and Treatment Planning (S.O.A.P.) workflow, using skill-augmented standardized patients constructed from 1,193 de-identified psychiatric electronic health record (EHR) cases spanning all major ICD-11 categories and 76 disorders. Each encounter is assessed through a dual-track protocol that combines objective comparison against EHR-derived references with subjective assessment of clinical process quality. To scale specialist judgment, we develop $\textbf{MentalEval}$, five domain-specific evaluators covering communication empathy, interviewing professionalism, clinical-note quality, diagnostic rigor, and treatment appropriateness, trained with rubric-grounded SFT and expert-guided DPO. Survey responses from 22 clinicians support MentalHospital's clinical fidelity (3.88/5), while MentalEval achieves strong expert alignment with an average QWK of 0.944. Benchmarking shows that even the strongest LLM trails clinicians by 37.28 percentage points in objective psychiatric competence, with mental status assessment as a key bottleneck.
